KṣemendraviracitāBodhisattvāvadānakalpalatā namaḥ sarvajñāya  prabhāsāvadānam cittaṃ yasya sphaṭikavimalaṃ naiva gṛhṇāti rāgaṃkāruṇyārdre manasi nikhilāḥ śoṣitā yena doṣāḥ akrodhena svayamabhihato yena saṃsāraśatruḥsarvajño sau bhavatu bhavatāṃ śreyase niścalāya  KAvk sacchāyaḥ sthiradharmamūlavalayaḥ puṇyālavālasthitirdhīvidyākaruṇāmbhasā hi vilasadvistīrṇaśākhānvitaḥ saṃtoṣojjvalapallavaḥ śuciyaśaḥpuṣpaḥ sadāsatphalaḥsarvāśāparipūrako vijayate śrībuddhakalpadrumaḥ  KAvk jāyate jagaduddhartuṃ saṃsāramakarākarāt matirmahānubhāvānāmatrānuśrūyate yathā  KAvk asti prabhāvatī nāma hemaharmyagṛhairvṛtā purī prabhāvatīva dyaurvimānaiḥ puṇyakarmaṇām  KAvk vidyādharavatī siddhagandharvagaṇasevitā gāṃ śritā śakranagarī sukṛtena satāmiva  KAvk sevitā satataṃ satyavratadānadayāmayaiḥ rājadhānīva dharmasya puṇyāvasathaśālinī  KAvk abhūdbhūtilakastasyāṃ prabhāso nāma bhūpatiḥ saprabhā sādarairyasya kīrtirabhyarcyate suraiḥ  KAvk guṇasaurabhasaṃbhārāḥ sarvāsāṃ hariṇīdṛśām yadyaśaḥpuṣpamañjaryo yātāḥ karṇavataṃsatām  KAvk upāyajñasya yasyājñāṃ suvaṇakusumojjvalām mālāmiva mahīpālā maulicakreṣu cakrire  KAvk taṃ kadācitsamāsīnamabhyetya bhuvaneśvaram uvāca kṣitivinyastajānurnāgavanādhipaḥ  KAvk deva divyadyutirdantī gṛhīto smābhiradbhutaḥ tvatkīrtiśravaṇādbhūmimairāvaṇa ivāgataḥ  KAvk dvāri sthito sau dviradastridaśārhaḥ pradṛśyatām bhṛtyānāṃ prabhunāṃ dṛṣṭaḥ saphalo hi pariśramaḥ  KAvk etadākarṇya nṛpatirnirgatyāmātyasaṃmataḥ dadarśa dviradaṃ dvāri kailāsamiva jaṅgamam  KAvk uddāmasaurabhāhūtairbhramarairgaṇḍaḍiṇḍimaiḥ śṛṅgārābharaṇodāraṃ vasantamiva sevitam  KAvk dantaparyantaviśrāntakaraṃ mīlitalocanam smarantaṃ vindhyakadalīsallakīkānanaśriyaḥ  KAvk agastyaśāsanād yātaṃ bhuvi kuñjararājatām sphuratsaptacchadāmodaṃ vindhyācalamivonnatam  KAvk taṃ vilokya kṣitipatirdantastambhavibhūṣitam lakṣmīvilāsabhavanaṃ vismayādityacintayat  KAvk aho navanavotkarṣā nirmāṇāścaryaśālinām karmaṇāmanavacchinnā saṃsārasargasaṃtatiḥ  KAvk amanthena sudhāmbhodheranāyāsena vāsukeḥ anākarṣeṇa śailasya kenāyaṃ janito gajaḥ  KAvk atha hastimahāmātraṃ saṃyātaṃ nāma bhūpatiḥ ādideśārcitādeśaṃ gajo yaṃ damyatāmiti  KAvk tadādiśya mahīpāle yāte ntaḥpuramandiram nāgaṃ jagrāha saṃyātaḥ sarvaśikṣābharakṣamam  KAvk sa sacchiṣya iva prājñaḥ prāgjanmābhyāsayantritaḥ nītastena prayatnena sarvaśikṣāvinītatām  KAvk bahudānanirudvegaḥ śaktyutsāhayutaḥ kṣamī ripupraghātasugatiḥ sa rājñastulyatāṃ yayau  KAvk damyakriyāsamuttīrṇaṃ tatastaṃ kuñjareśvaram nareśvarāya saṃyātaḥ kṛtakṛtyo nyavedayat  KAvk dṛṣṭvā tamaṅkuśāyattaṃ nirvikārabalodayam utsāhaśikharārūḍhaṃ mene rājā jayaśriyam  KAvk sa saṃjātapraharṣotthadākṣyaśikṣādidṛkṣayā tamāruroha sotsāhaḥ sahasrāṃśurivodayam  KAvk saṃyāto tha gajendrasya mantrīva vaśavartinaḥ sarvamaṇḍalasaṃcāracāturthaṃ samadarśayat  KAvk gajaprekṣāprasaṅgena mṛgayākelilālasaḥ rājā nijotsāhamiva vyagāhata vanaṃ mahat  KAvk sa yayau ratnakeyūrakiraṇairdūrasarpībhiḥ sallakīpallavavarairdignāgānāhvayanniva  KAvk vrajantaṃ tatra dadṛśustaṃ vane vanadevatāḥ praharṣavismayākīrṇakarṇapūrīkṛtekṣaṇāḥ  KAvk śabarīkabarīpāśapuṣpasaurabhanirbharāḥ vaindhyā vasuṃdharādhīśaṃ marutastaṃ siṣevire  KAvk atha vindhyopakaṇṭheṣu svacchandasukhaśākhiṣu smṛtvā vilāsavṛttāntaṃ gajaḥ sotkaṇṭhatāṃ yayau  KAvk kariṇyāḥ premabaddhāyā gandhamāghrāya sa dvipaḥ nītiṃ nṛpa ivotsiktastatyājāṅkuśayantraṇām  KAvk savegaṃ dhāvatastasya rāgākṛṣṭasya daṇḍinaḥ vimūḍhasyeva saṃsāre nābhavadviratiḥ kkacit  KAvk dṛṣṭvā prabhañjanajavaṃ kuñjaraṃ rājakuñjaraḥ vrajantaṃ jātasaṃdehaḥ saṃyātamidamabravīt  KAvk aho batāyaṃ bhavatā vinayaṃ grāhito gajaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ prayāto vaimukhyaṃ gurorasyāṅkuśasya yaḥ  KAvk bhramatīva diśāṃ cakramanuyāntīva pādapāḥ pādanyāsabhareṇāsya kṣībeṇādhūrṇate kṣitiḥ  KAvk asmin deva ivākāle prayāte pratikūlatām sarvāḥ puruṣakārasya niṣphalā yatnavṛttayaḥ  KAvk vacaḥ śrutveti saṃyātaḥ prabhorāyātasādhvasaḥ śikṣāpavādavailakṣyāduvāca racitāñjaliḥ  KAvk deva sarvakriyāyattaḥ kuñjaro yaṃ mayā kṛtaḥ kariṇīgandhamāghrāya yātaḥ kiṃ tvadya vikriyām  KAvk nopadeśaṃ na niyamaṃ na dākṣiṇyaṃ na sādhutām smaranti jantavaḥ kāmaṃ kāmasya vaśamāgatāḥ  KAvk kena ratirasotsiktā viṣayābhimukhī matiḥ adabhraśvabhravibhraṣṭaśaolakulyeva vāryate  KAvk śarīraśramaśikṣāyāṃ damakāḥ kuśalā vayam manoniyamaśikṣāyāṃ munayo pi na paṇḍitāḥ  KAvk rāgādagaṇitāyāsaḥ skhalitākhilasaṃyamaḥ eṣa dhāvatyamāreṇa mūrkhaḥ khala iva dvipaḥ  KAvk vṛkṣaśākhāṃ samālambya tyajemaṃ pṛthivīpate vyasanī patitaḥ satyaṃ pātayatyeva durjanaḥ  KAvk saṃyātasya vacaḥ śrutvā tatkālasadṛśaṃ nṛpaḥ tenaiva sahitaḥ śākhāmālalambe mahātaroḥ  KAvk avatīrya taroraśvamāruhya nṛpatau gate prāpyāliliṅga kariṇīṃ vigāhya gahanaṃ gajaḥ  KAvk tataḥ śāntasmaro hastī dinairabhyetya saptabhiḥ svayamālānasaṃbaddhastasthau bhuktvā yathāsukham  KAvk śikṣāsaṃyamayantritaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā svayamāgatam saṃyātaḥ kauśalotkarṣaharṣādrājñe nyavedayat  KAvk rāgavāgurayākṛṣṭaḥ prayayau yaḥ smarāturaḥ śikṣāyāmavisaṃvādī so yaṃ prāptaḥ svayaṃ gajaḥ  KAvk saṃketayantrito vaśyo rasajñaḥ sallakībhuvām saṃtaptalohakavalaṃ gṛhṇāti vinaye sthitaḥ  KAvk eṣa kāmarasākṛṣṭaḥ kaṣṭāṃ vikṛtimāyayau punaḥ prakṛtimāpannaḥ praśāntamadanajvaraḥ  KAvk śakyā damayituṃ deva siṃhavyāghragajādayaḥ na tu rāgāsavakṣībaviṣayābhimukhaṃ manaḥ  KAvk etadākarṇya bhūpālastattatheti vicintayan uvāca satyamucitaṃ saṃyāta kathitaṃ tvayā  KAvk apyasti kaścilloke smin yena cittamadadvipaḥ nītaḥ praśamaśīlena saṃyamālānalīnatām  KAvk ityukte de vatāviṣṭaḥ saṃyātastamabhāṣata deva santi jagatkleśaniḥśeṣonmūlanodyatāḥ  KAvk vivekālokitā loke vairāgyajanitāgrahāḥ śamasaṃtoṣaviśadā buddhā eva prabodhinaḥ  KAvk iti buddhābhidhāṃ śrutvā samyaksaṃbodhicetasaḥ rājñaḥ prāgjanmajābhyāsapraṇidhānamajāyata  KAvk vinimajjajjagadidaṃ saṃsāre makarākare saṃtārayeyaṃ saṃbodhimuktaḥ kuśalasetunā  KAvk athocurdevatā vyonmastaṃ śuddhāvāsakāyikāḥ samyaksaṃbodhisaṃbuddho bhaviṣyasi mahāmate  KAvk iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rājā virajasāṃ varaḥ jātismaro divyacakṣuḥ prayayau bodhisattvatām  KAvk atha sa vipulasattvastattvanikṣiptacakṣurbhavajalanidhimajjatsarvabhūtānukampī abhavadabhinavodyatsaṃvuditsāhayogāddalitakuśalasetuḥ sattvasaṃtāraṇāya  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ prabhāsāvadānaṃ nāma prathamaḥ pallavaḥ samāptaḥ  śrīsenāvadānam te jayanti jagatyasjin puṇyacandanapādapāḥ chedanirgharṣadāhe pi ye parārtheṣu nirvyathāḥ  KAvk gaṇanīyā guṇagaṇairastyariṣṭābhidhā purī spardhayā śakranagarī yasyā na syādgarīyasī  KAvk tasyāṃ babhūva bhūpālaḥ śrīsena iti viśrutaḥ samagraguṇaratnānāṃ ratnākara ivākaraḥ  KAvk paropakāraśaktasya caturasya prabhāvataḥ anuraktā diśaḥ sarvāḥ sūryasyeva prabhāvataḥ  KAvk yaśobhi śobhitaṃ yena dhanadānasugandhibhiḥ gajaiśca bhūtidhavalairjagatkalpadrumairiva  KAvk kalālayo pi saralaḥ saralo pi mahāmatiḥ yo babhūva prajāpuṇyairmatimānapyavañcakaḥ  KAvk yāvattapati tigmāṃśuryāvadvahati mārutaḥ tāvadājñā ca kīrtiśca yasyāpratihatābhavat  KAvk śamavyāyāmaviduṣāṃ ṣasṅguṇajñānacakṣuṣām yaṃ dvādaśasahasrāṇi mantriṇāṃ paryupāsate  KAvk tasmindharmapare rājñi babhūva sukṛtī janaḥ bhartṛtulyā bhavantyeva guṇaiḥ striya iva prajāḥ  KAvk tasya puṇyādhivāsena janāstridivagāminah vimānaiḥ śakranagarīṃ niḥsaṃcārāḥ pravakrire  KAvk dṛṣṭvā manujalokena suralokasamāvṛtim jātavairaḥ kṣitiopatau śatakraturacintayat  KAvk seneva lakṣmī vasudheṣu cārasyāścaryakartavya ca dattanityam kalyāṇaśīlena ca sa rvacetanyapravyahāsāmana asmakāśca   KAvk tasyākhaṇḍitacetasaḥ daddhidvalyānubhāvapām  kartavyā dhairyājijñāsā mayā māyāvidhāyinā  KAvk iti saṃcintya suciraṃ sarvairanugataḥ suraiḥ rūpaṃ śakraḥ parāvartya martyalokamavātarat  KAvk atrāntare prajākāryaparyālocanatatparaḥ rājyarakṣāgururmantrī nṛpamūce mahāmatiḥ  KAvk rājan virajasā rājyarājamānena nirjitaḥ nirvyājadānairbhavatā lajjate tridaśeśvaraḥ  KAvk parasya pūrṇaguṇatāmātmanastadvihīnatām dṛṣṭvā ko nāma nāyāti mātsaryasya vidheyatām  KAvk īrṣyālavaḥ parotkarṣasaṃgharṣasya juṣo janāḥ prāyeṇodvegamāyānti mahatām sukṛteṣvapi  KAvk sarvasvadānamaryādādānavyasanino stu te putradārātmadāne tu saṃkalpo hyatisāhasaḥ  KAvk dṛśyante dāruṇāste te svapnāḥ sādhvasahetavaḥ jagataḥ sūcyate tīvraṃ yaiścūḍāmaṇikhaṇḍanam  KAvk daivajñānāṃ pravādaśca śrūyate tattvavādinām śarīraṃ pṛthivīpālo dāsyatīti suduḥsahaḥ  KAvk śarīradānaṃ sarvārthisārthanaiṣphalyakāraṇam sarvaprado bhavatyeva tiṣṭhan kalpamahīruhaḥ  KAvk tasmādasmānmahīpāla virama tyāgasāhasāt rakṣāratnaṃ hi jagataḥ prajāyattaṃ vapustava  KAvk iti mantrireṇoktamākarṇya vasudhādhipaḥ tamūce sattvadhavalasmitaghautādharadyutiḥ  KAvk uktaṃ hitaṃ mhāmātya bhavatā sacivocitam kiṃ tvarthinavaimukhyasaṃtāpaṃ nāhamutsahe  KAvk dehīti vādiṣu giro niṣedhaparuṣākṣarāḥ sphuranti vadane yeṣāṃ sajīvāste gatāsavaḥ  KAvk idamasmādavāpsyāmītyādhāya hṛdi yācakaḥ prāpyaḥ prayāti vaimukhyaṃ yasmin kiṃ tena jīvatā  KAvk dhigjanma puṇyahīnasya tasya niṣkaruṇātmanaḥ yasyārtajanasaṃtāpaśravaṇe śītalaṃ manaḥ  KAvk etadarthamayaṃ kāyaḥ sāpāyo pi satāṃ priyaḥ yatkasyacit kkacid yāti kadācidupakāritām  KAvk śrutveti nṛpatervākyamamātyaḥ sattvaśālinaḥ novāca kiṃcidacalāṃ vicintya bhavitasyatām  KAvk tataḥ kadācidbhūbhartustasya līlāvihāriṇaḥ jāyāṃ jayaprabhāṃ nāma ratiṃ ratipateriva  KAvk dūrād yadṛcchayāyātāṃ cittasāsaṅgavāgurām muniradhyāpakaḥ kāntām dadarśa vinimeṣadṛk  KAvk prāgjanmābhyāsasaṃbandhasnehātparicitāmiva tāṃ dṛṣṭvā sa dhṛteḥ prāpa dhairyarāśiranīśatām  KAvk tasya vītaspṛhasyāpi vāsanollasitaṃ manaḥ utsṛjya bhavavaimukhyamabhilāṣabhuvaṃ yayau  KAvk iyaṃ hi satatasyūtā saṃtataprītitantubhiḥ nāpaiti sarvajantūnāṃ prāgjanmābhyāsavāsanā  KAvk tadāśramapadaṃ prāptaḥ samāptādhyayanavrataḥ śiṣyo māṇavakaḥ prāha dakṣiṇā gṛhyatāmiti  KAvk sa tamūce na me vatsa vane vṛttiḥ prayojanam tathāpi yadi nirbandhaḥ śrūyatāṃ yadabhīpsitam  KAvk śrīsenasya kṣitipateyadi devī jayaprabhā labhyate bhavatā dātuṃ tadasau mama dakṣiṇā  KAvk ityuktaṃ guruṇā śrutvā śiṣyaḥ kampitamānasaḥ aśakyaprārthanālābhe saṃśayākulito bhavat  KAvk sa gatvā satatasvecchāvivṛtadvāramarthinām viveśa svairaviśrambhabhavanaṃ bhūbhṛtāṃ prabhoḥ  KAvk alabhyārthārthanādainyacintātikliṣṭamānasaḥ namrānano tivailakṣyād vīkṣamāṇa iva kṣitim  KAvk taṃ dṛṣṭvārthinamāyātaṃ prahṛṣṭo bhūnmahīpatiḥ sudhāpradānasannaddhasamudbhūtirivāmbudhiḥ  KAvk kiṃ tavepsitamityuktvā pūjitaḥ sa mahībhujā uvācānucitākhyānavailajjaskhalitākṣaraḥ  KAvk anarthitaparaḥ pūrvamarthikalpatarostava garvarthamarthitāṃ yātaḥ sudurlabhapade pyaham  KAvk mama vidyāvrate pūrṇe dakṣiṇābhimatā guroḥ rājan jayaprabhā devī dīyatā yadi śakyate  KAvk ityukre muniśiṣyeṇa sahasaiva mahīpateḥ snehadānasāviddhaṃ dvidhābhūtamabhūnmanaḥ  KAvk sa jagād vijaṃ dantajyotiṣāgravisāriṇā gṛhyatāṃ dayitā svacchavāsasācchādayanniva  KAvk avicārya mayā deyamīpsitaṃ tava yadguroḥ viyogacakitaṃ cetaḥ satyaṃ na gaṇayāmyaham  KAvk ityuktvāhūya dayitām rājā rājīvalocanām sadā hṛdayasaṃsaktām jīvavṛttimivāparām  KAvk nivārito pi guruṇā viyogavyasanāgninā niṣiddho pyativṛddhena snehena smarabandhunā  KAvk pradadau muniśiṣyāya sahasā hariṇīmiva kimetaditi sāyāsasaṃtrāsataralekṣaṇām  KAvk dattāyāṃ tyāgaśīlena priyāyāṃ pṛthivībhujā cakampe tyāgabhīteva bhūmirlolābdhimekhalā  KAvk yatkṛte durdaśāṃ dehe sehire duḥsahāmapi indracandrādayo devāstāh priyāḥ kasya na priyāḥ  KAvk śīlaṃ keciddhanaṃ keciddharmaṃ kecittapaḥ pare lajjāṃ kecittanuṃ kecittyajanti yoṣitāṃ kṛte  KAvk yadeva rāgasarvasvaṃ puṃsāṃ jīvitajīvitam tadeva sphīṭasattvānām dāne tṛṇalavāyate  KAvk tāmādāya gate tasmin virahākulito nṛpaḥ viraheṇa sukhadveṣī manobhava ivābhavat  KAvk śiṣyeṇa munirānītām dṛṣṭvā bhūpativallabhām rahitāṃ jīviteneva paralokabhuvaṃ gatām  KAvk gāḍhānuśayasaṃtaptaḥ paraṃ lajjānimīlitaḥ acintayadanaucityamātmanaḥ karmavuplavāt  KAvk aho nu bālakeneva mayā kevalacāpalāt niḥśankamayaśaḥpaṅke svayamātmā nipatitaḥ  KAvk iyaṃ prajānāṃ jananī bharmyāṇāṃ dharmakāriṇā varṇāśramagurorjāyām mayā duḥkhānale rpitā  KAvk kiṃ tu nākalitaṃ śīlaṃ na smṛtaḥ saṃyamo mayā gaṇitaṃ naiva vairāgyaṃ viveko nāvalokitaḥ  KAvk aho tra nirvicārāṇāṃ sanmārgavimukhaṃ manaḥ asaṃyamāsavakṣībamapatheṣveva dhāvati  KAvk iti saṃcitya sa munirvailakṣyakṣapitadyutiḥ abhyetya rājadayitāmuvāca vinatānanaḥ  KAvk samāśvasihi he mātarna śokaṃ kartukarhasi bhavitavyatayaivāyaṃ kleśaste durnayaśca me  KAvk tyaktvā hi śramasaṃtāpamasya tīrataroradhaḥ adhunaiva nijaṃ dhāma sahāsmābhirgamiṣyasi  KAvk ityukte muninā devī sīktevāmṛtavṛṣṭibhiḥ avāptajīvitadhṛtistatyāja bhayasaṃbhramam  KAvk śrutvaitat tridivavyāpi dātuścaritamadbhutam rājñaḥ sattvadayām jñātuṃ vāsavaḥ samupāyayau  KAvk bhakṣitādhaḥśarīrārdho vyāghreṇa vijane vane putraiścaturbhirākrandairgṛhīto brāḥmaṇākṛtiḥ  KAvk prasravadbhūrirūdhiro lambamānāntramaṇḍalah kṛccheṣvapagataprāṇaḥ pāpairiva dṛḍhīkṛtaḥ  KAvk pratyagrāmiṣyāgandhena kravyādairbhṛśamanvitaḥ lubdhapārthivacaurotthairanarthairarthavāniva  KAvk nagarāntaramāsādya sa yayau puravāsinām kāruṇyadainyaduḥkhārto smayāvismayahetutām  KAvk sa śoka iva sākāraḥ sa trāsa iva duḥsahaḥ vidadhe sādhvasāyāsaṃ sahasā paurayoṣitām  KAvk so rthisaṃdarśanasthānasthitasyātha mahīpateḥ putrarūpaiścaturbhistairnyasto gre mañcikārpitah  KAvk taṃ dṛṣṭvā vaiśasāveśaviṣamakleśavihvalam niṣkūṇitānanavano jano bhūnmīlitekṣaṇah  KAvk sa kampavihvalaṃ vakṣo muktamudyamya dakṣiṇam bhujaṃ jagāda bhūpālaṃ vyathāśithilitākṣaraḥ  KAvk svasti tubhyaṃ mahīpate brāhmaṇo hamimāṃ daśām tīvrapāpa iva prātaḥ paśya māṃ karuṇānidhe  KAvk saṃsāreghoragahane vane vyāghreṇa bhakṣitaḥ jīvāmyavaśyabhogyatvādduḥkhasyāsya garīyasaḥ  KAvk asminnapi vipattāpe tīvrakleśasahiṣṇavaḥ vimuñcanti na māṃ prāṇāḥ sahṛdaḥ sajjanā iva  KAvk dadāti yadi te kaścit chittvā dehārdhamātmanaḥ tatte jīvitamastīti māmūce vyomadevatā  KAvk  ko dadāti jagatyasmin jīvitaṃ karuṇānidhe prāyeṇa svasukhānveṣī parārthavimukho janaḥ  KAvk sarvadā sarvadātāraṃ dīnavyasanabāndhavam dehadāne pyavimukhaṃ tvāmasmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  KAvk ekastvameva loke smin jātaḥ sukṛtapādapaḥ nirvyājamādarodāraṃ dānaṃ yasya phalodgatiḥ  KAvk kimanyairvā vadānyasya kīrtitairbhavato guṇaiḥ dānamevāhato yasya loke sukṛtaḍiṇḍimaḥ  KAvk āpannārtiparitrāṇapavitracaritavratāḥ prāyante puṇyapaṇyena vipatkāle bhavadvidhāḥ  KAvk amandānandasuhṛdo haricandanaśītalāḥ haranti santaḥ saṃtāpaṃ dakṣiṇāḥ pavanā iva  KAvk pūrṇendusundarādasmāduditā vadanāttava jyoptsneva jīvayatyeva vāṇī pīyūṣavarṣiṇī  KAvk ityuktastena sahasā hṛdi saṃkrāntatadvyathaḥ saṃmohamūrcchitaṃ rājā tamūce vācamākulam  KAvk samāśvasihi muñca tvaṃ bahyaṃ prāṇaviyogajam prayacchāmi śarīrārdhamavicāryaiva te dvija  KAvk dhanyasy ayātyayaṃ kāyaḥ paropakṛtaye kṣatim kṣaṇakṣayī hi deho yaṃ rakṣyamāṇo pi nākṣayaḥ  KAvk ityuktavati bhūpāle samutkampitamānasaḥ vajrāhata ivovāca mahāmātyo mahāmatiḥ  KAvk aho nu sāhasābhyāsādāyāsavyasanī prabhuḥ hitaṃ na gaṇayatyeva prajāpuṇyaparikṣayāt  KAvk prajānāṃ bhūtaye śaktaḥ ko nyastvatsadṛśo guṇī yadbhaktimukharo bhṛtyaḥ śrotā kartā ca bhūpatiḥ  KAvk na karoti hitaṃ svāmī gajalīlānimīlitaḥ gaṇanīyāḥ subhṛtyānāmiyatyo bhogasaṃpadaḥ  KAvk bhānti t e suciraṃ karṇe yaiḥ kṛtā madhumañjarī kalyāṇakarṇikākīrṇā vāṇī vinayavādinām  KAvk rākṣaso yaṃ piśāco ca chadmanā brāhmaṇākṛtiḥ rakṣāratnasya jagatāṃ śarīrairarthitām gatah  KAvk yadi nāma na māyeyaṃ kṛtā tena mahīyasī tatkathaṃ kṛttadehasya kṣaṇamapyasti jīvitam  KAvk avicāryaiva sukṛtaṃ kriyate durgraheṇa yat tadātmapīḍāoparuṣaṃ paraloke pi niḥsukham  KAvk śakyameva sadā dadyādaśakyaṃ dīyate katham sarvasvadehadānādipravāda eva śobhanaḥ  KAvk karṇāmṛtamidaṃ dūrādyanmahārthimaṇipradaḥ saṃprāptānāṃ punastatra pānamasyānyato rthinām  KAvk rakṣyaḥ sarvaprayatnena pareṣāmapi jīvitaiḥ prajānāṃ jīvitaṃ rājannarthicintāmaṇirbhavān  KAvk prasīda dayasvāsmāsu deva mā sāhasaṃ kṛthāḥ n akācaśakalasyārthe kriyate cātmavikrayaḥ  KAvk ityuktvā pādayoḥ patyuḥ papātāmātyapuṃgavaḥ śarīradānasaṃkalpānnoccacāla ca bhūpatiḥ  KAvk so vadat praṇayasmeracikasaddaśanadyutiḥ jīvitasnehasaṃmohatamah pariharanniva  KAvk kevalaṃ bhaktisaṃyuktamuktaṃ vyaktamidaṃ tvayā na sahe haṃ mahāmātya viprasya prāṇasaṃśayam  KAvk hāraistuṣāraiḥ kamalairmṛṇālairinducandanaiḥ nivartate ntaḥsaṃtāpo nārthivaimukhyaduḥkhajaḥ  KAvk sarvathā sarvaduḥkhārtiharaṇodyatacetasaḥ na bodherantarāyaṃ me sumate kartumarhasi  KAvk janmāntare pi dadato dehaṃ me na vyathābhavat smarāmyatītavṛttasya samyaksaṃbodhicetasā  KAvk purā dṛṣṭvodyatām vyāghrīṃ kṣutkṣāmāṃ potabhakṣaṇe tadrakṣāyai mayā dattaṃ śarīramavikṣariṇā  KAvk śibijanmani cāndhāya dattaṃ netrayugaṃ mayā rakṣitaśca svadehena kapotaḥ śyenakādbhayāt  KAvk candraprabhāvatāre ca raudrākṣāyārpitaṃ śiraḥ sarvasvaputradārādi dattaṃ cānyeṣu janmasu  KAvk ityukte bodhisattven abhūbhujāmātyapuṃgavaḥ na sajīvo n anirjīva ivābhūdvyathitendriyaḥ  KAvk alaṅghyaśāsanenātha rājñā krakacadhārayā niyuktau palagaṇḍākhyau śarīracchedakarmaṇi  KAvk tau tīvraśokavivaśau śakramāyāvimohitau kathaṃcidiva bhūbharturdehacchede samudyatau  KAvk nṛpaternirvikārasya krūrakrakacadhārayā vidāryamāṇe dehārdhe pṛthivī samakampata  KAvk bhraṣṭolkā raktavasanā virghātacyutatārakā dyauḥ saśabdaṃ rurodeva kīrṇāśrukaṇasaṃtatiḥ  KAvk vaiśasālokanedbhūtatīvraduḥkhāsahiṣṇunā tūrṇaṃ rajaḥpaṭeneva raviṇā pihitaṃ mukham  KAvk tasmin prajāh prajānāthe krakacākrāntavigrahe cakranduḥ pūritākrandā digvadhūmiḥ pratisvanaiḥ  KAvk akṣubdhasattvamālokya nṛpaṃ śakro dvihākṛtiḥ vismayānuśayākrāntacittaściramacintayat  KAvk aho mahāmaterasya karuṇākomalaṃ manaḥ prāptaṃ parārthapīḍāsu vajrādapi kaṭhoratām  KAvk sāgarādapi gambhīraṃ merorapi samunnatam tridivādapi sāścaryamaho vṛttaṃ mahātmanām  KAvk ahi prāṇapravāse pi sattvaṃ sattvamahodadheḥ sādhoriva vipatpāte mahattvaṃ nāvahīyate  KAvk iti cintayati kṣipraṃ sahasrākṣe kṣitiprabhoḥ nābheradhaḥśarīrārdhaṃ nikṛttamapatat kṣitau  KAvk sa dvidhābhūtadehoapi harṣotsāhamayo bhavat sarvabhūtaparitrāṇasattvena dhṛtajīvitaḥ  KAvk tadājñayā śarīrārdhe śleṣṭe saṃpūrṇavigrahaḥ svasthakṣatiḥ samutthāya brāḥmaṇastamabhāṣata  KAvk aho virājase rājan pūnjaṃ virajasastava nirvyājadehadānena viśeṣaṃ tu bnhavadyaśaḥ  KAvk tvanmanomaṇivaimalyatulyaṃ kiṃcidakurvataḥ upamānena dāridyramaho mugdhasya vedhasaḥ  KAvk kṛttaḥ suvṛttaḥ saralaḥ parārthe madhurāśayaḥ sahase duḥsahāṃ pīḍāmikṣukāṇḍa ivonnataḥ  KAvk ityuktvā brāhmaṇākāraḥ śakrasta smṛtijanmabhiḥ saṃjīvanaiṣadhijātaiḥ sudhāsyandairapūrayat  KAvk tataḥ prakaṭitākāraḥ paritoṣātpuraṃdaraḥ suśliṣṭanijadehārdhaṃ praśaśaṃsa mahīpatim  KAvk athābmarānnipatitaḥ sitakusumasaṃcayaḥ tatkālollāsitakṣoṇīharṣahāsa ivābabhau  KAvk atrāntare munistasmau priyāṃ jāyāṃ jayaprabhām ādāyābhyetya tadvṛttaṃ jātāścaryo nyavedayat  KAvk pūtayā saṃgataḥ patnayā svakīrtyeva viśuddhayā uvāca pṛṣṭaḥ śakreṇa nikāre nirvikāritah  KAvk tataḥ siṃhāsane divyae viśvakarmavinirmite ratnavarṣasamākīrṇe jambudvīpe sa bhūpatiḥ  KAvk abhiṣiktaḥ surendreṇa prasādya dayitāsakhaḥ dānapuṇyaprabhāvotthakuśalavyāpitaprajaḥ  KAvk samāptasattvasaṃsārasaṃtāraṇakṛtavratah samyaksaṃbodhisaṃbuddhamanāḥ pramudito bhavat  KAvk maitraṃ cetastaruṇakaruṇaṃ sattvasiddhaṃ viśuddhaṃ āpannārtipraśamanaphalasphūītamātmapradānam dṛṣṭvā rājñah pramudasalilakṣālitākṣo vilakṣaḥśakraḥ prāyādamaranagarīṃ pūritāṃ tadyaśobhiḥ  KAvk iti sa vibudhavṛndaiḥ siddhayakṣoragendraiḥ pulakaruciravarcairarcyamānaprabhāvaḥ avanimavanaśaktaḥ kalpayannākakalpāmabahvavibhavaśobhāmāptavān bodhisattvaḥ  KAvk pūrvāvatārasaṃvāde dānotkarṣamudāharan upadeśāya bhikṣūṇāmityāha bhagavān jinah  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ śrīsenāvadānaṃ nāma dvitīyaḥ pallavaḥ  maṇicūḍāvadānam asminnadbhutasarge makarākarajāyamānamaṇīvarte ko pi prakaṭitasugatiḥ puruṣamaṇirjāyate bhavyaḥ  KAvk asti saubhiprabhāpūrakarpūraparipāṇḍuram sāketaṃ nāma nagaraṃ saubhāgyatilakaṃ bhuvaḥ  KAvk sevyaiḥ prabhāsattvamayairgaṅgāvimalamānasaiḥ tīrthairiva sthitaṃ yatra pavitraḥ puṇyakartṛbhiḥ  KAvk yaśaḥkusumite yatra puṇyasaurabhanirbhare ramante sukṛtodyāne nandane puravāsinaḥ  KAvk tatrābhūd bhūpatirbhuriguṇaratnamahodadhiḥ bhīturyaśaḥśaśāṅasya mehacūḍa iti śrutaḥ  KAvk sadā sadāśrayārheṇa kalikālāpahāriṇā kṛtaḥ kṛtayugeneva yena dharmadharo janaḥ  KAvk mahīpatiḥ kṣamāśaktaḥ śrīvṛtaḥ karuṇārataḥ vallabho bhūt prajānāṃ yaḥ prakhyāto vijitendriyaḥ  KAvk amarāsavasaṃpūrṇamahiṃsāsatradīkṣitaḥ dadau yaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ puṇyāmabhayadakṣiṇam  KAvk nirmado yaḥ prabhāve pi vibhave pi priyaṃvadaḥ kṣamāśīlaḥ prabhutve pi yauvane pi jitendriyaḥ  KAvk gambhīreṇonnatimatā śūreṇa śaśikāntinā satpakṣeṇa kṣitibhṛtā yenātanyata vismayaḥ  KAvk rājñastasyādvitīyasya babhūvābharaṇadvayam tyāgapūrṇaṃ ca kāruṇyaṃ tārūṇyaṃ sukṛtaśriyaḥ  KAvk padmākarasya tasyābhūddevī kāntimatī priyā prabhātaśrīriva sadā nirdoṣābhyudayotsavā  KAvk nītiḥ prabhuguṇevena tyāgena śrīrivojjvalā rarāja rājacandreṇa sā śīleneva cārutā  KAvk sadānandanavikhyātayaśaḥprasarayā tayā merūstridivalakṣmyeva babhau bhūmibhṛtāṃ varaḥ  KAvk kāle kalyāṇanilayaṃ bhartuḥ sā garbhamādadhe bhūtyai bhuvanapadmasya divākaramivāditiḥ  KAvk araṇiḥ pāvakeneva velevābdheḥ sudhāṃśunā brahmābjeneva govindanābhirgarbheṇa sā babhau  KAvk tasyā garbhānubhāvena dohadābhimataṃ nṛpaḥ dadau sarvārthisārthebhyo vāñchitābhyadhikaṃ vasu  KAvk punarbhūmibhujā pṛṣṭā dohadaṃ śubhagarbhiṇī sarasvatīva sā cakre svayaṃ saddharmadeśanām  KAvk pūrṇapuṇyamaṇirdharmanidhirvidhisamuddhṛtaḥ vupadvipuladuḥkhebhyaḥ sadā rakṣati rakṣitaḥ  KAvk kāntāradurgeṣu paricyutānāṃ tāpāturāṇāṃ paralokamārge snigdhaḥ pravṛddhaḥ phalapūritāśaḥ chāyātarurdharmasamo sti nānyaḥ  KAvk ālokastimire vipadviṣamaṇiḥ pāte karālambanaṃyācñākalpatarurjagajjayarathaḥ pātheyamanthe pathi duḥkhavyādhimahauṣadhaṃ bhavabhayodbhāntāśayāśvāsanaṃtāpe candanakānanaṃ sthirasuhṛddharmaḥ satāṃ bāndhavaḥ  KAvk ityādi dharmadhavalaṃ śrutvā nṛpavadhūvacaḥ dharmaikaśaraṇaḥ śrīmān babhūva bhuvane janaḥ  KAvk tataḥ kālena saṃpūrṇaṃ dyaurivāmṛtadīdhitim asūta dārakaṃ devī jagattimiradārakam  KAvk ajāyatāsya sahajaścūḍālaṃkaraṇaṃ maṇiḥ prāgjanmāntarasaṃsakto viveka iva nirmalaḥ  KAvk sa babhau subhagastasya mūrdhni puṇyamayo maṇiḥ yasya prabhāprabhāveṇa yāminyo dinatām yayuḥ  KAvk soṣṇīṣasya maṇestasya pīyūṣasyandibindivaḥ nayanti hematām lohaṃ duritaṃ śamayanti ca  KAvk śiśorjātismarasyātha vacasā tasya bhūpatiḥ dadau hema sadārthibhyaḥ sarvaṃ maṇirasodbhavam  KAvk puṣparatnadhvajacchatrapatākāvyajanāṃśukaiḥ apūrayan puraṃ vyonmastasya janmani devatāḥ  KAvk suprakāśoditāśeṣavidyāvidyotitātmanaḥ maṇicūḍa iti khyātaṃ nāma tasyākaronnṛpaḥ  KAvk sa cakārāśayaṃ harṣapīyūṣocchalitaṃ pituḥ abhijātaḥ suto jātaḥ pārijāta ivodadheḥ  KAvk paulomīva jayanteṇa jananī pūjyajanmanā babhau tena kumāreṇa kumāreṇeva pārvatī  KAvk tataḥ kālena sukṛtasopānaiḥ pṛthivīpatau divyadhāmasamārūḍhe maṇicūḍo bhavannṛpaḥ  KAvk arthicintāmaṇestasya dānena paripūrite loke puṇyasukhāloke nārto bhūnna ca yācakaḥ  KAvk tasya bhadragirirnāma babhūvaṃ gajapuṃgavaḥ prabhorivānukāreṇa dānārdrakarapuṣkaraḥ  KAvk taṃ kadācinmahāsthānasthitaṃ bhuvananāyakam bhavabhūtiḥ samabhyāyādbhṛguvaṃśabhavo muniḥ  KAvk divyakānyāṃ samādāya lāvaṇyalalitānanām mūrtāmiva prabhālakṣmīmakṣīṇasya kṣapāpateḥ  KAvk kucayoravivekena rāgeṇa caraṇābjayoḥ netrayoścāpaleneva sā jagatyatilajjitā  KAvk tapaḥśriyeva sahitaṃ taṃ kanyānugataṃ munim aoūjayat prajānāthaḥ kṛtāsanaparigraham  KAvk kanyāpi nṛpamālokya dhīraṃ gambhīrasundaram parapīḍāsu kāruṇyānnyastacāpamiva smaram  KAvk cūḍāratnasya kīraṇairduritakṣayakāribhiḥ likhantaṃ kuṅkumeneva dikṣu rakṣākṣarāvalim  KAvk vikṣepakṣiptamarutā cāmareṇa virājitam socchāseneva sattvena jagatsaṃtāraṇaṃ vinā  KAvk ratnodāreṇa hāreṇa hṛdayagrahakāriṇā pātālavipadāṃ śāntyai śaiṣeṇeva niṣevitam  KAvk vahantaṃ mahatā doṣṇā kṣamāṃ cittena ca kṣamām prayayau sābhilāṣasya vismayasya vidheyatām  KAvk gṛhītvā munirutsaṅge kuraṅgataralekṣaṇām jīvanīṃ tāmanaṅgasya jagād jagatīpatim  KAvk uditena jagannetraśatapatravikāśinā bhavatā bhāti loko yaṃ devena ca vivasvatā  KAvk aho nu tava nāstyeva vibhūtisulabhodbhavaḥ sādhoriva guṇadveṣaḥ saṃmohopacito madaḥ  KAvk lokanāthasya te lokakāruṇyapūrṇacetasaḥ rājan maitrījuṣā kīrtiḥ sthirā pāramitā param  KAvk akhedasaralo dātā nirvyājasukṛto bhavān ata eva viśeṣeṇa mānanīyo manīṣiṇām  KAvk padmodarasamudbhūtā kanyā kamalalocanā homāvaśeṣapayasā vardhiteyaṃ mayāśrame  KAvk gṛhyatāmagramahiṣī patnītve bhavatā nṛpa viṣṇoḥ śrīriva yogyeyaṃ tavaiva puruṣottama  KAvk yajñapuṇyaphalaṃ pūrṇaṃ kālena mama dāsyasi ityuktvā vidhinā rājñe kanyāṃ datvā yayau muniḥ  KAvk priyāṃ padmāvatīṃ rājā ratiṃ prāpyeva manmathaḥ araṃsta rucirodyāne sukṛte puṇyavāniva  KAvk tataḥ kālena sā putraṃ vaṃśavalliva mauktikam asūta padmacūḍākhyaṃ guṇānāṃ darpaṇaṃ pituḥ  KAvk śakrādibhirlokapālairanullaṅghyamahodayaḥ saṃstūyamānacaritaḥ svayaṃ kamalajanmanā  KAvk yaśaḥsaurabhasaṃbhārasaṃpūritadigantaraḥ sarvārthisārthakalyāṇakalanākalpapādapaḥ  KAvk smṛtvā munervacaḥ kāle kartuṃ vipuladakṣiṇām ahiṃsāvasusaṃpūrṇāmājahāra mahīpatiḥ  KAvk tasmin yajñe samājagmuḥ sarvakāmairanargale munayo bhārgavamukhā nṛpā duṣprasahādayaḥ  KAvk vartamāne makhe tasmin niḥsaṃkhyavasuvarṣiṇi rakṣorūpaḥ samuttasthau vahnimadhyāt sureśvaraḥ  KAvk upasṛtya sa bhūpālaṃ kṛśo vikṛtavigrahaḥ kṣuptipāsārdito smīti yayāce pānabhojanam  KAvk śāsanādatha bhūbhartustasmai vividhabhojanam upaninyuḥ paricitāḥ pānaṃ ca paricārakāḥ  KAvk tataḥ kiṃcidvihasyaiva kṣitipaṃ prāha rākṣasaḥ nedamasmatpriyaṃ rājan vayaṃ hi piśitāśanāḥ  KAvk sadyohatasya māṃsena rudhireṇa ca bhūyasā tṛptirutpadyate smākaṃ dīyatāṃ yadabhīpsitam  KAvk sarvakāmaprado sīti tvamahaṃ samupāgataḥ dadāmīti pratiśrutya na niṣedhastavocitaḥ  KAvk iti rakṣavacaḥ śrutvā karuṇakulito nṛpaḥ ahiṃsāniyamenābhūdarthivaimukhyaduḥkhitaḥ  KAvk so cintayattadā daivājjāto yaṃ dharmasaṃśayaḥ na sahe duḥsahāṃ hiṃsāṃ naṃ naiṣphalyamarthinaḥ  KAvk na ca māṃsaṃ śarīrebhyo labhyate vaiśasaṃ vinā nāhaṃ pipīlakasyāpi kāyakleśalavaṃ sahe  KAvk datvāhaṃ sarvabhūtebhyaḥ puṇyāmabhayadakṣiṇam kathamasmai prayacchāmi māṃsaṃ prāṇivadhodbhavam  KAvk iti saṃcitya nṝpatistamūce karuṇākulaḥ svaśarīrasamutkṛttamasṛṅbhāṃsaṃ dadāmi te  KAvk ityukte bhūmipatinā babhūvākulitaṃ jagat na ca dehavyayotsāhaṃ sacivāstasaya sehire  KAvk praṇayādvāryamāṇo pi bhūpālairmunibhistathā dadau svadehamutkṛtya tasmai māṃsamasṛgvasām  KAvk ākaṇṭhaṃ pītaraktena rākṣasena kṣitiprabhoḥ bhakṣyamāṇeṣu māṃseṣu kṣḥaṇaṃ khṣitirakampataḥ  KAvk tataḥ padmāvatī devī patiṃ dṛṣṭvā tathāgatam vilapantī nipatitā mohamūrcchākulābhavat  KAvk manujendrasya devendrastaddṛṣṭvā sattvamūrjitam rakṣorūpaṃ parityajya tamuvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ  KAvk aho nu karmaṇā rājan duṣkareṇa tavāmunā romāñcakañcukākīrṇaḥ kāyaḥ kasya na jāyate  KAvk aho puṇyamasāmānyamaho sattvamanuttaram aho dhariyamamaryādaṃ rājān virajasastava  KAvk duḥkhitāḥ paraduḥkheṣu nirlobhā durlabheṣu ca vipakṣeṣu kṣamāvantaḥ santaḥ sukṛtasetavaḥ  KAvk samunmiṣati ko pyeṣa sattvotsāho mahātmanām trailokyaṃ karuṇārdrāṇāṃ yena yātyanukampyatām  KAvk uktveti divyauṣadhibhistaṃ kṛtvā svasthavigraham prasādya lajjāvanataḥ śakraḥ svanilayaṃ yayau  KAvk tataḥ samāpte vidhivadyajñe rājñāṃ mahīpatiḥ cakre munivarāṇāṃ ca pūjāṃ tridaśapūjitaḥ  KAvk sa ratnavarṣairyajñānte kanyāgrāmapurapradaḥ sahitaṃ tridaśārheṇa hariṇā hemamālinā  KAvk dadaru rājagajaṃ brahmarathākhyāya purodhase yojanānāṃ śataṃ tūrṇaṃ ekenāhnā prayāti yaḥ  KAvk tasmai samarpitaṃ dṛṣṭvā rājñā bnhadragiriṃ gajam abhūdduṣprasaho rājā tatspṛhākṛṣṭamānasaḥ  KAvk prayāteṣvatha bhūpeṣu vismiteṣu makhaśriyā samarpite yajñaphale bhārgavāya mahībhujā  KAvk tamuvāca samabhyetya svastivādapuraḥsaram marīciśiṣyo vāhīkaḥ prāptapūjāsano munoḥ  KAvk rājannadhyayanasyānte gururme gurudakṣiṇām īhate paricaryārthī sāmānyajanadurlabhām  KAvk ekastvameva vidhinā nirmito durlabhapradaḥ bahavo jātu jāyante na loke kalpapādapāḥ  KAvk devī padmāvatī putrasahitā gurave mama tapaḥkṛśāya vṛddhāya dīyatām paricārikā  KAvk ityukte muninā rājā dayitāviprayogajām rujaṃ saṃstabhya manasa tamūce dhairyabhūdharaḥ  KAvk prayacchāmi mune tubhyamīpsītām gurudakṣiṇām sahitāṃ yuvajārena jīvitābhyadhikāṃ priyām  KAvk ityuktvā sasutāṃ tasmai dadau padmāvatīṃ nṛpaḥ svajīvite vinisnehastyāgaḥ sattvamayātmanām  KAvk ādāya rājadayitāṃ virahakleśakātarām saputrāmāśramaṃ gatvā pradadau gurave muniḥ  KAvk atrāntare duṣprasahaḥ kururājaḥ kṣitīśvaram dṛpto yayāce dūtena bhūtyai bhadragiriṃ gajam  KAvk purohitārpitaṃ rājā na dadau d viradaṃ yadā tadā vipulasaunyena svayaṃ yoddhuṃ samāyayau  KAvk balinā kururājena ruddheṣu puravatmasu babhūva bhūmipālasya sainyaṃ raṇarasodbhaṭam  KAvk sa vīrakuñjarahariḥ śakto pyarividāraṇe janakṣayabhayodvignaḥ kāruṇyāt samacintayat  KAvk aho nukūlamitram me rājā duṣprasahaḥ param mātaṅgalobhamohena sahasā śatrutāṃ gataḥ  KAvk snehāntāḥ sujanaiḥ snehā niḥsnehāntāśca madhyamaiḥ durjanairghoravairāntā bhavanti prāṇahāriṇaḥ  KAvk aho bibhavalibhena kṣaṇakṣayiṇi jīvite samudyamo yamasmākaṃ paraprāṇanipātane  KAvk hiṃsayāpapraśāntānām saktānāṃ kalikarmasu raṇaraktābhiṣiktānāṃ bhaktārtho yaṃ samudyamaḥ  KAvk sevāvikrītajīvānāṃ caṇḍapiṇḍārthināmayam kalaho duḥsahaḥ kruryapiśunānāṃ śunāmiva  KAvk aho vibhavalubdhānām parasaṃtāpaśītalāḥ svasukhāyaiva dhāvanti nṛśaṃsacaritā dhiyaḥ  KAvk ye yudhi siddhisaṃnaddhā raktāntām bhuñjate śriyam kutaḥ kruratare teṣāṃ hṛdaye karuṇākaṇaḥ  KAvk eṣa duṣprahaso rājā lubdho vibahvamohitaḥ na vadhyaḥ sāparādho pi kāruṇyāyatanaṃ mama  KAvk iti cintayatastasya kāruṇyāta kānanaiṣiṇaḥ pratyekabuddhāścatvāraḥ svayaṃ vyomnā samāyayuḥ  KAvk prātapūjāsanāḥ śrutvā sarvajñāstatsamīhitam rājñaḥ praśamaśīlasya prasannāstattvamūcire  KAvk saṃmohapaṭalāndheṣu saṃsāriṣu dayālutā śobhate tava bhūpāla sattvalokavivekinaḥ  KAvk kriyatāmīpsitaṃ rājan bodhau buddhirnidhīyatām saṃprati pratirodhe smin vanameva vigāhyatām  KAvk svairanirjnarajnaṅkārakīrṇasaṃtoṣaśīkarāḥ viviktakānanoddeśāḥ śamināmeva vallabhāḥ  KAvk ityuktvānugrahadhiyā vidhāyāsya viyadgatim prabhāprasādhitadiśaste tena sahitā yayuḥ  KAvk yāteṣu svapadaṃ teṣu himavattaṭakānanam saṃprāpya pṛthivīpālaḥ prayatapraśamo bhavat  KAvk vivekavimalāstasya dhiyaḥ sattvavatāmiva babhuḥ priyanivuḥ pūrṇanirvāṇyo vanabhūmayaḥ  KAvk bhūdharāntarite tasmin sahasā bhūpabhāsvati śuśucurmohatimiraprāptaśokaprajāḥ prajāḥ  KAvk tatastatsacivā jagmurmarīcaṃ munimāśrame śaktaṃ rājyasya rakṣāyai rājaputraiṃ yayācire  KAvk muninā nirvikāreṇa dattamādāya mantriṇaḥ rājasūnuṃ svanagare cakruḥ sainyasamudyamam  KAvk muninā nirvikāreka dattamādāya mantriṇaḥ subhaṭāgresarah prāpa kururājaṃ raṇājire  KAvk sa tena hatavidhvastabhagnasyandnakuñjarah palāyanaparitrāṇaḥ prayayauḥ hastināpuram  KAvk balinā rājaputreṇa jite duṣprasahe yudhi mantribhistadbhujanyastā bhūmiḥ śeṣadhṛtiṃ yayau  KAvk rājño duṣprasahasyātha kālena kaluṣātmanah babhūvāvṛṣṭidurbhikṣamarakopalpavaḥ pure  KAvk sa vicintyānutāpārtastībrāṃ janapadāpadam na viveda paritrāṇaṃ viphalasvastikakriyaḥ  KAvk pṛṣṭhā vipatpratīkāraṃ tenāmātyāstamūcire duḥsaho yaṃ mahārāja prajānāṃ vyasanodbhavaḥ  KAvk maṇicūḍasya bhūbharturyadi cūḍāmaṇiḥ prabho labhyate sa sudhāsyandī teneyaṃ tīryate vipat  KAvk cārebhyaḥ śrutamasmābhiḥ sa rājā himavattaṭe sthitaḥ saṃsāravaimukhyavivekavimalāśayaḥ  KAvk arthitaḥ sa dadātyeva viśvacintāmaṇirmaṇim putradāraśarīrādi nādeyaṃ tasya kiṃcana  KAvk iti mantrivacaḥ śrutvā tathetyādhārya cetasi sa dvijān maṇiyācñāyau visasarja tadantikam  KAvk asminnavasare rājā maṇicūṣaścaran vane marīcerāśramopāntamavāpa vipulaṃ muneḥ  KAvk devī padmāvatī tatra phalamūladhṛtavratā vrajantī vijane bhītā vipune muniśāsanāt  KAvk śabarairmṛgayāyātairdṛṣṭvā kaṣṭadaśāṃ śritā jughṛkṣubhiḥ kampamān ācukrośa karuṇasvaram  KAvk ākarṇya karuṇākrande kurarūīkūjitopamam hā rājan maṇicūḍeti trāyasveti suduḥsaham  KAvk sahasābhidrutaḥ kāntām dadarśa nṛpatirnijām rāhusaṃtrāsitasyendordyutiṃ nipatitāmiva  KAvk vītarāgāṅgavasanāṃ nirañjanaparigrahām vadantīmiva saṃbhogasaṃyogānāmanityatām  KAvk tāṃ rājahaṃsasugatām vihārastanamaṇḍalām aśrukāṣāyanayanāṃ vilokya karuṇāvanīm  KAvk saṃsāracaritāścaryavicāreṣvapi karkaśam kṛpākṛpāṇīnirlūnamivāsīrbhūpatermanaḥ  KAvk ekākīnaṃ vane devī vigatacchatracāmaram dṛṣṭvā nāthamanāthaiva manovṛttiriva niḥsukhatāṃ gatā varjitā rājyabhogena rājarāja na rājate  KAvk etadārkarṇya nṛpatistaṃ vijñāya manobhavam antarāyaṃ vivekasya pratyabhāṣata sasmitaḥ  KAvk jānāmi tvāmahaṃ kāmamakāmaṃ śamasaṃyame saṃtoṣavatām ko nāma bhavatā na vimohitaḥ  KAvk itivādini bhūpāle sahasāntarite smare babhūva viklavā devī taptā virahavahninā  KAvk duḥkhitāṃ tāmārtaduḥkhāṃ patibhogaviyoginīm uvācāśvāsayan rājā jāyāṃ jitamanobhavaḥ  KAvk devi dharmakriyāyuktā na śokaṃ kartumarhasi duḥkhāvasānī virasaḥ sarvo yaṃ bhogacibhramaḥ  KAvk dehināṃ yaditāsaṅgāstaraṅgataralāyuṣām lolapadmapalāśāgraskhalajjalalavākulāḥ  KAvk imā muhūrtanartakyaḥ kālameghataḍillatāḥ saṃsārasarparasanā vilāsacapalāḥ śriyāḥ  KAvk bhogakṣaṇenaiva viyogarogo vibhūtayaḥ svapnavivāhatulyāḥ vātāhatā dīpaśikhā sukhaśrīrunmattanṝtyaṃ bhavavṛttametat  KAvk sarvopajīvyā karuṇā na lakṣmīḥ dharmaḥ prakāśaḥ satataṃ na dīpāḥ yaśāṃsi ramyāṇi na yauvanāni sthirāṇi puṇyāni na jīvitāni  KAvk satyavratastāmiti sāntvayitvā visṛjya jāyāṃ nilaye maharṣeḥ cacāra saṃsāraparāṅbhukhānāṃ saṃtoṣapuṇyeṣu tapovaneṣu  KAvk tadāgatāste tvarayā visṛṣṭāḥ pañca dvijā duṣprasahena rājñā viyogaḥduḥkhodbhavamārtanādam  KAvk ayaṃ maṇirmastakamūlajanmā niṣkṛttya tūrṇaṃ pratigṛhṛtāṃ me dhanyo smi yadyarthijanasya duḥkhakṣaye kṣaṇaṃ kāraṇatāṃ vrajāmi  KAvk ityuktamātre vasudhādhipena kṣitīśaṃ kṣatajokṣitāṅgamakṣīṇasattvaṃ patitaṃ pṛthivyām pṛthavyathākleśajuṣaṃ janānāmabhūdabhūtārthavikalpajalpaḥ  KAvk kuṭhārikaiḥ kaiścidaho dayārdraḥ sarvārthisevyaḥ saralaḥ suvṛttaḥ durātmabhiḥ kāyastvayāpāyapade niyuktaḥ  KAvk apyasti rājan sukṛtavrate smin phalaspṛhā prāṇapaṇe pi kācit asthārthihetostava pālubhedakhedādvikāraṃ bhajate na cetaḥ  KAvk ityadbhutāviṣkṛtamānasena munīndramadhye avāptasaṃjñā muninā prayuktā padmāvatī rājasutena sārdham patiṃ yayāve virahopaśāntyai siṃhāsanākrāntisukhaṃ prajānām  KAvk tatastamabhyetya kṛpākulāste pratyekabuddhā jagato hitāya svapurīmavāpya bheje nijaṃ rājyapadaṃ saputraḥ  KAvk iti sa vipulasattvaḥ satyavān bodhisattvaḥ suciravihitarājyaḥ saugataṃ dhāma bheje jinapuramaṇicaityacchatraratnapradīpaprakaṭitavividhaśrīrlakṣaṇābhyastabodhiḥ  KAvk ityāha bhagavān buddhaḥ svavṝttāntanidarśane dānopadeśe bhikṣūṇāṃ samyaksaṃbodhisiddhaye  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ maṇicūḍāvadānaṃ nāma tṛtīyaḥ pallavaḥ  māndhātravadānam śobhante bhuvaneṣu bhavyamanasāṃ yannākakāntākara prauḍhodañcitacārucāmarasitacchatrasmitāḥ saṃpadaḥ yaccotsarpati tarpitaśruti yaśaḥ karpūrapūrojjvalaṃsvalpaṃ dānakaṇasya tat phalamaho dānaṃ nidānaṃ śriyaḥ  KAvk abhūdupoṣadho nāma bhūbhṛdhyasya vibhāvataḥ vibudhābhimatā kīrtiḥ sudhā dugdhodadheriva  KAvk vasudhāmavato yasya vasudhāmavataḥ puraḥ nanāma praṇatau kasya na nāma nṛpateḥ śiraḥ  KAvk śuddhā dhīriva dharmeṇa dāneneva dayālutā vibhūtirvinayeneva bhūṣitā yena bhūrabhūt  KAvk guṇinaḥ prāṃśuvaṃśasya babhūvendudyuteḥ sthitiḥ yasya sarvātapatrasya mūrdhni sarvamahībhṛtām  KAvk yasyeśvaraśiraḥsthāyi śubhaṃ gaṅgājalojjvalam bhramatyadabhraṃ lokeṣu bhuvanābharaṇaṃ yaśaḥ  KAvk kartu kratusahasrāṇāṃ sahasrākṣādhikaśriyaḥ yasya ṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi kalatraṃ sudṛśāmabhūt  KAvk kadācinmunirakṣāyai rakṣaḥkṣayakṛtakṣaṇaḥ vicacārāśvamāruhya sa taponanabhūmiṣu  KAvk tatra phalaṃ dānavyasanena mahīpateḥ  KAvk tau dṛṣṭvā durnimittāni prādurbhūtāni śaṅkitau vyagrao babhūvaturnityaṃ śāntisvastikakarmasu  KAvk nimittadarśanodvignāstapivanagatā api viśvāmitraprabhṛtayaḥ svāmītyūcurmaharṣayaḥ  KAvk atrāṇtare brahmabandhuḥ prāgjanmabrahmarākṣasaḥ raudrākṣo nāma mātsaryakrauryadaurjanyaduḥsahaḥ  KAvk śrutvā dānodbhavām kīrtiṃ rājñaḥ sarvaguṇojjvalām nirguṇaḥ sa guṇadveṣi saṃtaptaḥ samacintayat  KAvk aho batāsya nṛpatergīyate gagane yaśaḥ aniśaṃ siddhagandharvagīrvāṇalalanāgaṇaiḥ  KAvk sadā viśanti me karṇe tadguṇastutisūcayaḥ kiṃ karomi prakṛtyaiva sahe nānyaguṇonnatim  KAvk tadgatvā dānaśīlasya tasya dānārjitaṃ yaśaḥ karomyeṣa śiroyācñāpratiṣedhena khaṇḍitam  KAvk yaśastyājyate dānotthaṃ śiraścenna pradāsyati atha dāsyati vidveṣapraśāntirme bhaviṣyati  KAvk iti saṃcintya suciraṃ sa kauryakaṭhinaḥ śaṭhaḥ gandhamādanapādāṇtavāsī bhadraśilāṃ yayau  KAvk indrajālaprayogajñaḥ sa kṛtvā praśamocitam veṣaṃ kaluṣasaṃkalpaḥ purīṃ prāpa mahīpateḥ  KAvk asmin bhavavane nityaṃ guṇadoṣasamākule kalpavṛkṣāḥ prajāyante jāyante ca viṣadrumāḥ  KAvk aśeṣanāśapiśunairghorasaṃtrāsakāribhiḥ durnimittairiva khalaiḥ khedaḥ kasya na dīyate  KAvk guṇidveṣaḥ prakṛtyaiva prakāśaparipanthinaḥ doṣaāśrayasya ko bhedaḥ khalasya timirasya ca  KAvk svacchandaghātī sādhūnāṃ vidveṣaviṣaduḥsahaḥ dīrghapakṣaḥ khalavyālakarālaḥ kena nirmitaḥ  KAvk tasmin praviṣṭe nagaraṃ rūpiṇī puradevatā uvācābhyetya bhūpālaṃ saṃtrāsataralekṣaṇā  KAvk śiroyācaka eṣa tvāṃ brahmabandhurupāgataḥ vadhyo sau jīvitocchedī jagato jīvitasya te  KAvk niruddho nagaradvāri sa mayā malināśayaḥ mama taddarśanatrastaṃ dhṛtiṃ na labhate manaḥ  KAvk iti bruvāṇāṃ bhūpālaḥ provāca puradevatām arthisaṃrodhasaṃjātalajjayā namitānanaḥ  KAvk devi yācñābhiyāto sau praviśatvanivāritaḥ dirghocchvāsaṃ sahe nāhamāśāvaiphalyamarthinaḥ  KAvk yācñā praṇayināmarthe puṇyaprāptastanuvyayaḥ yugasaṃkhyāmapi sthitvā vipadyante hi dehinaḥ  KAvk etadeva sujātānāṃ pūjyaṃ jagati jīvitam yadeṣāmagrato yāti nārthī bhagnamanorathah  KAvk kriyatāmānukūlyaṃ me bhavatyā kuśalocitam āśāvighāte saṃtāpastasya tūrṇaṃ nivāratām  KAvk iti bhūmibhṛtaḥ śrutvā vaco niścalaniścayam jagāmādarśanaṃ devī cintāsaṃtāpamānasā  KAvk athāyayau sa kuṭilaḥ khalaḥ krakacaceṣṭitaḥ dāruṇaḥ saralasyaiva cchedāya svayamudyataḥ  KAvk tasminnṛpagṛhaṃ prāpte vivṛtadvāramarthinām bhūrbhūpatikṣayabhayāccakampe sadharādharā  KAvk narendracandramāsādya sa rāhurica durmukhaḥ samabhyadhādvidhāya prāgaśivārthāmivāśiṣam  KAvk svasti rājan dvijanmā hi vijane siddhisādhakaḥ prātastvāmīpsitaprāptyai sarvārthisurapādapam  KAvk dṛṣṭirvṛṣṭirivāmṛtasya mahatī saujanyamitraṃ manaḥkṣāntiḥ krodharajaḥpramārjanadī duḥkhārtamātā matiḥ lakṣmīrdānajalābhiṣekavimalā satyopayujktaṃ vacaḥnityaṃ yasya sa eka eva hi bhavān jāto jagadbāndhavaḥ  KAvk siddhaye kathitaṃ kaiściccakravartiśiro mama dīyatāṃ ta tvadanyo vā dātuṃ śaknoti kaḥ parah  KAvk santi spaṣṭārthadāścintāmaṇikalpadrumādayaḥ durlabhārthapradātāro viralāstu bhavadvidhāḥ  KAvk ityukte tena nṛpatirniṣkampavipulāśayaḥ arthisaṃdarśanānandanirbharastamabhāṣata  KAvk dhanyo haṃ yasya me brahmannarthināmarthasiddhaye nirvikalpopakaraṇaṃ vyayaṃ yāti sujīvitam  KAvk kadā prāṇāḥ parārthe me prayāntīti manorathaḥ kimetāni na puṇyāni prārthyante te yadi tvayā  KAvk āhopakaraṇasiddhyai ślāghyaṃ me gṛhyatāṃ śiraḥ tattadeva sthiraṃ loke yadyadarthisamarpitam  KAvk ityukte harṣayuktena bhūbhujā sattvaśālinā tamūcaturmahāmātyau mahācandramahīdharau  KAvk nijajīvitarakṣaiva dharmaste prathamaḥ prabho tvayi jīvati jīvanti sarve jagati jantavaḥ  KAvk na dātumarhasi śiraḥ sarvādhāraṃ hi te vapuḥ dīyatāṃ brāhmaṇāyāsmai hemaratnamayaṃ śiraḥ  KAvk sarvārthairarthisārthānāṃ pūryante yairmanorathāḥ teṣāṃ saṃrakṣaṇenaiva sarvaṃ bhavati rakṣitam  KAvk saṃkalpo yaṃ dvijasyāsya krūraḥ kaluṣacetasaḥ mūlacchedopajīvyo hi na kalpatarurarthinām  KAvk hemaratnaśiraḥ prāpya yātveṣa śirasāsya kim cintāmaṇirviniṣprekṣyo bhujyate na bubhukṣitaiḥ  KAvk ityukte mantrimukhyābhyām hemaratnamayaṃ śiraḥ siddho naivopayogyaṃ tanmameti brāhmaṇo bravīt  KAvk athonmumoca nṛpatirmukuṭaṃ mauktikāṃṣubhiḥ śrirovirahaduḥkhena sāśrudhāramivābhitaḥ  KAvk mukuṭāni kṣaṇe tasminnipetuḥ puravāsinām digdāhonmukhatulyābhirulkābhiḥ saha bhūtale  KAvk rājñā pradāne śirasaḥ sarvathā parikalpite tau cakratustanutyāgaṃ mantriṇau draṣṭumakṣamau  KAvk ratnagarbhamathodyānaṃ praviśya pṛthivīpatiḥ utphullacampakasyādhaḥ śiraśchettuṃ samudyayau  KAvk udyānadevatā dṛṣṭvā taṃ śiraśchettumudyatam mā kṛthāḥ sāhasaṃ rājannityuvāca śucākulā  KAvk kampamānāḥ pralāpinyastaṃ mattālukulasvanaiḥ nyavārayannavalatā lolapallavapāṇibhiḥ  KAvk so pi niścalasaṃkalpaḥ prasādyodyānadevatām vimalāṃ bodhimālambya babhūva praṇidhānavān  KAvk asmin ratnamayodyāne puṇyarāśisamunnatam stūpamastu praśāstustu sattvasaṃtāraṇocitam  KAvk yatkiṃcidarjitaṃ puṇyaṃ saṃkalpena mayāmunā bhavantu tena saṃsāre niḥsaṃsārāḥ śarīriṇaḥ  KAvk dhyātveti campakataroḥ śākhāyāṃ nṛpatiḥ śiraḥ baddhvā kacakalāpena chittvā prādāddvijanmane  KAvk atha narapate sattvotsāhasphuṭapraṇidhānataḥkimapi vimalaiḥ puṇyālokairdigantavisāribhiḥ vigalitamahāmohaughāntaḥ śritaḥ parinirvṛtiṃpraviratabhavābhyāsāyāsaḥ kṣaṇādabahvajjanah  KAvk iti prāgjanmavṛttāntakathayā bhagavān jinaḥ bhikṣūṇām vidadhe śuddhadānasaddharmadeśanām  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ candraprabhāvadānaṃ nāma pañcamaḥ pallavaḥ  badaradvīpayātrāvadānam dānodyatānām pṛthuvīryabhājāṃ śuddhātmanāṃ sattvamahodadhīnām aho mahotsāhavatām parārthe bhavantyacintyāni samāhitāni  KAvk harmyārohaṇahelayā yadacalāḥ svabhraiḥ sahābhraṃlihāyadvā goṣpadalīlayā jalabharakṣobhoddhatāh sindhavaḥ laṅghyante bhavanasthalīkalanayā ye cāṭavīnāṃ taṭāstadvīryasya mahātmanām vilasataḥ sattvorjitaṃ sphūrjitam  KAvk purā hi bhagavān buddhaḥ śrāvastyāṃ puravāsināṃ upadeśaprakāśena jahārājñānajaṃ tamaḥ  KAvk bhikṣusaṃghaiḥ parivṝtaḥ sa kadācidvaṇigjanaiḥ kṛtānuyātro magadhāt svayaṃ cārikayā yayau  KAvk mahārthasārthānugataṃ vrajantaṃ vanavartmanā taṃ dṛṣṭvā taskaragaṇaḥ sālāṭavyāmacintayat  KAvk eṣa prayātu bahgavān puraḥ sattvahite rataḥ paścāt sārthaṃ grahīṣyāmaḥ pūrṇaṃ draviṇarāśibhiḥ  KAvk bhagavānatha sarvajñasteṣāṃ jñātvā samīhitam kimetaditi tānūce nirvikārasmitānanaḥ  KAvk te tamūcuḥ parityajya krauryaṃ madhurayā girā tatprasādasmitālokairvinaṣṭatimirā iva  KAvk bhagavan jīvikāsmākaṃ nindyeyaṃ karmanirmitā na bhṛtirna kṛṣirnānyarakṣaṇaṃ na pratigrahah  KAvk sahajaṃ krauryamasmākaṃ nisargakaluṣātmanām kriyate kiṃ svabhāvasya deva tīkṣṇā hi karṇikā  KAvk tasmānna vṛttilopo naḥ kartumarhasi gamyatām yāte tu tvayi sārthasya vayaṃ sarvārthahāriṇah  KAvk iti teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā karuṇāpūrṇamānasaḥ dolālolāyitamatirbabhūva bahgavān kṣaṇam  KAvk tataḥ sārthadhanaṃ sarvaṃ parisaṃkhyāya tatsamam sa dadau cauracakrāya tatkṣaṇāptanidhānataḥ  KAvk tadvidhena krameṇaiva punaḥ pathi gatāgataiḥ ṣaṭkṛtvaḥ pradadau tebhyaḥ so rthaṃ sārthasya muktaye  KAvk punaścopagate tasmin vartmanā tena sānuge babhūva buddhiścaorāṇāṃ tadbhojananimantraṇe  KAvk dṛśā diśanti vaimalyaṃ śubhaṃ saṃbhāṣaṇena ca vrajanti saṃgamābhyāsaiḥ santaḥ sanmārgasetutām  KAvk tatrātiryagdṛśā sarvaṃ sarvākuśalasaṃkṣayāt teṣāṃ samāhitaṃ śuddhaṃ vidadhe bhagavān jinah  KAvk yeṣāṃ saṃgrahavastūni vatvāri niyatātmanām arthacaryā samānārthabḥāvastyāgaḥ priyaṃ vacaḥ  KAvk yeṣāṃ brahmavihārāśca catvāraḥ sattvaśālinām karuṇā muditopekṣā maitrī ceti parigrahaḥ  KAvk yeṣāṃ kuśalamūlāni saktāni trīṇi cetasi alobhaścāparidveṣo pyamohaśca mahātmanām  KAvk dānaśīlakṣamāvīryadhyānaprajñājuṣāṃ sadā upāyapraṇidhijñānabalairāśritacetasām  KAvk paritrāṇaikavīrāṇāṃ sadaivādvayavādinām vidyātrayapradīptānāṃ caturvaimalyaśālinām  KAvk pañcaskandhavumiktānāṃ ṣaḍayatanabhedinām saptabodhyaṅgayuktānāmaryāṣṭāṅgopadeśinām  KAvk navasaṃyogahīnānām teṣāṃ daśabalātmanām kiṃ vastvaviditaṃ loke jinānāṃ janaceṣṭitam  KAvk tatasteṣvatikāruṇyāccaraṇālīnamūrdhasu tathetyuvāca bhagavāṃstadbhojyopanimantraṇe  KAvk taistatsaṃdarśanakṣīṇakilbiṣaiḥ samamarpitam bhikṣusṃghairvṛto bhojyaṃ vidhivat sarvamādade  KAvk tatastatpraṇidhānena jñānālokaśalākayā te samunmīlitadṛśaḥ prakāśaṃ dadṛśuḥ padam  KAvk te sadyastīvravairāgyaparipakkāḥ prasādinaḥ pravrajyāyogamāsajya jagmurjagati pūjyatām  KAvk tatteṣāṃ kuśalaṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasopanataṃ puraḥ babhāṣe bhagavān pṛṣṭaḥ kimetaditi bhikṣubhiḥ  KAvk etairyamāyaṃ saṃbandhaḥ sārtharakṣaṇaniṣkrayaiḥ dvīpayātrāgatasyāsīdanyasminnapi janmani  KAvk asti vistīrṇamārgasya svargavargāvadhirvidheḥ purī vārāṇasī nāma kauśalotkarṣaharṣabhūḥ  KAvk yasyāmamalakallolavāhinī suravāhinī sadā dayeva hṛdayaṃ prasādayati dehinām  KAvk ahiṃseva satām sevyā vidyeva viduṣāṃ matā kṣameva sarvabhūtānāṃ yā viśrambhasukhasthitiḥ  KAvk brahmakalpe nṛpe tasyā vikasatkamalāśraye brahmadattābhidhe lokaṃ trailokyamiva rakṣati  KAvk priyasenābhidhāno bhūt tatra vaiśravaṇopamaḥ sārthavāho rthasārthānām sthānamabdhirivāmbhasāṃ  KAvk tasyāsīt supriyo nāma saujanyanilayaḥ sutaḥ prayayau yaṃ samāśritya guṇasārthaḥ kṛtārthatām  KAvk dānaśīlakṣamāvīryadhyānaprajñāsamanvitah dhātrā vilobhavāyaiva yaḥ kṛtaḥ sukṛtaśriyaḥ  KAvk taṃ sarvavidyāḥ viśadāḥ kalāśca vipulāśayam viviśuḥ sarasodārā mahodadhimivāpagāḥ  KAvk guṇālaṃkṛtacāritraṃ lakṣaṇālaṃkṛtākṛtim puruṣottamalubdheva yaṃ ślāghyaṃ śrīraśiśriyat  KAvk kālena sukṛtakrītaṃ pitari tridivaṃ gate cakre skandhataṭe tasya vyavahārabharaḥ sthitim  KAvk so cintayadiyaṃ lakṣmīrvipulātmakramāgatā tathāpi manye paryāptā na sarvārthimanorathe  KAvk kiṃ tayā sumahatyāpi śriyā satpuruṣasthayā pūrvāgatārthiubhukteva yā śeṣārthiṣu niṣphalā  KAvk ratnākarasya vaipulyaṃ niṣphalaṃ vedhasā kṛtam adyāpi pūrito yena naiko pyarthī sa vāḍavaḥ  KAvk athavā pṛthusaṃkalpaḥ kenārthī paripūryate jagāmābdhiragastyasya culukācamanīyatām  KAvk kiṃ karomyatitāpo yaṃ śrīrekā bahavi rthinaḥ na tadāsādyate vittaṃ yat sarvārthibharakṣamam  KAvk pañca ṣaṭ pūritā evaṃ nānye śrīkaustukādibhiḥ itivādyāpi tapto ntarjvaladaurvānalo mbudhiḥ  KAvk tasmāt karomi yatnena niṃsaṃkhyadraviṇārjanam na sahe duḥkhaniḥśvāsaṃ vimukhasya mukhe rthinaḥ  KAvk iti saṃcintya sa ciraṃ sārthena mahatā vṛtaḥ ratnadvīpapuraṃ gatvā vidadhe ratnasaṃgraham  KAvk tataḥ pratīpamāyāntaṃ kṛtārthaṃ taṃ vanecarāḥ sārthārtharaṇonmuktā dadṛśurdasyavaḥ pathi  KAvk sārthārthaharaṇe dṛṣṭvā sa teṣāṃ sāhasodyamam nijasaravsvadānena saṃrarakṣānuyānim  KAvk punaḥ krameṇa tenaiva ratnadvīpagatāgatiḥ sārthatrāṇāya caurāṇāṃ ṣaṭkṛtvaḥ pradadau dhanam  KAvk tathaiva tvāṃ puṇyavipanvānisaṃprāptastathaiva tān  dadarśa caurān sārthārthaharaṇe adhikādarān  KAvk so cintayadaho vittairmahadbhiḥ paripūritāḥ mayaite na nivartante parārthaharaṇodyamāt  KAvk jagat saṃpūrayāmyarthairiyuktvāpi mayāsakṛt aho nu dasyavo naite varākāḥ paripūritāḥ  KAvk acitotsāhahīnasya vyāhatottaravādinaḥ vikatthanapratijñasya dhiṅme janma kujanmanaḥ  KAvk iti cintayatastasya taptasyānuśayāgninā vijane prayayau rātriḥ saṃvatsaraśatopamā  KAvk taṃ śokapaṅkasaṃmagnaṃ gajendramiva niścalam dīrghocchvāsaṃ maheśākhyā svapne provāca devatā  KAvk sumate mā kṛthāḥ śokaṃ śarīrocchoṣaṇaṃ vṛthā satsaṃkalpābhirūḍhasya bhaviṣyati tavepsitam  KAvk na tadasti jagatyasmin svapnasaṃkalpadurlabham yanna sidhyati yatnena dhīrāṇāṃ vyavasāyinām  KAvk sā kāpyanupamā śaktirekasyāpi dvijanmanaḥ yadājñāspanditenaiva vindhyaḥ kṣmāsamatām yayau  KAvk viṣamaṃ samatāṃ yāti dūramāyāti cāntikam salilaṃ sthalatāmeti kāryakāle mahātmanām  KAvk parārtho yaṃ tavārambhaḥ phalatyeva na saṃśayam na bhavanti visaṃvādasaṃdigdhāḥ sattvavṛttayaḥ  KAvk ratnāni badaradvīpe santi tridaśasevite yeṣāmekaprabhāvo pi trijagatpūraṇakṣamaḥ  KAvk martyabhūmimatikramya sā hi bhūmirmahīyasī āsādyate puṇyamayī nāsattvairnākṛtātmabhiḥ  KAvk viṣādastyajyatām putra sthirā buddhirvidhīyatām badaradvīpayātrāyāmutsāhaḥ parigṛhyatām  KAvk śrūyatāmeṣa tatprāptyau diṅbhātrānukramakramaḥ sphītasattvaprabhāvastvaṃ saṃsārottaraṇakṣamah  KAvk asti paścimadigbhāge samullaṅghya mahīyasām śatāni sapta dvīpānāṃ tathā sapta mahācalān  KAvk saptāpatāścānulomapratilomābhidho mbudhiḥ anukūlānilairyasmin pāramāpnoti puṇyavān  KAvk tatastattulyanāmādrirvātaistimiramihakṛt yatrākṣṇordiśati svāsthyamamoghākhyā mahauṣadhiḥ  KAvk athāvartābhidho mbhodhirvairambhairyatra vāyubhiḥ majjanonmajjanairjantuḥ saptāvarteṣu tāryate  KAvk āvartākhyastataḥ śailaḥ śaṅkhanābho niśācarah ghoraḥ prāṇaharo yatra tridaśatrāsakṛt sthitaḥ  KAvk kṛṣṇasarpāvṛtā yatra śankhanābhirmahauṣadhiḥ trāyate puṇyasaṃpannaṃ netre śirasi cārpitā  KAvk atha nīlodanāmābdhī raktākṣo yatra rākṣasaḥ makaryābhibhūtāṃ buddhavidyāvidvān vaśe   KAvk atha nīlodanāmādrirnīlagrīvaḥ kṣapācaraḥ pratīptanetro yatrāste rakṣasāṃ pañcabhiḥ śataiḥ  KAvk tatraoṣadhimamoghākhyām rakṣatyāśīviṣaḥ sadā dṛṣṭiniḥ śvāsasaṃsparśadaṃṣṭrotsṛjadviṣānalaḥ  KAvk upoṣadhavratavatā maitreṇa karuṇātmanā labhyate sā samutsārya kṛṣṇasarpaṃ mahauṣadhiḥ  KAvk taṃ rakṣaḥśakaṭaṃ śailaṃ niṣphalaślakṣṇakandaram tāmajjane śikhāyāṃ ca kṛtvā tarati puṇyavān  KAvk atha vairambhanāmādriḥ pāre yasyottarā taṭe ghorā tāmrāṭavī nāma mahāśālavanāntarā  KAvk mahānajagarastatra tāmrākṣo nāma duḥsahaḥ āsta yasyogragandhena vāyunaiva na jīvyate  KAvk ṣaṇmāsān svapato yasya lālā vyāpnoti yojanam kṣutsaṃtaptasya ṣaṇmāsānalpībhavati jāgrataḥ  KAvk veṇugulmaśilābaddhāṃ guhāmutpāṭya medinīm prāyauṣadhīṃ divārātraṃ jvalantīmañjanocitām  KAvk tasmādajagarād ghorādanyato vā mahaujasaḥ avairākhyāṃ buddhavidyāṃ japato na bhavedbhayam  KAvk tataḥ sapta mahāśailā veṇukaṇṭakasaṃkaṭāḥ tāmrapaṭāṅkapādena tīryante vīryaśālinā  KAvk tataśca śālmalīvanaṃ sapta kṣārataraṅgiṇīḥ uttīryāsādyate prāṅgustriśaṅkurnāma parvataḥ  KAvk tatra triśaṅkavo nāma kaṇṭakā vajrabhedinaḥ pādayorna viśantyeva tāmrapaṭṭāvanaddhayoḥ  KAvk triśankurnāma taṭinī tatrāyaḥśaṅkuparvataḥ upaskīlanadī tatra tato dvidhā dvidhā sarit  KAvk athāṣṭādaśavakrākhyaḥ parvato niravagrahaḥ tattulyasaṃjñātha nadī ślakṣṇi nāma giristataḥ  KAvk athādridhūmanetrākhyo dhūmanirdigdhadiktaṭaḥ dṛṣṭisparśaviṣairvyāptaḥ krūrāśīviṣamaṇḍalaiḥ  KAvk tanmūrdhni palvalasyāntaḥ śilābaddhā mahāguhā jyotīraso maṇiryasyāṃ jīvanī ca mahauṣadhiḥ  KAvk bhittvā guhām tadabhyakraśiraḥpādakarodaraḥ vajramantrabalopetaḥ krūrasarpairna bādhyate  KAvk athograsattvasaṃkīrṇāḥ saptāśīviṣaparvatāḥ nadyaśca tadvidhā yāsāmapāravārisaṃpadaḥ  KAvk etaduttīrya nikhilaṃ puṇyaiḥ parahitodyataḥ ārohati sudhāśailaṃ śṛṅgairāliṅgitāmbaram  KAvk tatastasyāpare pārśve kalpavṛkṣopaśobhitam puraṃ rohitakaṃ nāma dṛśyate svargasaṃnibham  KAvk asti tatra magho nāma maghavāniva viśrutaḥ sārthavāho mahāsattvaḥ sarvasattvahite rataḥ  KAvk badaradvīpayātrāyāmudyatasyānavadyadhīḥ mārgopadeśaṃ deśajñaḥ sa te sarvaṃ kariṣyati  KAvk ityuktvotsāhya bahuśaḥ śubhadrairiva supriyam vacobhiricitairdevī sahasāntaradhīyata  KAvk prabuddhaḥ supriyaḥ sarvaṃ tattatheti vicintayan pratasthe sattvamāruhya nijotsāhapuraḥsaraḥ  KAvk sa vrajan vinitāyāsastena nirdiṣṭavartmanā puṇyairdvādaśabhirvarṣaiḥ prāpa rphitakaṃ puram  KAvk atrāntare sa praveśamavāptavān upayogakathāprajñā na kasyādarabhūmayaḥ  KAvk āyurvedavidhānajñaḥ sa tasyāriṣṭalakṣaṇaiḥ ṣaṇmāsaśeṣamevāyurjñātvā cintāntaro bhavat  KAvk tasya priyahitaprāyo bhaiṣajyaparicaryayā atyalpenaiva kālena supriyaḥ priyatāṃ yayau  KAvk bhaiṣajyayuktistatprītyā tasya vallabhatāṃ yayau priyopanītaṃ yatkiṃ cit tatsarvaṃ manasaḥ priyam  KAvk priyopacāraistasyātha vyādhirādrāvamāyayau ādhiḥ śāmyati satsaṅgāt tao vyādhirviśīryate  KAvk tataḥ saṃjātaviśrambhaḥ supriyaḥ praṇayānmagham cakre viditavṛttāntaṃ paścānnijakathākṣaṇe  KAvk badaradvīpayātrāyāṃ tasyotsāhaṃ mahātmanah parārthe niścalaṃ jñātvā tamūce vismayānmaghaḥ  KAvk aho batāsmin saṃsāre viḥsāre sārarūpiṇaḥ jāyante maṇayaḥ kecit paracintāparāyaṇāḥ  KAvk navaṃ vayaḥ priyā mūrtiḥ parārthapravaṇaṃ manaḥ puṇyocitastathaivāyaṃ sthāne guṇasamāgamaḥ  KAvk iyatīṃ bhūmimullaṅghya parārthe tvamupāgataḥ karomi tava sāhāyyaṃ kiṃ tvahaṃ bhṛśamāturaḥ  KAvk nibaddhāvadhayaḥ prāṇāḥ prayāntyeva śarīriṇām te sarvabhāvānāmabhāvānubhavāṃ sthitim  KAvk kecid vyākaraṇaiḥ pare śrutipathaistarkapravādaiḥ pare kecittantraparigrahairbahuvidhairanyaiḥ kalākauśalaiḥ saṃsaktāḥ punaruktajanmaśaraṇau yātā sahaiva kṣayaṃtatrāpyakṣyayalīlayā kṣaṇapadaṃ mugdhaurnibaddhā dhṛtiḥ  KAvk viṣayaviṣamāpāyaḥ kāyaḥ prapañcamayāśayākharataramarusphārākāro mohabhāvo bhavaḥ hitabhūmi  tathākāryaṃ kāryaṃ vivekināṃ tathāniravadhirayaṃ dṛṣṭvā vyādhiryathā hinivartate  KAvk ityādyanityasaṃskārasaṃyuktaṃ yuktamudyate dharmopadeśakuśalaṃ vaktuṃ bhagavati svayam  KAvk ekā śākyavadhūstatra rūpasaubhāgyagarvitā sthitā śauśavatāruṇyasaṃghau vayasi duḥsahe  KAvk muktāhāraṃ stanataṭe lolāpāṅgairmuhurmuhuḥ āliloke yaśaḥsphārasāraṃ ratipateriva  KAvk hārāvalokinīṃ dṛṣṭvā tāmanekāgrahādasau acintayādviraktena magatpatnī śaśiprabhā  KAvk iyaṃ dharmopadeśe pi capalā hāramīkṣate bhāvānāṃ na śṛṇotyeva mūḍhā kṣaṇikatāmimām  KAvk svaṃ hāraṃ darśayitvāsyā hārotsāhaṃ harāmyaham adhikālokanenaiva darpaḥ śāmyati dehinām  KAvk iti saṃcintya sā dāsīṃ rohikākhyāmabhāṣata rohike gaccha me hāraṃ gṛhāt satvaramāhara  KAvk ityuktā sā tayā tatra pravṛtte dharmasaṃśrave akālagamanodvignā niḥśvasyācintayat kṣaṇam  KAvk aho batāntarāyo yaṃ saṃjātaḥ kuśale mama nāsmin śrotuṃ labhe dharmaṃ yatparāyattajīvitā  KAvk puṇyasaurabhasaṃbhārāt kīrṇakāruṇyakesarāt mukhapadmād bhagavato dhanyaḥ prāpnoti vāṅbhadhuḥ  KAvk aho svācchandyavicchedastanubhaṅgaḥ sukhakṣayaḥ sevā jagati jantūnāṃ duḥkhe duḥkhaparaṃparā  KAvk sevāprayāsasaṃprāptaṃ dhanamānakaṇodayam tatpamatyuṣṇaniḥśvāsairaho kṛcchreṇa pīyate  KAvk mānaglānirguṇaglānirojaḥpunaśamaḥ śramah prathamaṃ sevakasyaitat phalamīśvaradarśane  KAvk lauhī bandhanaśṛṅkhalā caraṇayorhelāvamānāvanīsvavyāpāraniṣedhanityaniyatī nidrāsukhadrohiṇī āśāsyasya viśālajālasaraṇiḥ satsaṅgabhogāśaniḥmugdhānāṃ mṛgatṛṣṭikāmarumahī sevā śarīrakṣayaḥ  KAvk iti saṃcintya suciraṃ sā jagāma tadājñayā sevāvikrītakāyānāṃ svecchāviharaṇaṃ kutaḥ  KAvk vrajantīṃ tām parapreṣyāṃ kṛpaṇāṃ karuṇākulaḥ nirīkṣya bahgavān divyacakṣuṣācintayat kṣasṇam  KAvk asmin janmani śeṣo syā saṃpūrṇo jīvitāvadhiḥ iyaṃ varākī saṃsārāduddhartavyā svayaṃ mayā  KAvk atha tām karmayogena vrahantīṃ sahasā pathi vatsavātsalyavivaśā śṛṅgābhyāmājaghāna gauḥ  KAvk sā pradaghyau bhagavataḥ prasādāt tanmayasmṛtiḥ janmāntarādhivāsena buddhālambanamānasā  KAvk aho karmormibhiḥ śīrṇe saṃsāramakarākare janmāvarteṣu jantūnāṃ majjanonmajjanakramaḥ  KAvk puṃso lalāṭavipulopalapaṭṭikāsu niḥśarmakarmaghaṭitaprakaṭāṅkaṭaṅkaiḥ nayastāni janmamaraṇaprasarākṣarāṇi naitāni pāṇiparimārjanayā calanti  KAvk iyaṃ karmāyattā pracuracitravaicitraracanānarāṇāṃ māyūracchadapaṭalatulyā pariṇatiḥ yayā garbhārambhe kramanipatane vṛddhisamayekṣaye vā nānyat prābhajata tanulekhācchavirati  KAvk saṃcintyātha puraḥ pravṛttasudaśāsannāvasannasthitiṃ prāptevāsamadāsabhāvakalanāvailakṣyaniḥ spandatām ādhāya praṇidhānadhāmni dhavale saddharmaśuddhāṃ dhiyaṃsaṃsāre vicikitsya eva malinaṃ tatyāja sā jīvitam  KAvk tataḥ sā siṃhaladvīpe samīpe svargasaṃpadām candralekheva dugdhābdhau divyadyutirajāyata  KAvk ādhānajanmanastasya muktāvarṣeṃ divaścyute sābhūnmuktālatā nāma siṃhalādhipateḥ sutā  KAvk sā puṇyamiva lāvaṇyaṃ vahantī vṛddhimāgatā lebhe vivekenāṅgānāṃ saṃtoṣamiva yaovanam  KAvk tataḥ kadācidvaṇijaḥ śrāvastīpuravāsinaḥ makarākaramuttīrya siṃhaladvīpamāyayuḥ  KAvk te tatra rātriparyante viśrāntisukhamājaguḥ dharmārthagāthāsaṃnaddhaprabuddhabuddhabhāṣitam  KAvk tdantaḥpuraharmyasthā śrutvaiva śravaṇāmṛtam kimetaditi papraccha tānānāyya nṛpātmajā  KAvk te tāmūcuḥ pramuditāmidaṃ buddhasya bḥāṣitam svabhāvārhaṃ bhagavataḥ sarvasattvānukampinah  KAvk buddhāmidhānaṃ śrutviva pulakālaṃkṛtākṛtiḥ sā babhūva samudbhūtasaṃvidbhavyānubhāvabhūḥ  KAvk unmubhī sāmayūriva śabdaireva payomucaḥ ka eṣa bhagavān buddha iti paparcchaḥ tān punaḥ  KAvk tataste nikhilaṃ tasyai śraddhāsaṃvardhitādarāḥ nyavedayan puṇyamayīṃ bhagavaccaritasthitim  KAvk atha sā tatkathāvāptaprāgjanmakuśalodayā vijñaptilekhaṃ pradadau teṣāṃ bhagavataḥ kṛte  KAvk kālena sindhumuttīrya saṃrpāptāste nijāṃ pirīm praṇamyāvedya tadvṛttaṃ dadurlekhaṃ mahātmane  KAvk bhagavānapi sarvajñaḥ pūrvameva vibhāvya tat muktālatāyāḥ kṛpayā svayaṃ lekhamavācayat  KAvk aho smaraṇameva te kimapi puṇyapaṇyaṃ satāṃbhavātibahvabhaiṣajaṃ vyasanatāpatṛṣṇāpahat bhavanmayakathākramopanatasaṃvidāsvādabhūḥsa eṣa bhagavan mahānamṛtasaṃvibhāgo mama  KAvk iti saṃkṣiptalekhārthaṃ vibhāvya bhagavān svayam īṣatsmitviṣā sattvaprakāśamadiśaddiśām  KAvk tataścitrakarāśakyāṃ prabhāvairanupūritām bhagavān prāhiṇot tasyai nyastāṃ svapratimāṃ paṭe  KAvk punaḥ pravahaṇārūḍhā vaṇijaste tadājñayā avāpya siṃhaladvīpaṃ tasyai paṭamadarśayan  KAvk hemasiṃhāsananyaste paṭe dṛṣṭvā tathāgatam janastanmayatādhyānādekībhāvamivāyayau  KAvk adhastāllikhitaṃ tasmin puṇyaprāptamadṛśyata tisraḥ śaraṇyā gatayaḥ pañca śikṣāpadāṇi ca  KAvk sapratītyasamutpādaḥ sānulomaviparyayaḥ āryāṣṭāṅgastathā mārgaḥ paramāmṛtanirbharaḥ  KAvk svayaṃ bhagavatā vyastaṃ tasyopari subhāṣitam śobhate bhāvanālīnaṃ bhrājiṣṇu kanakākṣaram  KAvk viṣamaviṣayālolavyālāvalīvalayākulāttaruṇatimirānniṣkramyāsmāt pramohamayādgṛhāt jananamaraṇakleśāveśapravṛttapṛthivyathāvrajata śaraṇaṃ bauddhaṃ dharmaṃ na cātra bhavādbhayam  KAvk jinapratikṛtiṃ puṇyām paśyantī pārthivātmajā anādikālopacitāṃ mumocājñānavāsanām  KAvk prāṃśuṃ kavatakāñcanakāntakāyaṃ suskandhamājānubhujābhirāmam dhyānāvadhānārthanimīlitākṣaṃ lāvaṇyadhārāyitatuṅganāsam  KAvk svabhāvabhavyaṃ pravibhāsamānaṃ pralambanirbhūṣaṇakarṇapāśam bālapravālāruṇavalkalāṅkaṃ saṃsaktasaṃdhyābhramivāmarādrim  KAvk tviṣā diṣāṃ śīlamivādiśantaṃ ānandadānodyatavaktracandram kṣamāguṇaṃ kṣāmiva śikṣayantaṃ puṇyocitā sā subhagaṃ vilokya  KAvk praṇāmaparyantakapolacumbikarṇotpalānāṃ parivartanena nirasya niḥsāraśarīratṛptiṃ satyānubhāvaṃ paramaṃ prapede  KAvk srotaḥsamāpattiphalaprakāśaṃ sāsādya tatra kṣaṇalabdhabodhiḥ vicintayantī sugataprabhāvaṃ samabhyadhādvismayaharṣabhūmiḥ  KAvk aho mahāmohatamohareṇa dūrasthitenāmi tathāgatena prasahya bḥāsvadvapuṣārpiteyaṃ vikāsalakṣmīḥ kuśalāmbujasya  KAvk tīrṇo bahvaḥ satpraṇidhānamāptaṃ prasannamantaḥkaraṇaṃ kṣaṇena aho nu tṛṣṇāparitāpaśāntyai samucchalantīva samāmṛtaughāḥ  KAvk ityuktvā sā bahgavate muktāratnānyupāyanam vitīrya saṃghapūjāyāṃ visasarja vaṇigjanam  KAvk te mahodadhimuttīrya prāptā bahgavato ntikam tanmuktāratnanikaraṃ praṇamyāsmai nyavedayan  KAvk vaṇigbhiḥ kathitāṃ śrutvā tatkathāṃ tatra bhikṣuṇā ānandanāmnā pṛṣṭho tha babhāṣe bhagavān jinaḥ  KAvk yāsau purā rohitākhyā dāsī śākyagṛhe bahvat saiva muktālatā jātā satkarmapraṇidhānataḥ  KAvk abhūnmahādhano nāma vārāṇasyāṃ vaṇik purā tasya ratnavatī nāma patnī puṇyocitābhavat  KAvk sā patyau pañcatāṃ yāte niḥputrā stūpaśekhare pūjāṃ kṛtvā mahāhārāṃ bhaktiyuktā nyavedayat  KAvk tena puṇyavipākena siṃhalādhipateḥ sutā jātā muktālatā saiva prātā ca parinirvṛtim  KAvk saiva janmani cānyasminnairvaryamadamohitā pūjādhikṣepadakṣābhūddhāsī tenātivatsaram  KAvk janmabhūmau janenātpaṃ yadyatkarma śubhāśubham tasya tasya sa tadrūpaṃ bhuṅkte pariṇataṃ phalam  KAvk nikhilakuśalamūlā kīrtipuṣpojjvalaśrīḥśubhaphalabharasūrirdharmavallī narāṇām bhavati ca viṣavallī kilbiṣakleśamūlabhramanipatanamohānantasaṃtāpahetuḥ  KAvk saṃtapte smin kharataramaruṣphārasaṃsāramārgepāpaṃ punyaṃ tyajata janatāḥ saktatīvrānutāpam puṇyaṃ puṇyaṃ kuruta satataṃ puṇyapīyūṣasiktāḥpuṇyacchāyātarutalabhuvaḥ śītalāḥ puṇyabhājām  KAvk iti satpraṇidhānasya phalaṃ kathayatā svayam bhikṣūṇāmupadeśo yaṃ bhaktyai bhagavatā kṛtaḥ  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpatāyāṃ muktālatāvadānaṃ nāma saptamaḥ pallavaḥ  śrīguptāvadānam kṛtāpakāre pi kṛpākulāni krūre pyalaṃ pallavakomalāni dveṣoṣmatapte pyatiśītalāni bhavanti cittāni sadāśayānām  KAvk purā surapurodāre pure rājagṛhābhidhe śrīguptākhyo gṝhapatirbabhūva dhandopamaḥ  KAvk dṛptaḥ sujanavidveṣī guṇeṣu viratādaraḥ sadā dhanamadādhmātaḥ sā jahāsa matiṃ satām  KAvk kaṭhine ṣvativakreṣu śūnyeṣu mukhareṣu ca śankheṣviva khaleṣveva lakṣmīrdākṣiṇyamāśritā  KAvk taṃ kadācit gururjñātiputraḥ kṣapaṇakaḥ khalah mithaḥ svairakathāsaktaḥ puṇyadveṣādabhāṣata  KAvk ya eṣa gṛdhrakūṭākhye girau bhikṣuśatairvṛtaḥ sarvajñakīrtiḥ sugatāstrijagatpūjyatāṃ gataḥ  KAvk naivāsya pratibhāṃ kāṃcid bhavyāmupalabḥāmahe nītaḥ kiṃ tūnnatiṃ mūrkhairbahgavān bhagavāniti  KAvk avicāyava satataṃ paroktamanubhāṣate gatānugatikaḥ prāyaḥ prasiddhasaraṇau janaḥ  KAvk vratādiniyamastasya dambha eva vibhāvyate aśnāti maunakṛt matsyānekapādavrato bakaḥ  KAvk tasmaāt tasyopahāsāya kriyatām kāpi vajṇcanā māyāmohito dhūrtānām paro pi parituṣyati  KAvk iti tenoktamākarṇya śrīguptaḥ karkmamohitaḥ patituṃ pāpaśvabhreṣu yuktyā tadupadiṣṭayā  KAvk pradīptakhadirāṅgārapūrṇāṃ gūḍhāṃ khadāṃ gṛhe kṛtvā saviṣamannaṃ ca yayau bhagavato ntikam  KAvk tena mithyāvihitayā bhaktyā bhoktuṃ nimantritaḥ vijñāya sarvaṃ sarvajñastatheti prāha sasmitaḥ  KAvk viṣagniyogakupitām patnīṃ saddharmavādinīm gṛhe babandha śrīguptaḥ śaṅkito mantraviśravāt  KAvk atha vijñātavṛtto pi bhagavān svayamāyayau vandyamāno jagadvandyaiścaturmukhamukhaiḥ suraiḥ  KAvk śrīguptasya tamārambhaṃ vivedaṃ nagare janaḥ dikṣu dhāvati pāpānāṃ suguptamapi pātamak  KAvk tataḥ kaścit samabhyetya bhagavantamupāsakaḥ uvāca caraṇālīnāścintayan dahanaṃ viṣam  KAvk mithyānamrah priyālāpī guḍhavahniviṣānnadaḥ parihāryaḥ prayatnena bhagavanneṣa durjanah  KAvk kuryādanārye nāśvāsi kāryaṃ mādhuryamāśriye antracchedī vigīrṇo hi madhudigdhamukhaḥ kṣuraḥ  KAvk nānyastutiṃ guṇadveṣī sahate guṇinām khalaḥ santastuṣyanti yenaiva tenakupyanti durjanāḥ  KAvk tvayi lokatraye netraśatapatravikāśini asya rāhoḥ padaṃ prāpte nāndhībhavati kiṃ jagat  KAvk tacchrutvā bhagavānūce kiṃcit smitasitāṃśubhiḥ tannikārogratimiraṃ dūrāt pariharanniva  KAvk na mamāṅgaṃ spṛśatyagniḥ prabahvatyapi vā viṣam paradveṣadaridrāṇāṃ doṣo pi nirupadravaḥ  KAvk aroṣaśītalaṃ cetaḥ siktaṃ yasya śamāmṛtaiḥ kiṃ karotyanalastasya viṣaṃ vā viṣayadviṣaḥ  KAvk viṣāyate tu pīyūṣaṃ kusumaṃ kuliśāyate dveṣadoṣottarasyaiva candanaṃ dahanāyate  KAvk tiryagyonigatasyāpi bodhisattvapadāsthiteḥ kāruṇyamaitrīyuktasya nāgnirdahati vigraham  KAvk purā kaliṅganṛpatiḥ khaṇḍadvīpābhidhāvanīm dadāha mṛgasaṃghānām saṃkṣepe sa samudyataḥ  KAvk kānane jvalite tasminnekastittiriśāvakaḥ maitryā bodhiṃ samālambya dahanapraśamaṃ vyaghāt  KAvk tasmādadrohamanasāṃ na bhayaṃ vidyate kkacit śrūyatāṃ sattvasaṃpatteridamanyacca kautukam  KAvk avṛṣṭiviṣame kāle muneḥ kasyacidāśrame manuṣyasadṛśālāpaḥ śaśakaḥ suciraṃ sthitaḥ  KAvk kṣutkṣāmaṃ munimālokya phalamūlaparikṣayāt uvācācalasaṃkalpastadvyathāvyathitāśayaḥ  KAvk bhagavan mam māṃsānāṃ saṃprati prāṇavartanam kriyatāṃ rakṣaṇīyaṃ tat śarīraṃ dharmasādhanam  KAvk ityuktvā dāvaśeṣāgnau vikṣepa śahskastanum vāryamāṇo pi yatnena praṇayānmuninā muhyuḥ  KAvk tasya sattvaprabhāveṇa jvalajjvālākulo nalaḥ prayayau majṇjuśiñjānabhramarāmbhojakhaṇḍatām  KAvk so pi divyavapustatra kamale mahati sthitaḥ praṇamyamāno munirbhirvidadhe dharmadeśanām  KAvk iti bodhipravṛttānāṃ na vahnerna viṣādbhayam bhagavān kathayitveti śrīguptabhavanaṃ yayau  KAvk tatra tena praviśyaiva nikṣipte dakṣiṇe pade babhūvāgnikhadā mañjuguñjadbhṛṅgasarojinī  KAvk dṛṣṭvopaviṣṭaṃ śrīguptastaṃ sarorihavistare taddṛṣṭinaṣṭakāluṣyaḥ provācaḥ caraṇānataḥ  KAvk bhagavan mama pāpasya kṣantavyo yaṃ vyatikramaḥ mohāndhapatite rucyaṃ kāruṇyamadhikaṃ satām  KAvk mamākalyāṇamitreṇa yo yaṃ pāpapathe kṛtaḥ upadeśaḥ pramoheṇa tatra trāṇaṃ bhavatsmṛtiḥ  KAvk viṣadigdharasaṃ sarvaṃ bhojyaṃ te kalpitaṃ mayā aho mamaiva saṃkrāntaṃ paścāttapamayaṃ viṣam  KAvk iti bruvāṇaṃ śrīguptaṃ sāśrunetraṃ kṛpānidhiḥ dṛṣṭvā babhāṣe bhagavān bhikṣusaṃghasya śṛṇyavataḥ  KAvk viṣādaṃ mā kṛthāḥ sādho na vayaṃ vimukhāstvayi ghoravairaviṣatyāgānnaivāsmāstapate viṣam  KAvk vārāṇasyāṃ purā śrīmān brahmadatto bhavannṛpaḥ abhūdanupamā nāṃ atasya prāṇasamāśrayā  KAvk suvarṇabhāsasaṃjñasya tatpurāntavanasthiteḥ ravaṃ mayūrarājasya sā kadācidathāśṛṇot  KAvk sā tasya śadamākarṇya veṇuvīṇāsvanopamam kimetaditi papraccha naranāthaṃ sakautukā  KAvk rājovāca vanānte sminnasti ratnacchadaḥ śikhī madhuraṃyojanavyāpi yasyaitat kaṇṭhakūjitam  KAvk iti bruvāṇo nṛpatistatsaṃdarśanamarthitaḥ premaprayatnaiḥ preyasyā prahasan punarabravīt  KAvk darśanaṃ durlabhaṃ mugdhe tadvidhādbhutarūpiṇaḥ tathāpi yadi nirbandhaḥ kriyate tatpariśramaḥ  KAvk ityuktvā nṛpatistasya grahaṇe jālajīvinaḥ vyasṛjat tasya saṃrpāptyaiḥ vidhāya vadhasaṃvidam  KAvk vaśīkṛto na vettyeva mohādakṣiparīkṣayā anurāgāhataḥ strībhirakarmāṇyapi kāryate  KAvk prāptānām praṇayāt patnyāḥ prauḍhāyāḥ pādapīṭhatām īrṣyayaiva vinaśyanti dhīdhṛtismṛtikīrtayaḥ  KAvk tataḥ śākunikairnyastāḥ pāśabandhāḥ pade pade prabhāvādbarhirājasy vyaśīryantaiva saṃtatam  KAvk duḥkhitān yatnavaiphalyādbhītān nṛpatiśāsanāt mayūrarājastān dṛṣṭvā karuṇākulatāṃ yayau  KAvk so cintayadaho bhītāḥ kṣmāpateḥ śrūraśāsanāt madbandhane visaṃvādādvarākā jālajīvinah  KAvk saṃcintya kṛpayā spaṣṭagbhirvisṛjya tān nṛpamānāyya tadveśma tenaiva sahito yayau  KAvk sa tatrāntaḥpure nityaṃ sabhāryeṇa mahībhujā pūjyamānaḥ paricayāduvāsa vihitādaraḥ  KAvk snigdhaśyāmāmbudatviṣā sunīlamaṇiveśmasu citrapatrarucā cakre saṃsaktendrāyudhabhamam  KAvk atha digjayayātrāyām kadācidvasudhādhipaḥ yayau tadupacārāya devīmādiśya sādaraḥ  KAvk tataścānupamā devī patyau yāte pramādinī rūpayauvanadarpāndhā nāluloke kulasthitim  KAvk taruṇaṃ prekṣya rāgiṇyāstasyāḥ kandarpaviplave bhūyaḥ pralambhabhīteva lajjā dūrataraṃ yayau  KAvk malinaḥ kuṭilastīkṣṇaḥ karṇasaṃsparśanocitaḥ
