sundarī samāsādya dayitām ratisundarīm vijahāra varodyānaṃ muhūrtavirahāsahaḥ  KAvk tataḥ kadācid bhagavān prakṛtyaiva guṇipriyaḥ svayaṃ nandasya bhavanaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaiḥ sahāyayau  KAvk sānandavadanaḥ kṛtvā nandastatpādavandanāṃ taṃ mahāharsanāsīnaṃ pūjayitvā vyajijñapat  KAvk keṣāṃ puṇyaprarohāṇāṃ paripāko yamīdṛśaḥ kṛto yaṃ yadbhagavatā darśanānugrahaḥ svayam  KAvk smaraṇaṃ śravaṇaṃ vāpi darśanaṃ vā mahātmanām seyaṃ kuśalavallīnāṃ mahatī phalasaṃtatiḥ  KAvk asya maitrasya mahatastadālokasya darśanāt hṛdayasya vikāsaśrīḥ kasya nāma na jāyate  KAvk dānādapi priyataraṃ puṇyādapi mahāphalam sadācārādapi śrlāghyaṃ mahatāṃ kilaṃ darśanam  KAvk iti tasya bruvāṇasya bhaktipraṇayapeśalam abhinandya puraḥ pūjāṃ bhagavān gantumudyayau  KAvk anuvavrāja taṃ nandaḥ svacche kanakabhājane varopacāramādāya madhuraṃ svamivāśayam  KAvk pahcādvrajantamālokya bhaktyā bhagavataḥ pathi niraikṣata kaṭākṣeṇa sundarī virahāsahā  KAvk gurūṇāmagre sā saralataralāṃ locanagatiṃvihāyaiva trāsāñcitamukutitākṣī priyatamā nirīkṣyālakṣyaṃ yat kṣaṇamavanatābhūttadadhikaṃna gantavyaṃ nāthetyavadadivaṃ maonādavacanam  KAvk nandaḥ praṇayiṇīṃ dṛṣṭvā socchvāsaṃ calitānanām ayamāgata evāhamacirādityabhāṣata  KAvk tataḥ svamāśramaṃ prāptaṃ bhagavantaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ vrajāmi svagṛhaṃ tāvadityāha virahāsahaḥ  KAvk tatastamāsanāsīnaḥ praṇataṃ bhagavān puraḥ uvāca sasmitaṃ keyaṃ gamane saṃprati tvarā  KAvk viṣayāsvādasauhārdasaṃmohārditavetasām aho gṛhasukheṣveva nirvedavimukhā matiḥ  KAvk guṇābharaṇamevāyurvivekābharaṇo guṇaḥ praśamābahraṇaścāsau vairāgyābharaṇaḥ śamaḥ  KAvk tajjāḍyaṃ tadasahyaśalyaśalakaṃ nyastaṃ suhṛccetasiprājñistadgaṇitaṃ virācasamayairvaiphalyamevāyuṣaḥ yadvairāgyavivekaśūnyamanasāmete paśūnāṃ yathāyāntyāyānti ca cakranemicalanairnirlakṣaṇānāṃ kṣaṇāḥ  KAvk puṇyaṃ sattvavatām śrutaṃ matimatām śīlaṃ ca vidyāvatāmsarvaṃ bhāgyavatām sukhaṃ śamavatāṃ naiva kkacit durlabham duṣprāpastu samastavastuvasateḥ svalpāṃśako pyāyuṣaḥtadyasya kṣayameti niṣphalatayā śocyāya tasmai namaḥ  KAvk vāmāvarte viṣayajaladhau pūrṇalāvaṇyasāre darpotsarpadviṣamamakarāṅkodbhavakṣobhyamāṇe nityāsannaprabalavirajaprajjvaladvāḍavāgnaupuṃsāṃ setustaraṇaśaraṇe tīvravairāgyameva  KAvk tasmādgṛhāṇa pravrajyāṃ rājaputra jitendriyaḥ etāḥ striya iva kṣipraṃ samagamasukhāḥ śriyaḥ  KAvk kriyatām kuśalāyaiva brahmacaryaparigrahaḥ tyajyatāmeṣa niḥsāragṛhasaṃsāradurgrahaḥ  KAvk iti śrutvā bhagavataḥ karuṇābahraṇaṃ vacaḥ pratyabhāṣata taṃ nandaḥ pūrvapraṇayayantritaḥ  KAvk sadā bhavadupāyaiva pravrajyā bhagavan mama bhikṣusaṃghopakārārthe gṛha evādaraḥ param  KAvk ityuktvā bhagavadvākyamatikrāntumanīśvaraḥ kṛṣyamāṇaḥ priyāpremṇā so bhūddolākulāśayaḥ  KAvk punaḥ punaścakārāsya bhagavān vratadeśanām upakārodyatāḥ santaścintayanti na yogyatām  KAvk yadā necchati nandastām pravrajyāmajitendriyaḥ tadāsya bahgavadvākyamapatadvapuṣi svayam  KAvk nandaḥ kāṣāyāvaraṇaḥ pātrapāṇiḥ sa tatkṣaṇam babhau cābhīkararucirmahāpuruṣalakṣaṇaiḥ  KAvk sa śāsanājjinasyābhūdāraṇyapiṇḍapātrikah ākārādanagāratām prayātaḥ pāṃśukūlikaḥ  KAvk priyāmuvāha satataṃ śyāmāṃ pravrajito pi saḥ śaśāṅka iva saṃvyaktāṃ hṛdaye lāñchanacchavim  KAvk manasaḥ sphaṭikasyeva na vidmaḥ kena vartmanā rāgaḥ ko pi viśatyantarnāpaiti kṣālito pi yaḥ  KAvk virahāpāṇḍuraruciḥ saṃsaktāruṇacīvaraḥ sa saṃdhyābhrakalaṅkasya jahāra śaśinaḥ śriyam  KAvk vicaran virahākṣamaḥ sa vismṝtadhṛtirvane janmavidyāmanaṅgasya na visasmāra sundarīm  KAvk saṃpūrṇacandravadanāvadanadhyānaniścalaḥ acintyacciraṃ tattadupaviṣya śilātale  KAvk aho bhagavatāpyeṣa kṛto yatnādanugrahaḥ nāyāti mama vaimalyaṃ rāgādhiṣṭhitacetasaḥ  KAvk śrutaṃ saṃsāracaritaṃ niḥsaṅgavratamāsthitam tathāpi mṛgasāvākṣīṃ na vismarati me manaḥ  KAvk kāntākuṅkumalagnarāgasubhage gātre kṛtaṃ cīvaraṃtatpīnastanamaṇḍalapraṇayinā pātraṃ dhṛtaṃ pāṇinā rāgo yaṃ mama vardhate sya yadi vānyasyeva vṛddhiḥ paraṃ yadbodhivyavadhānabhūtamaniśaṃ dhyānaṃ tadālambanam  KAvk kṣaṇena māṃ prāptamavehi mugdhe tāmevamuktvā gamane purastāt aho mayā darśanavighnabhūtaṃ paścāt kṛtaghnavratametadāttam  KAvk no gantavyamiti prakampataralā vākyaṃ yadūce na sāsaṃtyajya vyajanaṃ sthite gurujane jagrāha pāṇyañcalam yatpādena likhantyapi kṣititalaṃ māmaukṣatālakṣitātenātyantaniṣedhamugdhavidhinā baddhaṃ tayā me manaḥ  KAvk madviyuktā na sā nūnaṃ śete śokapralāpinī puline cakravākīva harmye hariṇyalocanā  KAvk hā priye taktasaktena kitaveneva kevalam śritaṃ taccittacaureṇa mithyāvratamidaṃ mayā  KAvk tyaktvā vratamidaṃ tāvad gacchām idayitāntikam anurāgāgnitaptānāṃ tapastāpo hi duḥsahaḥ  KAvk rājaputrī cirāyātaṃ nṛśaṃsamavalokya mām manyunā navalagnena na jāne kiṃ kariṣyati  KAvk na sarvatra vikārāya nikāraḥ premaduḥsahaḥ durnivāro bhavatyeva snehalīno rajaḥkaṇaḥ  KAvk yasmin kṣaṇe bhagavatā paśyāmi rahitaṃ vanam mayā tadaiva gantavyaṃ gṝhamityeṣa niścayaḥ  KAvk asminneva śilāpaṭṭe rucirairgiridhātubhiḥ likhāmi tām śaśimukhīṃ saṃrpāpyālambanaṃ dhṛteḥ  KAvk athavā kathamālekhyaviṣayaṃ yāti sā priyā saundaryabidnako yasyāḥ sudhākuvalayendavaḥ  KAvk dṛṣṭirmugdhakurangasaṃcaladalivyāptotpalodvātanīlāvaṇyodadhikūlavidrumavanaṃ bimbādharāgratviṣaḥ nirdoṣāmṛtaraśmisārthasaraṇiḥ sā kāpi vaktradyutiḥsaundaryaṃ kathameti citrapadavīścaryasāraṃ vapuḥ  KAvk iti saṃcintya sa śanairālilekha śilātale sundarīṃ mukhamuktāśrusnātakampākulāṅguliḥ  KAvk sa saṃkalpasamudgīrṇaṃ pratibimbamivāśritām kṛtvā puraḥ priyatamāmūce darbāṣpagadgadaḥ  KAvk priyāmālikhyāhaṃ nikhilasukhavṛṣṭiṃ nayanayorna paśyāmyudbāṣpaḥ kṣaṇamapi śaraccandravadanām ayaṃ nūnaṃ tanvīvirahanirapekṣavratavataḥsphurattāpaḥ śāpaḥ kimapi mama pāpādupanataḥ  KAvk phullāmbhojavanatviṣā spṛhāvaśāsaktāśrutoyaṃ vapustatkālopagatāntarāyajanitaḥ kopaḥ samutsṛjyatām haṃho sundari dehi me prativacaḥ kiṃ maunamālambasesatyaṃ tvanmayarāgavīcaramidaṃ cittavrataṃ me vratam  KAvk iti bruvāṇaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā dūrādālikhitaṃ ca tat sāsūyā bhikṣavo bhyetya bhagavantaṃ babhāṣire  KAvk bhagavan durvinītasya vātsalyādeva kevalam śunaḥ kusumamāleva pravrajyeyaṃ tvayārpitā  KAvk ākhilya sundarīmukhaṃ nandaḥ svairaṃ śilātale tatpralāpajapāsakto dhyānālambanatāṃ gataḥ  KAvk etadākarṇya bhagavān nandamāhvāyya kananāt kimetaditi papraccha priyāvirahamohitam  KAvk so bravīd bhagavan satyaṃ kāntāsaktasya me param bhikṣūṇāṃ saṃmate pyasmin vane na ramate matiḥ  KAvk iti dandavacaḥ śrutvā tamūce bhagavān jinah mīlayanneva vaktrendukāntyā rāgasaroruham  KAvk sādho tāvanna yuktā te saṃrāgānugatā matiḥ vighnairnākṛṣyate cetaḥ kalyāṇābhiniveśinām  KAvk kvāyaṃ yogastanutṛṇatulātyaktabhogābhiyogaḥkkāyaṃ nindyaḥ kṣaṇasukhalavāsvādasaṃvāda eṣaḥ jātyaivāyaṃ harati kuśalaṃ dustaro māramārgaḥpremāndhānām bhavati sahasā duḥsaho yoktrajātaḥ  KAvk ityasya bhagavān kṛtvā ciraṃ vairāgyadeśanām saṃsthātavyamihetyuktvā svakṛtyāya svayaṃ yayau  KAvk tamevāvasaraṃ nandaḥ saṃcintya gamanocitam pratasthe svagṛhaṃ hṛṣṭaḥ sundarīdarśanotsukaḥ  KAvk vrajan dvāri pidhānāptairvihārairbahubhiścirāt nagarābhimukhaṃ mārgaṃ sa kathaṃcidavāptavān  KAvk atha vijñāya sarvajñastaṃ rāgād gantumudyatam uvācābhyetya bhagavān nanda tūrṇaṃ kka gamyate  KAvk sa jagāda vane tāvat bhagavan nāsti me ratiḥ na hyaviśrāntacittānāṃ kriyā kācit prasīdati  KAvk sā śrīścāmarahāsinī maṇimayī sā ramyaharmyāvalīsā bālānilalolacārulatikā kāntā navodyānabhūḥ sā tanvī kusumeṣukārmukalatā kṣāmodarī sundarīno janmāntaravāsanā iva manaḥ saktaṃ vimuñcanti me  KAvk sarāgeṇaiva manasā brahacaryaṃ carāmyaham vratapañjarabandhena vihaṅga iva yantritaḥ  KAvk tyaktvā vrajāmi pravrajyāmastu me narako kṣayaḥ na vītarāgatāmeti mañjiṣṭhāraktamaṃśukam  KAvk iti bruvāṇamasakṛt svapadaṃ gantumudyatam nivāryānugrahadhiyā tamūce bhagavān jinaḥ  KAvk mā kṛthā viplavaṃ nanda ninditaṃ hi śrutāśrutam vidvajjanopadiṣṭena yathā yāti pṛthagjanaḥ  KAvk vivekavyastadoṣāṇāṃ viduṣāṃ śīlaśālinām niḥsārasukhalābhena nākārye dhīḥ pravartate  KAvk gāḍharāgagṛhītasya jugupsāyatane param jadhanyakarmaṇyāsaktiḥ kiṃ lajjājanane na te  KAvk yonijayonisaṃsaktāḥ stanapastanamardinaḥ aho bata na lajjante janmanyeva layaṃ gatāḥ  KAvk sadāsajjanavarjitā jananījaghanāsaktiḥ saṃmohāhatacittānāṃ paśūnāmeva dṛśyate  KAvk rāmāramaṇamāno yaṃ viramya tyajyatāṃ tvayā bhogaiḥ saha bhujaṅgānāṃ dṛṣṭo bhavabile kṣayaḥ  KAvk jaghanyā janayatyeva na kasya viratiṃ ratiḥ yasyāṃ bhavati paryanteṣvapi naiva parāṅmukhaḥ  KAvk gṛhajālavimuktastvaṃ kiṃ tatraivābhidhāvasi na hi nirgasya sāraṅgaḥ punarviśati vāgurāṃ  KAvk iti vākyād bhagavataḥ śāsanena niyantritaḥ cintayan sundarīṃ nandaḥ praviveśāśramaṃ punaḥ  KAvk tataḥ kadācidādiśya nanda māśramamārjane āsanānugrahavyagraḥ prayayau bhagavān punah  KAvk tacchāsanāt pravṛttasya nandasyāśramaśodhane no bhūtalādapayayau rajo rāga ivāśayat  KAvk tasyāhartuṃ gatasyātha salilaṃpārabhāgikam muhuḥ pūrṇasamutkṣiptah śūnya evābhavaddhaṭaḥ  KAvk tena vighnena gamane sutarām khinnamānasaḥ tyaktvā tuprayayau nandaḥ sundarīdarśanotsukaḥ  KAvk atha vijñāya sarvajñastaṃ yāntaṃ divyacakṣuṣā babhāṣe sahasābhyetya stambhamānamanorathah  KAvk pātrayogena taptasya śyāmaraktaruceḥ param aho snehakalaṅkaste dīpasyeva na śāmyati  KAvk alaṃ vāmābhilāṣeṇa nīlīrāga ivaiṣa te saṃsaktaḥ ko pi hṛdaye yannādyāpi virajyase  KAvk andhīkaroti prārambhe ratistatkālakātaram āliṅgati jugupseva vṛtte mukhyāṅgasaṃgame  KAvk viṣayākhvādasaṅgena pāpamitrairivendriyaiḥ duḥsahavyasanāvarte pātyate narake narah  KAvk adhivāsayati sparśalekhenāpi kusaṃgamaḥ praklinnamatsyakuṇapāt pūtigandha ivodgataḥ  KAvk kalyāṇamitrasaṃparkaḥ sarvathā kuśalāvahaḥ śubhāmeda iva vyāpto yaḥ karoti mahārhatām  KAvk ityukte tasya bhagavān sākṣāts adasatoḥ pathi ghrāṇasparśena saṃdarśya cakre tatsaṅgadeśanām  KAvk atha nandaṃ samādāya bhagavān gandhamādane yayau viriñciramarībālavyajanavījitaḥ  KAvk tatra dāvānalapliṣṭāmaniṣṭakliṣṭavigrahām kāṇāṃ karmaṭīkāmasmai darśayitvāvadajjinaḥ  KAvk imāṃ paśyasi kiṃ nanda māndyanindyatarākṛtim kasmaiciducitā ceyaṃ rocate priyadarśanā  KAvk sattā sadasatornāsti rāgaḥ paśyati ramyatām sa tasya lalito loke yo yasya dayito janaḥ  KAvk pakṣapātaṃ samṛtsṛjya satyaṃ nanda tvayocyatām asyāstasyāśca sundaryā lāvaṇyasya kimantaram  KAvk anarthitvādvayaṃ naiva saundaryāntaravedinaḥ arthipriyatvamāyāti prārthitaṃ tacca cārutām  KAvk paśyāmyahaṃ viśeṣaṃ tu tasyā nāsyāśca kaṃcana ramyatvaṃ māṃsavarmāsthiyantre samayamātrakam  KAvk iti pṛṣṭo bahgavatā nandastaṃ pratyabhāsata atyantānucitaḥ praśnaḥ ko pi gauravayantritaḥ  KAvk kimetad bhagavān vakti keyaṃ śoke biḍambanā kkāpi vā viśvaguravo vineyāḥ prabhaviṣṇavah  KAvk ratiḥ sādhikasundaryāḥ parabhāgeṇa rajyate yāṃ dṛṣṭvā jagatāṃ jetā na ratiṃ smarati smaraḥ  KAvk jyotsnayeva na tatkāntyā nodate kumudākaraḥ guṇāntaraṃ na jānāti prasiddhiśaraṇo janaḥ  KAvk baddhaṃ tayā vadanasaurabhasārahāramālokya puṣyanicayaṃ pṛthukeśapāśe manye vilāsagatilovanakānticauraiḥ bhītyeva haṃsahariṇairvanamiva yātam  KAvk analpaiḥ saṃkalpairbahuvidhavikalpairanupamāna sā sāraṅgākṣīlikhitumapi śakyā paricitaiḥ tulārohe ysyā vadanaparabhāge laghutaraḥsa nūnaṃ tārāṇāṃ gaganamadhirūḍhaḥ parivṛḍhaḥ  KAvk puṇyaprahvaṃ lalitalalitabhrūlatālāsyalīlāramyaṃ tasyā yadi na vadanaṃ nandanaṃ labhyate tat pravrajyeyaṃ sukṛtamadhikaṃ kiṃkarī kiṃkarī mekasmādetaṃ vrataparikaraṃ bhārabhūtaṃ vahāmi  KAvk iti nandavacaḥ śrutvā bhagavān rāganirbharam upakṣipya prabhāveta ta nināya surālayam  KAvk adarśayacca tatrāsya līlodyāne śatakratoḥ sudhāmanthasamudbhūtāḥ kāntāstridaśayoṣitaḥ  KAvk aruṇaiḥ kāntisaṃtānaiḥ pādapadmavanoditaiḥ anuyātā ivāmbhodhikūlavidrumakānanaiḥ  KAvk viśālalāsyasacivaiḥ pāṇibhirvijitāmbujaiḥ saṃsaktaiḥ sahajasyeva pārijātasya pallavaiḥ  KAvk kāntimādhuryalalitairmadanānandabāṇdhavaiḥ helānimīlitāmbhojavadanaiścandrasundaraiḥ  KAvk saṃmohanairjīvanaiśca kṛṣṇasārairvilokanaiḥ kālakūṭacchadaspṛṣṭairamṛtoghairivāvṛtāḥ  KAvk pūrṇayauvanalāvaṇyāḥ sahasaiva vilokya tāḥ nandaḥ sānandavadanaḥ svedasnāta ivābhavat  KAvk padmānanāsu vipulotpalalocanāsu kundastimātu nibiḍastabakastanīṣu nandasya tāsu hṛdayaṃ yugapannipatya dolāvilāsataralālitumavāpa  KAvk tataḥ provāca bahgavān nandaṃ tadgatamānasam āsāṃ saṃdarśane nanda prītyā te ramate matiḥ  KAvk āsāṃ tasyāśca sundaryā lāvaṇye kiyadantaram utkarṣaḥ parabhāgeṇa sphuṭamevābhibhāvyate  KAvk nirastasundarīrūpaṃ rūpamapsarasām yadi tadetā eva kālena kariṣyāmi tvadāśrayāḥ  KAvk ārogeṇaiva manasā brahmacaryaṃ prasannadhīḥ cara tāvattataste haṃ dāsyāmyapsarasām gaṇam  KAvk evaṃ bhagavato vākyānnandaḥ saṃjātaniścayaḥ tathetyuktvā vrate cetaścakre svargāṅganāśayā  KAvk mandādaraḥ svadāreṣu so bhūt tatsaṃgamecchayā guṇapṇyatulāvṛtternāsti snehasya satyatā  KAvk aho cismṛtasaṃvāsapravāsapariśoṣitā puṃsāmābhyāsikī prītiḥ sahasānyatra dhāvati  KAvk kṣaṇayauvanaramyāṇi premāṇi praṇayavyayaiḥ na satyāni na nityāni na sukhāni śarīriṇām  KAvk tato bhagavatā nandaḥ kṣaṇānītaḥ svamāśramam tanniścayād brahmacaryaṃ cacāra niyatavrataḥ  KAvk sa cisasmāra sundaryāḥ kāntisaṃpadamanyadhīḥ kṣaṇapramuṣitā prītirmalaṃ yāti guṇeṣvapi  KAvk tataḥ kadācidvicaran nandaḥ kkāpi vyalokayat karālanarakāsaktāṃ dhīmān kumbhībhṛtāṃ bhuvam  KAvk tām vilokyaiva sākampaḥ kimetaditi duḥkhitaḥ sa papraccha tadāsaktān ghoranarakakāraṇam  KAvk te tamūcuriyaṃ bhūmistaptakumbhīśatācitā kalpitā rājaputrasya nandasyānandarāgiṇaḥ  KAvk mithyāvrataḥ sa nādyāpi bhajate vītarāgatām brahamcaryaṃ caratyeva svargastrūīsaṃgamāśayā  KAvk mithyāvratānām lubdhānāṃ rāgadveṣakaṣāyiṇām etāsu nityataptāsu kumbhīṣvevākṣayaḥ kṣayaḥ  KAvk iti nanda samākarṇya jātaromāñcakañcukah tatra cyutāmiva tanūṃ paścāttāpādamanyataḥ  KAvk samamyetya tyaktarāgasaṃvāsavāsanah svayam babhūvānuttarabrahmacaryaparyāptāṃyamaḥ  KAvk ghanamohakṣayāttasya vimukte saṃśaye tataḥ mahaḥ prasādamāpede śaradīvedadheḥ payaḥ  KAvk niṣkāmaḥ praśamaṃ prāptaḥ parāṃ niṣṭhāmupāgataḥ śuddhadhīḥ sa samabhyetya bhagavantamabhāṣata  KAvk nāpsarobhirna sundaryā bhagavan kṛtyamasti me etāḥ paryantavicchāyāḥ sapātā viṣayaśriyaḥ  KAvk yathā yatheyaṃ bhāvānāṃ bhāvyate niḥsvabhāvatā tathā tathā prqsīdanti nirāvaraṇavṛttayaḥ  KAvk iti dandasya vadataḥ prāptasyārtapadaṃ śanaiḥ bhagavān nirvāṇaśuddhāmasya siddhimamanyata  KAvk keṣāṃ kuśalamūlānāṃ nandenāsāditaṃ phalam iti bhikṣubhirabhyetya pṛṣṭhastānavadajjinaḥ  KAvk janmāntarārjitaiḥ puṇyaiḥ sukṛtābhyāsakāriṇā prāptāḥ kuśalamūlānāṃ nandena phalasaṃpadaḥ  KAvk vipulavimala vaṃśe janma smarapratimā tanuḥsurajanasakhī lakṣī vṛttiḥ priyāḥ satataṃ satām praśamasalilasnātaṃ cetaḥ svabhāvagatirgatiḥkuśalakusumasyeyaṃ puṃsāṃ viśālaphalodgatiḥ  KAvk stūpe vipaśyinaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhasyādaraḥ purā nagaryāmaruṇāvatyāmaruṇena mahībhūhā  KAvk kriyamāṇo maṇimaye maitro nāma dvijanmajaḥ mahataḥ puṇyabhogasya bhāgī kārakatām yayau  KAvk tatpuṇyapraṇidhānena jāto gṝhapateḥ kule sa eva bhikṣusaṃghasya jantukāsnānasatrakṛt  KAvk sa puṇyaśīlaḥ pratyekabuddhopasthāyakah purā stūpaṃ cakre śobhamānaṃ mālabhivaraṇojjvalam  KAvk tatpuṇyapraṇidhānena kṛkeḥ kāśīpateḥ sutaḥ so bhvaddyutimān nāma divyalakṣaṇalakṣitaḥ  KAvk kāśyapasyārhataḥ samyaksaṃbuddasyāntanirvṛtau saptaratnamaye stūpe kṛte kāśīmahībhujā  KAvk tatsūnurdhyutimān haumacchatramāropya bhāsvaram jātastatpraṇidhānena nandaḥ śākyamuke dhunā  KAvk iti sukṛtasamutthaiḥ pūrvajanvakramāptaiḥ kimapi vipulapuṇyaireva nandaḥ prapede kulamamalamudāraṃ rūmamagryaṃ ca bhogaṃ śamaparicitamante satpadaṃ saugataṃ ca  KAvk kathayotveti bhagavān nandakalyāṇakāraṇam cakāra bhikṣusaṃghasya tāṃ tāṃ sukṛtadeśanām  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ sundarīnandāvadānaṃ nāma daśamaḥ pallavaḥ  virūḍhakāvadānam ārohati padamunnatamamalamatirvimalakuśalasopānaiḥ narakakuhareṣu nipatati malinamatirghoratimireṣu  KAvk śākyānāṃ nagare pūrvaṃ sphīte kapilavāstuni mahataḥ śākyamukhyasya sumukhī dāsakanyākā  KAvk śāstre kṛtaśramā sarvakalākauśalaśālinī mālikā nāma kāmasya mālikeva guṇocitā  KAvk prabhorgirā varodyāne kusumāvacayodyatā bhramantaṃ taṃ samāyāntaṃ dadarśa sugataṃ puraḥ  KAvk tasyānte syāstamālokya prasannamabhavanmanaḥ śaratkāla iva svacchaḥ prasādayati mānasam  KAvk sācintayattadā lokaprītyā dṛḍhīkṛtāspadā sukṛtaiḥ piṇḍapātaṃ me gṛhṇīyādbhagavānapi  KAvk vijñāya tasyāh sarvajñaḥ saṃkalpaṃ karuṇākulaḥ prasārya pātraṃ bhagavān bhadre dehītyuvāca tām  KAvk datvā praṇamya sā tasmai paripūrṇamanorathā praṇidhānaṃ pravidadhe dāsyaduḥkhanivṛttaye  KAvk tataḥ kadācidāyātaḥ pituastasyāḥ sakhā dvijaḥ naumittikastaṃ pradeśaṃ dṛṣṭvā tām vismito va dat  KAvk aho gṛhapatestasya putrī tvaṃ śrīmatah sutā bandhuhīnā gatā dāsyaṃ dhanabhogavivarjitā  KAvk aho mohaghanārambhakṣaṇoddyotanavidyutaḥ saṃsārasarparasanāvilāsacapalāḥ śriyaḥ  KAvk gamyānāṃ mā kṛthāścintāṃ jāne haṃ hastalakṣaṇaiḥ acireṇaiva bhūbharturvallabhā tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi  KAvk idaṃ paśyāmi te pāṇau lakṣmīkamalakomale mālācakrāṅkuśākāramityuktvā prayayau dvijaḥ  KAvk atha manmathasaṃbhogasuhṛnmadhupabāndhavaḥ latāliṅganasaubhāgyabhavyo dṛśyata mādhavaḥ  KAvk madhoḥ kesariṇastasya kāntāmānadvipadviṣaḥ vibabhau jihmamānasya jihvevāśokamañjarī  KAvk bālākapolalāvaṇyacauraścampakasaṃcayaḥ sudṛśāṃ keśapāśeṣu yayau bandhanayogyatām  KAvk sahakārairvirahiṇīnidhanaṃ vidadhe madhu nirapekṣāparavadhe vidhurāḥ prabhaviṣṇavaḥ  KAvk yayurmadhulihāṃ cūtalatā nirbharabhogyatām sahasauva vidgadhānāmiva mugdhavibhūtayaḥ  KAvk rūtāyudhaścūtalatācāpanyastaśilīmukhaḥ jayatīti jagau bandī kandarpasyeva kokilaḥ  KAvk asminnavasare śrīmān kosalendraḥ prasenajit mṛgayānirgato śvena hṛtastaṃ deśamāyayau  KAvk dhanvīmanobhavākāraḥ so vatīrya turaṃgamāt dadarśānanyalāvaṇyām kanyāṃ ratimivāparām  KAvk tadvilokanavistīrṇaṃ manastasya mahātmanaḥ vismayāddṛṣṭimārgeṇa praviveśa manobhavaḥ  KAvk tāṃ lajjāvanatāṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasodbhūītasādhvasām acintayannarapatiḥ kāntikallilinīhṛtaḥ  KAvk keyaṃ navā śaśimukhī śyāmā taralatārakā yatkāntiraniśaṃ netraśatapatravikāśinī  KAvk bakulāmodavibhrāntabhramare pāṭalādhare kāntaṃ vasantaṃ paśyāmi mukhe syāḥ kumudāyudham  KAvk aho lāvaṇyamamlānaṃ tāruṇyābharaṇaṃ tanoḥ dhīrasyāpi dhṛtiryena śaṅkhe saṃgaliteva me  KAvk aho nu madhumañjaryāḥ prārambhe pyadbhuto guṇaḥ yena gantuṃ na śaknoti ṣaṭpado pi padātpadam  KAvk iti saṃcintya bhīpālastāṃ matvā vanadevatām pṛṣṭvā viveda tadvṛttaṃ krameṇa kathitaṃ tayā  KAvk tatastatra kṛtātithyastayā pallavavījanaiḥ śuciśītaiśca salilaiḥ prāptavān nirvṛtiṃ nṛpaḥ  KAvk śrāntaḥ saṃvāhane tasya tayā caraṇapadmayoḥ kṛte karāptasaṃsparśe sa nidrām sahasā yayau  KAvk kṣaṇena pratibyddho tha viśrāntamṛgayāśramaḥ divyasparśena tām mene ratiṃ rūpāntarāgatām  KAvk mahānapi tataḥ śākyaḥ saṃprāptaṃ kosaleśvaram śrutvā taṃ deśamabhyetya pūjārhaṃ tamapūjayat  KAvk sādareṇārthitāṃ tena svasutāmiva mālikām ratnārhāya dadau tasmai smaramaṅgalamālikām  KAvk tāmādāya manojanmavaijayantīṃ sitasmitām nijaṃ jagāma nagaraṃ gajamāruhya bhūpatiḥ  KAvk tasminnāganagotsaṅge sā lolālakaṣaṭpadā babhau rājavasantena saṃgatā navamālikā  KAvk rājadhānīṃ samāsādya sundaryā sahitastayā ratnaharmyakarodāramandire vijahāra saḥ  KAvk varṣākārābhidhā devī rājñaḥ prathamavallabhā abhinnavṛttiṃ tām mene rājalakṣmīmiva kṣitiḥ  KAvk divyasparśena sā tasyāḥ sā cāsyā rūpasaṃpadā parasparaguṇotkarṣātparaṃ vismayamāpatuḥ  KAvk divyarūpavatī jyeṣṭhā divyasparśavatī par ā iti pravādaḥ sāścaryastayuorlokeṣu paprathe  KAvk atrāntare tayordivyarūpasaṃsparśakāraṇam āśrame bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ provāca bhagavān jinaḥ  KAvk purā śrutavarākhyasya dvijasya gṛhamedhinaḥ kāntā śirīṣikā ceti priye bhārye babhūvatuḥ  KAvk sa kadācidatho kāntābhrātā pravrajyayā śanaiḥ pratyekabuddhatāṃ yātaḥ svasurbhavanamāyayau  KAvk traimāsikopacāreṇa sa tayā patyurājñayā bhaktyā nimantritastasthau tatsaptnyāvapūjitaḥ  KAvk te cārumṛdubhirbhogaistamabhyarcyānyajanmani jāte dhunā cārurūpadivyasaṃsparśasaṃyute  KAvk kṛṣṭeṣu prathamaṃ prayuktavinayāmādāya gosaṃpadaṃsatkṣetreṣu tapaḥ pratatptanuṣu prāptiṣvatisvādutām yatkāle śubhabījamuptamucitaṃ satkarmaśakteḥ paraṃbhujyante phalasaṃpadaḥ sumatibhistasyaiva pākojjvalāḥ  KAvk iti sarvajñavacanam tathyamākarṇya bhikṣavaḥ tattatheti viniścitya babhūvuḥ śāntisaṃśrayāḥ  KAvk atha kālena bhūbharturmālikāyāmabhūtsutaḥ virūḍhaketimukhyākhyo vidyāsu ca kṛtaśramah  KAvk priyastulyavayāstasya purohitasuto bhavat māturduḥkhena jātatvādviśruto duḥkhamātṛkaḥ  KAvk kadācit sahitastena hayārūḍho virūḍhakah prāpa śākyavarodyānaṃ mṝgayāyām vinirgataḥ  KAvk nyakkāraṃ cakrire tatra śākyāstasyodyatāyudhāḥ ayaṃ dāsīsuto smākamiti darpapravādinah  KAvk gatvāsau svapuraṃ teṣāṃ vairaṃ darpyamacintayat kuladarpāpavādo bhedayuktibhiḥ  KAvk tataḥ kadācitsaṃjātavivekaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ dharmopadeśaśravaṇe vardhamānādaraḥ param  KAvk cārātyaṇagṛhītāśvaṃ rathamāruhya saṃyataḥ draṣṭuṃ jagāma sarvajñaṃ bhagavantam prasenajit  KAvk prāyāśramaṃ bhagavataḥ kṛtvā pādābhivandanam dharmānvayam sa śuśrāva tatprasādaprasannadhīḥ  KAvk cārāyaṇo pyāśu gatvā rathena nagaraṃ javāt akarodantare tasmin rājaputrābhiṣecanam  KAvk bhagavantamathāmantrya nṛpatirgantumudyataḥ dadarśa nānugānagre na rathaṃ na ca mantriṇam  KAvk sa padbhyāmeva śanakaiḥ prasthitām pṛthivīpatiḥ dūrādapaśyadāyāntīṃ varṣākārāṃ samālikām  KAvk te pṛṣṭvā tadgirā jñātvā so bhiṣiktaṃ virūḍhakam visasarja sutaiśvaryaparibhogāya mālokām  KAvk varṣākārāṃ samādāya sa mitrasya mahīpateḥ ajātaśatrornagaraṃ prāta rājagṛhābhidham  KAvk sa tatptaśchatravirahāt kṣuptipāsāśramānvitaḥ yayau vamanniva śvāsaṃ dīrgheśvāramamārutaiḥ  KAvk sukhamaskhalitaṃ kena prāptaṃ kasyāyurāyatam na kasyānupadaṃ dṛṣṭaḥ kṣayaḥ sapadi saṃpadaḥ  KAvk sa jīrṇamūlakaṃ bhuktvā karmamūlamivāyatam kṣaṇaṃ pītvā ca pānīyaṃ papātāptaviṣūcikaḥ  KAvk anityatāmavijñāya mohāya patate janah sa cāpāyanikāyasya kāyasyopāyatṛṣṇayā  KAvk ajātaśatruḥ śrutvaiva kosaleśvaramāgatam abhyetya pāṃśupūrṇāsyaṃ vigatāsuṃ dadarśa tam  KAvk tasya jāyānuyātasya sa kṛtvā dehasatkriyām bhagavantaṃ yayau druṣṭuṃ sugataṃ duḥkhaśāntaye  KAvk sa taṃ praṇamya provāca bhagavan kosaleśvaraḥ puraṃ me suhṝdaḥ prāya nirdhano nidhanaṃ gataḥ  KAvk dhiṅbhāmasaṃpadaṃ pāpaṃ mihādayaśasaḥ padam vibhavo yena naivāyaṃ mitropakaraṇīkṛtaḥ  KAvk hṛdaye viniveśyāśāṃ prāptaḥ suhṝdamāpadi suhṛnnaiṣphalyamāyāti yasya kiṃ tena jīvatā  KAvk mitropakaraṇaṃ lakṣmīrdīnopakaraṇam dhanam bhītopakaraṇaṃ prāṇā yeṣāṃ teṣāṃ sujīvitam  KAvk kukarma kiṃ kṛtaṃ tena bhagavan ūrvajanmani yasya pākena paryante prapede so tidurdaśām  KAvk iti pṛṣṭaḥ kṣitīśena bhagavān sāśrucakṣuṣā tamūce tāpaśamanīṃ diśan daśanacandrikām  KAvk mā śucaḥ pṛthivīpāla svabhāvo yaṃ bhavasthitaḥ evaṃvidhaiva bhāvānāmasatyānāmanityatā  KAvk visārisaṃsāravanāntare smin nisargalolaḥ kila kāmabhṛṅgaḥ svacchandajātajanapuṣkarajīvapuñjakiñjalkapuñjamaniśaṃ kavalīkaroti  KAvk taraṅganto bhogāścakitahariṇīlocanacalāḥ kṣaṇe lakṣyā pibhavāyāsaṃ nirvivekasya sarvathā kriyate kiṃ janasyāsya mohādakuśalaspṛśaḥ  KAvk purā vipraḥ suśarmākhyaḥ kutaścitprāpya mūlakam nidhāya jananīhaste yayau snātuṃ nadītaṭam  KAvk sāpi tanmayātithaye rpitam iti māturvacaḥ śrutvāso bhūdviddha iveṣuṇā  KAvk sadyo viṣūcikārtasya manmūlakamanalpakam kukṣiṃ bhittvā viniryātu prāṇaiḥ saha ta vātitheḥ  KAvk iti tasyāptapāpasya vākyāruṣyeṇa bhūyasā visūcikaiva paryante babhūvaparajanmani  KAvk prākpuṇyāntarapākena sa evādya prasenajit vipulaṃ rājyamāsādya tayaivānte kṣayaṃ gataḥ  KAvk saṃsārapathapānthānāmevaṃ karma śubhāśubham pātheyamiva hastastham bhogāyaivopapadyate  KAvk iti śrutvā bhagavatastathyaṃ pathyaṃ ca tadvacaḥ evametaditi dhyātvā taṃ praṇamya yayau nṛpaḥ  KAvk atrāntare prāptarājyaḥ śākyavairaṃ virūḍhakaḥ purohitasutenaitya smāritastatkṣayodyataḥ  KAvk prayayau śākyanagaraṃ gajāśvarathareṇunā moheneva diśāṃ kurvan nirvivekaṃ dhiyāmiva  KAvk sarvajño bhagavān jñātvā tasya tadduṣṭaceṣṭitam gatvā śākyapuropānte tasthau śuṣkataroradhah  KAvk dūrāttatra sthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā tamāgacchan virūḍhakaḥ avatīrya rathādagramabhyetya praṇato vadat  KAvk satsu snigdhapalāśeṣu ghanacchāyeṣu śākhiṣu bhagavannatra viśrāntiḥ kimu śuṣkataroradhaḥ  KAvk ityuktaḥ kṣitipālena taṃ prāha bhagavān jinaḥ jñāticchāyā narapateḥ candanādapi śītalā  KAvk nāsti jñātisamaṃ vittaṃ nāsti jñātisamā dhṛtiḥ nāsti jñātisamā chāyā saṃprāptaṃ tasya śāsanāt  KAvk śeṣāstu mūḍhamatayaḥ śākyāḥ prāpurna tatpadam santi ke pi khagā yeṣām vāsare timiro dbhavaḥ  KAvk nivṛttasyātha nṛpateḥ purohitasutastataḥ vairasarpasya suptasya vidadhe pratibodhanam  KAvk sa tena preritaścakre matiṃ śākyakulakṣaye vairānalaṃ pracalanaṃ karoti piśunānilaḥ  KAvk ghoradurjanamantreṇa sahasotthāpitāḥ khalāḥ vetālā kṣitipālāśca na kasya prāṇahāriṇah  KAvk sainye gajarathodagre tatastasmin prasarpati babhūva purasaṃkṣobhaḥ śākyānāṃ rūddhavartmanām  KAvk tasmin bhagavān rakṣārthaṃ śākyānāṃ pakṣapātinam samudyataṃ tatra mahāmaudgalyāyanamabravīt  KAvk śākyānāṃ karmadoṣo yaṃ sarvathā samupasthitaḥ tatra rakṣavidhānaṃ te gagane setubandhanam  KAvk puṃsamavintyavibhavāni śubhāśubhāni āyānti yānti ca muhurniravagrahāṇi karmākṣarāṇi nijajanmapadasvahastanyastāni nāma na bhavanti nirarthakāni  KAvk iti vākyādbhagavatastasmin yāte praṇamya tam cakrire saṃvidaṃ śākyāh pratyāsanne virūḍhake  KAvk hiṃsāsmābhirna kartavyā prāṇimātrasya kasyacit śarāḥ śarīramasmākaṃ viśantvarisamīritāḥ  KAvk iti saṃvidamādhāya te viyaṣṭikapāṇayaḥ dhīrḥ parodyame tasthuravārayitakārmukāḥ  KAvk atrāntare karmayogānnijadeśānavasthitaḥ ajñātvā saṃvidaṃ śākyaḥ śaṃpākah samupāyayau  KAvk sa dṛṣṭvā nagare baddhasaṃnāhaṃ vasudhādhipam kopādekaścakārāsya raṇe subhaṭasaṃkṣayam  KAvk yuddhe puruṣasiṃhena hatāste vīrakuñjarāḥ prayayuḥ spṛhaṇīyatvaṃ yaśobhirmaktikairiva  KAvk sa ko pi tasya jajvāla kopitasya parairasiḥ sa yayau yatpratāpena vipulāṃ ripuvāhinīm  KAvk praveśaṃ na daduḥ śākyāḥ śaṃpākasya dviṣāṃ vadhāt svajano pi parityaktaḥ sa tairnistriṃśakarmaṇā  KAvk nije pi vimukhāḥ krūre sādhave dahrambandhavaḥ dhānādapi vadānyatvaṃ sukṛtaṃ svajanādapi  KAvk          śatamaucityanityānāmāyuṣo pi yaśaḥ priyam  KAvk nirvāsitaḥ sa taiḥ prāptaḥ śanairbhagavato ntikam yayāce bhyudayāyāiva taṃ kiṃcinnijalāñchanam  KAvk ṛddhaṃ bhagavatā dattaṃ nijakeśanakhāṃśakam sa jagāma samādāya vākuḍaṃ nāma maṇḍalam  KAvk tatra prajñāprabhāveṇa śauryotsāhaguṇena ca sa prāpa rājyaṃ dhīrāṇāṃ sarvatra sulabhāḥ śriyaḥ  KAvk dakṣāṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ lakṣmīḥ sahajaṃ viduṣāṃ yaśaḥ vyavasāyasahāyānām kalatraṃ sarvasiddhayaḥ  KAvk tatra sthito bhagavataḥ so tha keśanakhāṃśake stūpapratiṣṭhāmakarodvarratnavirājitām  KAvk virūḍhako pi śākyānāṃ vairapāratitīrṣayā punaryuktyā puradvhārabhedena sahasāviśat  KAvk hatvā tatra sahasrāṇi śākyānāṃ saptasaptati baddhvā kanyākumārāṇāṃ sa sahasramathāharat  KAvk śatāni pañca śākyānām gajairlohaiśca mardanaiḥ saṃpramṛjya purīṃ cakre kṛtāntanagarīmiva  KAvk bhagavānapi śākyānām śatrūṇā bhedanaṃ kṛtam karmānubaddhaṃ vijñāyaṃ babhūva vimanāḥ kṣaṇam  KAvk papracchustaṃ samabhyetya bhikṣavaḥ karuṇākulāḥ kiṃ karma vihitaṃ śākyairghoraṃ yasyedṛśaṃ phalam  KAvk bhagavānaniti taiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ sarvajñastānabhāṣata nijakarmavipākena śākyānāmeṣa saṃkṣayaḥ  KAvk kṛṣṭau purā mahāmatsyau dhīvaraiḥ sarito ntarāt tadā nikṛttau śalyena bhūyo pyavyathayan dhṛtau  KAvk kālena cārutām yātaistaireva parajanmani hatau gṝhapatī dagdhvā tāveva dhanahāribhiḥ  KAvk tau matsyau tau gṛhasthau ca virūḍhakapurohitau dāsānāṃ taskarāṇām ca śākyānām mṛtyutām gatau  KAvk iti śrutvā bhagavataḥ karmaṇāṃ phalasaṃtatim avisaṃvādinīmeva menire sarvabhikṣavaḥ  KAvk virūḍhako tha svapuraṃ prāpya vijayadurmadaḥ jetānāmnā sutenoktaḥ praṇayādbālalīlayā  KAvk deva kiṃ nihatāḥ śākyān na te smākaṃ kṛtāgasaḥ iti bruvāṇamavadhīnnijasūnuṃ virūḍhakaḥ  KAvk nipātamatimṛdgati nihanti na karoti kim madalabdhanadhāyāso mātaṃga iva darjanaḥ  KAvk sa jagāda sabhāsīnaḥ svabhūjāvavalokayan aho nu mama tāpāgnau dvisadbhiḥ śalabhāyitam  KAvk kṛtāntatoraṇastambhau prājyau mama bhujāvimau niṣḥśeṣavadhadīkṣāyāṃ śākyānāṃ gurutāṃ gatau  KAvk taṃ tasya vikramaṃ ślāghyaṃ hṛtāstāḥ śākyakanyakāḥ śrutvā babhāṣire tīvramudveganamitānanāḥ  KAvk karmapāśanibaddhānāṃ khagānāmiva dehinām nidhanollaṅghane śaktirnāsti pakṣavatāmapi  KAvk yenāgniḥ śamameti tatkila jalaṃ prāpnotyalaṃ vāḍavaḥtigmāṃśugrahaṇaṃ karoti samaye helāvalehyaṃ tamah paryālocanavartmanāmaviṣayaṃ sāścaryacaryāspadaṃsarvaṃ kārmikatantrayantimidaṃ kaḥ kasya kartuṃ kṣamaḥ  KAvk etadākarṇya nṛpatiḥ padāntara iveragaḥ karacchedaṃ dideśāsāṃ ghorāmarṣaviṣotkaṭaḥ  KAvk tīre yasyāḥ kṛtaṃ tāsāṃ pāṇicchedanavaiśasam sādyāpi hastagabhati khyātā puṣkariṇī bhuvi  KAvk latāsvapi hkukūlāgniṃ krakacaṃ nalīnīṣvapi mālāsvapi śilāvarṣaṃ pātayantyeva nirghṛṇāḥ  KAvk tāśchinnapāṇikamalāstatra tīvravyathāturāḥ bhagavantaṃ dhiyā dhyātvā śaraṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ  KAvk tāsāṃ vijñāya sarvajñastīvrām marmāhativyathām śacīmacintayaddevīṃ tatsamāśvāsanocitām  KAvk tatsparśajātahastābjāstā divyavasanāvṛtāḥ yayuścittaprasādena tāh svargaṃ tyaktavigrahā  KAvk devakalpāstamāsādya divyapadmotpalāṅkitāḥ dharmadeśanayā śāstustāh prāpurvipulaṃ padam  KAvk bhikṣubhirbhagavān pṛṣṭastatkarmaphalamabhyadhāt pāṇicāpalyametābhiḥ kṛtaṃ bhikṣuviḍambane  KAvk karmaṇastasya pākena viśase patitāh param mayi cittaprasādena prāptāścaitāh śubhāṃ gatim  KAvk ityuktvā bhagavān karmaphalapākavicitratām bhukṣīṇāṃ tatprasaṅgena vidadhe dharmadeśanām  KAvk atrāntare gūḍhacārī rājñā praṇihitaścaraḥ bhagavaccaritaṃ jñātvā virūḍhakamupāyayau  KAvk so vadaddeva bhikṣūṇāṃ tenedaṃ kathitaṃ puraḥ svakarmaphalamāsannaṃ tasya paśyāmi bhūpateh  KAvk saptāhenāgninā dagdhaḥ sa pāpātmā purohitaḥ avīcināmni narake duḥsahe nipatiṣyati  KAvk iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā nṛpatiḥ sapurohitaḥ yatnāduvāsa saptāhaṃ jalānvitagṛhāntare  KAvk kṣaṇāvaśeṣe saptāhe tasminnantaḥpuraṃ gate sūryakāntārkasaṃtāpayogājjajvāla pāvakaḥ  KAvk udbhūtena pralayasavanāvartinevāśu vegānnirdagdho sau dhagiti śikhinā nārakaṃ prāpa vahnim asmiṃllike jvalanajaṭilāḥ pāpināṃ pretya rāgāḥsarvatraiva sthirasukhabhuvaḥ śītalāḥ puṇyabhājām  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ virūḍhakāvadānaṃ nāma ekādaśaḥ pallavaḥ  hārītikādamanāvadānam duḥkhaṃ nudanti sukhasaṃpadamādiśanti saṃjīvayanti janatām timiraṃ haranti sanmānasasya kalayanti vikāsahāsaṃ santaḥ sudhārdravadanāḥ śaśina karāśca  KAvk bimbisāraḥ kṣiteḥ sāre pure rājagṛhābhidhe sāraḥ samastabhūpānāmabhūdbhūmipuraṃdaraḥ  KAvk kṣamādhāre bhuje yasya kṣamādhāre ca cetasi bāhyaḥ samastacittānāmaśu nyastakaro janaḥ  KAvk kurvatastyāgaśauryābhyāmāśāyāḥ paripūraṇam pāṇau vimuktaratnaughe subaddho bhūdasigrahaḥ  KAvk kadācidabhavattasya viplavo nagare guruḥ navābhyudayasaṃjātadarpakāla ivākulaḥ  KAvk tamāsthānasamāsīnaṃ janacintākṛtakṣaṇam vyajijñipata saurājaṃ prajānāṃ janakopamam  KAvk deva divyaprabhāvasya niyataḥ śāsanena te janah sadā samudro yaṃ maryādāṃ nātivartate  KAvk yenāsya kṛtavṛttasya sanmārgeṇa prasarpataḥ upasargodgamaḥ kasmādakasmādayamāgataḥ  KAvk svadharmasaṃvṛttena hi karmaṇā śarmaṇā nṛṇām sunṛpe na ca guhyānāmāpatanti vipattayaḥ  KAvk hriyante naḥ prasūtīnāṃ gṛhiṇīnāṃgṛhe kayā apatyāni phalānīva satkriyāṇāmasaṃyamāt  KAvk kiṃtu bhūtānna vidmastān māyām cāpi mahīpate yatprabhāveṇa nīyante kulāni nirapatyatām  KAvk iti teṣāṃ girā bhūbhṛdabhūtsaṃkrāntatadvyathaḥ paraṃ duḥkhaṃ viśatyantaḥ satāṃ kedāravārivat  KAvk sarvāṅgavyāpinā tena janaduḥkhena bhūyasā viṣeṇevāvṛtaḥ so bhūdudbhrāntahṛdayaḥ kṣaṇam  KAvk so bravīt kiṃ karomyatrābhujādhīne vipaurūṣe kathaṃ nāma pravartante durlakṣyeṣu pratikriyāḥ  KAvk dinamekaṃ vrajantvadya bhavanto nijamāspadam savrataścintayāmyeva rakṣāṃ vaḥ prasvakṣaye  KAvk iti rājavacaḥ śrutvā hṛṣṭāḥ pauramahattamāḥ jagadustaṃ samāvarjya pūjāvyañjanamajṇjalim  KAvk deva tvadavadhānena praṇayākarṇanena ca tvayi vinyastacintānāṃ nāsmākamadhunā śramaḥ  KAvk anuddhatamudāraṃ c atvatprasādāvalokanam idameva janasyāsya jīvitānīva varṣati  KAvk kiṃ punaḥ priyametatte pīyūṣasadṛśaṃ vacaḥ tāpāpahaṃ mṛhu svādu kiṃ kiṃ na vidadhāti naḥ  KAvk kṛtī kṛtajñaḥ kāruṇyanidhiḥ sulabhadarśanaḥ labhyate bhāgyabhogyena saujanyasaralaḥ prabhu  KAvk pīyūṣādatipeśalaḥ paricayaḥ śrāvyaṃ vacaḥ pañcamamācāraḥ śaradinduvṛndamahaso syānandasaṃdohadaḥ saccitte vasatāṃ satām kimaparaṃ puṣpānmanah komalaṃsaujanyaṃ haricandanādapi paraṃ saṃtāpanirvāpaṇam  KAvk ityuktvā prayayuḥ paurāstaṃ praṇamya prasādinam kirantastadguṇodārāmāśākusumamālikām  KAvk rājāpi nagare kṛtvā bhūtapūjāvidhikramam śāntisvastikasaṃbhāraṃ cakāra niyatavrataḥ  KAvk yakṣī hārītikā nāma bālakān puravāsinī haratīti sa śuśrāva puradevatayoditam  KAvk tataḥ paurajanaiḥ sārdhaṃ sāmātyaḥ pṛthīvīpatiḥ kalandakanivāsākhye sthitaṃ veṇuvanāśrame  KAvk bhagavantaṃ yayau draṣṭuṃ sugataṃ doṣaśāntaye sarvaduḥkhajvarāyāsajuṣāmakaṭukauṣadham  KAvk taṃ dṛṣṭvā nṛpatirdūrātpraṇamya priyadarśanam upaviśyāgratastasmai pauraduḥkhaṃ nyavedayat  KAvk bhagavānapi vijñāya paurāṇāṃ saṃtatikṣayam cintāniścañcalaḥ kṣipramuvāca karuṇānidhiḥ  KAvk sa visṛjya jagadbandhuḥ sanṛpaṃ pauramaṇḍalam pātracīvaramādāya yayau yakṣīniketanam  KAvk tayā virahitaṃ prāpya tadgṛhaṃ bhagavān jinaḥ priyaṃkarākhyaṃ tatputraṃ nināyaikamadarśanam  KAvk yāte bhagavati kṣipraṃ yakṣī svagṛhamāgatā prabhūtaputrā nāpaśyat priyaṃ putraṃ priyaṃkaram  KAvk tamīkṣamāṇāṃ vivaśā hṛtavatseva dhenukā babhrāma saṃbhramodbhrāntā sā janeṣu cā  KAvk hā priyaṃkara hā putra kka nu paśyāmi te mukham iti pralāpinī tāraṃ niḥśeṣāḥ sā yayau diśaḥ  KAvk sā vicityāśu sarvāśā nirāśā putradarśane krośantī parvatadvīpaṃ samudravalayam yayau  KAvk martyabhūmimatikramya ghoreṣu nagareṣu sā svargoddeśeṣva śeṣeṣu vimānodyānaśāliṣu  KAvk śrāntā kkacinna viśrāntā yakṣiṇī praṇighātinī putramanviṣya nāpaśyallokapālapureṣu ca  KAvk kuberasyātha vacasā gatvā ca sugatāśramam bhagavantaṃ viyogārtā śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayau  KAvk tayā tadduḥkhavṛttāntaṃ sam niśamya niveditam tāmavocata śocantīṃ kiṃcit smitasitādharaḥ  KAvk hārīti tava putrāṇāṃ santi pañcaśatānyaho iti tenoktamākarṇya yakṣī duḥkhakṣatāvadat  KAvk putralakṣe pi bhagavan sahyā naikasutakṣatiḥ putrāt priyataraṃ nānyatkiṃ duḥkhaṃ tatkṣayātparam  KAvk putravāneva jānāti putrasnehaviṣavyathām sahajaiva sutaprītirakāraṇanibandhanā  KAvk          malino vikalaḥ kṣīṇaḥ kasya nendusamaḥ sutaḥ  KAvk iti yakṣavadhūvākyaṃ śrutvā vātsalyavihvalam bhūtānukampī bhagavān sasmitastāmabhāṣata  KAvk śoko yaṃ bahyputrāyā yadyekavirahe tava hṛte tvayaikavatsānāṃ putraike kīdṛśī vyathā  KAvk tvaṃ praviśya sadā gehaṃ strīṇāṃ putramalakṣitāṃ aśnāsi putramātāpi vyāghrīva mṛgaśāvakān  KAvk yena yena svadehasya duḥkhaṃ yātyupabhogatām na tatparasya kurvīta samāno nubhavaḥ śucām  KAvk tvaṃ buddhadharmasaṃghānāṃ trīṇi śikṣāpadāni cet gṛhṇāsi hiṃsāvimukhī tatprāpnoṣi priyaṃ sutam  KAvk ityuktā sā bhagavatā prāptaśikṣāpadā tataḥ hiṃsāvirāmāt taṃ gatvā putraṃ prāpa priyaṃkaram  KAvk tasyāḥ prāgjanmavṛttāntaṃ tasyāḥ karmaphalānvayam bhikṣubhirbhagavān pṛṣṭastadvṛttāntamabhāṣataḥ  KAvk purāsminneva nagare paurāh ke pyupabhoginaḥ parvatodyānamālāyāṃ vijahrurnartanādinā  KAvk atha tena pathā kāpi gopakāntā ghanastanī mathitaṃ paṇyamādāya hariṇākṣī samāyayau  KAvk garbhabhārālasagatiḥ pratyuptā gajagāminī sā śanairupasarpantī saspṛhaṃ tān vyalokayat  KAvk tasyā vanamṛgīmugdhairavadagdhā vilokanaiḥ asaṃvṛttā vilāsārdraiste pi sotkaṇṭhatāṃ yayuḥ  KAvk sā tairnimantritā tatra madanakṣībatām gatā hāritaṃ sahasā śīlaṃ na viveda pramādinī  KAvk tatasteṣū prayāteṣu tadā tasyā ratiśramāt papāta saha dhairyeṇa garbhaū kopādivāruṇaḥ  KAvk atrāntare samāyātaṃ tatpuṇyaistena vartamanā pratyekabuddhaṃ sādrākṣītkāyacittaprasādanam  KAvk sāsmai mathitamūlyāptamāmrāṇāṃ śatapañcakam dūrātpraṇāmavinatā manasaiva nyavedat  KAvk tataḥ puṇyarddhimatyasmin jātā yakṣakule dhunā jātamāmrārpaṇenāsyāḥ putrāṇāṃ śatapañcakam  KAvk hiṃsāvatī pāpatyāgāt śīlavismaraṇātparam pratyekabuddhapraṇateḥ prāptaśikṣāpadādya sā  KAvk iti vividhavipākaṃ karmatantraṃ vicitraṃ kimapisa kathayitvā tatra yakṣāṅganāyāḥ kalitakuśalasetuḥ saṃbhavābdhau janānāmakṛta sukṛtacittaṃ sarvalokasya śāstā  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ hārītikādamanāvadānaṃ nāma dvādaśaḥ pallavaḥ  pratihāryāvadānam yaḥ saṃkalpapathā sadaiva carati projjṛmbhamāṇādbhutaṃsvapnairyasya na saṃgatiḥ paricayo yasminnapūrvakramaḥ vāṇī maunavatī ca yatra hi nṛṇāṃ yaḥ śrotranetrātithistaṃ nirvyājajanaprabhāvavibhavaṃ manaurameyaṃ numaḥ  KAvk pure rājagṛhābhikhye bimbirāseṇa bhūbhujā pūjyamānaṃ jina dṛṣṭvā sthitaṃ veṇuvanāśrame  KAvk mātsaryaviṣasaṃtaptā mūrkhāḥ sarvjñamāninaḥ na sehire tadutkarṣaṃ prakāśamiva kauśikāḥ  KAvk malinaiḥ svavināśāya parabhāgoditaiḥ sadā kriyate vāsaraspardhā śārvaraistimirotkaraiḥ  KAvk maskarī saṃjayī vairairajitaḥ kakudastathā pūraṇajñātiputrādyā mūrkhāḥ kṣapaṇakāḥ pare  KAvk ūcurnṛpatimabhyetya māramāyāvimohitāḥ saṃgharṣadveṣadoṣeṇa dhūmenevāndhakāritāḥ  KAvk eṣa sarvajñatāmānī vane yaḥ śramaṇaḥ sthitaḥ ṛddhiprabhāvo bhavatā tasyāsmākaṃ ca dṛśyatām  KAvk ṛddhiprabhāvādyatkiṃcit janavyāvarjanorjitam drśyate mahadāścaryaṃ prātihāryaṃ taducyate  KAvk śaktiḥ saṃsadi yasyāsti pratihāryasya darśane asmākaṃ tasya vā rājan pūjāḥ santu jagatrtraye  KAvk iti teṣām vacaḥ śrutvā taddarpavimukho nṛpaḥ uvāca vāñchā keyaṃ vaḥ paṅgūnāṃ girilaṅghane  KAvk asamañjasamevaitat kā spardhāgneḥ pataṅgakaiḥ naitadvācyaṃ punarvādī mayā niṣkāsyate purāt  KAvk iti rājñā guṇajñena pratyākhyātodyamāḥ khalāḥ prayayuste nirālambe lambamānā ivāmbare  KAvk bimbisāro narapatirmūrkhatāpakṣapātavān anyaṃ vrajāmo bhūpālamiti te samacintayan  KAvk atrāṇtare bhagavati śrāvastīmabhitaḥ purīm prāpte tejavanārāmaṃ digantāneva te yayuḥ  KAvk te prasenajitaṃ tatra prāpya kosalabhūpatim prātihāryakṛtaspardhāṃ tāmevāsmai nyavedayan  KAvk guṇāntarajño nṛpatisteṣām darpakṣayecchayā ṛddhisaṃdarśanotsāhādyayau bhagavato ntikam  KAvk sa samabhyetya vinayāt praṇipatya tamabravīt bhagavan darpabalanaṃ tīrthyānāṃ kartumarhasi  KAvk ṛddhispardhānubandhena tvatprabhāvadidṛkṣayā svaguṇaślāghayāsmākaṃ taiḥ karṇau badhirīkṛtau  KAvk prakāśaya nijaṃ tejaḥ sajjanāvarjanam vibho tīrthyābhidhānāmakhilaṃ prayātu pralayaṃ tamaḥ  KAvk iti rājavacaḥ śrutvā nirvikāro mahāśayaḥ bhagavān viratāmarṣaḥ saharṣastamabhāṣataḥ  KAvk rājannānyopamardāya vivādāya madāya vā vivekābharaṇārho yaṃ kriyate guṇasaṃgrahaḥ  KAvk mātsaryamalinaiḥ kiṃ tairvicāraviguṇairguṇaiḥ ye haranti parotkarṣaṃ spardhābandhaprasāritāḥ  KAvk guṇācchādanamanyasya svaguṇena karoti yaḥ dharmastenāpraśastena svayameva nighātitaḥ  KAvk sadguṇānāṃ parikṣaiva paravailakṣyakāriṇī ucitā na hi śuddhānāṃ tulārohaviḍambanā  KAvk guṇavānapi nāyāti yaḥ pareṣu prasannatām sa dīpahastastatpātracchāyayā malinīkṛtaḥ  KAvk loka ta eva sarvajñā vidmaḥ kimadhikaṃ vayam parābhimānābhibhavaprāgalbhyaṃ svaparābhavaḥ  KAvk iti śrutvā bhagavataḥ praśamābhimataṃ vacaḥ bhṛśamabhyarthanāṃ rājā cakārāścaryadarśane  KAvk tataḥ dṛcchrādbhagavatā kṛtābhyupagamo nṛpaḥ rājadhānīṃ yayau hṛṣṭaḥ saptāhāvadhisaṃvidā  KAvk asminnavasare bhrātā bhūmibharturasodaraḥ cacārāntaḥpuropānte prāsādatalavartmanā  KAvk salīlaṃ vrajatastasya karmavātairiveritā kusumasrak papātāṃse rājapatnīkarāccyutā  KAvk tasya vijñātadoṣasya doṣaṃ saṃbhāvya sākṣibhiḥ piśunāḥ kiṃvadantīṃ tām cakrire rājagāminīm  KAvk chidramalpamapi prāpya kṣudrāḥ sarvāpakāriṇaḥ dvijihvāḥ praviśantyāśu prabhūnāṃ śūnyamāśayam  KAvk piśunapretiro rājā bhrāturīrṣyāviṣolbaṇaḥ chedamasyādideśāśu pāṇipādasya mūrcchitaḥ  KAvk nikṛttapāṇicaraṇaḥ kumāraḥ karmaviplavāt sa vadhyavasudhāśāyī viveśa viṣamāpadam  KAvk tīvravyathāparivṛtaṃ śocadbhirmātṛbandhubhiḥ dadṛśustaṃ kṣapaṇakāḥ kṣaṇaṃ nayanacālane  KAvk tān samabhyetya śokārtāste rājasutabāndhavāḥ jagadustatparitrāṇasaṃliptāḥ sarvaprāṇinah  KAvk doṣaṃ nigṛhīto yaṃ kālanāmā nṛpātmajam sarvajñavādino yūyaṃ prasādo sya vidhīyatām  KAvk iti tai prasaradbāṣpairarthyamānāh pralāpibhiḥ te maunino niṣpratibhā vailakṣyādanyato yayuḥ  KAvk atha tena yathāyāto bhikṣuḥ sugataśāsanāt ānando vidadhe ṅgāni tasya satyopayācanāt  KAvk rājaputrastu saṃjātapāṇipādaḥ prasannadhīḥ jinaṃ śaraṇamabhyetya tadupasthāyako bhavat  KAvk saptaratre vyatīte tha śrāntihāryaṃ gṛhaṃ mahat ṛddhiṃ bhagavato draṣṭuṃ mahīpatirakārayat  KAvk upaviṣṭe nṛpe tatra saha kṣapaṇakādibhiḥ kalpavṛkṣīkṛtā bhūmirabhavat sugatecchayā  KAvk tataḥ prāpteṣu deveṣu draṣṭuṃ bhagavataḥ prabhām ratnapradīpaṃ bhagavān bheje siṃhāsanam mahat  KAvk tejodhātuṃ prapannasya tasya gaṇḍasamudgataiḥ vyāptaṃ pāvakasaṃghātairabhūdbhuvanamaṇḍalam  KAvk śānte śanaiḥ kamalakānanasaṃnikāśe vahnau samastabhuvanasthitibhaṅgabhītyā dehāttato bhagavataḥ karuṇāmburāśeḥ pūrṇāmṛtormivimalā rucayaḥ prasasruḥ  KAvk lāvaṇyasāramaticandrasahasrakāntiṃ tejaḥ pratānaviphalīkṛtasūryacakram taṃ nāganāyakanikāyavilocanāni prītyā papuḥ sukṛtalabdhamapūrvaharṣam  KAvk vaidūryanālavipulāruṇaratnapātrakāntollasatkanakakesarakarṇikāni abhyudyayuḥ kṣititalādatha tatsamīpe padmāni saurabhabharāhṛtaṣaṭpadāni  KAvk teṣūpaviṣṭamatha kāñcanacārukāntiṃ snigdhekṣasṇaṃ sugatacakramadṛśyatārāt pīyūṣapeśalaśaśidyutiśītalena yasyodayena sahasā sukhamāpa lokaḥ  KAvk teṣāṃ prabhāvavibhavaṃ bahgavān babhāra madhye dhikaṃ kanakaśaila ivācalānām suskandhabandhuraghanadyutisaṃniveśaḥ prāṃśuḥ surakṣitiruhāmiva pārijātaḥ  KAvk svargāṅganākarakuśeśayakīryamāṇairamlānamālyavalayaiḥ kalitottamāṅgāḥ tasyānanāmbujavilokananirnimeṣe martyā api kṣaṇamavāpuramartyabhāvam  KAvk vyomāṅgaṇeṣu suradundubhiśaṅkhatūryaghoṣāvṛtaḥ kusumavarṣamahāṭṭahāsaḥ gandharvakinnaramunīśvaracāraṇānāṃ sphīṭaścacāra bhagavatstutivādanādaḥ  KAvk tatrāruṇādharadalāddaśanāṃśuśubhrād vyākīrṇakeśarakulāddaśanāravindāt satsaurabhaṃ bhagavataḥ svarasaṃnivṛttaṃ dhanyāḥ papurmadhuravāṅbhadhu puṇyasūtam  KAvk pāpaṃ vimuñcata niṣiñcata puṇyabījaṃ vairaṃ parityajata sāmyasukhaṃ bhajadhvam jñānāmṛtaṃ pibataṃ mṛtyuviṣāpahāri neyaṃ tanuḥ kuśalakarmasakhī cirāya  KAvk lakṣmīścalā taruṇatā ca jarānuyātā kāyo pyapāyanicayasya nivāsa eva prāṇāḥ śarīrakakuṭiṣu muhūrtapānthā nityodaye kuruta dharmamaye prayatnam  KAvk ityādibhirbhagavataḥ pravibhaktadīptajñānairvivekavimalaiḥ kuśalopadeśaiḥ vajrairivāśu dalanaṃ prayayau janānāṃ satkāyadṛṣṭisamaviṃśatiśṛṅgaśailaḥ  KAvk ṛddhiprabhāṃ bhagavataḥ pravibhāvya tīrthyā mantrahatā viṣadharā iva bhagnadarpāḥ dīpā ivārkakiraṇapratibhābhibhūtāścitrārpitā iva yayuściraniścalatvam  KAvk atrāntare bhagavataḥ satataṃ vipakṣaḥ sarvātmanā kṣapaṇako navadharmayakṣaḥ kṣiptaśravān sa vṛtavarṣavaraiścakāra vidravya randhraśaraṇān bhuvi vajrapāṇiḥ  KAvk addiśya tānatha kṛpārdrabhayāśaraṇyaḥ sarvopadeśaviṣayān bhagavān babhāṣe bhūbhṛdvanābanimaṇirvivarādi sarvaṃ tene bhayeṣu śaraṇaṃ kila kātarāṇām  KAvk buddhiṃ prabodha mama dhāmbi nidhāya buddhiṃdharmaṃ sasaṃghamapi ye śaraṇaṃ prapannāḥ teṣā jagatkṣayabhayeṣvapi nirbhayāṇāṃnaivānyataḥ śaraṇadainyaparigraho sti  KAvk durvāre paralokatīvratimire dharmaḥ pravṛddho śumāndānaṃ duḥsahapāpatāpavipadāmabhyudgame vāridaḥ prajñā mohamahāprapātaviṣamaśvabhre karālambanaṃdainyākrāntamahīnameva śaraṇaṃ sarvatra puṇyaṃ nṛṇām  KAvk iti timiravṛtākṣṇāṃ cakṣurunmīlanārhaṃ daśanamaṇimarīcivyajyamānaprakāśam sadasi sugatacandraḥ śuddhadharmopadeśaṃ sthirapadamiva kṛtvā kānanaṃ svaṃ jagāma  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ prātihāryāvadānaṃ nāma trayodaśaḥ pallavaḥ  devāvatāravadānam jayati mahatāṃ prabhāvaḥ paścādagre ca vartamāno yaḥ janakuśalakarmasaraṇiḥ prakāśaratnadīpo vaḥ  KAvk purā surapure pāṇḍukambalākhye śilātale samīpe pārijātasya kovidārasya suprabhe  KAvk kṛtvā tridaśasaṃghānāṃ bhagavān dharmadeśanām anugrahāya martyānāṃ jambūdvīpamavātarat  KAvk amarairanuyātasya tasyāvatarato bhuvam vimānakānanākīrṇaṃ babhūva bhuvanāṅgaṇam  KAvk tasya dantāṃśusaṃtānairupadeśamivācitam jagrāha candraruciram cāmaraṃ caturānanaḥ  KAvk chatraṃ śataśalākāṅkamanaṅkaṃ raṅkupāṇḍuram prasādamiva sākāramādade sya puraṃdaraḥ  KAvk saṃkāśyanagaropānte kānanodumbarāntike avatīrṇaṃ sukṛtinaḥ sānandāstaṃ vavandire  KAvk tasminnutpalavarṇākhyā bhikṣukī janasaṃgame alabdhāvasarā draṣṭuṃ nṛparūpamupādade  KAvk pradīptaratnamukuṭaṃ gaṇḍatāṇḍavikuṇḍalam dṛṣṭvaivāsya navaṃ rūpaṃ jahāsoṣṇīṣapallavaḥ  KAvk sā cintayantī ko vāyaṃ janairnirvivaraḥ puraḥ antaraṃ nṛparūpaṃ me dṛṣṭvā dāsyati sādaraḥ  KAvk atp nyathā tu bhagavatpraṇatirmama durlabhā na guṇaṃ gauravasthānamaiśvaryapraṇayī janaḥ  KAvk aho tṛṇatṛlālolairniḥsāravirasairdhanaiḥ hriyate vāsanābhyāsānnirvicāratayā janaḥ  KAvk dattāntarā sā sahasā janena nṛpagauravāt lolahāraṃ bhagavataḥ praṇāmamakārot puraḥ  KAvk asminnavasare bhikṣurudayī nāma saṃsadi tāṃ vilokya tathārūpāmavadat sasmitānanaḥ  KAvk iyamutpalavarṇākhyā bhikṣukī nṛparūpiṇī ṛddhyā bhagavataḥ pādau vandate janavanditā  KAvk utpalāmodavarṇābhuāṃ vijñāteyaṃ mayā purā ityuktvā virate tasmin bhagavānapyabhāṣata  KAvk ayuktameva bhikṣukyā darpadṛddhiprakāśanam karoti praśamaglānimabhimānena ca jvaraḥ  KAvk ityuktvā bhagavān kṛtvā tāṃ tāṃ śubhropadeśanām visṛjya devān prayayau svapadaṃ saha bhikṣubhiḥ  KAvk tatropaviṣṭaḥ pṛṣṭastaiḥ praṇatairbhikṣukīkathām prāgjanmakarmasaṃbaddhāṃ sarvajñastānabhāṣata  KAvk vārāṇasyāmabhūtpūrvaṃsārthavāho mahādhanaḥ patnī dhanavatī nāma tasya prāṇasamābhavat  KAvk pāṇipallavinī tanvīyaovanodyānamañjarī phalapuṣpavatī kāle sā tasmādgarbhamādadhe  KAvk atrāntare jalanidhidvīpānugamanodyatam pratyāsannaviyogārtā sā vallabhamabhāṣata  KAvk kiyatī dhanasaṃpattirvṛddhimadyāpi nīyate yatkṛte ghpragambhīrastīryate makarākaraḥ  KAvk bahvapāyaṃ dhanādānaṃ nirapāyā guṇārjanam svadeśāt paradeśaṃ hi gacchanti draviṇārthinah  KAvk kecidduḥkhānnivartante dūraṃ gatvāpi niṣphalāḥ niścalā dhaninaścānye karmaṇāmeṣa niścayaḥ  KAvk iti priyāvacaḥ śrutvā sārthavāhastato bhyadhāt mugdhe saṃbhāvanāpātro bhavatyevaṃ dhanodyataḥ  KAvk dhanārjanavihīnānāṃ puṅguvanmūlabhakṣaṇāt adya śvo vā sukhasthānāṃ bhogaiḥ saha parikṣayaḥ  KAvk svagṛhe pi daridrāṇāṃ janah krakacaniṣṭhuraḥ dhanināṃ paraloko pi premasnigdhajanaṃ bhuvaḥ  KAvk kṣīṇamapyudyataṃ vṛddhyai na veṇuṃ bandhate janaḥ na tu sa pūrṇatāṃ yāti pratyāsannaparikṣayaḥ  KAvk mūrkho pi viduṣāṃ vandyaḥ strīṇāṃ vṛddho pi vallabhaḥ klibo pi sevyaḥ śūrāṇāmāsannābhyudayo janaḥ  KAvk kenānyakaraṇaṃ bhuktvā pītvā kāvyāmṛtāni vā kṣaṇaṃ vicakṣaṇenāpi kṣuptipāse vivarjite  KAvk yasyārthaḥ sa guṇonnataiḥ kṛtanutiḥ kaṃ vā na dhatte guṇaṃdāridyrodayadoṣadūṣitarucāṃ nirmālyatulyā guṇāḥ vittenaiva guṇā guṇī na tu dhanī dhanyo dhanī no guṇī kāyādduṣkṛtasaṃnipātaśamanādāyurguṇānāṃ dhanam  KAvk iti prāṇādhikārthasya patyurākarṇya sā vacaḥ sāñjanāśrukaṇotkīrṇā latevābhṛtaṣaṭpadā  KAvk atha pravahaṇaṃ bheje sārthanāthastayā saha tīvratṛṣṇāgṛhītānāṃ hastapātraṃ mahodadhiḥ  KAvk tasya jāyāsakhasyāsau karmavātānuvartinaḥ abhajyata pravahaṇaṃ samanorathajīvitam  KAvk tataḥ phalakamāsādya bhāgaśeṣācca karmaṇaḥ kaśerudvīpamāsādya tatpatirvipadaṃ gataḥ  KAvk anāthām tatra śocantīṃ vihaṅgaḥ puruṣākṛtiḥ tāmāpa pādadīrṇāśāṃ suvarṇakulasaṃbhavaḥ  KAvk sa kāntāṃ sumukho nāma tāmuvāca rucākṛtaḥ samāśvasihi lolākṣi nirbhayo yaṃ tavāśrayaḥ  KAvk divyeyaṃ subhagā bhūmirvayaṃ tvatpraṇayaiṣaṇaḥ puṇyāyātāsi kalyāṇi ghoro yaṃ makarākaraḥ  KAvk ityuktvā tena śanakairnītā ratnālayaṃ gṛham saṃpūrṇagarbhā tanayaṃ cārurūpamasūta sā  KAvk vardhamāne śiśau tasmin sā śanaiḥ priyavādinā mugdhā tena vidagdhena saṃbhogābhimukhīkṛtā  KAvk saralatvānmṛdutvācca samīpapraṇayī janaḥ svayamāliṅgyate strībhirlatābhiriva pādapaḥ  KAvk divyodyāneṣu sā tena ramamāṇāṃ ghanastanī kumāraṃ rucirākāraṃ suṣuve sadṛśaṃ pituḥ  KAvk tasmin padmamukhābhikhye yauvanālaṃkṛtākṛtau sumukhaḥ pakṣiṇāṃ rājā kāle lokāntaraṃ yayau  KAvk tataḥ padmamukhaḥ śrīmānāsasāda padaṃ pituḥ guṇināmavivādena svādhīnāḥ kulasaṃpadaḥ  KAvk prāptaiśvaryaṃ tamavadadvijane jananī sutam tatprabhāvasya saṃbhāvya sarvatra prabhaviṣṇutām  KAvk putra prāptā tvayā lakṣmīriyaṃ nijakulocitā ayaṃ tu sārthavāhānme jātaḥ putro niraṃśakaḥ  KAvk vārāṇasyāmayaṃ rājā śaśaktyā kriyatāṃ tvayā prītīsaṃvādasāsvādaḥ svadeśe seva saṃpadaḥ  KAvk iti māturgirā pakṣī pakṣapātena bhūyasā skandhe bhrātaramāropya vyomnā vārāṇasīṃ yayau  KAvk tatra siṃhāsanāsīnaṃ brahmadattaṃ mahīpatim saṃjaghānaikadainaṃ sa vajragranakharaiḥ kharaiḥ  KAvk abhiṣicyāgrajaṃ pūrṇaṃ tasminneva nṛpāsane amātyān so vadadbhītān samagrānagravikramaḥ  KAvk yasya rājño bhiṣiktasya mayā yaḥ pracalīkaraḥ  so pyatītaḥ prabho bhaktyā tamevānugamiṣyati  KAvk ityuktvā pravarāmātyān svairaṃ vihagapuṇgavaḥ yayau bhrātaramāmantrya punardeśanasaṃvidā  KAvk sa eva brahmadatto yamiti mantrita mantriṇām  sa nṛpaḥ khyātimāyātaḥ svajaneṣu pareṣu ca  KAvk atrāntare samānītā sagarbhā hastinī vanāt na mumocārdhaniryātagarbhaṃ ruddhamivāntare  KAvk sādhvīkarāgrasaṃsparśādiyaṃ garbhaṃ vimuñcati iti mauhūrtikādiṣṭaṃ rājñe mantrī nyavedayat  KAvk śāsanādatha bhūbhartuḥ spṛṣṭvā hastena hastinīm antaḥ purāṅganāścakrustatra satyopayāvanam  KAvk tāsāṃ satyagirā garbhaṃ nātyajat kariṇī yadā tadā vilakṣyaḥ sarvo bhūt bhūpasyāntaḥpure janaḥ  KAvk atha gopāṅganābhyetya śīlasatyopayācanam kṛtvā pasparśa kariṇīṃ yenāsau garbhamatyajat  KAvk kṛtvā nijajāyānāṃ jñātvā śīladaridratām mene gopāṃ manaḥsveva tāṃ jagatrtritaye satīm  KAvk sa satījātilobhena sośumbāṃ nāma tatsutām pariṇīyānināyāgre devīśabdasya pātratām  KAvk tasyāḥ saṃcintya lāvaṇyaṃ capalatvaṃ ca yoṣitām sa sarvagāmīnīṃ nidrāmapi tatyāja śaṅkitaḥ  KAvk asminnavasare druṣṭuṃ bhrātaraṃ vihagādhiyaḥ yayau padmamukhastatra snehādatiśayotsukhaḥ  KAvk bhūpālo pi tamāliṅgya prītyā vihitasatkṛtiḥ vijane svakathāmasmai nivedya punarabravīt  KAvk śīlasatyatulārohāt dṛṣṭadoṣeṇa yoṣitām mamāntaḥpuravaimukhyāt vivāho bhinavaḥ kṛtaḥ  KAvk rūpayauvanagāminmyām tasyāmapi na me dhṛtiḥ ekatra dṛṣṭadoṣāṇāṃ sarvatrāśaṅkate manaḥ  KAvk tasmāttava pure bhrātarvimānuṣye nidhīyatām śīlaśankāṃ parityajya bhavāmi vigatajvaraḥ  KAvk tasmāt pratiniśaṃ pakṣī śāsanāt tava madgṛham prāpayiṣyati tāṃ svairamityayaṃ me manorathaḥ  KAvk iti bhrāturvacaḥ śrutvā tamuvāca vihaṅgamaḥ īrṣyāśaṅkākalaṅkena rājan mithyaiva mā kṛthāḥ  KAvk na nāma ramate ramye nāsvādaṃ vetti bhojane na paśyati na nidrāti nityamīrṣyāvaśāturaḥ  KAvk klībaḥ kāmī sukhī vidvān dhanī namraḥ prabhuḥ kṣamī arthī mānyaḥ khalaḥ snigdhaḥ strī satīti kathaiva kā  KAvk saralatve pi kuṭilāḥ sthāyinyo pyaticañcalāḥ kulīnā apui pārśvasthamāliṅgantyabalā latāḥ  KAvk dṛṣṭirlolādharo rāgī bhrūrvākrā kaṭhinau stanau dṛśyate naiva nirdoṣaḥ strīṇāmavayaveṣvapi  KAvk bhujyante kuśalaiḥ śyāmā bhramadbhramaravibhramaiḥ mūlānveṣī sarojinyāḥ paṅkenaivāvalipyata  KAvk naikasmin vismayabhuvāṃ sasmitānāṃ niyantrite śuciśīlavirāmāṇāṃ rāmāṇāṃ ramaṇe matiḥ  KAvk tathāpi matpurodyāne nirjane sā nidhīyatām  KAvk ityuktaḥ pakṣiṇā bhrātā nṛpatirvisasarja tām kāntāṃ kaśerukadvīpe taṃ ca satkṛtya sādaraḥ  KAvk sāpi pratiniśaṃ vyomnaḥ khagārūḍhā samāyayau divyagandhamayīṃ mālāmādāya dvīpasaṃbhavām  KAvk pārijātānvayatarostāni puṣpāṇyavāpa sā khyātāni timirāṇīva bhramadbhṛṅgāndhakārataḥ  KAvk atha vārāṇasīvāsī kadācinmānavābhudhaḥ prayayau samidhāhārī dvijanmā kānanaṃ yuvā  KAvk tatra kinnarakāminyā sa dṛṣṭaḥ spaṣṭamanmathaḥ yasya saṃdarśanenaiva sābhavadvismṛtasmṛtiḥ  KAvk asau navābhilāṣeṇa janakeneva sārpitā kāntā kāntimayī nāma vijahāra guhāgṛhe  KAvk tatrābharaṇaratnāśuḥ pratītatimirotkare ramamāṇā ciraṃ tena kāle putramavāpa sā  KAvk balavān marududbhavaḥ sa bālye pi yadā śiśuḥ tadā mātā tasya saṃjñāṃ śīghraga ityasādhayat  KAvk sāpi nivāghnasaṃbhogā sukhātṛptā guhāntare priyaṃ dhṝtvā sadā yāti pidhāya śilayā gṛham  KAvk kadācidatha vṛttāntaṃ nijapitrā niveditam ākarṇya śīghragaścintāvismayākulito vadat  KAvk śilānibaddhadvāre sminnandhasyaiva gṝhāntare aho sneho pyayaṃ tāta tava bandhanatāṃ gataḥ  KAvk ehi vārāṇasīmeva gacchāvaste nijāspadam vioulāmapyayatnena śilāmutsārayāmyaham  KAvk svadeśavirahakleśaṃ dyḥśaṃ sahase katham tyaktuṃ na śakyate kauściddeśo deha iva svakaḥ  KAvk bhāraṃ draviṇasaṃbhāraṃ vetti granthiguṇāguṇaḥ bhogaṃ nirupabhogaṃ ca svadeśavirahī janaḥ  KAvk ityuktvā sa guhāgohādutpāṭya vipulāṃ śilām kṛtābhyupagamenāśu janakena yayau saha  KAvk prayātayostatastūrṇaṃ samabhyetyātha kinnarī śūnyaṃ dṛṣṭvā guhāgehaṃ nirvedādityavintayat  KAvk aho me vismṛtasnehaḥ sa gataḥ kkāpi durjanaḥ dvijihvānāṃ bhujaṃgānāṃ kauṭilyaṃ vā kimadbhutam  KAvk na ramante palāyante paryante sukharāgiṇaḥ cirasthā api niḥsnehāḥ śukā iva dvijātayaḥ  KAvk iti saṃcintya sā patyurnikārātprītimatyajat puṣpopamāni premāṇi na sahante kadarthanām  KAvk vidyāguṇena kenāsau putro me bhuvi jāīvati iti dhyātvā sakhīhaste tasmai vīṇāṃ dideśa sā  KAvk saṃbhogasukhapaṇyaiva prītiḥ patiṣu yoṣitām aparyuṣitavātsalyā putraprītistu niścalā  KAvk javena vrajatostūrṇaṃ tayordaurjanyalajjayā śīgragāya dadau vīṇāṃ tatsakhī vegagāminī  KAvk ādyā tantririyaṃ nāsyāḥ spraṣṭavyā vighnakāriṇī ityābhāṣya tayā dattāṃ vīṇāṃ prāpya jagāma saḥ  KAvk tataḥ svadeśe janakaṃ svagṛhe viniveśya saḥ vīṇāpravīṇaḥ sarvatra lābhapūjāmavāptavān  KAvk tataḥ kadāvidvāṇijā ambudhidvīpagāminā āropitaḥ pravahaṇaṃ divyavīṇānurāgiṇā  KAvk vīṇāmūrcchanayā tasya śrotrapīyūṣadhārayā kṣaṇe kṣaṇe samudro pi nistaraṅga ivābhavat  KAvk athādyatantrisaṃsparśādutpannopaplavoplute bhagne pravahaṇe sarvavaṇijāmabhavat kṣayaḥ  KAvk tato balāhakāvāptyā pavanapretitaḥ kṣaṇāt kaśerudvīpamāsede karmaśeṣeṇa śīghragaḥ  KAvk tatrābdhikūlasaṃlīnaṃ divyodyānaṃ praviśya saḥ śyāmāṃ dadarśa sośumbāṃ mūrdhanyastabakastanām  KAvk grandhantīṃ timirākhyānāṃ puṣpāṇāmujjvalasrajam nibandhanaṃ tanuguṇaiḥ kurvāṇāmapyacetasām  KAvk sāpi taṃ rucirākāraṃ dṛṣṭvā vismayamāyayau dhīraṃ śaiśavatāruṇyasaṃdhimadhyasthatāṃ gatam  KAvk māramārutasaṃcālasakampakarapallavā sā śīrṇaśīlakusumā lateva praṇanāma tam  KAvk cirārūḍheva sahasā prītiḥ prauḍhā tayorabhūt prāgjanmasnehasaṃlīnaṃ na muñcati mano manaḥ  KAvk ramamāṇāṃ divā tena niśāyāṃ ca mahībhujā mene vāmācaritatāṃ tām priyo gūḍhakāmukaḥ  KAvk tena vārāṇasīṃ gantuṃ jñātvā vṛttaṃ samarthitā tannināya khagārūḍhā tadgirā mīlitekṣaṇam  KAvk vārito pi tadā vyomni nayanonmīlane tayā so bahvatsahasaivāndhaścāpalādvivṛtekṣaṇaḥ  KAvk sā tamantaḥpurodyāne nidhāya bhayakātarā viveśa śokasaṃtaptā śayyāveśma mahīpateḥ  KAvk dūyamānena manasā rajanīmativāhya tām prātarna gantuṃ na sthātuṃ cintākrāntā śaśāka sā  KAvk atrāntare samudbhūtaścyutasaurabhanirbharaḥ madhumāso vilāsānāṃ yauvanaṃ puṣpadhanvanaḥ  KAvk kokilālikulaiḥ kālaḥ kālaḥ kālo viyoginām śīrṇaśokanavāśokaduḥsahaḥ pratidṛṣyate  KAvk rājāpyaviratautsukyādudyānaṃ gantumudyataḥ dinamekaṃ na tatyāja sośumbāṃ kāmamohitaḥ  KAvk sa tayāsaha rāgasya madasya madanasya ca saṃsāramiva viśrāntipadapuṣpavanaṃ yayau  KAvk tatra bālānilālolalatāvailakṣyakāriṇīm paśyan pramodamāsede yaditāmeva bhūpatiḥ  KAvk anyarāgaviṣākrāntā sāpyabhūnmalinasmṛtiḥ sukhamapyasukhaṃ vetti cintāśalyākulaṃ manaḥ  KAvk antargatabhujaṃgābhiḥ strībhiratyantarāgiṇaḥ kaṇṭhe kṛtābhirnṛtyanti mālābhiriva mohitāḥ  KAvk tatraikāntalatākuñjanikuñjanihitasthitiḥ andhaḥ saurabhamāghrāya sośumbātimirasrajaḥ  KAvk sahasaiva vikāreṇa rāgādvismṛtasaṃvṛtiḥ agāyanmadanakṣībā gaṇayanti bahyaṃ kutaḥ  KAvk tanupavanavilāsaiḥ kīryamāṇaḥ priyāyāḥsamadabadanapadmāmodasaṃbhārasāraḥ timirakusumagandhaḥ so yamāyāti dūrātbhramarasaraṇivīṇāvibhramārāvaramyaḥ  KAvk śrutvā hṛdayasaṃvādagītaṃ tattasya bhūpatiḥ udyānavicayaṃ kṛtvā taṃ dadarśa latāntare  KAvk gāḍharocamadakṣībaṃ sa taṃ papraccha śaṅkitaḥ api jānasi sośumbāṃ tasya vā lakṣaṇaṃ tanoḥ  KAvk so bravīt kiṃ na jānāmi sośumbāṃ bimbapāṭalām upaviṣṭo dhare yasyā rāgarājye manobhavaḥ  KAvk nyastaṃ smareṇeva tadūrūmūle lekhāmayaṃ svastikamasti kāntam āvartaśobhā stanamaṇḍale vā lāvaṇyakallolanibhāsti tasyāḥ  KAvk etadākarṇya nṛpatiḥ sadyaḥ saṃtāpaśoṣitam mumoca rāgakusumaṃ nirmālyaminva cetasaḥ  KAvk so bravīnnāsti nārīṇāṃ śīlarakṣā śatairati khapuṣpamāleva satī sarvathā naiva jāyate  KAvk ityuktvāndhena tāṃ rājā saha śmaśānakānanam gardabhāropitāṃ tūrṇaṃ tatyāja nagarādbahiḥ  KAvk sā tena saha nirlajjā vrajantī dinasaṃkṣaye aṭavyāṃ caurapatinā prāptaiva saha saṃpadā  KAvk janairabhidrute tasmin sahasā cauramaṇḍale niraparāśa evāndhaścaurabhrāntyā nipātitaḥ  KAvk cauro pi niśāṃ bhuktvā sośumbāṃ kṣasṇasaṃgataḥ gṛhītvābharaṇānyasyā jagāmottīrya nimnagām  KAvk kāraṇḍavāyāh saritastasyāstīre nirambarā śuśova sāñjanairaśrujālaiḥ sā malinastanī  KAvk tasmin kṣaṇe mukhāsaktaṃ māṃsamutsṛjya jambuke yāte jalotplutaṃ matsyaṃ tajjahāraṃ vihaṅgamaḥ  KAvk matsye nimagne sahasā khagena piśite hṛte sa babhūvobhayabhraṃśāccintāniścalalocanaḥ  KAvk tasyāstaṃ vīkṣyaṃ duḥkhe pi mukhe smitamadṝśyata hāsaḥ parasya skhalite duḥsthasyāpyupajāyate  KAvk sa tāṃ vailakṣyakupitaḥ provācānucitasmitām aho hasasi māṃ loke hāsyāyatanatām gatām  KAvk nṛpaṃ tyaktvāgatā hyandhamtyaktavāndhaṃ cauramāśritā tavāhamubhayabhraṣṭaḥ tribhraṣṭāyāḥ smitāspadam  KAvk āstām vaḥ parihāso yaṃ taṃ yuktyāhaṃ karomi te khalāste viṣamasthānām ye biḍambanapaṇḍitāḥ  KAvk ityuktvā nagarīṃ gatvā sa nṛpāya nyavedayat sośumbā te nadītīre tapoyukteti manmatiḥ  KAvk atha nināya tām rājā vitīryābharaṇāmbaram doṣamācchādayatyeva rāgadveṣaḥ śarīriṇām  KAvk saivādyotpalavarṇeyamudāyī śīghrago pyasau prāgjanmāntarapuṇyena bhikṣḥuvratamupāgatau  KAvk abhavadatirasārdraṃ mānāsṃ rāgayogeyadu madanavidheyaṃ rāgayuktaṃ yadasyāḥ virataśamavirārā tena tasmin muhūtrekṛtanarapatirūpānandinaṃ mām vavande  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ devāvatārāvadānaṃ nāma caturdaśaḥ pallavaḥ  śilānikṣepāvadānam balabhatuladhairyavīryaṃ sāścaryaṃ bhavati saprabhāvāṇām mahadāśrayayogādyasmai sarvaṃ mahimatvamāyāti  KAvk purā kuśīpurīṃ ramyāṃ mallānāṃ balaśālinām svecchāvihārī bhagāvān pratasthe sugataḥ svayam  KAvk te tadāgamanaṃ śrutvā kalyāṇaṃ kuśalaiṣiṇaḥ vartmasaṃśodhanaṃ cakrurupacārapadodyatāḥ  KAvk deśaṃ bhūṣayatāṃ teṣāṃ saṃsiktaṃ candanodakaiḥ tṛṇakaṇṭakapāṣāṇasarkarāreṇuvarjitam  KAvk madhye samāyayau bhūminimagnā mahatī śilā avasannā visannā ca vadhūrvindhyagireriva  KAvk tāmutpāṭayatāṃ teṣāṃ kuddālabhujarajjubhiḥ māso jagāma na tvasyāḥ sahasrāṃśe pyabhūta kṣatiḥ  KAvk atha samsārasaṃtāpapraśamāmṛtadīdhitiḥ āyayau bhagavān sarvamānasollāsabāndhavaḥ  KAvk ghanāndhakāravirativyaktasatphaladarśanaḥ prasādasaṃvibhaktāśaḥ prakāśa iva śāradaḥ  KAvk sa tān dṛṣṭvā pariśrāntān viphalakleśapiḍāītān śrutvā ca tadvyavasitaṃ tānūce praṇatānanān  KAvk aho kleśaphalārambhaḥ prayāsavyavasāyinām saṃsārakarmaṇīvāsmin vyāpāre vaḥ samudyamaḥ  KAvk prārambhe viṣamakleśaṃ kriyamāṇaṃ sasaṃśayam siddhamapyanupādeyaṃ na prājñāḥ karma kurvate  KAvk ityuktvā caraṇāṅguṣṭhaghaṭṭitām vāmapāṇinā vinyasya dakṣiṇe pāṇau bhagavān vipulāṃ śilām  KAvk visṛjya brahamlokāntamaparyantaparākramaḥ cacārāścaryacaryāyāṃ dūtamiva jagattraye  KAvk kṣiptāyāṃ sahasā tasyām tenātyadbhutakāriṇā udabhūdganodbhūta iva vyāptajanaḥ svanaḥ  KAvk anityaḥ sarvasaṃskāra ityabhrāntavidhāyinaḥ sarvadharmā nirātmānaḥ śāntanirvāṇameva tat  KAvk iti sphuṭodite śabde śilā bhagavataḥ kare girīndraśīrṣakākārā sthitā punaradṛśyata  KAvk kṣaṇena sā bhagavatā kṣiptā vadanamārutaiḥ kṛtā visāriṇī dikṣu paramāṇuparaṃparā  KAvk punarekīkṛtāmeva bhagavān paramāṇubhiḥ śilāmanyatra nidadhe vismayaṃ ca jagattraye  KAvk āścaryaniścaladṛśastato mallā balirjitam vīryaṃ bhagavato vīkṣya praṇatāstaṃ babhāṣire  KAvk aho mahāprabhāvo yaṃ balavīryodayastava niścayādhigame yasya na pragalbhāḥ surā api  KAvk anugrahapravṛttena balena guruṇā tava adhogatinimagneyaṃ janateva dhṛtā śilā  KAvk vīryaprajñābalādīnām pramāṇāvadhiniścayam api jānāti te kaścidāścaryatarakāriṇaḥ  KAvk iti bruvāṇānāścaryaniścalānavalokya tān tasyāṃ śilāyāmāsīnaḥ provāca bhagavān jinaḥ  KAvk ekībhūtabalaṃ yaddhi bhūtānām bhuvanatraye sugatasya tadekasya loke naiva samaṃ balam  KAvk ambhāṃsi kumbhairambhodherjaganti paramāṇubhiḥ śakyānyalaṃ laṅghayituṃ prabhāvo na tu saugataḥ  KAvk saṃkhyāṃ sumeroryo vetti tulāmānena tattvataḥ sugatānām na jānāti so pi sudguṇagauravam  KAvk kathayitveti bhagavān saṃprāpte suramaṇḍale saśakrapadmanilaye cakre kuśaladeśanam  KAvk mallāstadupadeśena tattadbodhisamāśrayāt saśrāvakākhyāṃ pratyekasamyaksaṃbuddhatāṃ yayuḥ  KAvk srotaḥprāptiphalaṃ kauścitsakṛdāgāmi cāparaiḥ anāgāmiphalaṃ cāṇyaiḥ prāptamarhatpadaṃ paraiḥ  KAvk ityāśyayānuśayadhātugatiṃ nirīkṣya jñātvā tathāprakṛtimapratimopadeśam teṣāṃ cakāra bhagavāṃścaturāryasatyasamyakprakāśaviśadaṃ kuśalodayāya  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ śilānikṣepāvadānaṃpañcadaśaḥ pallavaḥ  maitreyavyākaraṇāvadānam asaṃgamo nāma ratnamayaḥ pūrvaṃ yūpo bhūdadbhutadyutiḥ darśayāṃi tamatraiva draṣṭuṃ vaḥ kautukaṃ yadi  KAvk ityuktvā bhagavān bhūmau pāṇinā divyalakṣmaṇā spṛṣṭvā nāgagaṇotkṣiptaṃ ratnayūpadarśayat  KAvk taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhikṣavaḥ sarve nirnimeṣekṣaṇāściram babhūvuścitralikhitām iva niścalavigrahāḥ  KAvk tatkathāmatha taiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ provāca bhagavān punaḥ atītānāgatajñānaṃ dantālokaiḥ kirannivaḥ  KAvk devaputraḥ purā kaścit kāle svargaparicyutaḥ mahāpraṇādanāmābhūnnṛpatiḥ śakraśāsanāt  KAvk dharmavṛttānusaraṇasmaraṇāya mahītale ucitaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ kiṃcit sa yayāce śatakratum  KAvk tataḥ surapatervākyādviśvakarmā tadālaye bhāsvaraṃ vidadhe ratnayūpaṃ puṇyamivonnatam  KAvk tatastaddarśanāsakte jane kautukaniścale kṛṣyādikarmaṇyucchinne rājñaḥ koṣakṣayo bhavat  KAvk tatastena kṣitibhujā kṣipto yaṃ jāhnavījale tiṣṭhatyadyāpi pātāle ratnaiḥ sūryairivācitaḥ  KAvk bhaviṣyatyasya kālena paricchinnaḥ parikṣayaḥ na tajjagati nāmāste pariṇāme yadakṣayam  KAvk āgāmisamaye puṃsāṃ varṣāśītisahasrake śaṅkhaśubhrayaśāḥ śaṅkho nāma rājā bhaviṣyati  KAvk puṇyalabdhamimaṃ yūpaṃ nṛpaḥ kalpadrumopamaḥ sa purohitaputrāya maitreyāya pradāsyati  KAvk maitreyo pyanmumādāya kṛtvā sapadi khaṇḍaśaḥ arthicintāmaṇirlokamadaridraṃ prāgjanmapraṇidhānena śaṅkhasya kuśalodayaḥ kṛtasyāvaśyabhogyatvātpariṇāme phaliṣyati  KAvk madhyadeśe purā rājā vāsavo vāsavopamaḥ dhanasaṃmatanāmā ca nṛpo bhūduttarāpathe  KAvk tayorvibhavasaṃgharṣo bhūto vairāgnitaptayoḥ abhūd yuddhasamārambhasaṃbhārarabhasaṃ manah  KAvk nagaraṃ ca praviśyātha sametya dhanasaṃmataḥ cakre garajathānīkairgaṅgātīraṃ nīrantaram  KAvk tatra ratnaśīkhī nāṃa samyaksaṃbuddhatām gataḥ dṛṣṭastenārcyāmānāṅghrirbrahmaśakrādibhiḥ suraiḥ  KAvk so cintayadaho rājā vāsavaḥ pṛthipuṇyavān viṣayānte vasatyeṣ ayo hi tridaśavanditaḥ  KAvk tatastasyānubhāvena tatra bhūpālayostayoḥ yayau vairarajaḥ śāntyā mithyāmohaparikṣayam  KAvk kṝtasaṃghiḥ pareṇātha vāsavaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ bhagavantaṃ samabhyetya sarvabhogaurapūjayat  KAvk praṇidhānaṃ ca vidadhe pūjānte praṇamāmi tam ahaṃ kuśalamūlena syāmetena mahāniti  KAvk asminnavasare ghore śankhaśabde samudgate provāca taṃ ratnaśikhī praṇataṃ purataḥ sthitam  KAvk śankho nāma mahīpālaścakravartī bhaviṣyasi paryante bodhiyuktaśca kuśalaṃ samāvāpsyasi  KAvk evaṃ satpraṇidhānatah kṣitipatiḥ puṇyodayādvāsavaḥśaṅkho nāma nṛpa sa ratnaśikhinādiṣṭaḥ śriyaṃ prāpsyati maitreyaḥ praṇayātkariṣyati tathā bodhau viśuddhāṃ dhiyaṃkalyāṇābhiniveśapuṇyataraṇirāḍya hi satsaṃgamaḥ  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ maitreyavyākaraṇāvadānaṃ nāma ṣoḍaśaḥ pallavaḥ  ādarśamukhāvadānam cittaprasādavimalapraṇayojjvalasya svalpasya dānakusumasya phalāṃśakena hemādrirohaṇanagendrasudhābdhidānasaṃpatphalaṃ na hi tulākalanāmupaiti  KAvk purā manojñe sarvajñaḥ śrāvastyāṃ jetakānane anāthapiṇḍadārāme vijahāra mahāśayaḥ  KAvk āryo mahākāśyapākhyastacchiṣyaḥ karuṇānidhiḥ nagaropavanasyāntaṃ janacārikayā yayau  KAvk tatra sudrugatiryoṣinnagarāśravalambikā apaśyat kuṣṭharogārtā kāśyapaṃ taṃ yadṛcchayā  KAvk sā taṃ dṛṣṭvā prasādinyā śraddhayā samacintayat pātre sya piṇḍapātārhā kiṃ na jātāsmi puṇyataḥ  KAvk vijñāya tasyā āścaryaśraddhāyuktaṃ manoratham prasārya pātraṃ jagrāha piṇḍaṃ taṃ karuṇākulaḥ  KAvk tīvracittaprasādena bhaktasārasamaraṇe kuṣṭhinyā nipapātāsyāḥ pātre śīrṇakarāṅguliḥ  KAvk tataḥ sā pātakamiva tyaktvānityakalevaram devānāṃ tuṣitākhyānāṃ nilaye samajāyata  KAvk śakrastadadbhutaṃ jñātvā dānapuṇypditādaraḥ yatnātkāśyapasatpātraṃ sudhayā samapūrayat  KAvk sudhārpaṇe pyasau bhikṣurnispṛhastṛṇalīlayā praśamāmṛtasaṃpūrṇaścakre pātramadhomukham  KAvk bhajante praṇayaprītiṃ kṛpaṇeṣu kṛpākulāḥ santaḥ saṃpatsamādhmātavadane mīlitādarāḥ  KAvk śrutvā tāṃ tuṣite devanikāye niratām nṛpaḥ prasenajit bhagavataścakre bhojyādhivāsanām  KAvk rājñastasya gṛhe dṛṣṭvā lakṣmīmāścaryakāriṇaḥ āryānandena bhagavān pṛṣṭastatpuṇyamabhyadhāt  KAvk purā gṛhapateḥ sūnurdāridyrāddāsatāṃ gataḥ kṣetrakarmāṇi saṃsaktaḥ kṣutkṣāmaḥ klāntimāyayau  KAvk svajananyā samānītāṃ niḥsnehalavaṇāṃ cirāt kulmāṣapiṇḍimāsādya bhoktuṃ sādaramāyayau  KAvk dhautahastaḥ kṣaṇe tasmin saṃprāptāya yadṛcchayā dadau pratyekabuddhāya tām prasannena cetasā  KAvk jātaḥ sa eva kālena bhūpālo yaṃ prasenajit tasya dānakaṇasyaivaṃ vibhūtiḥ prathamaṃ phalam  KAvk śrutveti bhagavadvākyaṃ bhikṣūrvismayamāyayau rājāpi vipulāṃ pūjāṃ cakre bhagavataḥ puraḥ  KAvk rājārhairakhilairbhogaiḥ kṛtvā bhaktinivedanam sa koṭīstailakumbhānāṃ dīpamālāmakalpayat  KAvk dīpamekaṃ dadau tatra svalpakaṃ durgatāṅganā snehakṣayātprayāteṣu sarveṣu na jagāma yaḥ  KAvk vicintya praṇidhānena tayā vimalacetasā bhāvinīm śākyamunitāṃ sarvajño syāh samabhyadhāt  KAvk ratnadīpāvaliṃ datvā rājā bhagavataḥ purah upaviśya praṇamyāgre praṇayāttaṃ vajijñapat  KAvk bhagavatpraṇidhānena tattatpuṇyānubhāvataḥ na kasyānuttarā samyaksaṃbodhirbhavadarpitā  KAvk bhavatprasādapraṇayāt prāptumicchāmi tāmaham nirvikalpaphalāvāptyai sevyante kalpapādapāḥ  KAvk iti rājavacaḥ śrutvā bhagavān samabhāṣata durlabhānuttarā samyaksaṃbodhiḥ pṛthivīpate  KAvk sūkṣmā mṛṇālatantubhyo giribhyo pi garīyasī samudrebhyo pi gambhīrā sā sukhena na labhyate  KAvk na dānairbahubhirlabdhaṃ mayaivānyeṣu janmasu cittaprasādaviśadaṃ jñānaṃ tatkāraṇaṃ jaguḥ  KAvk caturdvīpādhipatyena mayā māndhātṛjanmani ciraṃ dānaphalaṃ bhuktaṃ bodhirnādhigatā tu sā  KAvk dānena cakravartīśrīḥ sā sudarśanajanmani bhuktā mayāmahīyasī bodhirnādhigatā tu sā  KAvk purā datvā gajānaṣṭau velāmadvijajanmāni mayā prāptaṃ mahatpuṇyaṃ bodhirnādhigatā tu sā  KAvk kurūpaḥ kuśalātmāhaṃ rājaputraḥ purābhavam yaḥ piśāco yamityuktvā nijalatnyā vivarjitaḥ  KAvk śriyai śrīskandho bhūtyāge prītiryasya sadā sthitā sa duḥkhī rūpavaikalyāt kka vā sarvaguṇodayaḥ  KAvk taṃ rūpavirahe dehatyāgārūḍhaṃ śacīpatiḥ divyacūḍāmaṇiṃ datvā cakre pañcaśaropamam  KAvk ṣaṣṭiḥ purasahasrāṇi tasya yajñeṣu yajvanaḥ hemayūpābhirūpāṇi prāpurmerubalaśriyam  KAvk tasmin mayātidānādrikṛte kuśalajanmani tāni puṇyānyavāptāni bodhirnādhigatā tu sā  KAvk mayā satyaprabhāveṇa triśaṅkunṛpajanmani kṛtā vṛṣṭiḥ sudurbhikṣā bodhirnādhigatā tu sā  KAvk mithilāyāṃ mahādevanṛpajanmani yajvanā mayāptā puṇyasaṃpattirbodhirnādhigatā tu sā  KAvk mithilāyāṃ purā puṇyaṃ nimibhūpālajanmani prāptaṃ dānatapoyajñairbodhirnādhigatā tu sā  KAvk purā nandasya nṛpateścatvāraḥ piśunāḥ sutāḥ babhūvurādarśamukhaḥ pañcamaśca guṇādhikaḥ  KAvk kālenāpannaparyantaḥ sa bhūpatiracintayat ete madante catvāro rājyaṃ nārhanti karkaśāḥ  KAvk putre mamādarśamukhe rājyaśrī pratibimbitā suvṛtte labhate śobhāṃ prajñāvaimalyaśālini  KAvk dhyātvetyamātyān so vādīt sa bhavadbhirnareśvaraḥ kṛto ntaḥpuravargeṇa yo bhyutthānena pūjyate  KAvk maulirna kampate yasya sameva maṇipādukaiḥ dvāradrumādrivāpīṣu nidhiṣaṭkaṃ sa paśyati  KAvk ityuktvā tridivaṃ yāte nṛpatau mantriṇaḥ kramāt taduktrairlakṣaṇaiścakrurādarśamukhamīśvaram  KAvk dharmanirṇayakāryeṣu yaṃ vādiprativādinah vilokyaiva svayaṃ tasthurnyāyairjayaparājaye  KAvk purā nirabhiasṃghena prātavaiśasakilbiṣam brāhmaṇaṃ daṇḍinaṃ nāma dayāluḥ prayayau puraḥ  KAvk guyugārthe gṛhasthena mṛtena vaḍavāhateḥ kuṭhārapātataḥ patnyā takṣavāsī vivāditaḥ  KAvk śauṇḍikenātmajavadhāddīkṣitaṃ tulyanigraham tadvipakṣabhayenoktvā tatsaṃtyaktaṃ vyamokṣayat  KAvk amānuṣāṇāṃ sattvānāmadhyāśayaviśeṣataḥ cakāra cittaśodhanaṃ tattatsaṃdehanirṇayam  KAvk avṛṣṭimṛṣṭe durbhikṣe yena dvādaśavarsake vihitaṃ sarvasattvānāmaśanaprāṇavartanam  KAvk ityamūnmama puṇyāptirādarśamukhajnmani na tu sā samyaksaṃbodhirvibodhitā mahodayā  KAvk bahujanmaśatābhyāsaprasāsena mahīyasā adya tu jñānavaimalyaṃ mayāptaṃ lutpasaṃvṛti  KAvk jñānaprajñādhigamyā kimapi paratarānuttarā satyāsaṃvitsamyaksaṃbodhireṣā na ca khalu nṛpate labhyate dānapuṇyaiḥ mohaśyāmāvirāme gataghanagaganavyaktavaimalyabhājāṃnirvyājānandabhūmirbhavati bhavatamaśchedinī sā dinaśrīḥ  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ ādarśamukhāvadānaṃ nāma saptadaśaḥ pallavaḥ  śāriputrapravrajyāvadānam nedaṃ bandhunoṃ suhṛt sodaro vā nedaṃ mātā na pitā vā karoti yatsaṃsārāmbhodhesetuṃ vidhatte jñānācāryaḥ ko pi kalyāṇahetuḥ  KAvk kalandakanivāsākhye ramye veṇuvanāśrame bhagavān viharan buddhaḥ pure rājagṛhe purā  KAvk kilitaṃ copayiṣyaṃ ca dvau parivrājakau purā prapannau bhikṣubhāvena cakāra śamasaṃvṛtau  KAvk tataśca śāriputrasya bhikṣoḥ saṃdeśanāṃ vyaghāt yayā sākṣātkṛtārhattvo so bhūnmokṣagatikṣamaḥ  KAvk tasya tadadbhutaṃ dṛṣṭvā dhanārhaṃ sarvabhikṣubhiḥ papracchuḥ pūrvavṛttāntaṃ sa ca tebhyo vyabhāṣata  KAvk brāhmaṇasyāgnimitrasya bhāryā guṇavarābhavat śūrpiketi kṛtaṃ pitrā krīḍānāma ca bibhratī  KAvk bhrātā prathamaśīlākhyaḥ tasya śūrpasamābhidhaḥ pratyekabuddhatāṃ yātaḥ kadācid gṛhamāyayau  KAvk sa tayā bharturādeśād gṛhībhaktyādhivāsitaḥ praṇatipraṇayācāraistoṣitaḥ paricaryayā  KAvk kadāciccīvare tasya kurvāṇasya vipātraṇam  sūcīkarmavahād dṛṣṭvā praṇidhānaṃ samādadhe  KAvk yatheyaṃ kartarīṃ tīkṣṇā yathā gambhīragāmiṇī sūcī tathāparā prajñā mama syāditi sādarā  KAvk pratyekabuddhavinayāt praṇidhānena tena ca gatāsmin janmani saiva saprajñaśāriputratām  KAvk sa eṣa śāriputro dya bhikṣuṣtīkṣṇatarāgradhīḥ kalyāṇapātratām yātaḥ kalpavallī hi sanmateḥ  KAvk vākyaṃ bhagavataḥ śrutvā papracchurbhikṣavaḥ punah kasmānnāṭyakule jātaḥ śāriputro narādhame  KAvk tatastān bhagavānūce pūrvasminneṣa janmani abhūnmahāmatirnāma rājaputraḥ satāṃ mataḥ  KAvk śrīmato pi matistasya pravrajyāyāmajāyata paripākaprasannānāṃ kāluṣyāya na saṃpadaḥ  KAvk pravrajyā rājaputrāṇāṃ yūnāṃ naiva kulocitā ityuktvā janakaḥ prītyā taṃ yatnena nyavārayat  KAvk kadācit kuñjarārūḍhaḥ sa vrajan janavartmani dṛṣṭvā daridraṃ sthaviraṃ kāruṇyādidamabravīt  KAvk adhanyā dhanīno loke bandhubandhanayantritāḥ pravrajyāṃ nāpnuvantyeva tvaṃ tu kena nivāritaḥ  KAvk sa nyavedayanme daridrasya na pātraṃ na ca cīvaram dhanopakaraṇānyeva śamopakaraṇānyapi  KAvk rājasūnuriti śrutvā gatvā munitapovanam pravrajyāṃ kārayitvāsya pradadau pātracīvaram  KAvk so cireṇaiva kālena yātaḥ pratyekabuddhatām rājaputraṃ samabhyetya divyāmṛddhimadarśayat  KAvk tasya prabhāvamālokya sa pradadhyau nṛpātmajaḥ aho mahodayatvānme pravrajyā durlabhābhavat  KAvk dāridyrādavivekācc nīcānāmapi durlabhā jāyeyamadhame kule tasmadasmi vivekavān  KAvk sa eva śāriputro yaṃ jñātastatpraṇidhānataḥ pravrajito bhagavatā kāśyapenānyajanmani  KAvk tenāyaṃ niyamapraṇayavinayī samyakprasādodayādādiṣṭaḥ kuśalāya satyanidhinā prajñāvatāmagraṇīḥ kāle śākyamunerbhaviṣyati mataḥ śiṣyatvayogādvaraṃmaudgalyāyana eṣa cātra kathitaḥ saṃvinmayānāṃ vadaḥ  KAvk anyajanmani daridraḥ kārmikaḥ kenacidapi dayayā maharṣiṇā dattapātracīvaro bhavaddarśitarddhirāsīdatulaprabhāvavān  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ śāriputraprajajyāvadānam nāmāṣṭādaśaḥ pallavaḥ  śroṇakoṭikarṇāvadānam sa ko pi puṇyātiśayodayasya varaḥ prabhāvaḥ paramākṣayo yaḥ pratyakṣalakṣyaḥ śubhapakṣasākṣī janmāntare lakṣaṇatāmupaiti  KAvk ramye purā bhagavati śrāvastyāṃ jetakānane anāthapiṇḍadārāme vihāriṇi tathāgate  KAvk babhūva vāsavagrāme balasenābhidho gṛhī pūritāśaḥ phalabharaiśchāyātarurivārthinām  KAvk jāyāyāṃ jayasenāyāṃ kāle kamalalocanaḥ ajāyata sutastasya puṇyairmīrta ivotsavaḥ  KAvk sajahā ratnadīpārcirabhūtkarṇasya karṇikā nābhūnmūlyatulā yasya hemakoṭiśatairapi  KAvk śravaṇānakṣatrajāto sau ratnakoṭyarhakarṇikāḥ sa śroṇakoṭikarṇākhyaḥ kumāro bhūdguṇocitaḥ  KAvk sa nirmalaruciḥ kāntaḥ kalābhiṃ paripūritaḥ amandānandaniṣyandī na kasyendurivābhavat  KAvk sa yuvā vāryamāṇo pi pitrā dhanadasaṃpadā jananī sāśrunayanā paraṃ puruṣayā girā  KAvk priyaṃvado pi nirbhartsyo viṣavarṣīva candramāḥ mahāsārthena ratnārthī dūradvīpāntaraṃ yayau  KAvk makarākaramuttīrya vrajatasyasya nirjane karmormiviplavenābhūt svasārthavirahaḥ pathi  KAvk sārtho pi tamanāsādya vinivṛttaṃ śucā śanaiḥ svadeśamarjitakleśaḥ praviveśa viśṛṅkhalāḥ  KAvk so pi taptamaruśreṇīlakṣaṇāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ diśam śrāntaḥ praśāntaviśrāntirvāpigāhaṃ vyagāhata  KAvk so cintayadaho vitte pratinittārjanodyamaḥ mamāyamanayenaiva jātakleśaḥ phalodayaḥ  KAvk aho dhanārjanāveśaḥ saṃtoṣavirahānnṛṇām sarvāpavādasaṃvādo nindyānām vipadāṃ padam  KAvk hemācale pi saṃprāpte na paryāptirhanārjane saṃsāre vāsanābhyāsadveṣamohaḥ śarīriṇām  KAvk pṛthuprayāsavirasā dīpitā śrīrivāyatā tṛṣṇāṃ tanoti nitarāmiyaṃmarumahītale  KAvk aho bata kuraṅgāṇāṃ tṛṣṇāndhānāṃ pade pade mamāpi janayantyeva mohaṃ marumarīcikāḥ  KAvk iyaṃ tṛṣṇā śramaścāyamimā nirudakā bhuvaḥ kiṃ karomi kka gacchāmi paśyāmi jvalitā diśaḥ  KAvk iti saṃcintya sa śanaiḥ prasarpan salilāśayā āyāsamiva sākāraṃ dadarśa puramāyasam  KAvk ghoraṃ dvāri sthitaṃ tatra saṃtrāsasyeva sodaram dadarśa puruṣaṃ kālakarālaṃ raktalocanam  KAvk sa tena pṛṣṭaḥ pānīyaṃ yadā novāca kiṃcana tadā svayaṃ praviṣṭena pretaloko vilokitah  KAvk dagdhakaṣṭhopamān dhūlimalaliptānnirambarān śuṣkāsthinsāyuśeṣāṅgān pretān dṛṣṭvā sa vivyathe  KAvk tairyācitah sa pānīyaṃ pānīyavirahārditaḥ parityajya nijāmārtimabhūttadduḥkhaduḥkhitaḥ  KAvk tīvratṛṣṇāturānūce sa tānārtapralāpinah mamāsmin marukāntāre niṣkṛpasya kutaḥ payaḥ  KAvk kṛcchre smin duḥsahe nyastāḥ ke yūyaṃ kena karmaṇā yuṣmadaprakriyabandhaścātaḥ kṛcchraścarāmyaham  KAvk nidrā niḥśalyakalpasya sukhasikteva tasya yā nārtānnapaśyati dṛṣṭvā teṣāṃ kleśakṣaye kṣamā  KAvk te tamūcurviruddhena karmaṇā mohasaṃcayāt anivartya vayaṃ martyāḥ kṣiptā vyasanasaṃkaṭe  KAvk adhikṣepāt kṣepakṣatipataradhairyairmadabharād anāryairmānavyasanerṣyābhiravāryavyatikaraiḥ kṛtāsmābhirnityaṃ suhanahṛdaye nirdayatayāvacobhirnārācairviṣaparicitaiḥ śalyakalanā  KAvk dānaṃ nadattaṃ hṛtameva vittaṃ hiṃsānimittīkṛtameva cittam asmārbhiraṅgairvihitā vikārāḥ parasya dārāpahṛtiprakārāḥ  KAvk te vayaṃ kuhakāsaktā dakṣāḥ kṣudreṣu karmasu prayātāḥ pretanagare ghore smin kleśapātratām  KAvk iti teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā so nyatra ca tathāvidhān pretān dṛṣṭvānabhipretān karuṇakulito bhavat  KAvk nirgamya durgamāt tasmāt purātpuṇyabalena saḥ vimalaṃ śītalacchāyamāsasāda vanāntaram  KAvk atha dūradhvasaṃtaptaḥ pariśrāntaḥ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ nipapātācalādandhastṛṣṭārta iva bhāṣkaraḥ  KAvk dine puṇya iva kṣīṇe niḥśeṣāśāprakāśake saṃmohamalinaṃ loke tamaḥ pāpamivodyayau  KAvk kṣīṇabhṛṅgavihaṅgānāṃ nalinīnāṃ prasaṅginī vikāsāsṃpasā mudrā nidreva samajāyata  KAvk kāruṇyādiva śītāṃśurjyotsnāmṛtaśalākayā sphāratāraṃ jagannitraṃ cakre vitimitaṃ tataḥ  KAvk kṣayodayaparāvṛttirdrśitānekavibhramaḥ saṃsāradinayāminyorjahāseva sudhākaraḥ  KAvk netrānandasudhāvarṣe sukhasparśe niśākare digvadhūvadanādarśe harṣe mūrta ivotite  KAvk śroṇakoṭirdadarśāgre vimānamānanadyutim kautukādanyarūpeṇa svargādbhuvamivāgatam  KAvk tasminnapaśyatsamadāścatasrastridaśāṅganāḥ diśaścandrodayānandavihārāyeva saṃgatāḥ  KAvk tāsāṃ madhye varākāraṃ ramamāṇaṃ vyalokayat taruṇapremasaṃbhāramiva sākāratām gataḥ  KAvk ratnamaṇḍaleyūrakirīṭikacirāmśubhiḥ ālikhantamivāścaryamamaryādaṃ diśāṃ mukhe  KAvk tasya tāmadbhutām dṛṣṭvā saṃbhogasukhasaṃpadam mene sa sukṛtākhyasya taroḥ sphītāṃ phalaśriyam  KAvk prītyā tena kṛtātithyaḥ svādupānāśanādibhiḥ tāṃ śroṇakoṭikarṇo tha nināya rajanīṃ sukham  KAvk tārākusumavātāliprabhā prābhātikī tataḥ anityateva śaśinaścakre lakṣmīparikṣayam  KAvk kṣayaṃ kṣapāyāṃ yātāyām bhānau bhuvanacakṣuṣi udite sarvabhūtānām sukhaduḥkhaikasākṣiṇi  KAvk vimānaṃ suranāryaśca kṣasṇādadṛśyatāṃyayuḥ vinaṣṭavadanacchāyaḥ puruṣaścāpatatkṣitau  KAvk tatastasyāpatat pṛṣṭhe śunāṃ saṃgho tibhīṣaṇaḥ trailokyaśāpapāpotthaḥ kleśarāśirivākhilaḥ  KAvk sa taigrīvāmukhārabdhamāṃsagrāsāgrakarṣaṇaiḥ ākrandirudhirakṣīrairbhakṣyamāṇaḥ kṣayaṃ yayau  KAvk dinānte punarāyāntaṃ tadvimānamapaśyata catasro psarāsastāśca puruṣaḥ sa ca kāntimān  KAvk taṃ śroṇakoṭikarṇo tha papracchātyantavismitaḥ sakhe kimetadāścaryaṃ dṛśyate kathyatāmiti  KAvk sa tena pṛṣṭaḥ provāca vayasya śrūyatāmidam tvāṃ śroṇakoṭikarṇākhyaṃ jānāmi sukṛtocitam  KAvk abhavaṃ vāsavagrāme duṣkṛtī paśupālakaḥ paśūnāṃ māṃsamutkṛtya vikrītaṃ satata mayā  KAvk piṇḍapātāya saṃprāpto māmāryaḥ karuṇānidhiḥ kātyāyanākhyaḥ provācaḥ viramāsmāt kukarmaṇaḥ  KAvk hiṃsāmayo hyayaṃ kleśo duḥsahaḥ sāhasaiṣiṇām svaśarīre patatyeva chinnamūla iva drumaḥ  KAvk ityahaṃ vāryamāṇo pi tenānāryaḥ kṛpātmanā yadā na virataḥ pāpāt tadā sa prāha māṃ punaḥ  KAvk divā tvaṃ kuruṣe hiṃsāṃ sarvathā yadi nirdayaḥ rātrau śīlasamādānaṃ gṛhāṇa samayānmama  KAvk ityuktvā tena yatnena sarvasattvahitaiṣiṇā dattā śīlasamādānamayī puṇyamatirmama  KAvk kālena kālavaśagaḥ prāptaḥ so hamimāṃ daśām taptāṅgārasudhāvarṣairiva kīrṇo divāniśam  KAvk rātrau śīlasamādānaphalaṃ hiṃsāphalaṃ dine caryā matpuṇyapāpābhyām patitaḥ sukhaduḥkhayoḥ  KAvk tasya me kuru kāruṇyaṃ sakhe kalusakāriṇaḥ gatvā svadeśaṃmatputraṃ brūhi madvacasā rahaḥ  KAvk asti me gṛhakoṭānte nikhātaṃ hemabhājanam taduddhṛtya parityaktapāpavṛtti vidhīyatām  KAvk āryakātyāyano nityaṃ piṇḍapātena pūjyatām ityuktastena vinayāt tathetyuktvā jagāma saḥ  KAvk sa dadarśa vrajan divyavimānamaparaṃ punaḥ ratnapadmalatākāntaṃ dvitīyamiva nandanam  KAvk tasmin sāṅgamivānaṅgaṃ saṃgataṃ divyayoṣitā apaśyadvāsarārambhe puruṣaṃ ratnabhūṣitam  KAvk tena prītyupacāreṇa kṛtātithyastathaiva saḥ dinaṃ nināya dīrghaṃ ca kleśamadhye sudhāmayam  KAvk atha vyomavimānāgrāt patite padminīpatau apūryata jagad ghorairduḥkhairiva tamobharaiḥ  KAvk tataḥ kṣapāpatirjyotsnāṃ vamanneva kṣapājaḍaḥ śanakaiḥ pāṇḍurogīva gauradyutiradṛśyata  KAvk sukumāre dināloke rātrau rākṣasayoṣitā bhakṣite lakṣyata śaśī kapālabalasaṃnibhaḥ  KAvk vyāpte candrikayā loke kālacandranacarcayā vimānamagamat kkāpisā ca svargamṛgekṣaṇā  KAvk vimānapatitaḥ so pi puruṣaḥ sarvarūpayā śanaiḥ saptabhirāvartaiḥ śatapadyā viveṣṭitaḥ  KAvk sā tasya mūrdhni vivaraṃ kṛtvā mastiṣkaśoṇitam āsvādayantī śanakaiścakāra śuṣiraṃ śiraḥ  KAvk athāruṇakaracchanne socchvāsavadāne dine bībhatsadarśanakleśādiva mīlitatārake  KAvk prādurāsan punardivyavimānaṃ sā ca kāminī yuvā sa cādbhutatanurdivyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ  KAvk pṛṣṭo tivismayāt tena svavṛttāntaṃ jagād saḥ dvijo haṃ vāsavagrāmanivāsī manasābhidhaḥ  KAvk taruṇī prātiveśyasya patnī malayamañjarī abhūnmama bhujaṅgasya svairiṇī vallabhā bhṛśam  KAvk paradāraratergrāme vyagrā me kṣamate matiḥ minagnā viṣayagrāme samagrā me kṣayaṃ gatā  KAvk āryakātyāyanaḥ pāpaṃ jñātvā mām cauryakāmukam dayāvidheyaḥ kāruṇyāt provāca vijane śanaiḥ  KAvk parāṅganāṅgasaṃsargaprītyā rūparateḥ kṣaibam  anaṅgāgnau patannāśaṃ pataṅgaṃ iva mā gamaḥ  KAvk aho āsaktaraktānāṃ saṃpatanapramādinām kāminām hiṃsakānāṃ ca paradārādaraḥ param  KAvk pṛthu pravepathu svāpaśramavihvalānām gṛdhrāṅganāmukhanikhātanakhakṣatānām saṃmohane paravadhūvihitaspṛhāṇāṃ romāñcakāriṇi paraṃ narake ca kāmaḥ  KAvk tasmādasmānnivartasva vatsa kutsitakarmaṇaḥ jāyate pātakaṃ sparśe śunāmevāśucau ratiḥ  KAvk ityahaṃ kṛpayā tena niṣiddho pyaviśuddhadhīḥ aniruddhena rāgeṇa baddhastāmeva nātyajam  KAvk vijñāya māmavirataṃ tataḥ kātyāyano dadau mahyaṃ śīlasamādānaṃ dinacaryāhitodyataḥ  KAvk dinaśīlasamādānāt parastrīgamanānniśi iyaṃ me puṇyapāpotthā sukhaduḥkhamayī sthitīḥ  KAvk gatena vāsavagrāmaṃ vācyaḥ putro mama tvayā suvarṇamagniśālāyāmasti gūḍhaṃ dhṛtaṃ mayā  KAvk vṛttiḥ kāryā tadudbhṛtya pūjyaḥ kātyāyanaśca saḥ praṇayāditi tenoktaḥ śroṇakoṭiryayau tataḥ  KAvk so paśyaddivyalalanāmagre maṇivimānagām lakṣmīṃ lāvaṇyadugdhābdheranāyāsodgatāmiva  KAvk tasya vimānapādeṣi caturṣu snāyusaṃyutam sa dadarśātidurdaśaṃ baddhaṃ pretacatuṣṭayam  KAvk sāpi taṃ pratyabhijñāya saṃbhāṣya snigdhayā girā surocitaṃ dadau tasmai rasavat pānabhojanam  KAvk bhuñjānasaṃjñayāṃ dūrāt pretairdainyena yācitaḥ sa dadau kṛpayā tebhyaḥ kākebhya iva piṇḍikāḥ  KAvk piṇḍo busatvamekasya prayāto nyasya lohatām svamāṃsatvaṃ tṛtīyasya caturthasya prapūyatām  KAvk vilokya tatkṛpāviṣṭaḥ sa teṣāṃ kaṣṭaceṣṭayā papraccha tanmukhacchāyām vicchāyīkṛtapaṅkajām  KAvk pṛṣṭā tadadbhutaṃ tena uvāca sā mṛgekṣaṇā na śroṇakoṭirṇaiṣāṃ dattaṃ bhavati tṛptaye  KAvk brāhmaṇasyāsya bhāryāhaṃ pūrvapādābalambinaḥ nandanāmnaḥ sunandākhyā vāsavagrāmavāsinaḥ  KAvk dvitīyapādasaṃsaktaḥ putro me niṣṭhurābhidhaḥ paścātpādāvalambinyau dāsī ceyaṃ snuṣā ca me  KAvk nakṣatrayogapūjāyām purā sajjīkṛate mayā bhaikṣyopahāre me gehamāryakātyāyano viśat  KAvk mayā cittaprasādinyā piṇḍapātena so rcitaḥ kurvanneva yayau kāntyā vaimalyānugrahaṃ diśām  KAvk tataḥ snātvā samāyātastūrṇaṃ patirayaṃ mama patpiṇḍapātamākarṇya pramidāya mayoditam  KAvk kopāduvāca māṃ kasmād viśikhaḥ śramaṇaḥ śaṭhaḥ apūjiteṣu pūjyeṣu busārhaḥ pūjitastvayā  KAvk iti mohādanenokte putro pyeṣa jagād mām pāke pūrvāśanāyogyaḥ sa kiṃ nāśnātyayoguḍān  KAvk iyaṃ snuṣā me satataṃ pūrvabhakṣyāvabhoginā mayokte śapathaṃ cakre svamāṃsādanavādinī  KAvk iyaṃ dāsī ca bhaikṣyāṇā cairyāttadvyayakāriṇī ākṣiptā cākarot satyaṃ pūyaśoṇitavādinī  KAvk tatra te pretatām yātāḥ svavākyasadṛśāśanāḥ ahaṃ tvāryaprasādena divyabhogopabhoginī  KAvk tvayā tvāryaśamāptena vaktavyā duhitā mama santi hemanidhānāni gṛhe catvāri te pituḥ  KAvk tānyuddhṛtya yathāyogaṃ bhajasv asvajanisthitim pūjanīyaḥ piturbhrātā nāmnā kātyāyana sadā  KAvk sa ḥ śroṇakoṭikarṇastvaṃ gaccha deśaṃ tyaja śramam varṣā dvādaśa saṃpūrṇāḥ svagṛhānnirgatasya te  KAvk ityuktvā taṃ samādiśaya tasya pretacatuṣṭayam suptasyaiva muhūrtena
