svadeśāptimakārayat  KAvk utthitaḥ so pi sahasā svadeśodyānakānanāt viyogaśokātpitarau śuśrāvāndhyamupāgatau  KAvk bhikṣudvijātithigaṇe pūjyamāne surālaye svakaṃ pitṛgṛhaṃ dṛṣṭvā paraṃ vismayamāyayau  KAvk niścitya sarvaṃ bhāvānāṃ kṣaṇikatvādanityatām sneharāgaṃ samutsṛjya tatrasthaḥ samacintayat  KAvk aho saṃmohanidreyaṃ nirantato divāniśam svapnamāyāvilasitaiḥ karotyadbhutavibhramam  KAvk janmavartmapradā mātā pitā bījavapatkhagaḥ pānthapūjāsanaṃ kāyaḥ ko yaṃ niyamasaṃgamaḥ  KAvk śriyaḥ saṃsārābhrabhramaparicitāḥ kāñcanarucāāśā dig  nirbandhāstaḍita iva nirlepacapalāḥ vapuḥ sarvāpāyaiḥ kṣayabhayanikāyaiḥ parigataṃjarārogodvegaistadapi na virāgastanubhṛtām  KAvk śriye svastisamāptaye svajanasyāyamañjaliḥ dākṣiṇyaiḥ kṣamataṃ śrīṣu pravrajyaiva priyā mama  KAvk iti dhyātvā sa pitarau samāśvāsyāptalocanau buddhau dharmapathe śuddhe śamadhāmni nyaveśayat  KAvk sārthabhraṣṭaścirāyāt kṛśo pi svajanasya ca aluptasattvavibhavānnakṛpāspadatāṃ yayau  KAvk anukampasva yadyetaṃ saṃsārakleśavihvalam sataḥ kasyānukampyāste saṃpatsaṃparkanitspṛhāḥ  KAvk paśupālakaviprastrīsaṃdeśādi yathoditam nigadya tebhyaḥ kanakaprāptipratyayalakṣaṇam  KAvk śāntaḥ kātyāyanaṃ prāpya pravrajyāṃ sa samādade mugdhānām yadviṣādāya tatprasādāya dhīmatām  KAvk sa samāsādya viśadaṃ sritaḥprāptiphalaṃ tataḥ sakṛdāgāmyanāgāmiphalamarhatphalaṃ tathā  KAvk traidhātuko vītarāgaḥ samaloṣṭāśmakāñcanaḥ ākāśapāṇitulyo bhūdasicandanayoḥ samah  KAvk śrāvastyām veṇugahane jinaṃ jetavane sthitam bhagavantaṃ yayau draṣṭuṃ so tha kātyāyanājñayā  KAvk praṇitātakṛtātithyaḥ prītyā bhagavatā svayam sa śroṇakoṭīkarṇo tha babhāṣe harṣanirbharaḥ  KAvk bhagavān dharmakāyena dṛṣṭo yaṃ śrotravartmani adhunā rūpakāyena puṇyairālokito mayā  KAvk analpasukṛtaprāpyamidaṃ taddarśanāmṛtam pītvā na tṛptimāyānti vañcitā eva te param  KAvk aspṛhasyāpi te mūrtiḥ kurute kasya na spṛhām nirlopasyāpi te dṛṣṭiraho harṣeṇa limpati  KAvk tvatkathā tvadanudhyānaṃ tvatprāptistvanniṣevaṇam etāḥ kuśalamūlānāṃ sphītāḥ phalasamṛddhayaḥ  KAvk iti śrutvā bhagavatā prasādenābnhinanditaḥ tadādiṣṭaṃ śamārāmaṃ sa vihāramavāptavān  KAvk tasyāspadaṃ samabhyetya praṇayādbhagavānapu śrutvāsya madhuraṃ dharmaṃ svādhyāyaṃ praśaśaṃsa saḥ  KAvk tāṃ śroṇikoṭikarṇasya dṛṣṭvā praśamasaṃpadam bhikṣubhirbhagavān pṛṣṭaḥ pūrvavṛttamabhāṣata  KAvk vārāṇasyāṃ purā samyaksaṃbuddhe kāśyapābhidhe nirvāṇadhātau niḥśeṣakāryatvāt parinirvṛte  KAvk kṛkināmanṛpaścaityaṃ tasya ratnairakārayat svayaṃ tatpuṇyasaṃbharaṃ svargaṃ vaktumivodgatam  KAvk śīrṇasthāpitasaṃskāre tasmin saṃjñādhṛtaṃ dhanam tatputraḥ prāptarājyo tha na dadau lobhamohitaḥ  KAvk athottarāpathāyātaḥ sarthavāho rthadābhidhaḥ pradadau pṛthivīmūlyaṃ tatkṛte karṇabhūṣaṇam  KAvk kālāntaropagato pi datvā cānyaddhanaṃ mahat praṇidhānaṃ sa kṛtavān bhūyāsaṃ puṇyavāniti  KAvk sa śroṇakoṭikarṇo yaṃ puṇyaiḥ prātapadaṃ mahat tadvidhenaiva saṃyātaḥ karṇabhūṣaṇalakṣaṇaḥ  KAvk prasthānasamaye mātā śrāvitā paruṣaṃ vacaḥ yasmādanena tenāsya babhūvāsya śramo mahān  KAvk madhyeṣu mahataḥ śuklaguṇasatkarmavāsasaḥ kṛṣṇakarmalavāṃśo pi sphuṭa evāvadhāryate  KAvk sukṛtasacivaḥ sattvetsāhaḥ pravāsasakhī dhṛtiḥviṣamataraṇe vīryaṃ seturvipadyadhikā kṛpā śamaparicitā paryante ca prasādamayī matiḥpariṇatiriyaṃ puṇyaprāpteḥ sphuratphalaśālinī  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ śroṇakoṭikarṇāvadānaṃ nāmonaviṃśatitamaḥ pallavaḥ  āmrapālyavadānam dvijihvasaṅge kathamasti vṛttiranekamukhye kathamasti saukhyam karmāntabandhe sti kathaṃ svaśaktiḥ prajñāprakarṣe kathamastyapāyaḥ  KAvk mithilāyāṃ videheṣu jalasattvābhidho nṛpaḥ abhūd bhujabhujaṅgasya viśrāntapṛthivībharaḥ  KAvk khaṇḍo nāma mahāmātyastasyākhaṇḍalasaṃpadaḥ babhūvāśeṣaṣāṅguṇyaparijñānabṛhaspatiḥ  KAvk nītijñagauravāttasya nṛpe vyaktaṃ nalokini sadābhavanmukhaprekṣī sarvaḥ kāryavaśājjanaḥ  KAvk gatānugatikatvena pravāhapraṇayī bharaḥ vardhate vāryamāṇasya svajanasya jalasya ca  KAvk sarvaṃ tanmayamālokya janaṃ mātsaryamūrcchitāḥ mantriṇaḥ saṃhatāstasya vinipātamacintayan  KAvk te praviśyāśramam rājñastāṃ tasya prabahviṣṇūtām muhuḥ śaṅkāspadaṃ kṛtvā śaśaṃsurbhedakovidāḥ  KAvk tadgirā śaṅkito rājā tasya vaimukhyamāyayau abalābālabhūpālā varṇapratyayāḥ param  KAvk aśaṅkyādapi śaṅkante śaṅkādoṣe pyaśaṅkitāḥ aviśeṣajñacapalā bhūpālāḥ kākaśaṅkinaḥ  KAvk prabhorviraktiliṅgāni vilokyāmātyapuṃgavaḥ svasutau gopasiṃhākhyau saśaṅkaḥ svairamabravīt  KAvk dhūrtairme vītaviśvāsaḥ piśunairnṛpatiḥ kṛtaḥ pratyayaṃ naiti hṛdaye vidāryāpi pradarśite  KAvk viraktaḥ sthagitālāpadarśanaśravaṇaḥ prabhuḥ śepha iva vṛddhasya yātaḥ śithilatāṃ mama  KAvk piśunodbhūtabhedasya premṇaḥ saṃdhirna vidyate na maṇiḥ śliṣyāti punaḥ pāṣāṇaśakalīkṛtaḥ  KAvk dvijihṇakuṭilakrāntaḥ prabhuścandanapādapaḥ na yātyarthakriyākārī guṇavānapi sevyatām  KAvk kathaṃ nṛpanidhānārthī kuśalaṃ bhajate naraḥ ghoradveṣaviṣāviṣṭadvijihvāghātavihvalaḥ  KAvk tasmādvrajāmaḥ saṃtyajya dveṣadoṣeṇa bhūpateḥ śaṅkāśalyamaye vṛtte me smin deśe sthitena kim  KAvk dakṣā rakṣākṣamāḥ śūrāḥ prabhutārthāḥ susaṃhatāḥ santaḥ santi viśālāyāṃ vāsastatra mamepsitaḥ  KAvk iti bruvāṇaḥ putrābhyāṃ tathetyuktaḥ sa sānugaḥ udyānagatimānena prayayau saparicchadaḥ  KAvk prayāṇaṃ nṛpatirjñātvā nivartanasamudyataḥ yatnenāpi na taṃ prāpa notsṛṣṭaṃ labhyate punaḥ  KAvk mūrkhāḥ satsu kṛtāvajñā vimuhyante kṣaṇena taiḥ yāti teṣāṃ tu sarvatra ko pi nārthī kṛtārthatām  KAvk dhīmānamātyaḥ prāpto tha kṛṣṭo vaiśālikairguṇaiḥ pūjitaḥ praṇayācāraiḥ saṃghamukhye pade sthitaḥ  KAvk tadbuddhivibhavāptaśrīḥ so tha tatpramukho gaṇaḥ kadācidanayāllekhe na parābahvapātratām  KAvk atha kālena siṃhasya mantrisūnoḥ kanīyasaḥ ajāyata sutā kāntā cailā nāma guṇocitā  KAvk dvitīyā copacailākhyā sutā jātāsya sundarī nanmanyeva tayoḥ prāha nimittajño vicakṣaṇaḥ  KAvk cailāyāstanayo bhāvī pitṛhantā mahīpatiḥ guṇavānupacailāyāḥ pūrṇalakṣahṇavāniti  KAvk jyeṣṭho mantrisutaḥ śauryādgopaḥ prauḍhamadoddhataḥ udyānamardanakṣepairgaṇānāṃ dveṣyatām yayau  KAvk tatpiturgauravāttasmai sānujāya vimanyavaḥ viśālaśālatāmante jīrṇodyānadvayaṃ daduḥ  KAvk sugatapratimāṃ cakre tatraikaḥ sukṛtocitām vihāraṃ vaibhavodāraṃ bhuvanābharaṇaṃ paraḥ  KAvk atha pitrā balotsiktaḥ sutaḥ pratyantamaṇḍale gaṇakopabhayādgopaḥ karmāntopārjane dhṛtaḥ  KAvk kālena tridivaṃ yāte tasmin mantrivare gaṇaiḥ kanīyasastu sādhutvāt siṃhastasya pade dhṛtaḥ  KAvk gopaḥ piturasaṃprāpya padaṃ gaṇavimānitaḥ taddeśavāsavirasaḥ parihāramacintayat  KAvk vāstavya kaṇṭakākīrṇe vyāghrāghrāte varaṃ vane anekasvāmisaṃbhinnajane na tu viśṛṅkhale  KAvk nānāmatakriyālāpaḥ kathamārādhyate gaṇaḥ samīhitaṃ yadekasya datanyasmai na rocate  KAvk itmānī sa saṃcintya gatvā rājagṛhaṃ puram bimbisāraṃ narapatiṃ guṇaśriyamaśiśriyat  KAvk sa tena mānitaḥ prītyā tasya viśrambhabhūrabhūt cirarucyeva tatkālamābhāti guṇasaṃgatiḥ  KAvk rājño tha bimbisārasya vallabhā pañcatāṃ yayau tadviyogāgnisaṃtaptaṃ taṃ vicintya sa buddhimān  KAvk upacailāṃ sutāṃ bhrātustadvivāhocitā vadhūm gūḍhacārī tadādeśāt vaiśālakapurīṃ yaya  KAvk kanyā gaṇopabhogyauva na kasmaicitpradīyate iti vaiśālikaiḥ pūrvaṃ svadeśe niyamaḥ kṛtaḥ  KAvk tatpure dvārarakṣāyai yakṣasthānāvalambinī parapraveśe kurute śabdaṃ ghaṇṭī paṭīyasī  KAvk sa praviśya tato bhrāturgūḍhamudyānacāriṇīm upacailāṃ samāhatuṃ gataścailāmavāptavān  KAvk yātastaṃ rathamāruhya ghaṇṭāśabdādabhidryutam sa hatvā vīrapuruṣānavāpa nṛpateḥ puram  KAvk tamūce devakanyeyaṃ prātā vimanasātmanā pitṛhantā suto hyāsyā nimittajñena sūcitaḥ  KAvk tasmādeṣā narapatermahiṣī na tavocitā tvayi jīvati jīvanti prajānāṃ sarvasaṃpadaḥ  KAvk ityuktastena tāṃ dṛṣṭvā tyuktaṃ naiva śaśāka saḥ niruddhaḥ karmaṇā hyeva tanmukhālekhyalekhayā  KAvk so vadat kka kadā dṛṣṭa putreṇa nihataḥ pitā svayaṃ mayābhiṣektavyaḥ suto yady bhaviṣyati  KAvk ityuktvā nṛpatiḥ kanyāṃ pariṇīyābhavatsukhī kṛtakarmorminirmāṇe prabhavanti na buddhayaḥ  KAvk bhoginastasya kālena tasyām sūnurajāyata jyotiṣkacarite yasya vṛttamuktaṃ pitṛdruhaḥ  KAvk tapovanamṛgādhānamṛgayāvyasane vane evaṃvidho hyabhūttasya muniśāpaḥ sutākṛtiḥ  KAvk atrāntare mahānnāma vaiśālikagaṇāgraṇīḥ kanyāmāmravanātprāpa kadalīskandhanirgatām  KAvk sā tasya bhavane kāntā vardhamānā śanaiḥ śanaiḥ vidadhe vipulāṃ prītiṃ dānacintāṃ ac cetasi  KAvk praṇayādāmrapālīti bandhubhiḥ sā kṛtābhidhāḥ sūnuhīnamina tyaktvā bālyaṃ yauvanamādade  KAvk tadvivāhodyatasyātha na sehe tatpiturgaṇaḥ gaṇopabhogyā kanyeti samayasya vyatikramam  KAvk pitaraṃ duḥkhasaṃtaptaṃ sametyātha jagād sā bhavāmi gaṇabhogyaiva kiṃ tveṣa samayo yadi  KAvk ekasyopari nānyasya praveśaḥ svapade sthitiḥ paṇaḥ kārṣāpaṇaśataiḥ pañcabhiḥ pratyahaṃ mama  KAvk saptāhenaiva vicayaḥ karyo veśmani nānyadā ityasmin samaye va dhyaḥ sarvaścaiva vyatikramī  KAvk iti tatsamayaṃ jñātvā tatpiturvacasā gaṇaḥ akārod bāḍhamityuktvā dṛḍhaniścayamādarāt  KAvk tataḥ saratnabhavane varābharaṇabhūṣite hemaharmyasamārūḍhā dideśa dinacandrikām  KAvk tataḥ paṇīkṛtaḥ kāmī yo yastāṃ samupāyayau tasya tasyābhavat tasyāḥ prabhāveṇaujasaḥ kṣayaḥ  KAvk draṣṭumeva na śekuste kiṃ punaḥ spraṣṭumākulāḥ bhujaṅgabhogasaṃruddhāṃ tāṃ candanalatāmiva  KAvk tataḥ sā sundarī bheje yauvanasyāpi yauvanam guruṇā stanabhāreṇa madhyabhaṅgabhayapradam  KAvk smarasaṃbhogarahitaṃ tattasyā rūpamadbhutam śvabhrahemalatāpuṣpamiva niṣphalatāṃ yayau  KAvk kautukāśāvinodāya nānādeśāntarāgataiḥ akāri citrakārairbhūpālapratikṛtirgṛhe  KAvk vidhāya citralikhitān sā krameṇa nareśvarān dadarśa bimbirāsaya rūpaṃ ratipateciva  KAvk tamālokyaiva sahasā samudbhūtamanobhavā sa yena likhitastatra taṃ papraccha kutūhalāt  KAvk ko yaṃ sakhe prītilatāmādhavo vasudhāpatiḥ prīṇāti locane yasya sudhāparicitā ruciḥ  KAvk dhanyā kā nāma bhūbharturasya praṇayabhāgiṇī lakṣyaṃ saubhagyajaṃ garvamurvaśyāḥ saṃhṛtaṃ yayā  KAvk iti pṛṣṭatayā svairaṃ tāmūce citrakovidaḥ bhūpatirbimbasāro yaṃ sāraṃ sukṛtasaṃpadām  KAvk śuaryarūpatulārohe devāḥ ke nākanāyakāḥ śaṅke karoti naivāsya manmatho vā manoratham  KAvk ityukte tena sā tasthau bhūpālanyastalocanā sahasaivābhilāṣeṇa navīnābhimukhīkṛtā  KAvk atrāntare bimbisāraḥ svairaveśmani nijane kathānte gopamavadat kiṃcitsmitasitādharaḥ  KAvk śrūyatāṃ yanmama sakhe kiṃcinmanasi vartate niryantramitrasvacchandavādaḥ ko pi sudhārasaḥ  KAvk vaiśālikaurvarārohā gaṇaiḥ sādhāraṇikṛtā rambhorūḥ śrūyate kāntā rambhāgarbhasamudbhavā sā tairna dūṣitādyāpi mātaṅgairiva padminī  KAvk śravaṇādeva sānandamaparyuṣitakautukam na karoti manaḥ kasya tatstrīratnamayonijam  KAvk abhilāṣi manastasyāṃ śrotāya jātaṃme saha cakṣuṣā tadguṇaśrutidhanyāya śrotrāya spṛhayāmyaham  KAvk ityukte bhūmipatinā gopastaṃ prayabhāṣata bhujaṅgagaṇasaṃruddhaḥ sa rājan mānmatho nidhiḥ  KAvk atyalpaskhalitaṃ prāpya duḥsahāpātadurgamaḥ eṣa te viṣamaḥ panthā darśito viṣameṣuṇā  KAvk labhate sā na nirgantuṃ na yuktaṃ gamanaṃ ca te kimasmin viratopāye vadāmyubhayasaṃśaye  KAvk ityuktastena nṛpatirnotkaṇṭhāgrāhamatyajat vidvāṃso pyucitām nītiṃ na smaranti smarāturāḥ  KAvk vaiśālikapurīṃ yāto gopena sahito tha saḥ praviveśānyaveśena mandiraṃ hariṇīdṛśaḥ  KAvk sā citradarśanenaiva dṛṣṭvā paricitaṃ dṛśoḥ naranāthaṃ savailakṣyalakṣaṇaṃ kṣitimaikṣata  KAvk lajjāniruttare tasyāḥ kampavyatikare param raṇantī rasanā cakre svāgataṃ nṛpaterivaḥ  KAvk vilokya dhanyatāmānī tatra citre nijaṃ vapuḥ tāṃ lāvaṇyanadīṃ rājā nayanāñjalinā papau  KAvk lajjāveśena sundaryāmābhijātyena bhūpatau ābaddhamainayoḥ kṣipraṃ gopastāṃ sasmito vadat  KAvk ayaṃ te citralikhitākāradhyānāvadhānataḥ vyaktaṃ bhakṣiviśeṣena devaḥ pratyakṣatāṃ gataḥ  KAvk tvayāyaṃ likhitaścitre tvamanena tu cetasi na jāne yuvayoḥ ko nu prayātaḥ premadūtatām  KAvk ityādibhiḥ kathābandhaiḥ parīpūrṇapramodayoḥ yadyadeva smarādiṣṭam tattadāsvādatām gatam  KAvk ghaṇṭāravākule loke rājā pracchannakāmukah saptarātramanālokye tasthau tadbhavane rahaḥ  KAvk lateva puṣpitā kāle tasmādgarbhamavāpya sā cakre viditavṛttāntaṃ taṃ lajjāvanatā śanaiḥ  KAvk āsanne viśmavicaye datvāsmai nṛpatiryayau bhāviputraparijñānapratyayādaṅgulīyakam  KAvk yāte bhāsvadvapiṣu nṛpatau saṃmate locanānāṃ sadyaḥ prodyadvirahatimirākrāntimīrākrāntimīlanmukhābjā sābhūtsāyaṃtanatanutarāpāravātābhibhūtāśokocchvāsavyatikaravatī hāsahīnā niśeva  KAvk kapolaṃ pāṇipadmena saṃkalpena mahīpatim navaṃ tānavamaṅgena vahantī nimimīla sā  KAvk tataḥ kālena kalyāṇī pratibimbopamaṃ pituḥ ajījanatsā natayaṃ vinayaṃ sādhudhīriva  KAvk vardhamāne śanaistasmin kāle bimba ivaindave bimbisārasya putro yamiti lokeṣu paprathe  KAvk apavādaparaistaistaistaṃ pratyanucittairyadā bādhante śiśavaḥ krīḍāprasaṅge marṣasaṃyatāḥ  KAvk tataḥ sā preṣayāmāsa putraṃ vidyārjanocitam vaṇiksārthena mahatā sāṅgulīyaṃ pituḥ padam  KAvk bimbisāro pi saṃprāpya sadṛśākāramātmajam harṣadṛptaḥ pariṣvajya cakre tasya parigraham  KAvk vṛttāṇte viśrute tasminnāmrapālyāh sakautukaiḥ bhikṣubhirbhagavān pṛṣṭastatkathāmavadajjinaḥ  KAvk pure rājagṛhe rājavallabhodyānakānane babhūva mālatī nāma pūrvamudyānapālikā  KAvk sā kadācit prasādārdraṃ puraḥ prāptaṃ yadṛcchayā pratyekabuddhaṃ rājaṣiṃ cūtapuṇpaipūjayat  KAvk ayonijā nṛpasyāhaṃ patnī syāmiti tatra sā praṇidhānaṃ puraścakre tasya cittaprasādinī  KAvk puṇyapuṣpaphalabhogaśālinī saiva divyatanurāmrapālikā ityudāracaritā niśamya te bhikṣavaḥ sapadi vismayaṃ yayuḥ  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ āmrapālyavadānaṃ nāma viṃśatitamaḥ pallavaḥ  jetavanapratigrahāvadānam dṛṣṭaṃ muṣṭiniviṣṭapāradakaṇākāraṃ narāṇāṃ dhanaṃdhanyo sau yaśasā sahākṣayapadaṃ yadyasya vidyotate dīnānāthagaṇārpaṇopakaraṇībhūtaprabhūtaśriyaḥpuṇyārāmavihāracaityabhagavadbimbapratiṣṭhādibhiḥ  KAvk śrīmān babhūva śrāvastyāṃ datto nāma gṛhābhipaḥ sutastasya sudatto bhūdākaraḥ puṇyasaṃpadām  KAvk sa bālya evālaṃkāraṃ yācakebhyaḥ sadā dadau prāgjanmavāsanābhyāsaḥ kasya kena nirvāyate  KAvk nityamābharaṇatyāgātparaṃ pitrā nivāritaḥ nadīsamuddhṛtānyasmai sadaivānyānyadarśayat  KAvk nidhidarśī sa sarvatra pitari tridivaṃ gate dīnānāthapradānena babhūvānāthapiṇḍadaḥ  KAvk kṛtadānah sa kālena putravān putravtsalaḥ abhūt putravivāhārthī kanyānveṣaṇayatnavān  KAvk kanyakāṃ yācituṃ kāṃcit puraṃ rājagṛhaṃ tataḥ madhuskandhābhidhaṃ dakṣaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ visarsarja saḥ  KAvk āsādya magadhān rājagṛhaṃ nagarametya saḥ mahādhanaṃ gṝhapatiṃ yayāce kanyakām dvijaḥ  KAvk anāthapiṇḍado nāma śrāvastyāmasti viśrutaḥ tatputrāya sujātāya kanyāyām dehītyuvāca saḥ  KAvk so bravīdeśa saṃbandhaḥ paramo smatkulocitaḥ vaṃśe smākaṃ tu kanyānām śuklamādīyate mahat  KAvk śataṃ śataṃ rathāgryāṇāṃ gajāśvāśvatarasya ca dāśīnicayaniṣkānāṃ dīyatāṃ yadi śakyate  KAvk ityukte tena taṃ vipraṃ sasmitaḥ pratyabhāṣata anāthapiṇḍadagṛhe dāsye śulkaṃ tadalpakam  KAvk brāhmaṇenākhile tasmin kanyāśulke pratiśrute tamādarādgṛhapatirbhojanāya nyamantrayat  KAvk sa bhuktvā vividhaṃ tatra bhakṣyabhojyamayantritaḥ rātrau visūcikākrāntaścukrośa vipulavyathaḥ  KAvk ye nnamaśnanti laulyena niśi nidrāsukhāpaham janmakarma kathaṃ kuryuḥ paralokasukhāya te  KAvk tatyājāśucibhītyā taṃ gṛhātparijano bahiḥ āspadaṃ nairapekṣyasya jātyā dāsajanaḥ śaṭhaḥ  KAvk śubhena karmaṇā tasya saṃprāptastena vartmanā samaudgalyāyanaḥ śāriputraḥ kāruṇyapeśalaḥ  KAvk taṃ vaṃśasya dalāgreṇa nirlikhyāpi tathā mṛdā prakṣālya dharmamādiśya tau tasya yayatuḥ śanaiḥ  KAvk so pi cittaṃ tayoragre prasādya tyaktavigrahaḥ caturmahārājikeṣu deveṣu samājāyata  KAvk tatra viśravaṇādeśānmartyaloke niketane sa cakre śibiradvāre pūjādhiṣṣṭhānasaṃnidhim  KAvk lekhavijñātasaṃbandhaviścayo tha yathoditam anāthapiṇḍadaḥ śulkamādāya svayamāyayau  KAvk sa saṃbandhigṛhaṃ prāpya dadarśāścaryakāriṇīm śikharākārarājārhabhakṣyasaṃbhārasaṃpadam  KAvk sa vismayādgṛhapatiṃ papraccha svacchamānasaḥ bhūribhakṣyptsavaḥ ko yamapi rājā nimantritaḥ  KAvk sa taṃ babhāṣe bhagavān buddhaḥ saṃghaparigrahaḥ mayā nimantritaḥ saṃghe so yam mama mahotsavaḥ  KAvk iti buddhābhidhānena jātaromāzncakaṇṭakaḥ indusyandirivālkinnaḥ sahasaiva babhūva saḥ  KAvk aviditaparamārthe kasyacinnāmamātresphurati sahajabhāvaḥ ko pi janmānubandhaḥ abhinavaghananāde vyaktaharṣabhilāṣaḥspṛśati lalitanṛtyodvṛttavṛttiṃ mayūraḥ  KAvk so vadadvadanāmbhojasaṃjātābhinavadyutiḥ ka eṣa bhagavān buddhaḥ kaśca saṃgho bhidhīyate  KAvk iti pṛṣṭo gṛhapatistena provāca sasmitaḥ aho bata na jānīṣe śāstāraṃ bhuvanatraye  KAvk saṃsārapāśabhītānāṃ śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaiṣiṇām jina yastaṃ na jānāti sa loke vañcitaḥ param  KAvk kiṃ tena mohalīnena viphalīkṛtajanmanā ajñānataraṇopāyaṃ vayo yena vyayīkṛtam  KAvk gotamo bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyarājakuladbhivaḥ saṃbudhyānuttaraṃ samyaksaṃbodhimanagārikaḥ  KAvk paścāt pravrajitānām ca tasyaivānugrahātparam bhikṣūṇāṃ gatarāgāṇām samūhaḥ saṃgha ucyate  KAvk sa eṣa buddhapramukhaḥ saṃghaḥ svakuśalaiṣiṇāḥ mayā puṇyapaṇaṃ prāpyaṃ praṇayena nimantritaḥ  KAvk iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā tatsmṛtvānāthapiṇḍadaḥ buddhālambanabhāvena niśi nidrāṃ samāyayau  KAvk rajanyāṃ yāmaśeṣāyāṃ samākṛṣṭa ivetsukaḥ prabhātamiti sa jñātvā puradvāreṇa niryayau  KAvk śibikādvāramāsādya saṃprāpta iva devatām madhuskandhena nirdiṣṭaṃ śreyaḥpanthānamāptavān  KAvk bhagavāṃstaṃ tataḥ prāpya sa tṛṣṇārta ivāmṛtam babhūvānupamāsvādaṃ pramodāmodanirvṛtaḥ  KAvk taṃ dṛṣṭvā sādaraṃ dūrāt chāyātarumivādhvagaḥ avāpa gatasaṃtāpaḥ śrāntiṃ viśrāntiśītalām  KAvk tasya taddarśaneva vimalābhigataḥ manaḥ śaratsamāgameneva ghanadhvāntojjhitaṃ nabhaḥ  KAvk sa ko pi puṇyaśīlānāmanubhāvaḥ prasādinām bhavanti yatprasādena nirvighnāścittavṛttayaḥ  KAvk so cintayadaho mohavihīnasya hi me tathā anucchedavikāro yaṃ jātaḥ praśamasaṃpadaḥ  KAvk vañcito smi na yatpūrvaṃ dṛṣto yaṃ bhagavān mayā nādhanyānāmiyaṃ yāti mūrtirlocanagocaram  KAvk amṛtamadhirodārā dṛṣṭirdyutiḥ śaśipeśalā taruṇakaruṇāyattā vṛttiḥ prasādamayī matiḥ ayamatiśayaṃ pratyāsannaḥ karoti virāgatāṃ vigatarajasāṃ niḥsaṃsāraḥ priyo pi parigrahaḥ  KAvk iti cittaprasādena cintayannupasṛtya saḥ vidadhe tasya sānandaḥ pādapadmābhivandanam  KAvk bhagavānapi tatprāptiprasādānandalakṣaṇam uvāha vadanacchāyaṃ pūrṇakāruṇyapūritam  KAvk dṛṣṭimāśvāsajananīṃ kāmaṃkāmapi tasya saḥ visasarjojjvalāṃ janmarajaḥśuddhyai sudhānadīm  KAvk athāsya bhagavān bhradrāṃ vidadhe dharmadeśanām caturṇāmāryasatyānāṃ pratibhāvavidhāyinīm  KAvk sa śāsanāddhi saṃvyastasamastakleśasaṃtatiḥ nijaṃ janma nivedyāsmai praṇatastamabhāṣataḥ  KAvk atikrānto smi bhagavan bhavantaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ vipannavāsanābhyāsaḥ saṃsāre na rame param  KAvk karotyakuśalaṃ dūre śubhamāśu prayacchati sūcayatyucitācāraṃ mahatamavalokanam  KAvk sukhārhaṃ tvadvihārāya vihāraṃ paramādarāt ratnasārapurodāraṃ svapuraṃ kārayāmyaham  KAvk karotu tatra bhagavān satataṃ sthityanugraham dhanairāsevito smābhiḥ saparyāparicaryayā  KAvk ityarthanāṃ tathetyasya bhagavān pratyapadyata praṇayuprārthanābhaṅgapragalbhā na hi sādhavaḥ  KAvk bhagavantamathāmantrya śrāvastīṃ sa purīṃ yayau tadādiṣṭena sahitaḥ śāriputreṇa bhikṣuṇā  KAvk tatra jetakumāreṇa hiraṇyārghoṇa bhūyasā dattaṃ kāñcanamādāya vihāraṃ tamasūtrayat  KAvk bhaktyutsāhādathārambhakṛtasāhāyyakah suraiḥ vihāraṃ tridivākāraṃ cakārānāthapiṇḍadaḥ  KAvk tatra jetakumāro pi bhaktyā bhagavataḥ param yaśaḥpuṇyapratiṣṭhāyai vidadhe dvārakoṣṭhakam  KAvk ath atīrthyāstamālokya vihārārambhamadbhutam sāpavādavivādena cakrurdveṣākulāḥ kalim  KAvk raktākṣapramukhasteṣām mātsaryātkṣudrapraṇḍitaḥ sapakṣa iva kṛṣṇāhiścakitaḥ purataḥ sadā  KAvk ruddhe vihārasaṃbhāre tena vādajayāvadhi anāthapiṇḍadagirā śāriputraḥ samāyayau  KAvk raktākṣo tha tamāhūya prabhāvotkarṣadarśane indrajālabalotphullaṃ sahakāramadarśayat  KAvk śāriputraprabhāvotthairvipulaistanmukhānilaiḥ unmūlitaḥ śakalatāṃ tīrthyotsāha ivāpa saḥ  KAvk raktākṣavihitāṃ phullakamalāṃ padminīṃ tataḥ paṅkaśeṣāṃ dvipaścakre śāriputravinirmitaḥ  KAvk ratkākṣavakṣonikṣiptaḥ saptaśīrṣamahoragaḥ śāriputreṇa nikṣiptastārkṣyapakṣāgramārutaiḥ  KAvk tadāhūto tha vetālaḥ śāriputreṇa kīlitaḥ prerito mantravirtyeṇa raktākṣaṃ hantumudyayau  KAvk vetālābhihatastrāsānnaśyanmānamadajvaraḥ śaraṇaṃ pādapatitaḥ śāriputraṃ jagāma saḥ  KAvk raktākṣastena bhaṅgena śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ pravrajyāyām vītarāgaḥ śuddhāṃ bodhismavāptavān  KAvk tīrthyāstvanye paridveṣakrodhapāramitāṃśavaḥ tatra karmakaravyājāttasthurbhikṣavadhodyatāḥ  KAvk te tha dharmadruhaḥ kāle śāriputreṇa lakṣitāḥ taddṛṣṭipātamātreṇa babhūvurmaitramānasāḥ  KAvk āśayānuśayaṃ dhātuṃ prakṛtiṃ ca vicārya saḥ dharmadeśanayā teṣāṃ dideśānuttarāṃ daśām  KAvk atha tasya vihārasya nirvighnārambhakarmaṇi anāthapiṇḍadaṃ prāha śāriputraḥ smitānanaḥ  KAvk vihārasūtrapātasya tulya eva kṣaṇe mahān haumo vihāraḥ saṃvṛttastuṣite devasadmani  KAvk etadākarṇya saṃjātaprasādadviguṇāntaraḥ hemaratnavarāgāraṃ vihāraṃ samakārayat  KAvk vibhavairatha rājārhaiḥ pathi tenopakalpitaiḥ vijñaptistridivaiḥ sārdhamāyayau bhagavān jinah  KAvk tadāgamanaharṣeṇa prasanne bhavanatraye anāthapiṇḍadastasmai vāridhārāmapātayat  KAvk tasmin yadā na pradeśe vāridhārā papāta sā tadā bhagavato vākyāt tvaritaṃ patitānyataḥ  KAvk taṃ dṛṣṭvā kautukāt pṛṣṭo bhikṣubhirbhagavān punaḥ uvāca śrūyatāmetad vāristambhasya kāraṇam  KAvk anena pūrvabuddhebhye asminnevedamāspadam pratipāditamityeṣā vāridhārānyataścyutā  KAvk anenaiva purā samyaksaṃbuddhāya vipaśyine ayameva varārāmapradeśaḥ pratipāditaḥ  KAvk buddhāya śikhine prādāt puṣyajanmanyayaṃ punaḥ tato dadau viśvabhuve jināya raghijanmani  KAvk bhavadattābhidho bhūtvā kakucchandāya dattavān dadau bṛhaspatirbhūṭvā kanakākhyāya tāyine  KAvk kāśyapāya punaścāyaṃ prādādāṣāḍhajanmaniḥ anenaivādhunā mahyaṃ deśo yaṃ pratipāditaḥ  KAvk kālena sudhanākhyo yaṃ maitreyāya pradāsyati sattvavān kṣāntiśīlatvānnidhānānyeṣa paśyati  KAvk punaścāyaṃ gṝhapatirbhūtvā hemapradābhidhaḥ cakre pratyekabuddhasya saṃskāraṃ parinirvṛtau  KAvk ratnakumbhe tadasthīni dhṛtvā tatpraṇidhānataḥ adhunā ratnakośārhaḥ saṃjāto yaṃ suvarṇabhās  KAvk śrutveti śāsturvacanābhidhānaṃ te bhikṣavaḥ sāramivāmṛtasya kartuḥ pratiṣṭhārjitapūrṇapuṇyapuṣpādhivāsena bhṛśaṃ nananduḥ  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ jetavanapratigrahāvadānaṃ nāma ekaviṃśaṃ pallavaḥ  pitāputrasamādānam aho mahārhaṃ maṇivanmahattvaṃ bhavyā bhajante guṇagauraveṇa vinā guṇaṃ yadvapuṣām gurutvaṃ sthūlopalānāmiva niṣphalaṃ tat  KAvk śrīmān purā śākyapure narendraḥ śuddhodanaḥ śuddhisudhānidhānam vairāgyayogātsugatatvamāptaṃ smṛtvā sutaṃ sutsukatāmavāpaṃ  KAvk so cintayatpuṇyaguṇādhivāsaṃ sarasvatīvāsasaroruhaśri manaḥ prasādasya vilāsasaudhaṃ drakṣāmi sūnorvadanaṃ kadāham  KAvk ehīti taddarśanalālasena ye ye mayā jetavanaṃ visṛṣṭāḥ te te tadālokananirnimeṣaṃ tatraiva tiṣṭhantyamṛtaṃ pibantaḥ  KAvk saṃpreṣitastasya mayā sa nāyayau yo pyātmatulyaṃ praṇayādudāyī sa lekhahastastridivābhirāme tatraiva lekhatvamirābhiyātaḥ  KAvk saṃdeśavākyaṃ prahitaṃ mayā yat tadvismṛtaṃ tasya mukhena nūnam sarvo hi nāma svahitābhilāṣī dhatte parārthe kila śītalatvam  KAvk vilokanenaitya niṣiñca tūrṇaṃ pīyūṣapūreṇa mamāṅgasaṅgam niḥsaṅgato viśramatāṃ muhūrtaṃ dayāvidheyaḥ kuru bandhukāryam  KAvk ityetadākarṇya kathām sa kuryāt kṣaṇaṃ vilambaṃ mama darśane pi taccetasaḥ pallavapeśalasya na hi svabhāvaḥ praṇayāvabhaṅgaḥ  KAvk manoratheneti puraḥ prayāte taddarśanāyeva dharādhināthe pravrajyā vyañjitatatprasādaḥ samāyayau harṣarasādudāyī  KAvk dṛṣṭvā tamānandavipūrṇamānasaṃ pravrajyayā tatsadṛśānubhāvam utkaṇṭhitaḥ kuṇṭhitadhairyavṛttiḥ saṃmohamūrcchāṃ nṛpatiḥ prapede  KAvk sa labdhasaṃjñaḥ śiśiraiḥ payobhiḥ papraccha taṃ kiṃ nu sameṣyatīti so pyabravīddeva dinairbhavantamasaṃbhṛtaiḥ sādarameṣyatīti  KAvk tataḥ prayāteṣu dineṣu keṣu vyomnā śanairbhikṣugaṇānuyātaḥ sahāyayau nākasadām nikāyaiḥ sarvārthasiddhairbhagavān kumāraḥ  KAvk dyusundarīpāṇisarojamuktamandāramālākalitaścakāśe svargīyagaṅgāsphuṭaphenakūṭavilāsahāsāṅga ivāmarādriḥ  KAvk saṃghaṭṭabhinnābhrasakhaiḥ skhalidbhiḥ saśabdajāmbūnadakiṅkiṇīkaiḥ babhurvimānaiḥ kakubhāṃ mukhāni bhaktyeva śāsturvihitastavāni  KAvk nirantarairantarivārkatāraiḥ suraiḥ savidyādharasiddhasaṃghaiḥ paryāptasaṃsaktasitātapatrairvyāptaḥ samāptiṃ gaganaṃ jagāma  KAvk taṃ sarvalokopakṛtiprapannaṃ sarvākṛtiṃ sarvamayāvabhāsam samāpatantaṃ nabhaso tha digbhyaḥ kṣiteśca sarve dadṛśuḥ kṣaṇena  KAvk praharṣarāśiṃ janalocanānāṃ puṇyapramāṇaṃ sukṛtotsavānām lokastamālokanidhiṃ vilokya samullalannucchalitādbhutormiḥ  KAvk āścaryabhūtaṃ ruciraprabhāvamudāyinā sūcitamākalayya jagadguruṃ bhūmipatiḥ kumāraṃ kṛtāñjalistaṃ praṇanāma dūrāt  KAvk athāvatīryāryajanānuyātaḥ saṃpūjyamānaḥ praṇayena rājñā sphīṭaprabhābhāsitadigvibhāgāṃ nyagrodhinīṃ ratnabhuvam viveśa  KAvk hemāsanaṃ śāsanasaṃniviṣṭalokatrayaḥ saṃgatapādapīṭham sa tatra ratnāṅkuracitrapatraṃ bhāsvadvapurmerun  KAvk tanmānasendornayanāmṝtaughaṃ manorathaprārthanayopayātam vilokayannirvṛtinirnimeṣaḥ kṣaṇaṃ kṣitīśastridaśatvamāpa  KAvk sa taṃ jagādāśruniruddhakaṇṭhaḥ sotkarṣaharṣākulitaṃ kumāram hārāgraratnapratibimbasaktaṃ praveśayan prītirasādivāntaḥ  KAvk saṃtoṣaśītācalavat svabhāvāt sarve ramante kuśalasthalīṣu kṛtastvayāsmākamayaṃ tu kasmāt satsūpakārī virahopadeśaḥ  KAvk snehātpramodādguṇagauravācca dhīrdhāvatīyaṃ tvayi me prasahya āliṅganāya sthirasaṃgamāya pādapraṇāmāya ca tulyameva  KAvk yadvastu kiṃcidgaditaṃ mayā tat śrotavyameva praṇayoparodhāt guṇojjhitaṃ vā virasakramaṃ vā na snehamohasya bhavatyavācyam  KAvk pratyarṇaratnapratibimbitārkaprauḍhaprabhāprāvaraṇānyamūni tvaṃ hemaharmyāṇi vihāya kasmāt vigāhase śūnyavanāntarāṇi  KAvk kāntākarāvarjitahemakumbhasatsaurabhāmbhaḥpravarābhiṣiktaḥ ekaḥ kathaṃ snāsi vikāsipāṃśusaṃtaptatoyāsu marusthalīṣu  KAvk gaṇḍasthalāt kuṇḍalaratnakānti kiṃ lambitaṃ maṇḍanameva vetsi kasmādakasmāttava niḥsukhasya na candanaṃ nandanaminduśubhram  KAvk mahāvitāne śayane nṛpārhe śeṣe na kiṃ śeṣaviśeṣaśubhre lakṣmīnavāliṅganabhogayogyā kathaṃ tanuste sahate kuśayyām  KAvk kāntāsmitormipratimāṃśukārhaṃ kiṃ cīvarasyocitametadaṅgam pāṇau ca līlākamalāspade smin pātraṃ kathaṃ te priyamadya jātam  KAvk ayaṃ vihārastava kaṇṭhapīṭhaḥ sotkaṇṭhakāntābhujabandhanārhaḥ saṃbhogalakṣmīkṣapitapramodaḥ karotyakasmāt praṇayāvabhaṅgam  KAvk rūpaṃ vilakṣīkṛtapuṣpacāpaṃ mattebhakumbhoccakucā vibhūtiḥ ratervilāsppavanaṃ vayaśca kenāsamaste kalito virāgaḥ  KAvk śratveti taṃ śīlanidhirbadhāṣe śaśāṅkalekhālalitasmitena saṃkrāntanānānṛparatnarāgāṃ kurvannalakṣāmiva rājalakṣmīm  KAvk rājan jarārogahateva na syāttaraṅgalolā yadi jīvavṛttiḥ tatkasya na syādaniśaṃ praharṣapīyūṣavarṣī viṣayābhilāṣaḥ  KAvk śamāmṛtāsvādanasusthirāṇāmapātanaṃ śūnyavanāntabhūmeḥ vibhūtilīlāmadavihvalānāṃ harmyāṇi paryantanipātanāni  KAvk sakuṅkumaiḥ snāntiḥ nṛpāḥ payobhiḥ sarāgatāṃ yaiḥ satataṃ prayānti saṃtoṣaśīlastu manaḥ prasādaśuddhāmbudhautā vimalībhavanti  KAvk śrotraṃ śrutenaivana kuṇḍalena dānena pāṇirna tu kaṅkaṇena vibhāti kāyaḥ karuṇākulānāṃ paropakāreṇa na candanena  KAvk etāni mohāhatavallabhāni saṃsaktamuktāṃśusitasmitāni satāṃ na bhogyāni bhavanti bhūbhṛducchiṣṭaśiṣṭāni vibhūṣaṇāni  KAvk rāgāturāṇāṃ ritupāpitānāṃ nidrā dhanadhyānavatāṃ na nāma śayyāsu susparśavatīṣu rājñā sarvatra śāntaḥ sukhameva śete  KAvk nirmokakāntena varāmśukena bhujaṅgavṛttirna tu cīvareṇa pātraṃ pavitrāṇi samāplitāni pīyūṣamaitrāṇyaśanāni sūte  KAvk chatrāṇi vakrkraṃ bhṛśamaprakāśaṃ manivilolaṃ vyajanānilaughāḥ saṃsaktajāṅyaṃ hṛdayaṃ nṛpāṇāṃ kurvanti hārā haricandanārdrāḥ  KAvk viyogarogānugatā vibhūtiḥ kāntāh kṣaṇāntā viraso vilāsaḥ yasminnapāyaḥ satatānuśāyī sa kasya bhogaḥ subhagopayogaḥ  KAvk jāḍyaṃ sajṛmbhaṃ janayatyajasraṃ tanoti tṛṣṇābhramamohamūrcchāḥkarotyasahyaṃ sarasatvameva bhogopabhogaḥ prasabhaprayogaḥ  KAvk yadā sukhaśrīrnavacandralekhā prabhātapuṣpāṇyapi yaivanāṇi karmormimālāgrahaṇaṃ śarītaṃ tadā mamāyaṃ gamito nurāgaḥ  KAvk sacāmarāh sadhvajapuñjapaṭṭāḥ savājivālā dvipakarṇatālāḥ svabhāvalolāḥ kila rājalakṣmyaḥ sarve vilāsāh kṣaṇabhaṅgasaṅgāḥ  KAvk uktveti tattatkuśalāya rājñaścittaprasādaṃ paramaṃ vidhāya sa śāntikallolasudhāpravāhaṃ kiran dṛśā pārṣadamāluloke  KAvk manīṣiṇāṃ śākyakulodgatānāṃ saptāyutāni pratipādya dharmam cakre sahasrāṇi ca sapta tatra saṃprāptaparyāptaviśeṣabhāñji  KAvk śaklodanādyaiḥ kuśalopapannaiḥ gaṇe tha tattulyasahasrasaṃkhyaiḥ droṇodanādyairamṛtpdanādyaiścittaprasādaḥ sumahānavāptaḥ  KAvk kecidyayuḥ śrāvakabodhiyuktapratyekabodhau niratāśca kecit samyak tathānuttarabodhisaktāḥ pare babhūvurgaganaprasannāḥ  KAvk srotaḥ pariprāptaphalaṃ tato nye sakṛttathāgāmiphalaṃ tathānye anye pyanāgāṃiphalaṃ tadāpurarhatphalaṃ kleśavimuktimanye  KAvk ekastu tatrārjitapāpaśāpastamaḥsamūhopahitapramohaḥ māyeyamityāha hasan janānāṃ satyasthitiṃ saṃsadi devadattaḥ  KAvk nṛpaṃ tu vātsalyanilīnameva putrodayātpratyupajātadarpam maudgalyabhikṣurjinaśāsanena maharddhibhirvītamadaṃ cakāram  KAvk dṛṣṭvāpi rājā bhagavatprabhāvaṃ nātyadbhutam pauruṣameva mene abhyāsalīnāni janasya nūnaṃ sotkarṣakṛtyāni na vismayāya  KAvk athāparedyurbhagavān surendrasaṃpādite hemamahāvimāne sumeruśīrrṣṇīva samānakāntau siṃhāsane ratnamaye nyaṣīdat  KAvk brahmendramukhyeṣu tataḥ sureṣu tatropaviṣṭeṣu pṛthuprabheṣu babhustaduṣṇīṣaśikhāvilāsaiścandrāṃśumālājaṭīlā ivāśāḥ  KAvk anyonyasaṃghaṭṭavilolahārairdhanāvahāraistridaśairviśadbhiḥ nirantarām tām bhavametya rājā dvāreṣu mārgānna caturṣu lebhe  KAvk sabhrūbhramaistatra kuveramukhyairnivāryamāṇābhimatapraveśah vicchāyavakraḥ skhalitābhidhāyī bhūbhṛtparaṃ niṣpratibho babhūva  KAvk praveśitastairjinaśāsanena kadācidāsādya tadagrabhūmim śuddhodanast apraṇipatya mūrdhnā cittaprasādena puro sya tasthau  KAvk śāstā tu tasmai caturāryasatyaprabodhikāṃ dharmakathām dideśa jñānena yā viṃśatiśṛṅgamasya satkāyadṛgbhūdharamapyabḥāṅkṣīt  KAvk tataḥ sa gatvā kṛtakṛtyajanmā śuklodanaṃ prāpta bhajasva rājyam svasyāvratīttaṃ bhagavatpradiṣṭaṃ tacchāsanaṃ modayituṃ na rājyam  KAvk droṇodane rājyaparāṅbhukhe pi vairāgyayogādamṛtodane ca jagrāha śuddhodanasaṃpradiṣṭāṃ tāṃ rājalakṣmīmatha bhadrakākhyaḥ  KAvk rājārhabhogairatha pūjayitvā jinaḥ janeśaḥ śucisaṃpraṇitaiḥ nyagrodhadhāma pratipādya cāsmai śuddhodanaṃ śuddhamanoratho bhūt  KAvk droṇodanasyāpi sutau yuvānau rājājñayā preraṇayā ca mātuḥ ekastu yaḥ pravrajito niruddhaḥ paro mahānnāma gṛhī babhūva  KAvk athābhavaccetasi bhadraksya rājño viraktasya vanābhilāṣaḥ vivekabhājāṃ praśamapravṛttaṃ navāpi lakṣmīrna mano ruṇaddhi  KAvk tataḥ samāhūya sa devadattaṃ rājyābhiṣekapratipannacittam uvāca me pravrajanasya kālaḥ samāgataḥ kiṃ bhavatābhidheyam  KAvk taṃ pratyuvācāttavivekadambhaḥ susaṃvṛtaṃ saṃsadi devadattaḥ rājanna rājye sti mamābhilāṣaḥ pravrajyayā tvatsadṛśo bhavāmi  KAvk śrutveti rājā kuṭilasya tasya mithyāvinītasya kadarthavākyam udīritaṃ śākyagaṇastavāyaṃ saṃkalpasākṣīti hasannuvāca  KAvk athārthatāpopahataḥ pradadhyau bhogānurāgāditi devadattaḥ mayā kimetadavipātamuktaṃ bhajeta vā pravrajito pi rājyam  KAvk rājyaṃ samutsṛjya nijaṃ vrajantaḥ śākyaṃ kumārāḥ saha bhadrakādyāḥ śuddhodanaṃ niryayurāyavṛttaprītiṃ puraskṛtya rathairdvipaiśca  KAvk vrajatsu sarveṣvatha devadattaḥ kirīṭasaktaṃ pṛthipadmarāgam jahāra raktāktamivāmiṣārthī śyenaḥ prabhāpallavitāmbarārkam  KAvk naimittikairuktamathāsya lakṣmadṛṣṭvā tadugraṃ narakaprayāṇam cittaṃ sadoṣaṃ kila durnimittaṃ nimittamanyat punaruktameva  KAvk kokālikhaṇḍotkaṭamorakāṇāṃ tithyādināmnām madadurmadānāṃ saṃsūcitānyatyadhikāni tatra tathāvidhānairbahulakṣaṇāni  KAvk bhūpapramodādatha bhadrako pi tairdevadatapramukhaiḥ sahaiva pravrajyayā cīvarapātrayogāt cakāra vairāgyamayīmiva kṣmām  KAvk rājñastathā rājakumārakāṇāmutsṛṣṭahārāṅgadakuṇḍalānām sāsro virāgādavatārya teṣāṃ keśānupālī kila kalpako bhūt  KAvk mūrkhaḥ sa nīco pi jinājñayaiva pravrajyayā pūjyataro babhūva cittaprasādasya parasya manye na kāraṇaṃ paṇḍitatā najātiḥ  KAvk sāmīcikāyāmatha bhadrako pi jñātvā nṛpaḥ pārṣadikaṃ tamenam nīcasya pādau kathamasya vande mahīpati sanniti niścalo bhūt  KAvk tamabravīdaskhalitābhimānaṃ vikalpabhinnaṃ bhagavān vihasya pravrajyayā mohamahānuvandhī saṃtyajyate jātimayo bhimānaḥ  KAvk śrutveti rājñā saha rājaputraiḥ kṛte praṇāme pṛthivī cakampe na devadattaḥ paruṣābhidhāyī padau vavande bhagavadgirāsya  KAvk kampāt kṣitervismitamānasena pṛṣṭastato bhikṣugaṇena śāstā uvaca rājā kila kalpasya janmāntare pyasya kṛtaḥ praṇāmaḥ  KAvk purā yuvā kāśipure vilokya bhadrābhidhānām gaṇīkāṃ daridraḥ sevām vyaghāt sundarakastadāsyai rāgo hi sarvavysanopadeṣṭā  KAvk tayā visṛṣṭaḥ kusumoccayāya punahpunarbhṛṅga ivādhikārthī tatsaṅgamānaṅgamanorathena śrāntaḥ sa babhrāma vanāntareṣu  KAvk atrāntara śrāntataraḥ kṣitīśaḥ prāpto vanāntaṃ mṝgayārasena taṃ brahmadattaḥ prasamīkṣya gītaṃ tasyāśṛṇocchannatanurlatābhiḥ  KAvk navanavakusumāśayā kimevaṃ madhukaraṃ tāpahato si gaccha tūrṇam vikasitakamalānanābjinī sā bhavati hi saṃkucitā dināvasāne  KAvk tasyā hi gītaṃ nṝpatirniśamya smitaprabhāghaṭṭitahārakāntiḥ uvāca taṃ tīvrakarārkatāpaḥ ko yaṃ sakhe gītarasābhioyogah  KAvk so pyabravīdbhūmipate na nāma tapto ravistaptatarastu kāmaḥ svakarmaduḥkhāni vihanti loke na grīṣmadagdhāni marusthalāni  KAvk ityarthavadvākyaguṇārpaṇena sa bhūpatervallabhatāmavāpa saṃvādasaṃsparśasubhāṣitaṃ hi keṣām c asatkārapadaṃ na yāti  KAvk tenātha rājā vijane śramāturaḥ śītopacārairapanītatāpaḥ prītyā tamādāya tataḥ sahaiva svarājadhānīmagamat kṛtajñah  KAvk tatrāsya jīvaprada ityudantasaṃtoṣa saṃpūritacittavṛttiḥ rājyārdhadānābhimukhaḥ sa tasthau cittānuvṛttasya kimasya deyam  KAvk rājyārdhadānaprasṛte tha tasmin nācintayat sundarakaḥ kṛpāyāmbhadrāṃ vinā rājyasukhena kiṃ me dhanyo hi tatprītisudhābhiṣiktaḥ  KAvk mahmaṃ na rājyādyapi rocate rdhamakhaṇḍitālpāpi hi śobhate śrīḥ ekārthayoge hi sadā vivādaḥ dvayorhi bhogaiḥ kalireva mūrtaḥ  KAvk tasmānnṛpaṃ kuṇṭhamahaṃ nipātya samastarājyena bhavāmi pūrṇaḥ kṣaṇaṃ vicintyetyanutāpataptaḥ tīvraṃ manaḥ svasya punaḥ pradadhyau  KAvk kiṃ cintitaṃ nindyaparaṃ mayaitat ko yaṃ prakāraḥ khalu tīkṣṇatāyāḥ kṛtaghnasaṃkalpakalaṅkalepādaho nu lajjā nijacetaso pi  KAvk svastyastu rājyāya namaḥ sukhebhyaḥ saṃmohamātā kṣamatāṃ ca lakṣmīḥ yeṣāmanāsvāditacintitānāmevaṃvidhā dhīḥ prathamaḥ svabhāvaḥ  KAvk bhramaṃ vidhatte vidadhāti mūrcchāṃ nipātayatyeva tamastanoti āghrātamātraiva karoti puṃsāmaho vināśaṃ viṣavallarī śrīḥ  KAvk ciraṃ vicintyeti sa jātacittaḥ pratyekabodhirvimalaḥ prabhāte abhyarthamāno pi nareśvareṇa rājyaṃ n ajagrāha nivṛttatṛṣṇaḥ  KAvk pratyekabuddhatvamavāptamenaṃ kālena dṛṣṭvā nṛpatirmaharddhiḥ tatpādapadmacyutamaulimālyaścittaprasādocitamityavecat  KAvk sa ko pi satkarmavipākajanmā vandyo vivekaḥ praśamābhiṣekaḥ yasya prabhāvādvirataspṛhāṇāṃ tyājyeva ratnākaramekhalā bhūḥ  KAvk śrutveti rājñā kathitaṃ tadarthajātaṃ tadabhyarthanayā vidhāya tatkalpakaḥ śāntipadaṃ prapede sevāntaraṅgaḥ kila gaṅgapālaḥ  KAvk prāptaṃ tamayuttamakarmayogāt pravrajyayā sajjanapūjyabhāvam rājā vavande praṇataḥ pṛthivyāḥ kampastadābhūdapi ṣaḍvikāraḥ  KAvk so yaṃ rājā vihitavinatirbhadrako brahmadattopaśyopālī sa kila kuśalī kalpako gaṅgapālaḥ ityāścaryaṃ bhagavaduditaṃ bhikṣavaste niśamyasvacchaṃ cittaṃ sukṝtaśaraṇe menire hetumeva  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ pitāputrasamādānam nāma dvāviṃśatitamaḥ pallavaḥ  viśvaṃtarāvadānam cintārantādadhkarucayaḥ sarvalokeṣvanindyāvandyāste nyaiḥ puruṣamaṇayaḥ ke pyapūrvaprabhāvāḥ yeṣāṃ naiva priyamapi paraṃ putradārādi datvāsattvārthānām bhavati vadanamlānatā dainyadūtī  KAvk bhagavān bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ purā śākyapure jinaḥ jagāda pūrvavṛttāntaṃ devadattakathāntare  KAvk purī babhūva viśvākhyā viśvāsavasatiḥ śriyaḥ viśvopakārasaktasyasukṝtasyeva janmabhūḥ  KAvk saṃjayākhyo bhavat tasyāmamitratimirāṃśumān netrānandasudhāsūtirvicitracarito nṛpaḥ  KAvk tasya viśvaṃtaro nāma vadānyastanayo bhavat apūrvatyāginā yena hṛtaṃ kalpatayoryaśaḥ  KAvk īrṣyāvirahitāstulyaṃ vidagdhena prsādhitāḥ satyena bhāratī yena dānena śrīḥ śrutena dhīḥ  KAvk adyāpi yasya dikkāntākarṇābharaṇatām gatam vibhāti ketakīgarbhapalāśaviśadaṃ yaśah  KAvk sa kadāciddadau divyaratnālakāramarthine athaṃ vijayasāmrājyamanorathaharaṃ tviṣā  KAvk datte rathavare tasmin vismayenākhilo janaḥ babhūvākrāṇtahṛdayaścintayā ca nareśvaraḥ  KAvk mahāmātyānathāhūya harṣahīno mahīpatiḥ uvācopacitodvegacintākrāntamanorathah  KAvk datto rathaḥ kumāreṇa sa jaitraḥ śatrumardanaḥ yatprabhāvārjitā seyaṃ mahārathavarūthinī  KAvk lakṣmī sukhaniṣaṇṇā me yātā niścalatām tayā rathe sauryapathe tasmin jayakuznje ca kuñjare  KAvk iti rājavacaḥ śrutvā tamabhāṣanta mantriṇaḥ rājan doṣastavaivāyaṃ vātsalyena pramādyataḥ  KAvk dharmaḥ kasya na harṣāya dānaṃ kasya na saṃmatam kiṃ tu mūlahatādvṛkṣānnivartante palārthinaḥ  KAvk vikrītaḥ paradeśe ca rathastena dvijanmanā ityuktvā mantriṇaḥ sarve śalyaviddhā ivābhavan  KAvk atha kālena saṃprāpte vasante madanotsave vipāke sukṛtasyeva hṛdayānandadāyini  KAvk svayaṃgrahopajīvyasya madhormadhukarārthinaḥ lokaḥ puṣpavanairyāto yaśobhiriva śubhratām  KAvk aśokaṃ lokasacchāyamupakārodyataṃ drumam madhu vidhūtaṃ saṃnaddhe kalikālaṃ kṛtaṃ jagat  KAvk rājaputraḥ samāruhya kuñjaraṃ rājavardhanam yayau phullān vane druṣṭumarthikalpatarustarūn  KAvk vrajantaṃ prati sāmantaprayuktātaṃ dvijāḥ pathiḥ babhāṣire samabhyetya svastivādapuraḥsarāḥ  KAvk cintāmaṇirgīyase tvaṃ ślāghyo jagati jaṅgamaḥ yasya saṃdarśanenārthī gāḍhamāliṅgyate śriyā  KAvk dvāveva viśrutotkarṣavideṣau bhadrajanmani dānārdrahastastvaṃ loke gajaścāyaṃ sthironnatiḥ  KAvk asmabhyaṃ sukṛtpdāra kuñjaro yaṃ pradīyatām tvadanyena vadānyena dātumeṣa na śakyate  KAvk ityarthitastaiḥ sotsāhaḥ sa tebhyastu dadau dvipam sajīvamiva sāmrājyaṃ saśaṅkhadhvajacāmaram  KAvk datvā bodhipradhānena praṇidhānena śuddhadhīḥ ratharatnaṃ dvipendraṃ ca so bhūdānandanirbharaḥ  KAvk śrutvaiva nṛpatirdattaṃ viśrutaṃ jayakuznjaram rakṣāprakārarahitāṃ rājalakṣmīmamanyata  KAvk sa rājyabhraṃśabhītena kupitena mahībhujā niṣkāsitaḥ kumāro tha pratasthe praṇipatya tam  KAvk mādrīdayitayā sārdhaṃ jālinaṃ nāma dārakam kṛṣṇābhidhāṃ tathā kanyāmādāya sa yayau vanam  KAvk vane pi śeṣa ṃ sa dadau vāhanādikamarthine samaṃ hi mahatāṃ sattvaṃ saṃpatsu ca vipatsu ca  KAvk mādyrāṃ kadācidyātāyāṃ puṣpamūlaphalāptaye brāhmaṇaḥkaścidabhyetya rājaputramabhāṣata  KAvk paricārakāhīnāya caturau bālakāvimau dehi mahyaṃ mahāsattvaṃ sarvado hyasi viśrutaḥ  KAvk śrutvaitadavicāryaiva dārakau dayitau param datvā sa tasmai sahasā sehe tadvirahavyathām  KAvk dhanaputrakalatrādi loke kasya navallabham dānādanyadvadānyānāṃ na dayāvatām  KAvk atha mādrī samabhyetya bālakau bālavatsalā apaśyantī puraḥ patyuḥ patitāpannamūrcchitā  KAvk sā labdhasaṃjñā dīptena vyāptā śokakṛśānunā śiśupradānavṛttāntaṃ śrutvaivābhūtpalāpinī  KAvk tasyāścetasi duḥkhāgnirapatyasnehaduḥsahaḥ priyapremānusṛtyaiva prayayau puṭapākatām  KAvk atrāṇtare samabhyetya viprarūpaḥ sureśvaraḥ bhṛtyārthī dayitām patnīṃ rājaputramayācata  KAvk yācitastena sahasā śucaṃ jāyāviyogajām dhiyā saṃstabhya sattvābdhiḥ sa tasmai vitatāra tām  KAvk sadyaḥ pradānataralāṃ saṃtrastāṃ hariṇīmiva so vadaddayitāmantaḥ kalayan bodhivāsanām  KAvk samāśvāsihi kalyāṇi na śokaṃ kartukarhasi svapnapraṇayakalpo yamasatyaḥ priyasaṃgamaḥ  KAvk śuśrūṣayā dvijasyāsya dharme te ramatām matiḥ vilolalokayātrāyāṃ dharmaḥ sthirasuhṛt satām  KAvk dṛṣṭvā sarve svajanasujanā bāndhavāścānubhūtāḥnyastā kaṇṭhe kṣaṇaparimalamlāyinī mitrālā dāre putre kṣapitamaniśaṃ yauvanaṃ jīvitaṃ caprāpto nāptaśtiraparicayaḥ ko pi dharmādṛte nyaḥ  KAvk ityuktvā vallabhāṃ lobhaparityāgāduvāha saḥ dyutiṃ vadanapadmena dhairyavṛttiṃ ca cetasā  KAvk viyogaśokavikalāṃ mādrīṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛpākulaḥ nijarūpaṃ samādhāya śacīpatiruvāc atām  KAvk viṣādaṃ mā kṛthāh putri devo haṃ tridaśeśvaraḥ arthibhyastvā dadātyeṣa tasmādasi mayarthitā  KAvk adhunā saiva patyustvaṃ nyāsībhūtā mayārpitā taṃ dadātyeṣa nānyasmau dīyate katham  KAvk kariṣyāmi tavāvaśyaṃ dārakābhyāṃ samāgamam ityudīrya sahasrākṣaḥ sahasāṇtaradhīyataḥ  KAvk atha tau dārakau vipraḥ samādāyārthalipsayā viśvāmitrapuraṃ gatvā lobhādvokretumudyatah  KAvk viśyāmitraḥ parijñāya rājaputrasya dārakau jagrāha mahatārthena bāṣpasaṃruddhalocanaḥ  KAvk kālena tridivaṃ yāte viśvāmitramahīpatau bheje viśvaṃtaro rājyaṃ paurāmātyagaṇārthitaḥ  KAvk rājye viraktasya tasya dānavyasaninaḥ param sattvena vardhamānarddhirna kaścid yācako bhavat  KAvk tadvittapūrṇavibhavo brāhmaṇaḥ so pi jambukah kṛtaghnaḥ svaprabhāvānme saṃpadityabhyadhājjanam  KAvk viśvaṃtaraḥ sa evāham devadattaḥ sa ca dvijaḥ uktveti cakre bhagavān bhikṣūṇāṃ dānadeśanām  KAvk ālambanaṃ śvabhraśatāvapāte ghorāndhakāre suciraprakāśaḥ āśvāsanaṃ duḥsahaduḥkhakāle dānam narāṇāṃ paralokabandhuḥ  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ viśvaṃtarāvadānam nām atrayoviṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  abhiniṣkramaṇāvadānam hasati sakalalolālokasargāya bhānuḥ paramamamṛtavṛṣṭayai pūrṇatāmeti candraḥ iyati jagati pūjyaṃ janma gṛhṇāti kaścit vipulakuśalasetuḥ sattvasaṃtāraṇāya  KAvk purā śuddhodanaḥ śrīmān rājā śākyapure bhavat yaśaḥśaśāṅkajanakaḥ sudhāsindhurivāparaḥ  KAvk khalāsaktā svabhāvena lakṣmīrguṇigaṇārpitā āścaryakāriṇā yena kṛtā satpakṣapātinī  KAvk adyāpyakhiladiktīryavanāsaktairvivekibhiḥ yaśobhiḥ śucibhiryasya munivratamivohyate  KAvk syāmahaṃ śuddhamāteti purā praṇidhitaḥ kila viśvakarmasuto martyamājagāmāmaladyutiḥ  KAvk kīrtiḥ satpuruṣasyeva tasyābhūdvallabhā param mahāmāyābhidhā devī candrasyeva kumudvatī  KAvk sāpaśyaddantinaṃ śvetaṃ svapne kukṣau vihāyasā gatamārohaṇaṃ śaile praṇatiṃ ca mahājanāt  KAvk atrāntare bodhisattvastuṣitāt tridaśālayāt garbhaṃ tasyāḥ samāpede svayaṃ lokānukalpayā  KAvk vahantī bodhisattvaṃ sā garbhe bhuvananandanam induṃ dugdhābdhiveleva babhūva pāṇḍuradyutiḥ  KAvk ikṣvākurājavaṃśyena tena garbhasthitena sā bhūrnidhānavatīvābhūd bhavyalakṣaṇalakṣitā  KAvk babhūva dohadastasyā dānapuṇyamayodayaḥ aṅkure pyavisaṃvādi sahakārasya saurabham  KAvk atgha kālena saṃpūrṇaṃ sā lumbinīvane sthitā asūta tanayaṃ devī divākaramivāditiḥ  KAvk māturgarbhamalāspṛṣṭaṃ kukṣiṃ bhittvā sa nirgataḥ tāṃ cakre tha svabhāvena svasthāṅgī vigatavyathām  KAvk nirgacchanneva ruddho sau balajijñāsayā kṣaṇam śakreṇa vajrasārāṅgastasyāśakyatvamāyayau  KAvk jātamātaḥ śuiśurgatvā svayaṃ sapta padāni saḥ diśo vilokayannūce suvyaktākṣarayā girā  KAvk iyaṃ nirvṛtiḥ pūrvā ca gatirlokeṣu dakṣiṇā paścimā jātirapyeṣā saṃsārādiyamuttarā  KAvk iti tasya bruvāṇasya pṛthivī samakampata tamakṣayabalaṃ dhartumaśakteva jagadgurum  KAvk chatraṃ tasya yaśaḥ śubhraṃ sattvasmeraṃ sacāmaram vyomāmbudhārādhautasya jagṛhustasya devatā  KAvk asminnavasare pṛṣṭaḥ s vastrīyeṇāsitābhidhaḥ nāradena prabhāṃ dṛṣṭvā kiṣkindhādristhito muniḥ  KAvk kasmādarkaśatāloka ivālokaḥ pradṛśyate tamodaridrāṃ yeneti girayaḥ saguhāgṛhāḥ  KAvk vismayāditi tenoktaḥ so vadaddivyalocanaḥ jātaḥ puṇyaprabhāso yaṃ bodhisattvasya janmani  KAvk acireṇaiva taṃ vatsa drakṣāvaḥ kuśalāptaye ityuktvā munirānandād viśrāntisukhito bhavat  KAvk putrajanmani sarvārthasiddhiṃ śuddhodanaḥ param dṛṣṭvā sarvārthasiddho yamiti nāmāsya nirmame  KAvk śākyavardhananāmābhūd yakṣaḥ śākyapurāśrayaḥ yatpraṇāmeṇa śākyānāṃ śiśavo nirupadravāḥ  KAvk tatsthityā preṣitaḥ pitrā praṇāmāya saguhyakaḥ taṃ bodhisattvamālokya nipapātāsya pādayoḥ  KAvk athotsaṅge samādāya hṛṣṭastaṃ pṛthivīpatiḥ lakṣaṇāni nimittajñaistasya dehe vyalokayat  KAvk lakṣaṇajñāstataḥ sarve nṛpamūcuḥ savismayāḥ deva divyakumāro yaṃ lakṣaṇairupalakṣyate  KAvk jāyate lakṣaṇairetairviśvaviśrāntaśāsanaḥ śakrādhipaścakravartī bhagavān sa tathāgataḥ  KAvk dīrghāṅgulidalau cakralāñchanau supratiṣṭhitau aruṇau caraṇāvasya kāntau kamalakomalau  KAvk rājahaṃsa iva prāṃśuḥ sajālāṅgulipallavaḥ eṣa jānuyugaḥ śrīmānājānubhujabhūṣitaḥ  KAvk sakośabastiguhyaśca nyagrodhaparimaṇḍalaḥ dakṣiṇāvartaromāṅkaḥ pariṇāhasamonnatiḥ  KAvk rajomalalavāspṛṣṭastajāmbūnadadyutiḥ hastapādāṃsakaṇṭhāgraspaṣṭasaptacchadākṛtiḥ  KAvk siṃhapūrvārdhakāyaśca bṛhatspaṣṭāṅgavigrahaḥ catvāriṃśatsamāprotaśukladantaḥ sunāsikaḥ  KAvk dīrghapratanujihvaśca meghadundubhiniśvanaḥ abhinīlākṣagokṣmaḥ sahajoṣṇīṣamastakaḥ  KAvk sitorṇāṅko bhruvorbhāgaḥ svastikoraḥsthalojjvalaḥ lekhāśṛṅgābjahasto yaṃ chatrākāraśirāḥ śiśuḥ  KAvk rājannayam te tanayaścakravartī bhaviṣyati samyaksaṃbodhisaṃbuddhaḥ sarvajño vā bhaviṣyati  KAvk ityuktvā teṣu jāteṣu lebhe harṣaṃ mahīpatiḥ saptabhidivasaiḥ śāsturjananī tridivaṃ yayau  KAvk tasya janmani śākyānāṃ munīnāmiva śāntatā dṛṣṭvā yadā śākyamunirnāmābhūtsa tadā śiśuḥ  KAvk devānāmapi devo yamiti niścitya tejasā devātideva ityasya nāma cakre mahīpatiḥ  KAvk nāradenātha sahitastattvadarśī tapovanāt taṃ samabhyāyayau draṣṭumādarādasito muniḥ  KAvk sa bodhisattvaṃ bālārkamiva kalpaprakāśanam dṛṣṭvā vikāsivakrkraśrīrlebhe kamalatulyatām  KAvk so brāvīdvihitātithyaṃ nṛpatiṃ praṇataṃ muniḥ rājan guṇagaṇeneva spṛhaṇīyo si sūnunā  KAvk etāni lakṣaṇānyasya mokṣalakṣmīsamāgamam vadanti cakravartiśrīḥphalaṃ naiṣāṃ vinaśvaram  KAvk asya bodhiprabhāveṇa saṃbuddhasy mukhāmbujam dhanya padmākarasyeva netrapātraṃ kariṣyati  KAvk vibudhāḥ śuddhasattvasya bodhidugdhamahodadheḥ dhanyā vāgamṛtairasya bhaviṣyantyupajīvinaḥ  KAvk puṇyabhāji jagatyasminneka evāsmi vañcitaḥ etatsaṃdarśanaṃ yasya pūrṇakālasya durlabham  KAvk ityuktvā nṛpamāmantrya gatvā vyomnā tapovanam suprasannaṃ manaḥ kṛtvā dehatyāgamacintayat  KAvk sa paryantopadeśāya nāradenābhicoditaḥ tamuvācāmṛtaṃ vatsaṃ kumāraḥ kathayiṣyati  KAvk adhigamyāmṛtaṃ tasmānnṛpasūnoranāmayam tariṣyasi bhavāmbodhimityuktvā tanumatyajat  KAvk śrīrasatkriyāṃ tasya kṛtvā sapadi nāradaḥ yayau vārāṇasīṃ siddhyai lebhe kātyāyanābhidhām  KAvk vardhamānaḥ kumāro tha sarvavidyāsu pāragaḥ lipipravīṇo bhinavām lipiṃ brāhmīṃ vinirmame  KAvk nāgāyutasamaprāṇe tasmin jagati viśrute vaiśālikaiḥ priyāyāsmai preṣito mattakuñjaraḥ  KAvk bhaviṣyati cakravartītyasya prātamupāyanam devadattaḥ paridveṣāt taṃ jaghāna mahāgajam  KAvk cyutaṃ cakarṣaṃ dvidataṃ nandaḥ sapta padāni tam kumārastu tadutkṣipya prākārād bahirakṣipat  KAvk ekanārāvanirbhinnasaptatālamahītalaḥ chedyabhedyāstraśastreṣu sa evātiśayaṃ yayau  KAvk tatatulyaguṇāṃ patnīṃ rājasūnuryaśodharām avāpa viśrutāṃ loke śuddhaśīla ivonnatim  KAvk atrāntare mahāvātavicyutaḥ saptayojanaḥ saritpravāhasaṃrodhaṃ vidadhe vipuladrumaḥ  KAvk sāṃ sphāratarusaṃruddhā rohikā nāma nimnagā śīlabhraṣṭeva vanitā prayayau pratilomatām  KAvk rājaputrastamutkṣipya bhaṅktvā vikṣupya taṃ drumam nyavārayat prajāmatsyajalakallolaviplavam  KAvk tataḥ kadācidudyāne haṃsaṃ niśitayantriṇā devadattena nihataṃ kumāraḥ samajīvayat  KAvk saṃtāpaṃ tadvivādena devadatto dhikaṃ yayau na sahante hi kuṭilāstulyakulagoṇonnatim  KAvk kadācid gopikā nāma kumāraṃ rājakanyakā kandarparūpamālokya kimapyautsukyamāyayau  KAvk śuddhodanaḥ sutasthaitāṃ jñātvā cittocitāṃ vadhūm apūrayadvivāhena manmathasya manoratham  KAvk naimittikāstato bhyetya nṛpamūcuḥ suniścayāḥ putraste cakravartī vā munirvā saptame hani  KAvk tacchrutvā nṛpatiḥ sūnoścakrāvrtipadāptaye pravrajyācakitaścintāṃ dinasaṃkhyāmayīṃ yayau  KAvk lolāṃ sarvaḥ srhiyaṃ vetti śāntasthirasukhāmapi atthāpi bhogaraktānāṃ saṃpatsvevādaraḥ param  KAvk tataḥ kadācidudyānavihārāya nṛpātmajaḥ prayayau rathamāruhya valgutuṅgaturaṅgamam  KAvk sa vivarṇaṃ jarājīrṇam kīrṇaśīrṇaśiroruham suśuṣkaparuṣākāraṃ dadarśa puruṣaṃ pathi  KAvk sa taṃ dṛṣṭvā nijaṃ kāyamālokyācintayacciram aho paryāptapāko yaṃ kāyasyāsya jugupsitaḥ  KAvk vayaḥ paryāptamāpto pi paryāptaṃ nāśrayatyayam atīva palitavyājājjarā vṛddhaṃ hasatyasau  KAvk śarīre saṃtatasnāyupāśaprotāsthipañjare vṛddhaḥ puṣṇāti manye hamaho mohavihaṅgamam  KAvk sārathe kiṃ karotyeṣa kiṃ na yāti tapovanam asṃkocameti vṛddhasya dehena saha sā matiḥ  KAvk vṛddho valambate yaṣṭiṃ na tu dharmamayīṃ dhiyam jarākuṭilakāyasya svabhāvo nirvivekatā  KAvk jugupsāṃ janayatyeṣa vṛddhaḥ praskhalitākṣaraiḥ vacobhiścyutadantābhairgalallālālavākulaiḥ  KAvk naṣṭā dṛṣṭiḥ kṛśaḥ kāyaḥ śaktirluptā hatā śrutiḥ tathāpi mohād dṛṣṭaiva vṛddhasya taruṇīpriyā  KAvk dhatte dhavalatāṃ vṛddhaḥ kimetāmatigarhitām lolā paraṃ viraktāpi yadyasyātipriyā tanuḥ  KAvk iti cintayatastasya nirvedaḥ samajāyata manyamānasya sāpāyaṃ kāyaṃ nicayamāpadām  KAvk punaśca samaye nyasminnapaśyad vyādhitaṃ naram vipakkakūṇapaprāyaṃ sapūyamiva pāṇḍaram  KAvk sa pradadhyau tamālokya samuddiśya nijāṃ tanum aho nu sahajaivāsmin kāye rogagaṇodgatiḥ  KAvk idameva mahaccitramiyaṃ māṃsamayī tanuḥ na yāti kledavaiklavyaṃ kṣaṇaṃ paryuṣīte pi yat  KAvk iti dhyātvā sa sodvegaḥ śarīravicikitsayā babhūva rājyasaṃbhopgarāge vigatitādaraḥ  KAvk athānyasmin kṣaṇe mālyavastrācchāditavigraham dadarśa dehasatkāravyagrabandhujanaṃ śavam  KAvk taṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasodvegadayāduḥkhaghṛṇākulaḥ ciraṃ niḥsārasaṃsāraparihāramacintayat  KAvk eṣa pretavanaṃ yāti saṃsaktāṃ hṛdaye vahan  KAvk aho nu viṣayābhyāsavilāsādhyavasāyinām nṛṇāmantyakṣaṇe kaṣṭā kāṣṭhapāṣāṇatulyatā  KAvk udvegavāribhavasāgarabudbude smin kālānilākulitakarmalatāgrapuṣpe māyāvadhūnayanavibhramasaṃvibhāge puṃsāṃ ka eṣa vapuṣi sthiratābhimānaḥ  KAvk noktaṃ kiṃcit parahitayutaṃ na śrutaṃ dharmayuktaṃnaiva ghrātaṃ kuśalakusumaṃ satyarūpaṃ na dṛṣṭam naiva spṛṣṭaṃ śamapadamiti vyaktamāsaktacintāviśrānto yaṃ vahati sahasā niścalatvaṃ gatāyuḥ  KAvk rājasūnurvicintyeti śarīraṃ vipadāplutam aśeṣaviṣayāsaṅge parām naḥ snehatām yayau  KAvk athāgre nirmitaṃ devaiḥ sa śuddhāvāsakāyikaiḥ vyalokayat pravrajitaṃ pātrakāṣāyadhāriṇam  KAvk taṃ dṛṣṭvaiva babhūvāsya pravrajyābhimukhī matiḥ īpsitālokanaprītyā svabhāvo hi vibhāvyate  KAvk virāgyakāraṇam tatra nṛpasūnoḥ pade pade vilokya sārathiḥ sarvaṃ kṣitipāya vyanedayat  KAvk kumāro tha piturvākyāt grāmālokanakautukī vrajan pathi nidhānāni vivṛtāni vyalokayat  KAvk tatpūrvapuruṣanyastaiḥ strīkarairutthitānyapi yadā sa nāgrahīttāni tadā viviśurambudhim  KAvk tataḥ sa karṣakān pāṃśuvyāptapāṇḍuśiroruhān vidīrṇapāṇicaraṇān kṣutpipāsāśramāturān  KAvk halakaddālaviṣamollekhapakṣavraṇāditān vilokya kleśavivaśān babhūva karuṇākulaḥ  KAvk vidhāya dayayā teṣāṃ draviṇauradaridratām sa vṛṣāṇāṃ vṛṣarataḥ kleśamuktimakārayat  KAvk tataḥ pratinivṛtto tha sānujaḥ pārthivātmajaḥ madhyāhnapṛthusaṃtāpe taralastaraṇitviṣaḥ  KAvk rathaghoṣonmukhaśikhiśyāmīkṛtadigantaraḥ svedavārikaṇākīrṇaḥ prabhāsnigdhavanasthalīm  KAvk so varuhya rathāttatra gaṇḍaskhalitakuṇḍalah viśrāṇtyai viśrutayaśā jambucchāyāmaśiśriyat  KAvk sa babhārorasi vyaktāṃ svedāmbukaṇasaṃtatim vapurāśleṣalalitāṃ hārasyeva kuṭumbinīm  KAvk chāyāsu parivṛttāsu śanakaiḥ sarvaśākhinām tasya jambūtarucchāyā na cacāla tanustanoḥ  KAvk sā tasya śītalacchāyā tāpaklāntimavārayat saṃsāraviratasyeva tīvravairāgyavāsanā  KAvk putradarśanasotkaṇṭhastaṃ deśamatha bhūpatiḥ ājagāma gajotsarpatrastabhramaracāmaraḥ  KAvk chāyāṃ sa niścalāṃ dṛṣṭvā kumārasya prabhāvataḥ gauravādbhutasaṃprāptaḥ praṇataṃ praṇanāma tam  KAvk tataḥ sa sahitaḥ pitrā nagaraṃ gantumudyataḥ apaśyat puraparyante śmaśānaṃ śavasaṃkulam  KAvk sa dṛṣṭvā kuṇapākīrṇamaśivaṃ śivakānanam sodvegaṃ sārathiṃ prāha sthagitasyandanaḥ kṣaṇam  KAvk sārathe paśya jantūnāṃ kāyāpāyamatīṃ daśām dṛṣṭvedamapi rāgārdraṃ mano mohapramādinām  KAvk parastrīdarśanāttṛptaṃ netramāsvādya sādaram asyāsatyavatī jihvā paśya kākena kṛsyate  KAvk asyāḥ stanamukhanyastanakhollekhasukhasthitiḥ khṇḍayatyadharaṃ gṝdhraḥ kāmīva madanirbharah  KAvk ete dṛṣṭaniṣakṭavāyasaśakṛnniṣṭhivinaḥ pādapāmūrcchantīva vipākapūyakuṇapāghrāṇena niṣkūṇitāḥ dṛṣṭvā gṛdhravidāryamāṇamasakṛt kīrṇārdratantra śavaṃbhūyo vātavilolapallavakarairācchādayantīva ca  KAvk kṣībasyevācalasya drutahṛtahṛdayā jambukī kaṇṭhasaktāraktābhivyaktakāmā kamapi nakhamukhollekhamāsutrayantī āsvādyāsvādya yūnaḥ kṣaṇamadharadalaṃ dattadantavraṇāṅkaṃ lagnānaṅgakriyāyāmiyamatirabhasotkarṣamāviṣkaroti  KAvk ityuktvā jātaviratirbhavabībhatsakutsayā kalayan kleśanirvāṇaṃ praviveśa purāntaram  KAvk tatra harmyagatāpaśyat taṃ kanyābhijanojjvalā mṛgajā nāma mṛgajānodinī mṛgalocanā  KAvk sarāgataralā dṛṣṭḥ śrotrasaṃcāriṇī param abhūttaddarśane tasyāḥ sahasaiva virekiṇī  KAvk sā tadālokanenaiva bālā lajjāsahiṣṇūnā smareṇeva samākṛṣṭā sakhīṃ prāha puraḥsthitām  KAvk kā dhanyā lalanā loke sparśenāsya śaśitviṣaḥ yasyā madanasaṃtaptā tanurnirvāṇameṣyati  KAvk nirvāṇaśabdaṃ śrutvaiva rājaputraḥ samīhitam tāṃ dadarśonmukhaḥ padmavanānīva diśan dṛśā  KAvk sa tasyāstena vacasā vapuṣā va prasāditaḥ hāraṃ suvṛttaṃ cittaṃ ca vikṣepāsyai guṇojjcalam  KAvk ālokanānukūlyena bhāvaṃ vijñāya bhūpatiḥ putrasyāntaḥpurapade tāmādāya nyaveśayat  KAvk ṣaṇṇāṃ kāṇtāsahasrāṇāṃ vṛtamantaḥpuraṃ tataḥ viveśa rājatanayaḥ priyāṃ śāntiṃ vicintayan  KAvk atrāṇtare narapatiṃ prāhurnaimittikāḥ sphuṭam munirvā cakravartī vā prātaste bahvitā sutaḥ  KAvk tataḥ saṃcintya nṛpatiḥ pravrajyām cakitaḥ param akārayat puradvāraguptiṃ ruddhagamāgamām  KAvk droṇodanamukhān bhrātṝn dvāreṣu viniveśya saḥ nagarasya svayaṃ makhye tathā sāmātyasainikaḥ  KAvk rājaputrādatha prāptagarbhā devī yaśodharā vabhāṣe śāradīva dyauḥ pratyāsannendupāṇḍurā  KAvk ekarātrāvaśeṣe tha nagaradvārarakṣaṇe śamapravṛttārkamabhūt pravrajyābhimukhaṃ dinam  KAvk ciraṃ vicarya saṃsāraṃ śāntiṃ yāte divaspatau kāṣāyāmbaramālambya yayau saṃdhyāvadṛśyatām  KAvk aśeṣāśātamomohavirāmavimalāṃ śanaiḥ indurgāmuditaścakre pūrṇālokavilokinīm  KAvk sarāgatāpe vabhasaścetasīva gate ravau śuddhenduhṛdayasyābhūt prasādaḥ ko pyaviplavaḥ  KAvk athāsminnantare kāntāsaṃtatāntaḥpurodare ratnaharmyapraviṣṭendudyutisaṃdohahāsini  KAvk niḥsāravirasaṃ sarvaṃ rājasūnurvilokayan jagāa gaganasvacchasvacchandocchalitasmṛtiḥ  KAvk gaṇo yaṃ nārīṇāṃ madanadahanolkāparikaraḥparityājyastīvravyasanaśatasaṃtāpasacivaḥ idānīṃ yuktā me tarutalalatāśītalareparityaktāgārapraśamasukhasāre pariṇatiḥ  KAvk etāścandradyutimadamayā yāmi nāryo vane sminnidrāmudrāniyamitadṛśaḥ saṃstarasrastavatrāḥ svapnotpannānucitavacanāḥ keśasaṃchāditāṃsāḥkṣipraṃ mandānilavicalitān lajjayantīva dīpān  KAvk saralasrastagātrāṇāṃ nirlajjānāṃ vivāsasām suptānāṃ ca mṛtānāṃ ca bhedaḥ ko nāma dehinām  KAvk iti tasya bruvāṇasya saṃjāte gamanodyame mithaḥ kathā samabhavannagaradvārarakṣiṇām  KAvk bho bhoḥ kaḥ ko tra jāgarti jāgrato nāsti viplavaḥ prabhucittagrahavyagrāḥ samagrā eva jāgrati  KAvk jāgarti saṃsāragṛhe manīṣī mohāṇdhakāre svapiti pramattaḥ jjīvitameva loke mṛtasya suptasya ca ko viśeṣaḥ  KAvk iti marhyasthitaḥ śrutvā rātrau rājasutaḥ kathāḥ prasthitaṃ satpatheneva nijaṃ mene manoratham  KAvk nivṝtterlakṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā sa svapnaṃ kṣaṇanidrayā  KAvk tataḥ prabuddhā sahasā trastā devī yaśodharā tatkālopanataṃ svapnaṃ dayitāya nyavedayat  KAvk paryaṅkābharaṇāngāni svapne bhagnāni me vibho śrīrvrajantī mayā dṛṣṭvā candrārkau ca torihitau  KAvk ityākarṇya sa tāmūce mugdhe satyavivarjitaḥ saṃsāra eva svapno yaṃ svapne svapno pi kīdṛśaḥ  KAvk svapne dya nābhisaṃjātā latā vyāptā vihārasā merūpadhānaśirasā pūrvapaścimavāridhau  KAvk bhujābhyāṃ caraṇābhyām ca dakṣiṇābdhirmayā dhṛtaḥ bhadre svapnaḥ śubho yaṃ te strīṇāṃ bhartuśubhaṃ śubham  KAvk ityukte bodhisattvena noce kiṃcid yaśodharā punaśca nidrābhimukhī babhūva mīlitekṣaṇā  KAvk śakrabrahmamukhāḥ sarve sametyātha sudhābhujaḥ cakrire bodhisattvasya sattvotsāhaprapūraṇam  KAvk tairdevaputrāścatvāraḥ samādiṣṭā mahājavāḥ sahāyā gamane tasya bhūśailābdhidhṛtikṣamāḥ  KAvk śakrādiṣṭena yakṣeṇa pāñcikākhyena nirmitaiḥ saharmyāsaktasopānairavatīrya viniryayau  KAvk suptaṃ sārathimādāya chandakākhyaṃ prabodhya saḥ utsādamiva jagrāha kaṇṭhakākhyaṃ turaṅgamam  KAvk taṃ tīkṣṇaruciraṃ lakṣmīkaṭākṣataralaṃ harim sa cakre saṃyamālīnaṃ mūrdhi saṃspṛśya pāṇinā  KAvk śamodyame sumanasā s ako pyantarbahiḥ samah śiśavo pi vimuñcanti yatprabhāveṇa cāpalam  KAvk balajijñāsayā nyastaṃ tenātha caraṇaṃ kṣitau na te kampayituṃ śekurdevaputrāḥ savismayāḥ  KAvk chandakena sahāruhya nistaraṅgaṃ turaṅgamam sa jagāhe mahadvyoma vimalaṃ svamivāśayam  KAvk prayayau taralāvartinartitoṣṇīṣapallavaḥ saṃsarpipavanollasaiḥ śokocchvāsa iva śriyaḥ  KAvk tasyābharaṇaratnāṃśulekhābhiḥ śabalaṃ nabhaḥ jagrāha sūtrapatrālīvicitramjiva cīvaram  KAvk kīrṇāśrubindukalitā vilolanayanotpalāḥ vrajantaṃ dadṛśurdṛśyāstamantaḥpuradevatāḥ  KAvk saṃsāramiva vistīrṇaṃ puraṃ sanṛpabāndhavam dūrāt pradakṣiṇīkṛtya kṣamyatāmityabhāṣata  KAvk kṣapāyāṃ kṣaṇaśeṣāyām jane nidrābhimudrite taṃ dadarśa mahānnāma prabuddho rājabāndhavaḥ  KAvk divi dṛṣṭvā vrajantaṃ taṃ śaśāṅkaśaṅkayā hṛtaḥ ūce ciraṃ vicāryoccairbāṣyāzncitavilocanah  KAvk citrametad viraktavtaṃ bandhujīvopamasya te kumāra rucirākāra na yuktaṃ yuktakāraṇam  KAvk vaṃśotkarṣaviśeṣārthū nibaddhāśaḥ pitā tvayi kasmānnirāśa kriyate sarvāśābharaṇa tvayā  KAvk iti śākyasya mahataḥ śrutvā vākyaṃ nṛpātmajaḥ tamūce bāndhavaprītirbandho vandhanaśṛṅkhalā  KAvk ayaṃ kāyaḥ kṣayaṃ yāti mithyāgṛhasukhapriyaḥ viṣayograviṣrtānāmamṛtāyatanaṃ vanam  KAvk hastākṛṣṭastriphaṇiphaṇabhṛnmastakanyastamṛtyukaṇṭhābaddhitkaṭaviṣalatāpallavālolamālaḥ dīptāṅgāraprkaragahanaṃ gāhate durgamārgaṃsaṃsāre smin viṣayanicaye sapramodaḥ pramādī  KAvk ityudīrya vrajan vyomnā vilaṅghya nagaraṃ kṣaṇāt bahirbhūtalamabhyetya sa yayau vājinā javāt  KAvk mahatā śākyamukhyena bodhitasyātha bhūpateḥ antaḥpure ca kāntānāmudbhūtaḥ karuṇaḥ svaraḥ  KAvk atha brahmendradhanadapramukhastridaśairvṛtaḥ rājasūnurvanaṃ prāpa gatvā dvādaśayojanam  KAvk avaruhyātha turagātg vimucyābharaṇāni saḥ uvāca sūcitānandaśchandakaṃ vadanatviṣā  KAvk gṛhītvābahraṇāni tvaṃ hayaṃ ca vraja mandiram medānīmasti me kṛtyametairmāyānibandhanaiḥ  KAvk vane sminnahamekākī śamasaṃtoṣabāndhavaḥ ekaḥ saṃjāyate jantureka eva vipadyate  KAvk viṣamaviṣayayogaṃ bhogamutsṛjya re kaḥ sarasarati viśeṣakleśaśoṣapravṛttaḥ paribhavabhuvane sminneṣa naḥ saṃniveśaḥ śamitamadanakāntiḥ śāntimeva śrayāmi  KAvk ityuktvābharaṇānyasya dīptānyaṅke mumoca saḥ tyaktaśokānvitānīva muktāpakkaṇasaṃcaye  KAvk cūḍāṃ niskṛṣya khaṅgena sa cikṣepa nabhaḥsthale śakraśca tam samādāya nināya divamādarāt  KAvk keśaḥ kleśa ivotkṛtto yatra tena mahātmanā keśapratigrahaṃ caityaṃ sadbhistatra niveśitam  KAvk chandako pyaśvamādāyaṃ prayātaḥ saptabhirdinaiḥ śanaiḥ prāpa puropāntaṃ śokārtaḥ samacintayat  KAvk śūnyaṃ turagamādāya parityajya nṛpātmajam draṣṭuṃ śaknomi nṛpatiṃ kathaṃ putrapralāpinam  KAvk vicintyeti hayaṃ tyaktvā sa tatraiva vyalambata śūnyāsanaḥ paraṃ vājī mūrtaḥ śoka ivāviśat  KAvk taṃ dṛṣṭvāntaḥ purajanaḥ sāmātyaśca mahīpatiḥ pratipralāpamukharāścakrire nikhilā diśaḥ  KAvk udbhūtārtasvaraiḥ kaṇṭhaiḥ sotkaṇṭhaiḥ sa viṣādavān sarvairgṛhītakīrṇāśrurvājī jīvitamatyajat  KAvk sa bodhisattvasaṃsparśapuṇyaprāptipavitritaḥ jagrāha brāhmaṇakule janma saṃsāramuktaye  KAvk śakradattaṃ kumārastu yatra kāṣāyamagrahīt kāṣāyagrahaṇam tatra caityaṃ cakre mahājanaḥ  KAvk vibhavamabhavavṛttyai janma janmapramuktyaivijanamapi janānāṃ mohagartānnivṛttyai iti sa kuśalakāmaḥ kāmamutsṛjya bhejeguṇakṛtajanarāgaḥ ślāghyatāṃ tyaktarāgaḥ  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāmabhiniṣkramaṇāvadānaṃ caturviśaḥ pallavaḥ  māravidrāvaṇāvadānam jayanti te janmabhayapramuktā bhavaprabhāvābhibhavābhiyuktāḥ yaiḥ sundarīlocanacakravartī māraḥ kṛtaḥ śāsanadeśavartī  KAvk tatastapovane cāsmin bodhisattve tapojuṣi tadupasthāpakāḥ pañca vārāṇasyāṃ pravavrajuḥ  KAvk spṛhaṇīyo munīndrāṇāmatha śākyamuniḥ śanaiḥ svayaṃ senāyanīgrāmaṃ janacārikayā yayau  KAvk tatra senābhidhānasya kanye gṛhapateḥ sute nandā nandabalākhyā ca cāruvṛtte babhūvatuḥ  KAvk śuddhodanasya bhūbhartuste śrutvā viśrutaṃ sutam cakrāte tadvivāhārthaṃ vrataṃ dvādaśavārṣikam  KAvk āmodinīnāṃ hṛdaye sadā sūtravadāsthitaḥ mālānāmiva bālānāmabhilāṣaḥ svabhāvajaḥ  KAvk dhenūnāṃ pītadugdhānāṃ dugdhaṃ tābhyāṃ punaḥ punaḥ gṛhīṭvā sphaṭikasthālyā vratānte pāyasaṃ śubham  KAvk vidhivatpāyase siddhe viprarūpaḥ sureśvaraḥ taṃ samabhyāyayau deśaṃ devaśca kamalāsanaḥ  KAvk harṣādatithibhāge tha kanyakābhyām samuddhṛte śakro vadatsarvaguṇodayāyāgre pradīyatām  KAvk matto yamadhikastāvadbrahmaṇaḥ prathamo pi ca ityukte surarājena provāca caturānanaḥ  KAvk matto dhiko deva āste śuddhāvāsanikāyikaḥ ityukte brahmaṇā te pi jagadurgaganasthitāḥ  KAvk sarvaprativiśiṣṭo sau bodhisattvastapaḥkṛśaḥ nadyāṃ nirājanākhyāyāṃ vigāhya salile sthitaḥ  KAvk etadākarṇya kanyābhyāmāhūya maṇibhājane avatīryārpitaṃ bhaktyā tadasmai madhupāyasam  KAvk bodhisattvastadādāya ratnapātrīṃ dadau tayoḥ datteyaṃ na punargrāhyetyuktvā jagṛhaturna te  KAvk sā tena nadyāṃ nikṣiptā nāgairnītā prabhāvatī vikṣobhyāpyāhṛtā tebhyastārkṣyarūpeṇa vajriṇā  KAvk prasādī bodhisattvo tha kanyāyugalamabhyadhāt dānasya praṇidhānena bhavatyoḥ kiṃ samīhitam  KAvk te tamūcaturānandanidhiḥ śuddhodanātmajaḥ sarvārthasiddho bhimataḥ kumāraḥ patirāvayoḥ  KAvk udyamaṃ māralīlāyāḥ sarasaṃ tadvacastayoḥ na lilimpa manastasya pādmaṃ dalamivodake  KAvk sa jagāda kumāro sau na kiṃ pravrajitaḥ śrutaḥ na tasya lolanayanāḥ priyāh śriya iva striyaḥ  KAvk ityanīpsitamākarṇya dīrghaṃ niśvasya kanyake ūcaturdānadharmo yaṃ siddhau tasyaiva jāyatām  KAvk adṛṣṭasnehasaṃśliṣṭaḥ praviṣṭo ntaḥ parāṅbhukhaḥ na nāma sucirābhyastaḥ pakṣapāto nivartate  KAvk iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā bodhisattvaḥ prasannadhīḥ prayātaste samāmantrya viśrāntyai kānanāntaram  KAvk pāyasāmṛtabhāgena labdhadivyabalodayaḥ pracchāyatarusucchāyamāruroha mahīdharam  KAvk paryaṅkabandhamādhāya tatra tasmin sukhaṃ sthite ahaṃkāra ivātyuccaśirāh so drirvyagīryata  KAvk viśīrṇabhūdhare tasmin sa pradadhyau viṣaṇṇadhīḥ sapakṣālāni karmāṇi mayā kāni kṛtānyaho  KAvk iti cintāśatocchvāsaṃ tamūcurvyomadevatāḥ na tvayā vihitaṃ sādho karma kiṃcidasāṃpratam  KAvk acchinnottaptakuśalaṃ dhartuṃ na kṣamate kṣitiḥ sa tvamuttaptakuśalaḥ proccaśailaśatāgdguruḥ  KAvk nirañjanīṃ samuttīrya saritaṃ vraja niścalam siddhidaṃ bodhisattvānām deśaṃ vajrāasnābhidham  KAvk devatādiṣṭamārgeṇa prasthitasyāsya bhūtale pādanyāsairabhūttasya hemapadmaparaṃparā  KAvk pṛthivī vrajatastasya prollasatsalilākulā raṇantī kāṃsyapātrīva pronnanāma nanāma ca  KAvk tāni tāni nimittāni pravṛttāni dadarśa saḥ yeṣāmanuttarajñānanidhānasādhanaṃ phalam  KAvk nirañjanāya bhuvane nāgo ndhaḥ kālikābhidhaḥ buddhotpāditadṛrabhūmeḥ śabdamākarṇya niryayau  KAvk sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannaṃ dīptajāmbūnadadyutim sa bodhisattvamālokya provāca racitāznjaliḥ  KAvk nalinanayana kāntastvaṃ vane yauvane sminviharasi virahārtiṃ saṃpadāmarpayitvā aśamaśamaviśeṣonmeṣasaṃtoṣaheturbhavasi bhavasamudre dehināṃ satyasetuḥ  KAvk athāmuñcantyete bhayataralatāmatra hariṇāḥyathā līlācakraṃ viharati samīpe khagagaṇaḥ sasattvāsattvānā kimapi hṛdayāśvāsasadanaṃtathā manye bauddhaṃ vapuridamanāyāsasukhadam  KAvk karikalabhakah padmaprītyā karoti hareḥ karaṃsukhayati śikhī snigdhālāpaṃ kalāpaśikhānilai bhavati hariṇī lolāpāṅgā puraḥ praṇayonmukhīpraśamasamayasyeyaṃ puṇyaprasādamayī sthitiḥ  KAvk adyaiva buddhatvamavāpya śuddhaṃ tvaṃ bodhimeṣyatyakhilāṃ trilokīm sadyaḥprasādapramadāvadātāṃ kumudvatī pūrṇa ivāmṛtāṃśuḥ  KAvk anyonyaṃ dinanāthadīptamahasaḥ sadyastavālokanāllokānāṃ kanalaprabodhakalayā divyaprakāśaspṛśām niryātī hṝdayānnibaddhamadhupaśreṇiva saṃbandhanatrastāntarna punaḥ kariṣyati padaṃ mohāndakārāvaliḥ  KAvk iti bruvāṇāṃ vinayānnāgarājaḥ prasannadhīḥ bodhisattvaṃ samābhāsya samuttīrya nadīṃ yayau  KAvk vajrāsanapadaṃ prāpya bodhimūlamanākulam dakṣiṇāgraiḥ kuśaiścakre śaktadattaiḥ sa saṃstaram  KAvk tatropaviśya paryaṅkabaddho niścalaniścayaḥ manthāvasānaviśrāntaḥ sa dugdhābdhirivābabhau  KAvk asādhāraḥ kṣamādhāraḥ sa dhīrasaralākṛtiḥ ruruce kāñcanaruciḥ paro merurivācalaḥ  KAvk asāvakṣayaparyantaḥ paryaṅko yaṃ mama sthiraḥ babandheti sa saṃkalpaṃ kṛtvā pratimukhīṃ smṛtim  KAvk atrāṇtare samabhyetya māraḥ saṃyamamatsaraḥ lekhahārastatra tūrṇaṃ bodhisattvamabhāṣataḥ  KAvk akāmakāmatā keyaṃ loke bandhanadā matā akālakalikākārā matiste kāsya kāmanā  KAvk gṛhītaṃ hataśaṅkena devadattena te puram niruddhantaḥpuraśreṇīrbaddhaḥ śuddhodano nṛpaḥ  KAvk iti śrutvaiva vacanaṃ śokāmarṣaviṣojjhitaḥ aśikṣitavikāreṇa cetasā sa vyacintayat  KAvk aho batāntarāyaṃ me māraḥ kartuṃ samudyataḥ nartayatyeṣa durvṛttaḥ śisvaṇḍikrīḍayājagat  KAvk māra māra virāmaste daurjanyasya na jāyate ekena hiṃsāyajñena prāpteyaṃ kamratā tvayā  KAvk yajñadāṇatapaḥślāghāṃ nātmanaḥ kartumutsahe svaguṇodīraṇamlānaṃ puṇyapuṣpaṃ hi śīryati  KAvk iti nirbhatsitastena cittastenaḥ śarīriṇām sāmarṣaḥ prayayau māraḥ samārambhād hatodyamaḥ  KAvk athādṛśyanta lalitā lālityāñcitalocanāḥ bhramadbhṛṅgaraṅgiṇyaḥ kāntāścūtalatā iva  KAvk cārutaccaritātṛptāstisrastāḥ kāmakanyakāḥ sarāgaṃ pādanalinīnyāsaiścakrustapovanam  KAvk vilocanena hariṇī kariṇī gativibhramaiḥ tatra tābhirmukhāmbhojairnalinī malinīkṛtā  KAvk yauvanābharaṇairaṅgauranurāgāvilepanaiḥ lāvaṇyavasanaistāsāṃ kāmo bhūdapyacetasām  KAvk vajrāsanasamādhānadhyānaniścalalocanam taṃ vilokyābhavat tāsāṃ vismayadhyānadhāraṇā  KAvk tā bodhisattvasaṃkalpān madarāgamayaṃ vayaḥ parityajyaiva sahasā salajjā bhejire jarām  KAvk pratīpagamanāttāsāmatha bhagnamanorathaḥ manmathaḥ prathitārambhaḥ sainyasaṃbḥāramādade  KAvk sarvapraharaṇairvyāptaṃ nānāprāṇimukhairbhayaiḥ ṣaṭtriṃśatkoṭīvipulaṃ balaṃ tasya samudyayau  KAvk svayamākarṇaniṣkṛṣṭakopakrūraśarāsanaḥ māraḥ sphāravikāreṇa bodhisattvaṃ samādravat  KAvk śastravṛṣṭistadutsṛṣṭā saha pāṃśuviṣāśmabhiḥ prayayau bodhisattvasya mandārāmbujatulyatām  KAvk punarmārabalotsṛṣṭā śastravṛṣṭirghṛtakṣame cakrire devatāstasya vajrapratisamāśrayam  KAvk smaro pi naṣṭasaṃkalpaḥ samādheḥ śrotrakaṇṭakam ghaṇṭāpaṭuraṭatpatraṃ nirmame sphaṭīkadrumam  KAvk taṃ tāramukharaṃ vṛkṣaṃ māraṃ ca sabalāyudham cakravāṭe samutkṣipya cikṣipurvyomadevatāḥ  KAvk bhagavānatha saṃprāptaprasannajñānanirmalaḥ sarvavitsarvagaḥ saravjātismṛtiparo bhavat  KAvk sa tatrānuttarajñānasamyaksaṃbodhimāpitaḥ dadarśa sarvabhutāṇi gatiṃ karmorminirmitām  KAvk atha śākyapure māraḥ pravādamasṛjaddivaḥ bodhisattvaḥ prayāto staṃ tapaḥkleśavaśāditi  KAvk tatra śuddhodano rājā putrasnehaviṣāturaḥ nipapāta tamākarṇya vajrāhata iva kṣitau  KAvk antaḥpure sahanṛpe prāṇatyāgakṛtakṣaṇe suvṛttapakṣapātinyastamūcurvyomadevatāḥ  KAvk putrastavāmṛtaṃ pītvā samyaksaṃbuddhatām gataḥ tenāvalokitasyāpi nāste bhṛtyubhayaṃ kutaḥ  KAvk iti sāntaḥpurāmātyaḥ śrutvā narapatirvacaḥ abhūtpratyāgataprāṇaḥ sudhāsikta iva kṣaṇāt  KAvk tasmin mahotsavānande bodhisattvavadhūḥ sutam kāntaṃ yaśodhaāsūta rāhugraste niśākare  KAvk rāhulākhyaḥ sa bālo pi nṛpaterjanmaśaṅkinaḥ jananyā saśilaḥ śuddhyai nikṣipto mbhasi pupluve  KAvk bhagavānapi saptāhaṃ sthito niścalavigrahaḥ vajraparyaṅkabandhena devānām vismayaṃ vyadhāt  KAvk sa brahmakāyikākhyābhyām devatābhyāṃ virodhitaḥ avadatparamānandasudhāsaṃdohasundaraḥ  KAvk aho tava mayā jñātā pūrvameṣā sukhasthitiḥ yayā surāsuraiśvaryasukhaṃ duḥkhagaṇāyate  KAvk lāvaṇyāmbhaḥplāvitāṅgāstaruṇyaḥ pīyūṣārdraḥ svargasaṃbhogavargaḥ asyāśeṣatyāgahelāsukhasya spardhābandhe pāṃśuniḥsāra eva  KAvk saṃtapto haṃ viṣayaviṣamakleśasaṃsārapānthaḥklāntaḥ śāntyāśritimupagataścandanacchāyayeva saṃjāteyaṃ sakalakaraṇavyāpinī nirvṛtimeviśrāntānām śamahimavane kiṃ sukhasyopamānam  KAvk asminnavasare puṇyaparipākeṇa tadvanam vaṇijau pṛthusārthena prāptau trapusabhallikau  KAvk devatāpretitau bhaktyā bhagavantamupetya tau praṇatau piṇḍapāto yaṃ gṛhyatāmityabhāṣatām  KAvk dayāvidheyaḥ sarvajñastadākarṇya vyacintayat pūrvaiḥ pātre gṛhīto yaṃ na pāṇī pātravarjite  KAvk iti cintayatastasya mahārājābhidhāḥ surāḥ datvā sphaṭikapātrāṇi catvāri tridivaṃ yayuḥ  KAvk kṛtvātha bhagavān pātre piṇḍapātapratigraham anugrahaṃ tayoścakre śaraṇyatrayaśāsanāt  KAvk vitatasukṛtasākṣī puṇyanikṣepadakṣaḥ kṣayitavipadaśeṣaḥ prārthanākalpavṛkṣaḥ bhavati kuśalamūlaiḥ kasyacidbhāgyabhājaḥ śubhapariṇatidīkṣādakṣiṇaḥ sādhusaṅgaḥ  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ māracidrāvaṇāvadānam nāma pañcaviṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  śākyotpattiḥ vaṃśaḥ sa ko pi vipulaḥ kuśalānubandhī yaścāruvṛttamucitaṃ guṇasaṃgrahasya ratnaṃ viśuddharucisūcitasatprakāśaṃ muktāmayaṃ jagadalaṃkaraṇaṃ prasūte  KAvk nyagrodhārāmanirataṃ purā kapulavāstuni śākyāḥ svavaṃśaṃ papracchurbhagavantaṃ tathāgatam  KAvk taiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ svakulotpattiṃ sa maudgalyāyanaṃ puraḥ vaktuṃ nyayuṅkta kṛtvāsya vimalajñānadarśanam  KAvk sa vilokya yathātattvamatītaṃ jñānacakṣuṣā tānavocata saṃsmṛtya śrūyatāṃ śākyasaṃbhavaḥ  KAvk aśeṣe smin jalamaye jagatyekārṇave purā sthite pavanasaṃsparśātpayaḥ paya ivābhavat  KAvk jale tasmin ghanatayā yāte kaṭhinatām śanaiḥ abhūdvarṇarasasparśaśabdagandhamayī mahī  KAvk tasyāmābhāsvarā devāścyutāḥ karmaparikṣayāt tattulyavarṇasaṃbhūtāḥ sattvāḥ sattvabalādhikāḥ  KAvk aṅgulyā rasamāsvādya tattṛṣṇātīvramohitāḥ āhāradoṣātsaṃprāpourgururūkṣavivarṇatām  KAvk annaprasavinī teṣāṃ krameṇābhūdvasuṃdharā tamobhiśca viluptānām kṣetrāga  KAvk tatasteṣāṃ kṣatatrāṇāt kṣatriyaḥ kṣitipālane mahāsaṃmatanāmābhūjjanasya mahato mataḥ  KAvk tasyānvaye mahatyāsīnṛpaḥ śrīmānupoṣadhaḥ amlānakīrtikusumaḥ pārijāta ivodadhau  KAvk cakravartī sutastasya māndhātābhūdayonijaḥ jagatyekātapatrasya yasya vaṃśo mahānabhūt  KAvk vaṃśe sahasravaṃśasya kṛkistasyābhavannṛpaḥ cittaprasādamakarod bhagavān yasya kāśyapaḥ  KAvk ikṣvākuranvaye tasya tasya cābhūd virūḍhakaḥ prītyā kanīyasaḥ sūnorjyeṣṭhāstena vivāsitāḥ  KAvk ekībhūya tataḥ sarve svadeśavigataspṛhāḥ kumārāḥ kapilākhyāsya maharṣerāśramaṃ yayuḥ  KAvk dhyānakālāṇtarāyāṇāṃ bālyāduccaiḥ pralāpinām so nyatra nirmame teṣāṃ puraṃ kapulavāstviti  KAvk kālena putravātsalyādanutāpena bhūpatiḥ ānīyantāṃ kumārāste sacivānityabhāṣata  KAvk tamūrcurmantriṇaḥ sarve rājan prāptapurottamāḥ pratyānetumaśakyāste jātāpatyapṛthuśriyaḥ  KAvk iti teṣāṃ pitustatra śakyāśakyavicintane babhūvuḥ śākyasaṃjñāste nṝpurasteṣu vaṃśakṛt  KAvk tadvaṃśeṣu pañcapañcasahasreṣu mahībhujām atīteṣu kṣitipatiḥ śrīmān daśaratho bahvat  KAvk tasyānvaye siṃhahanurbabhūva pṛthivīpatiḥ na raṇe siṃhamiva yaṃ sehire rājakuñjarāḥ  KAvk jyeṣṭhaḥ śuddhodanastasya sutaḥ śuklodanaḥ paraḥ droṇodanastadanujaḥ kanīyānamṛtodanaḥ  KAvk kanyāścatasraḥ śuddhākhyā śuklā droṇāmṛtā tathā śuddhodanasya bhagavān sūnurnandastathāparaḥ  KAvk śuklodanasya tanayau dvau tiṣyākhyo tha bhadrikaḥ droṇodanasya dvau putrāvaniruddho mahāṃstathā  KAvk ānandadevadattākhyāvamṛtodanasaṃbahvau śuddhāsutaḥ supraśuddhaḥ śuklāsūnuśva mālikaḥ  KAvk droṇāputraśca bhadrāṇirvaiśālyakhyo mṛtāsutaḥ rāhulo bhagavatsūnuryasmin vaṃśaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ  KAvk ityujjvalajñānamayena tena vaṃśaṃ yathāvatkathitaṃ niśamya śākyā babhūvarbhagavatprabhāvaiḥsaṃbhāvitotkarṣaviśeṣaśuddhāḥ  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ śākyotpattīrnāma ṣaḍviṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  śroṇākoṭīviṃśāvadānam sa ko pi sattvasya vivekabandhoḥ puṇyopasannasya mahān prabhāvaḥ nāpaiti yaḥ kāyaśateṣu puṃsaḥ kastūrikāmoda ivāṃśukasya  KAvk jine sarvajagajjantusaṃtāpakaruṇāhrade pure rājagṛhe veṇuvanāntaravihāriṇi  KAvk śrīmānabhūdbhūmipatiścampāyāṃ potalābhidhaḥ jahāra dhanadarpāndhyaṃ dhanena dhanadasya yaḥ  KAvk ajāyata sutastasya manorathaśatānvitaḥ dhanānāmīpsitāvāptya sukhasakhyo vibhūtayaḥ  KAvk śravaṇarkṣeṇa jātasya sa sūnostasya janmani prītyā dadau daridrasya koṭīnāṃ viṃśatiṃ tadā  KAvk sa śroṇakoṭiviṃśākhyaḥ śiśuḥ khyātastadābhavat vibhavaḥ sukṛtenaiva yena vaṃśo vibhūṣitaḥ  KAvk prāptavidyaḥ sa sarvārthaiḥ saha vṛddhimupāgataḥ cakāra sukhaviśrāntiṃ vyavahāradharaḥ pituḥ  KAvk sa kadācitprabhāpuñjamiav sūryasya maṇḍalāt avatīrṇaṃ puraprātaṃ maudgalyāyanamabravīt  KAvk ko bhavānarkasaṃkāśaḥ prakāśitadigantaraḥ tridaśeśaḥ śaśāṅko vā devo vā draviṇeśvaraḥ  KAvk sa taṃ babhāṣe na suraḥ śiṣyo bhagavatastvaham buddhasya vibudhādhīśavandyamānaguṇaśriyaḥ  KAvk svacchaṃ tasya prayacchantaṃ piṇḍapātaṃ mahāmuneḥ sattvaśuddhodayāvāptaṃ bhogyaṃ bhagavataḥ priyam  KAvk iti śroṇasya bhagavannāmnā śravaṇagāminā ravibhakrasya jātyāpi romāñcaḥ samajāyataḥ  KAvk prāgjanmavāsanāyuktaḥ svabhāvo yasya yaḥ sthitaḥ sa tasyodīraṇenāpi sphuṭa eva vibhāvyate  KAvk sa tasmai viṃśatisthālībhāgaṃ nākajanocitam prahiṇodbhaktisaṃsaktaśraddhāyuktena cetasā  KAvk tatastaṃ preṣitaṃ tena bhagavān bhaktisaṃsadā anugrahāgrahavyagraḥ samagraṃ svayamagrahīt  KAvk asminnavasare bhaktyā sthālībhāgaṃ nṛpocitam samādāya svayaṃ rājā bimbisāraḥ samāyayau  KAvk śroṇaprahītabhogānāmāmodaṃ tatra pārthivaḥ āghrāya śakraprahitaṃ sarvaṃ divyamamanyata  KAvk pātraśeṣaṃ bhagavatā dattamāsvādya bhūpatiḥ śroṇena preṣitaṃ śrutvā tadanu vismayaṃ yayau  KAvk bhagavantaṃ praṇamyātha rājadhānīṃ nareśvaraḥ praviśyācintayatsphītāṃ divyāṃ śroṇasya saṃpadam  KAvk gacchāmi taṃ svayaṃ gatvā draṣṭavyo sau amhāyaśāḥ iti niścitya sacivaiḥ sa yātrārambhamādiśat  KAvk potalaḥ kṣitipaṃ jñātvā svayamāgamanodyatam nītijñaṃ putramekāṇte śroṇakoṭimabhāṣata  KAvk putra tvām draṣṭumāyāti varṇāśramagururnṛpaḥ ityeṣa bhṛśamutkarṣaḥ sadoṣaḥ pratibhāti me  KAvk kṣitīśā lakṣatāṃ yātaṃpakṣapātodyatā iva avilambitamāghnanti śarā iva guṇacyutāḥ  KAvk bhṛtyānāmapi vidveṣyo bhavatyatiśayonnatiḥ abhimānaikasārāṇāṃ kiṃ punaḥ pṛthivībhūjām  KAvk rūpe vayasi saubhāgye prabhāve vibhave śrute svasutasyāpi saṃgharṣānnotkarṣaṃ sahate janaḥ  KAvk jane dveṣamaye putra guṇamācchādya jīvyate ācchāditaguṇaḥ padmaḥ priyastīkṣṇarucerapi  KAvk uddhataḥ kasya na dveṣyaḥ praṇataḥ kasya na priyaḥ drumaṃ pātayati stabdhaṃ namtraṃ rakṣati mārutaḥ  KAvk sa cābhigamyo bhūpālastvāṃ yadi svayameṣyati tadeṣaṃ darpamohaste śreyase na bahviṣyati  KAvk tasmāditaḥ svayaṃ gatvā praṇamyaṃ praṇama prabhum nakṣatrarāśisadṛśaṃ datvā hāramupāyanam  KAvk pituḥ śrutveti vacanaṃ śroṇakoṭirhahīpatim prayayau nāvamāruhya draṣṭuṃ ratnavibhūṣitaḥ  KAvk sa rājadhānīmāsādya prāpya dṛṣṭvā ca bhūpatim dadau hāraṃ parṇamyāsmai harṣahāsamiva śriyaḥ  KAvk taṃ dṛṣṭvā svayamāyātaṃ nṛpatiḥ snigdhayā dṛśā hemaromāṅkacaraṇaṃ vismayādityabhāṣata  KAvk aho puṇyamaheśākhyaḥ ko pi tvaṃ sattvabāmdhavaḥ yasya saṃdarśanenaiva manovṛttiḥ prasīdati  KAvk guṇebhyaḥ paramaiśvaryamaiśvaryātsukhamuttamam sukhebhyaḥ paramārogyamārogyātsādhusaṃgamaḥ  KAvk api dṛṣṭastvayā sādho bhagavān veṇukānane tatpādapadmayugalaṃ draṣṭumarhasi me mataḥ  KAvk ityukte kṣitināthena saujanyātpakṣapātinā taṃ śroṇakoṭīviṃśo pi praṇayātpratyabhāṣata  KAvk asmādatulyakalyāṇātprasādāddevadeva te adhunā yogyatāyātā bhagavaddarśane mama  KAvk ityukte tena sahitaḥ pratasthau sthitikovidaḥ bhaktyā tathāgataṃ draṣṭuṃ padbhyāmeva mahīpatiḥ  KAvk aspṛṣṭapādasya bhuvā śruṇasyājanmavāsarāt mahārhavastraiḥ prasthāne bhṛtyairācchāditā mahī  KAvk bhagavadbhaktivinayādgauravācca sa bhūpateḥ vastrāṇyavārayadbhṛtyairavācca iva kṣitau  KAvk vāriteṣvatha vastreṣu divyavastrairvṛtā mahī aprayatnopakaraṇāḥ saṃpadaḥ puṇyaśālinām  KAvk nivārya dinyavastrāṇi bhūmau tenārpite pade vicacālācalā pṛthvī saśailavanasāgarā  KAvk tataḥ sa bhūmipatinā saha prāpya jināśramam bhagavantaṃ vilokyāsya vidadhe pādavandanam  KAvk upaviṣṭasya tasyāgre hṛṣṭasyālokanāmṛtaiḥ cakre śamavivekasya bhagavānabhiṣecanam  KAvk āśayānuśayaṃ dhātuṃ prakṛtiṃ ca vicārya saḥ satyasaṃdarśanāyāsya vidaśe dharmadeśanām  KAvk satkāyadṛṣṭiśailo sya tayā viṃśatiśṛṅgavān jñānavajreṇa nirbhinnaḥ srotaḥprāptipadaspṛśaḥ  KAvk pravrajyāyāṃ tatastasya jātāyāṃ sahasā svayam bhagavantaṃ praṇamyātha vismitaḥ prayayau nṛpaḥ  KAvk tīvravrate pi śroṇasya kadācitsamajāyata vāsanāśeṣasaṃskārādbandhabhogasukhasmṛtiḥ  KAvk sa tamāhūya bhagavān vilakṣaṃ prāha sasmitaḥ ko yaṃ parivitarkaste pratisaṃlīnacetasaḥ  KAvk viśliṣṭātyantakṛṣṭā vā tantrī bahvati visvarā samā mādhuryamāyāti tasmātsāmyaṃ samāśrayet  KAvk ityādeśādbhagavataḥ sarvasāmyamupāgataḥ sa prāpa vimalajñānaṃ paścāttāpavivarjitaḥ  KAvk tasya tāmadbhutāṃ siddhiṃ vilokya pṛthuvismayāḥ papracchurbhikṣavaḥ sarve bhagavantaṃsa cābhyadhāt  KAvk śroṇasya śrūyatām śreyaḥkarma janmāntarārhitam na hyapuṇyānubhāvānāṃ bhavantyadbhutasaṃpadaḥ  KAvk vipaśvī bhagavān samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ sugataḥ purā purīṃ bandhumatīṃ nāma janacārikayā yayau  KAvk tatra bhaktyā sukṛtibhirbhaktāyopanimantritaḥ vāreṇa pratyahaṃ gehaṃ yayau teṣāṃ sahānugaḥ  KAvk tato daridraḥsaṃprāptavāro brāhmaṇadārakaḥ indrasomābhidhaścakre yatnāt yadyogyabhojanam  KAvk sa prayatnena mahatā bhojyaṃ bhaktipavitritam āchādya vastrairvasudhāṃ prahvastasmai nyavedayat  KAvk tadbhogapraṇidhānena jātaḥ so yaṃ mahādhanaḥ sauvarṇaromacaraṇaḥ śroṇakoṭī suropamaḥ  KAvk na vastrarahitā bhūmiḥ spṛṣṭānena kadācana kampastaccaraṇasparśādata evābhavadbhuvaḥ  KAvk iti sugatavacaḥ sudhāvadātaṃ daśanamayūkhamivonmiṣatsvabhāvam praṇihitahṛdayaḥ paraṃ nipīya sthirakuśalāya babhūva bhikṣusaṃghaḥ  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ śroṇakoṭīviṃśāvadānaṃ saptaviṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  dhanapālāvadānam daurjanyaduḥsahaviśālakhalāpakārairnaivāśaye vikṛtirasti mahāśayānām vyālolvaṇakṣitibhṛdākulito pi sindhurnaivotsasarja hṛdayādamṛtasvabhāvam  KAvk pure purā rājagṛhe bahgavān veṇukānane kalandakanivāsākhye vijahāra manohare  KAvk tatra vitrāsitānekaśatrinistriṃśabāndhavaḥ ajātaśatrunāmābhūd bimbisārasuto nṛpaḥ  KAvk śākyavaṃśyaḥ suhṛttasya devadattābhidho bhavat kṣudramantreṇa yasyāsīt sa vetāla ivotkaṭaḥ  KAvk sa kadācitsukhāsīnaṃ rahaḥ prāha mahīpatim na rājan phalito dyāpi mamāpi tvatsamāśrayaḥ  KAvk nithopacārarahitaḥ sukhaniryantratantrayoḥ mitho manorathatrāṇānmitraśabdaḥ pravartate  KAvk ya eṣa śākyaśramaṇaḥ sukhe veṇuvane sthitaḥ taṃ hatvā prāptumicchāmi tatpadaṃ devavanditam  KAvk kṣīyate na yayā śatrurlabhyate na yayā yaśaḥ vardhate na yayā mānaḥ kiṃ tayā mitrasaṃpadā  KAvk mahādhanābhidhānena tatpaureṇa nimantritaḥ sa puraṃ prātarāgantā dāmbhikaḥ saha bhikṣubhiḥ  KAvk rājamārgaṃ praviśataḥ sa tasya vyālakuñjaraḥ utsṛjyatāmabhimukhaḥ krodhāndho dhanapālakaḥ  KAvk ityukte devadattena nṛpatirmitravatsalaḥ buddhaprabhāvaṃ saṃcintya nāha kiṃcidavāṅbhukhaḥ  KAvk devadatto pi nirgatya rājasauhārdadurmadaḥ prāha hastimahāmātraṃ hāraṃ datvāsya toṣaṇam  KAvk śramaṇaḥ prātarāgantā puraṃ bhikṣuśatairvṛtaḥ preraṇīyastvayā tasmai gaja ityāha bhūpatiḥ  KAvk devadattavacaḥ śrutvā tathetyuce dvipādhipaḥ śreṇī hi meṣamūrkhāṇāmekayātānupātinī  KAvk jñātvāpi tamabhiprāyaṃ sarvajñaḥ pāpacetasām prātaḥ samāyayau sārdhaṃ bhikṣūṇāṃ pañcabhi śataiḥ  KAvk atha hastipakotsṛṣṭaḥ kṛṣṭaprāsādapādapaḥ tamabhyadhāvadāviddhaḥ krodhāndhaḥ krūrakuñjaraḥ  KAvk anāyattaḥ paricayādaṅkuśasya gurorapi khalaviddhāniva dveṣī madena malinīkṛtaḥ  KAvk sevavyasanasaktānāmasakṛtkarṇacāpalāt prāṇāpahārī bhṛṅgāṇāṃ bhṛtyānāmiva duṣpatiḥ  KAvk mandaropadrave tasmin drumadrohiṇyabhidrute vidrute sahasā loke hāhākāro mahānabhūt  KAvk tasyāñcatkarṇatālānilatulitasaratsāndrasindūrapūraiḥsaṃpūrṇe rājamārge cyutacakitavadhūraktavastrāsamānaiḥ uddaṇḍoccaṇḍaśuṇḍabhramaṇaravalasatsādhvasāyāsitāśāvyālolālakābhabhramaramiladvibhramaḥ saṃbhramo bhūt  KAvk purapramāthavyathite jane kolāhalākule āruroha mahāharmyaṃ devadattaḥ pramattadhīḥ  KAvk bhagavadgrahaṇaṃ draṣṭuṃ so bhavadbhṛśamutsukaḥ unmūlanena guṇināṃ mātaṅgaḥ parituṣyati  KAvk vidruteṣu gajatrāsāt teṣu sarveṣu bhikṣuṣu ānanda eka evābhūd bhikṣurbhagavato ntike  KAvk tatra pañcānanāh pañca niryayurbhagavatkarāt karālakesarasaṭāstannakhāṃśucitā iva  KAvk dvipastadgandhamāgrāya pardāpasmāravāraṇam abhūt srutaśakṛnmūtraḥ sahasaiva parāṅmukhaḥ  KAvk javena vidrutastatra dantī darpadaridratām prāptaḥ pradīpadahanāḥ sa dadarśa diśo daśa  KAvk sa vilokya jālavahnijvalajjvālākulaṃ jagat pādapadmāntikaṃ śāstuḥ śītalaṃ samupāyayau  KAvk saṃkocābhiruceḥ sacintamanasaḥ pradhvastavaktradyuter dainyāpannavihīnadānamadhupaprārabdhakolāhalaḥ lobhāndhasya mahāvyayotsava iva kleśoṣmaniśvāsinas tasyābhūtparitāpaniślathagaterbhārāyamāṇaḥ karaḥ  KAvk taṃ pādamūlamāyāntaṃ bhītaṃ kāruṇyasāgaraḥ śāstā kareṇa pasparśa cakrasvastikalakṣmaṇā  KAvk kumbhavinyastahastastaṃ provāca bhagavān jinaḥ putra svakarmaṇainemāṃ prāpto si tvamimāṃ daśām  KAvk vivekālokahaladaḥ kāyo yaṃ māṃsabhūdharaḥ bhāraste mohasaṃbhāraḥ pāpādupanataḥ paraḥ  KAvk ityukte karuṇardreṇa bhito bhagavatā gajaḥ sa labdhaścāsamālānalīno niścalatām yayau  KAvk devadattasya saṃkalpe kuñjare ca mahotkaṭe bhagne nirvighnaharṣo bhūtsamudgatādbhuto janaḥ  KAvk tataḥ kṛtvā gṛhapatergṛhe bhojyapratigraham bhagavān bhikṣubhiḥ sārdhaṃ kānanaṃ gantumudyayau  KAvk abhisṛtya gajendro pi jinasya caraṇābjayoḥ kṛtvā kareṇa saṃsparśaṃ vapustatyāja kauñjaram  KAvk cāturmahārājikeṣu deveṣu viśadadyutiḥ upapannaḥ sa sahasā sugataṃ draṣṭumāyayau  KAvk svamāśramapadaṃ prāptaṃ bhagavantamupetya saḥ praṇanāmārkasaṃkāśaṃ pradīptamaṇikuṇḍalaḥ  KAvk tasya keyūramukuṭaprabhāpallavapūritāḥ śakracāpairiva vyāptā virejurghanarājayaḥ  KAvk vinayādupaviśyāgre sa śāstuḥ srastakalmaṣaḥ taṃ divyapuṣpairākīrya sattva śubhrairabhāṣataḥ  KAvk bhagavan bhavataḥ pādapadmasaṃsparśanena me durdaśāduḥkhasaṃtāpaḥ śāntaḥ saṃtoṣaśālinaḥ  KAvk śamaślāghyā kāpi vyasanaviṣadoṣoṣmaśamanīsudhāvṛṣṭirdṛṣṭirbata bhagavataḥ snigdhamadhurā yayā spṛṣṭaspṛṣṭaṃ kharataravikāravyatikaraṃvimutyāntaḥśāntiṃ śrayati hatamoha paśurapi  KAvk iti tasya bruvāṇasya bhagavān bhavaśāntaye satyadarśanasaṃśuddhāṃ vidadhe dharmadeśanām  KAvk maulimuktāṃśuśubhreṇa śirasā caraṇadvayam sa śāstuḥ prayayau natvā hasanniva bhavabhramam  KAvk gate tasmin mukhaśaśiprakāśitanabhastale bhagavān bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭastadvṛttāntamabhāṣata  KAvk pūrvakalpāntare śāstuḥ kāśyapākhyasya śāsane abhūtpravrajito pyeṣa śikṣāpadanirādaraḥ  KAvk anādarātkuñjaratābhogaḥ saṃghopasevanāt satyadṛṣṭibalenānte saṃprāptaḥ śāsanagrahaḥ  KAvk prāgjanmavihitaṃ karma kasyacinna nivartate karmopadiṣṭasaṃbandhabhaktibhogaiḥ sacetasaḥ  KAvk tasmin vyatikare ghore sarvaistyakro smi bhikṣibhiḥ na tvānandena tatrāpi śrūyatām pūrvasaṃgatiḥ  KAvk śaśāṅkaśītasarasi bhrātarau rucirau purā pūrṇamukhaḥ śukhaśceti rājahaṃsau babhūvatuḥ  KAvk kadācidbrahmadattasya vārāṇasyāṃ mahīpateḥ brahamamatīṃ puṣkariṇīṃ ramyāṃ pūrṇamukho yayau  KAvk sa tasyāṃ lolakamalakiñjalkaparipiñjaraḥ vijahāra sarojinyāṃ haṃsānāṃ pañcabhiḥ śataiḥ  KAvk pūrvapuṇyānubhāvena taṃ rūpātiśayojjvalam dadarśaṃ kāryāṇyutsṛjya jano niścalalocanah  KAvk taṃ śrutvā bhūpatistatra sthitaṃ taddarśanotsukaḥ kuśalān grahaṇe
