tasya vyasṛjajjālajīvinaḥ  KAvk tasmin gṛhīte nalīnīlīlāsmitasitatviṣi śatāni pañca haṃsānāṃ tyaktvā taṃ prayayurjavāt  KAvk ekastu tasya saujanyādabaddho pi subaddhavat tadarthaṃ vyathitastasthau premapāśavaśīkṛtaḥ  KAvk tatastaiḥ prāpitaṃ rājā rājahaṃsaṃ vilokya tam snehabaddhaṃ dvitīyaṃ ca vismitastāvavalokayat  KAvk haṃsaḥ pūrṇamukhaḥ so hamānandastasya cānugaḥ gatāstadadya ca tyaktvā māṃ gaṃsā eva bhikṣavaḥ  KAvk pūrvasminnabahvatkāle vārāṇasyāṃ mahīpatiḥ tutturnāma manaḥpaṭṭe likhitaṃ yadyaśaḥ paraiḥ  KAvk sahasrayodhastasyābhūd dākṣiṇātyo niratyayaḥ karadaṇḍīti vikhyātaḥ saṃgrāmāgresaraḥ priyaḥ  KAvk kadācid ghorasamare pañcāmātyaśatāni tam nṛpaṃ tyaktvā yayurbhītyā karadaṇḍī tu nātyajat  KAvk ahameva sa bhūpālaḥ sacivāste ca bhikṣavaḥ karadaṇḍī sa evāyamānando na jahāti mām  KAvk janmāntare pi siṃho haṃ māsaṃ kūpe nipātitaḥ upekṣitaḥ kṣaṇādbhṛtyaiḥ śṛgālairye dya bhikṣavaḥ  KAvk ekena ca nakhaiḥ khātaṃ dīrghaṃ kṛtvāsmi mokṣitaḥ jambukena sa evāyamānando dya mamānugaḥ  KAvk kūṭapāśanibaddhasya mṛgayūthapateḥ purā lubdhakāgamane eva jagmustadanugā mṛgāḥ  KAvk anuraktā na tatyāja taṃ mṛgī sāśrulocanā prītiśṛṅkhalayā baddhā yātā nispandatāmiva  KAvk atha lubdhakamāyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā mṛgavadhodyatam sāvadanmama bāṇena prathamaṃ hara jīvitam  KAvk iti spaṣṭagirā tasyāḥ snehena ca sa vismitaḥ mumoca lubdhakaḥ prītyā hariṇaṃ hariṇīsakham  KAvk mṝgayūthapatiḥ so hamānandaḥ sā kuraṅgikā ityeṣa prītisaṃbandhaḥ prāgvṛttamanuvartate  KAvk śrutveti vākyaṃ sugatasya sarve lajjānilīnā iva bhikṣavaste sānandamānandamukhāravindaṃ prabhābhirāmaṃ dadṛśuḥ spṛhārdrāḥ  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ dhanapālāvadānaṃ aṣṭaviṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  kāśīsundarāvadānam jayati sa sattvaviśeṣaḥ sattvavatām sarvasattvasukhahetuḥ dehadalane pi śamayati kopāgniṃ śāntimuccairyaḥ  KAvk dharmopadeśe bhagavān kauṇḍinyasyāgravartinaḥ bhikṣoḥ kathāprasaṅgena pṛṣṭp bhikṣubhirabhyadhāt  KAvk brahmadattasya tanayo vārāṇasyāṃ mahīpateḥ kāśisundaranāmā va kālabhūśca babhuvatuḥ  KAvk yauvarājyabharaikarhaḥ kumāraḥ kāśisundaraḥ dharmādharmamayaṃ rājyaṃ vicāryācintayacciram  KAvk kṣaṇakṣayiṇi tāruṇye jīvite vīcicañcale rājye svapnavivāhe smin mohamūle na me matiḥ  KAvk rāgapralāpabahule māyāmphamahe muhuḥ veśyārodananiḥsāre saṃsāre nāsti satyatā  KAvk pravrajyāmanaghastasmādagārādanagārikam nistriṃśavṛttisaṃsaktābhirāgaḥ kiṃ vibhūtibhiḥ  KAvk rājasūnurvicintyeti vivekavimalāśayaḥ uvācābhyetya bhūpālamaraṇyagamanotsukaḥ  KAvk mama saṃbhogavargo yaṃ rājannaivopayujyate yauvarājyābhiṣekārhaḥ samārambho nivāryatām  KAvk krodhāgnitaptāḥ sutarāmetāstāta na me matāḥ baddhabandhabhayāyāsajananyo rājasaṃpadaḥ  KAvk vyāptāḥ krūratarācārairjvalitāḥ pārthivaśriyaḥ kurvanti kasya nodvegaṃ śmaśānāgniśikhā iva  KAvk chatrasaṃchāditā lokāścāmarānilalolitāḥ patanti pātakaśvabhre madakṣībāḥ kṣitīśvarāḥ  KAvk mṛdubhogāṃśukābhyāsasukumāre mahībhujām kāye patati paryante kleśaḥ kuliśadāruṇaḥ  KAvk cintāsaṃtatasaṃtāpatīvratṛṣṇāpralāpinām rājyajvarajuṣāṃ naiṣāṃ mohamūrcchā nivartate  KAvk vakrāṇāṃ ratnadīptānāṃ dvijihānāṃ pade pade chidrasaṃdarśināṃ rājñāṃ vyāpāraḥ paramāraṇam  KAvk nṛpavaṃśaśatocchiṣṭāṃ manyate māmananyagām itīva śrīḥ kṣītīśānāṃ hāracāmarahāsinī  KAvk vyañjitavyajanocchvasā lakṣmīrmuktāśrusaṃtatiḥ rājñāṃ mohābhṛtātītabhūpatismaraṇādiva  KAvk tasmādvrajāmi pravrajyāvivarjitajanasthitiḥ saṃtoṣaśītalacchāyaṃ saṃtāpaśamanaṃ vanam  KAvk aviśrāntasya saṃsārapathapānthasya durvahaḥ kāyo sya yatsadāpāyaḥ kiṃ punaḥ pṛthivībharaḥ  KAvk iti putravacaḥ śrutvā bhūptirbhṛśamapriyam pravrajyāśabdacakitaḥ sodvegastamabhāṣataḥ  KAvk asya vaṃśasya mahataḥ sāmrājyasya vṛddhaye āśānibaddhavṛddhena tvayi putra mayā param  KAvk vatsa saṃkalpabhangaṃ me na kāle krtumarhasi idaṃ tava mahacchāyaṃ yauvanaṃ na vanocitam  KAvk samantrābhyāsayuktānām śaktānāṃ sādhudarśane jitendriyāṇāṃ saravtra nṛpāṇāmavanaṃ tapaḥ  KAvk svapade pi sarojasya niḥsaṅgasalilasthitiḥ dṛṣṭvā vane pyaśokasya lalanācaraṇāhatiḥ  KAvk svagehasulabhairbhogairyāvaddṛṣṭivisūcikā tāvadete parityuktaṃ śakyante viṣayāḥ kṣaṇam  KAvk sukhamantaḥ parityajya svajanaṃ gṛhanirgataḥ abhyastabhogacirahakleśaṃ na sahate janaḥ  KAvk śrūyate smaryate dharmaḥ kriyate ca sukhād gṛhe vane śuṣyanti śuṣkāṇāṃ śravaṇāsmaraṇakriyāḥ  KAvk kṣaratkṣatajapādasya darbhasaṃdarbhasūcibhiḥ tataḥ kiṃ duḥkhamaparaṃ paralole bhaviṣyati  KAvk bhuñjānaṃ janamīkṣante yātāścarmāsthiśeṣatām paradataṃ sadāśnanti pretā iva tapasvinaḥ  KAvk vane nivasanaṃ putra pāṃśuprāvaraṇaṃ samam pālanaṃ brahmacaryasya makarākaraśoṣaṇam  KAvk dāvāgnidhūmavikaṭabhrukuṭimukheṣu gonāsavāsaghanaghūkaguhāgṛheṣu siṃhāhatadviradalohitalohiteṣu tyaktvā gṛhaṃ bhavati kasya dhṛtirvaneṣu  KAvk kāmī saṃyamamicchati smarati ca śyāmārateḥ saṃyamītṛptastīvrataravrateṣu ramate bhakṣyaṃ kṣudhā kāṅkṣḥati ekākī janamīhate janavanodvegī vanaṃ vāñchatityaktvānveṣaṇatatparāḥ punarapi prāpyāvamānaṃ janāḥ  KAvk na māṃ putra parityajya gahanaṃ gantumarhasi bhavantu tava śatrūṇāṃ vanavāsamanorathāḥ  KAvk vyaktamauktikahāsinyaḥ karavālalatā iva tyaktā na punarāyānti māninyo nṛpasaṃpadaḥ  KAvk ityukro pyasakṛt pitrā niścayānna cacāla saḥ vajraratnaśikhākalpaḥ saṃkalpo hi mahātmanām  KAvk jananībhiramātyaiśca bandhupauramahattamaiḥ sa prārthito pyabhūnmaunī nirāhāro dinatrayam  KAvk rājabhogī tapasvī vā jīvatveṣa nijecchayā kāmānuvartī lolo yamityūciḥ sacivā nṛpam  KAvk sa kathaṃcidanujñātaḥ sāśrunetreṇa bhūbhujā yayau paurajanākrandamaunī munitapovanam  KAvk vairāgyaparipākeṇa tatra maitrīpavitritām bheje sa sarvasattveṣu vivekadayitāṃ dayām  KAvk babhūvustatprabhāveṇa tatra sarvavanaukasāṃ jātivairājalatyāgaśītalāścittavṛttayaḥ  KAvk tyakte prāṇavadhe prasaktahariṇīvṛndaiḥ pulindaiḥ paraṃsiṃhairvāraṇadāraṇanyuparame sarvāṅgasaṅgīkṛte māyūrāvaraṇairdaridrajaghanā muktākalāpojjhitāstatrocchvāsavirāgaśuṣyadadharā jātāḥ kirātāṅganāḥ  KAvk kṣamāṃ tyaktvābdhivasanāṃ saravbhūtakṣamāśritaḥ so bhavat kṣāntivādīti viśutaḥ kāśisundaraḥ  KAvk atrāntare mahīharṣe brahmadatte divaṃ gate udvega iva bhūtānāṃ bhūpālaḥ kalibhūrabhūt  KAvk athadabhrabhramadbhṛṅgabhrūbhaṅgamalinānanaḥ munisaṃyamavidveṣī vasantaḥ pratyadṛśyata  KAvk madanonmādabhutasya prodbhūtasya mṛgīdṛśām mānavidhvaṃsadūtasya cutasya ruruce ruciḥ  KAvk raktāśokasya pārśvasthalatāliṅganaśaṅkitaḥ īrṣyāluriva puṣpāṇi jahāra malayānilaḥ  KAvk udyānayauvane tasmin kāle kokilasaṃkule sāntaḥpuro nṛpaḥ prāyād vanālokanakautukī  KAvk nānāvarṇapatatpuṣpaprakārapracitāni saḥ paśyan vanāni ramyāṇi śanaiḥ prāpa tapovanam  KAvk vanasthalīṣu kāntāsu tatra kanyāsakhaściram vihṛtya rativiśrāntaḥ kṣasṇaṃ nidrāmavāptavān  KAvk apūrvakusumasmerāścinvānāstatra mañjarī antaḥpurāṅganāśceruḥ saṃcāriṇyo latā iva  KAvk atrāntare kṣāntivādī viviktoddeśanirvṛtaḥ ekānte niścalastasthau śāntimantarvicintayan  KAvk amandānandaciṣyandī vandanīyo manīṣiṇām kṛśo pyakṛśasaundaryaḥ śaśīva prathamoditaḥ  KAvk pariṇāmamanojñena rekhāsaṃsthānaśobhinā purāṇacitrarūpeṇa naiva śūnyā tadākṛtiḥ  KAvk taṃ dṛṣṭvā rājalalanāścittadarpaṇamārjanam tatraiva varocūpahalāhalamivotkaṭam  KAvk kastvaṃ munivyañjanayā citrakṛtrimamātrayā muṣṇāsi mugdhagṛdayā nūnaṃ nārīpratārakaḥ  KAvk parastrīharaṇe dhyāna japastadvighnavāraṇe dhūrtānāṃ paramopāyaḥ saralāśvāsanaṃ tapaḥ  KAvk mukhamādhuryadhūrtasya vṛttirvalkalinastava aho nu mohajananī vane viṣataroriva  KAvk munikalpasamākalpaścaritaṃ punarīdṛśam siddhiṃ saṃbhāvitāṃ vāpi vetti kastattvamāntaram  KAvk ityukte bhūbhujā krodhādakrodhamadhurāśayaḥ nirvikāreṇa manasā kṣāntivādī jagād tam  KAvk kṣāntivādī munirahaṃ na māṃ śankitumarhasi etāsu nirviśeṣo me kāntāsu ca talāsu ca  KAvk iti tenoktamākarṇya kṣāntaṃ paśyāmi te dhunā iti bruvāṇaściccheda hastau tasyāsinā nṛpaḥ  KAvk viśase pi kṣamāśīlaṃ nivikāraṃ vilokya tam cakarta caraṇau tasya praśamāya samatsaraḥ  KAvk pradiśantyaśivaṃ mārge jihvayā dūṣayanti ca lumpantyaṅgāni paryante khalāḥ kauleyakā iva  KAvk tāḍane pi kṣamāsaktāḥ skandhacchede pi mauninaḥ śītalāstīvratāpe pi saralāḥ saralā iva  KAvk nikṛttapāṇicaraṇaḥ sa saṃstabhya pṛthuvyathām rakṣan manyumanaḥkṣobhaṃ kṣamayā samacintayat  KAvk tyaktānyakarmaṇānena cchinnānyaṅgāṇi me yathā saṃsāraviṣamakleśacchedaṃ kuryāmahaṃ tathā  KAvk kopamohādavajñāya nṛpatau bhrātaraṃ munim purīṃ prayāte rajasā śokamlāneva bhūrabhūt  KAvk tatastadduḥkhakupitā rājñe tatkṣāntidevatā cakre nagaryāṃ durbhokṣamarakāvṛṣṭiviplavam  KAvk naimittikebhyo vijñāya rājāmuniparābhavāt devatākoapajaṃ doṣaṃ taṃ prasādayituṃ yayau  KAvk nipatya pādayostasya kṣamasvetyabhidhāya saḥ paścāttāpaviṣādena niścetana ivābhavat  KAvk tamabravītkṣāntivādī rājan manyurna me ṇvapi karmarekhāparicchedādīdṛśī bhavitavyatā  KAvk sarvāṇi na gaṇayati svacchandā bhavitavyatā na dhairyaṃ na guṇaṃ nārthaṃ na tapo nāpi gauravam  KAvk antrasthitaprasavabījaparaṃparāṇi bhinnāni kālaparipākavicitritāni janmasthale vipulamūlabalasya janturbhuṅkte phalāni nijakarmamahīruhasya  KAvk tvayi tasmānna me kaścid vikāro sti mahīpate satyenānename paśya rudhiraṃ kṣīratāṃ gatam  KAvk aṅgacchede pyakaluṣi babhūva yadi me manaḥ satyenaitena ściṣṭāni tānyevāṅgāni santu me  KAvk iti śuddhadhiyastasya tībrasayopayācanāt śliṣṭānyaṅgāni tānyeva sahasā sv āsthyamāyayuḥ  KAvk mukuṭaspṛṣṭacaraṇastamuvāca nṛpastataḥ mune mahāprabhāvo si tapasā tatkimicchasi  KAvk puṇyahastāvalambena mphāndhaṃ karuṇānidhe pāpāvasāne patitaṃ māṃ tvamuddhartumarhasi  KAvk ityarthitaḥ kṣitīśena pratyabhāṣata taṃ muniḥ saṃtāraṇāya magnānāṃ baddhānāmapi muktaye  KAvk āśvāśanāya bhītānāṃ nirvāṇāya vimuhyatām  KAvk yadā tu samyaksaṃbodhiṃ tāmavāpnoṣyanuttarām mohacchedaṃ kariṣyāmi tadā jñānāsinā KAvk iti sugatamukhāravindanirmitamadhuramadhupratimaṃ vacaḥ prasannam bhramarabhava ivoditapramodaḥ kimapi babhūva nipīya bhikṣusaṃghaḥ  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ KAvk prasādaḥ kriyatāṃ deva mṛgaṃ saṃdarśayāmyamah dṛṣṭaḥ kanakasārāṅga sāraṅgaḥ samayā vane  KAvk ityākarṇya kṣitipatiḥ praharṣitphullalocanaḥ bhadra saṃdarśaya kkāsau kkāsāvityavadanmuhuḥ  KAvk svasthaṃ bhavatu me param  KAvk satyopayācaneneti sahasaivāsya locanam dvitīyamapi vaimalyamavāpa saha cetasā  KAvk tato viditavṛttena puṇyasenena bhūbhujā kṛtasāhāyyakaḥ prāpa svarājya sa priyāsakhaḥ  KAvk kalyāṇkārī yaḥ so haṃ devadattaḥ sa cānujaḥ tena pūrvānubhāvena tadvidho dyāpi vartate  KAvk ityudāramupakāranirmalaṃ bodhisattvacaritaṃ niśamya te bhikṣavaḥ khalviceṣṭitaṃ ca tattulyamapratimavismayaṃ yayuḥ  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ kalyāṇākāryavadānamekatriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  viśākhāvadānam vāmāḥ sajjanavāmāḥ prāyeṇa bhavanti nīrogiṇyaḥ timironmukhī sarāgā kṣipati raviṃ bhūdharātsaṃdhyā  KAvk devadattasya carite bahujanmāntarāśraye kathite pi punaḥ prāha bhagavān jñānasāgaraḥ  KAvk purā kaliṅgaviṣaye nṛpatiḥ śatrubhaṅgakṛt śrīmānabhūdaśokākhyaḥ prakhyātāsaṃkhyavikramaḥ  KAvk tasya śākhaḥ praśākhaśca catvāraḥ sadṛśāḥ sutāḥ anuśākho viśākhaścetyabhavan bhuvi viśrutāḥ  KAvk tāruṇyamattāste pitrā sapatnīkāḥ pravāsitāh savikāranikāreṇa putrasneho pi naśyati  KAvk te śanaiḥ kṣīṇapātheyā durdaśāmiva duḥsahām vikaṭāmaṭavīṃ prāpyaṃ kṣutkṣāmāḥ samacintayan  KAvk etāḥ striyo vipatkāle gulphabandhanaśṛṅkhalāḥ kṛcchralabdhe ca bhāginyaḥ sthitāḥ parṇāśane pi naḥ  KAvk iti cintayatāmāsīt teṣāṃ strībadhaniścayah durdaśādagdhabhāgyānāṃ ghorā saṃjāyate matiḥ  KAvk teṣāṃ madhyādviśākhastu pāpasaṃkalpaśaṅkitaḥ bhāryāmādāya kṛpayā palāyya prayayau pṛthak  KAvk sā kalaṅkavatī nāma bhṛśaṃ vaiklavyamāgatā dūrādhvadhāvanaśrāntā mūrcchitā nyapatadbhuvi  KAvk tataḥ sā karuṇārdreṇa bhartrā prāṇakṣayakṣaṇe śarāvedhasamudbhūtaṃ pāyitā nijaśoṇitam  KAvk tām raktapānasaṃprāptajīvitām sattvasāgaraḥ svāṅgaṃ niṣkṛtya māṃsena prāṇavṛttimakārayat  KAvk nirjalaṃ ghorakāntāraṃ samuttīrya krameṇa tau pracchāyapādapaśyāmaṃ prāptau girinadītaṭam  KAvk viśrāntayostayostatra kṛttapādakaro naraḥ tīvrākrandī nadīvegenohyamānaḥ samāyayau  KAvk dṛṣṭvaiva karuṇāśliṣṭaḥ kaṣṭāṃ vipadamāśritaḥ vigāhya saritaṃ dorbhyāṃ viśākhastamatārayat  KAvk tataḥ pratyāgataprāṇāṃ toyamūlaphalādibhiḥ sa taṃ cakre dinaireva saṃrūḍhacchedanirvyatham  KAvk svastho pi gativaikalyānnaiva gantuṃ kkacit kṣamaḥ sa tasthaui tatra tatpatnyā kāle kalitabhojanah  KAvk rājaputrastu jāyāyāmabhūdviralasaṃgamaḥ siṃhālparatayaḥ śūrāḥ prāyeṇa vijigīṣavaḥ  KAvk divyauṣadhirasāhāraparipūrṇatanuḥ śanaiḥ tatpatnī vikalāyāsmau cakāra surataspṛhām  KAvk snehena nopalipyante na badhyante guṇena ca gurave na ca sajjanti svecchasparśasukhāḥ striyaḥ  KAvk sā tena niśi niḥśabdaṃ ramamāṇā ghanastanī niḥśaṅkasuratātṛptā patiṃ vighnamamanyata  KAvk sā patyuḥ svairiṇī tena vidadhe vadhasaṃvidam pāpeṣu śikṣākuśalāḥ kaluṣāḥ kila yoṣitaḥ  KAvk sā śiraḥśūlamatulaṃ vadantī svasya chadmanā cakre likhitapāpāsyā lalāṭe paṭṭabandhanam  KAvk tasyāḥ śirorujāṃ tīvrāṃ vyatītaḥ pārthivātmajaḥ kāruṇyāttatpratīkāre tāṃ tāṃ yuktimacintayat  KAvk viṣādacintāstimitaṃ śvasantaṃ sā jagād tam śītārtakūjadbhramarā himamlāneva padminī  KAvk evaṃvidhaṃ me kanyāyāh śiraḥśūlaṃ purābhavat pāṣāṇabhedalepena bhiṣagbhiśca nivāritam  KAvk pāṣāṇabhedavyāpto yaṃ prāgbhāgo sy mahībhṛtaḥ rājjvāvatīrya bhavatā gṛhyatāṃ yadi śakyate  KAvk dhārayiṣyāmi pāṇibhyāmahamālambanaṃ tava ityuktaḥ praṇayātpatnayā tathetyāha nṛpātmajaḥ  KAvk tatpāṇidhṛtarajjvātha vihitālambanaḥ śanaiḥ so vatīrṇaḥ śilāsphālagarjadgirinadītaṭam  KAvk bheṣajādānasaṃsaktaḥ saṃtyaktālambanastayā sa papāta mahāśvabhre strīcittacapalāmbhasi  KAvk śubhasya karmaṇaḥ śeṣādabhagnatanureva saḥ uhyamānaḥ pravāheṇa dhīraścitamacintayat  KAvk nārīcittābhamāvartaṃ darśayantyā nijāśayam mama strīniyame nūnamupadeśaḥ kṛto nayā  KAvk durvijñeyāḥ pratatamatibhiḥ svapnasaṃkalpakalpārāgadveṣavyasanaviṣamāyāsavinyāsasaktāḥ kāmātkāmī sakalajanatāmohane saṃpravṛttāḥpātāyaiva kṣasṇaparicitasyāpi māyāḥ striyaśca  KAvk iti saṃcintayanneva nadīvegena bhūyasā prāpitaḥ sukṛteneva sa purīṃ puṣkarāvatīm  KAvk tasminnavasare tatra niṣputre nṛpatau mṛte nimittajñairmahāmātyairgṛhītaḥ sa sulakṣaṇaḥ  KAvk abhiṣiktaḥ sa taistatra vidhivanmaṅgalodakaiḥ abhūdvivāhavidveṣī dṛṣṭastrīcaritādbhutaḥ  KAvk kalaṅkavatyapi girau bodhisattvavivarjite mandvīryauṣadhiḥ kāle vṛtticchedākulābhavat  KAvk skandhe bhagnāṅgamāropya sā grāmapuravartmasu janaṃ pativratāsmīti girā bhikṣāmayācata  KAvk parivratāgauraveṇa sarvastasyau dadau bahu mithyāśīlapravādo pi sūte vipadi saṃpadam  KAvk aṭantī sā śanaiḥ prāptā nagarīṃ puṣkarāvatīm satīti vanditā sarvairvṛpadvārāntike yayau  KAvk rājā strīvṛttavidveṣī vandate tu pativratām iti saṃcintya tadbhaktyā nṛpaṃ prāha puhohitaḥ  KAvk dūredeśāntarāddeva prāptā kāpi pativratā yayeyaṃ caraṇanyāsairbhūtadhātrī pavitritā  KAvk he deva paśya tāṃ śādhvīṃ skandhāropitabhartṛkām pativratāpraṇāmena puṃsāmāyurvivardhate  KAvk nṛpaḥ purohiteneti tatsaṃdarśanamarthitaḥ tamuvāca na jānīṣe brāhmaṇaḥ sarale bhavān  KAvk snigdhā strīti pravādo yaṃ nirvyājeti matibhramaḥ satīti vyomapuṣpāptiḥ pāpā strīti na saṃśayaḥ  KAvk niṣphalāścagnurohiṇyaḥ saralā janasaṃgame nāryo vetasavallarya iva nirmūlabandhanāḥ  KAvk bhedadrohaikaśīlābhyo duḥśīlābhyaḥ svabhāvataḥ namaḥ strībhyo namaḥ strībhyo namaḥ strībhyo namo namah  KAvk dṛṣṭastrīvṛttadoṣāya taccintāvyathitānmane apyeṣā pṛthivī mahyaṃ ratnapūrṇā na rocate  KAvk nagamṛgavadhūmugdhāstīkṣṇāḥ paraṃ paravañcanetanuvitaraṇe saktāḥ puṃsāṃ haranti ca jīvitam dadhati ca bhayaṃ puṣpāyāte pibanti ca pāvakaṃsaralakuṭilā naiva jñātā vicāraśataiḥ striyaḥ  KAvk tathāpi yadi nirbandhastava paśyāmi tāṃ striyam ityuktvā harmyamāruhya tām dadarśa nareśvaraḥ  KAvk tāmeva sa parijñāya pāpāṃ kṛttāṅgasaṅginīm sacivebhyaḥ kṣitipatistadvṛttāntaṃ nyavedayat  KAvk nṛpaṃ sāpi parijñāya pāpā kṣaṇamadhomukhī nirastā prayayau tūrṇaṃ pihitaśravaṇairjanaiḥ  KAvk viśākhanāmā naranāthasūnuḥ so haṃ vadhūḥ sāsya ca devadattaḥ śrutvetivṛttaṃ kathitaṃ jinena bhikṣuvrajastaccaritaṃ nininda  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ viśākhāvadānaṃ dvātriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  nandīpanandāvadānam sa ko pi puṇyapraśamānubhāvaḥ śuddhātmanāmastyamṛtasvabhāvaḥ yasya prabhāveṇa bhavanti sadyaḥ krūrā api krodhaviṣapramuktāḥ  KAvk purā tathāgate jetavanārāmavihāriṇi tadājñayā bhikṣugaṇe girikānanacāriṇi  KAvk sumerupariṣaṇḍāyāṃ sthitvā dhyānaparāyaṇāḥ āyayurbhikṣavaḥ pāṇḍuvicchāyavadanāḥ kṛśāḥ  KAvk te tha kṛtvā bhagavataḥ pādapadmābhivandanām ūcire bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭā dehadaurbalyakāraṇam  KAvk sumeruṃ triguṇāvṛttyā veṣṭayitvā vyavasthitau adṛṣṭau vainateyasya nāgau nandopanandakau  KAvk tau sadā trividhocchvāsaṃ sṛjataḥ kīrṇapāvakam bhavanti bhasma sparśena sahasaiva śilā api  KAvk vayaṃ tadviṣaniśvāsairnidagdhā dhyānayoginaḥ vivarṇavadanacchāyāh kevalaṃ kṛśatāṃ gatāḥ  KAvk iti taiḥ kathite śāstā bhikṣusaṃghārthitaḥ puraḥ nāgayordamane yogyaṃ maudgalyāyanamādiśat  KAvk sa sumeruṃ samāsādya śṛṅgairāliṅgitāmbaram suptau dadarśa nāgendrau yogenāntarhitākṛtiḥ  KAvk yodhyamānau śanaistena bubudhāte yadā na tau tadā mahānāgavapurbhūtvā sa samaveṣṭayat  KAvk prabuddhau pīḍitau tena dṛṣṭvā taṃ bhīṣaṇākṛtim viṃdrutau nararūpeṇa tasthaturbhayavihvalau  KAvk nāgarūpaṃ parityajya kṛtvā rūpaṃ svakaṃ tataḥ palāyamānāvanyonyaṃ t au maudgalyāyano vadat  KAvk nāgau kka gamyate tūrṇa bhayaṃ saṃtyajyatāmidam na sa nāgaḥ sthitastatra yena vidrāvitau yuvām  KAvk sarvathā yadi nastyea tadbhayād yivayordhṛtiḥ kriyate kiṃ śaraṇyasya na buddhasyābhivandanam  KAvk iti tenoktamākarṇya vinayāttau tamūcatuḥ prasādaḥ kriyatāmārya bhagavaddarśanena nau  KAvk iti bravāṇau nāgendrau nītvā bhagavato ntikam sa ta dvṛttāntamāvedya praṇamya samupāviśat  KAvk bhagavānatha nāgendrau babhāṣe śaraṇāgatau praṇāmaṃ cakratū ratnaprabhābhūṣītabhūtalau  KAvk śikṣāpadāni saṃprāpya sarvabhūtābhayapradau śaraṇaprāptisamayādadhunā nirbhayau yuvām  KAvk ityālokanamātreṇa doṣadveṣavivarjitau kṛtau bhagavatā samyak jagmatustaṃ praṇamya tau  KAvk saṃdarśanenaiva mahāśayānāṃ prabhāpadeśena śarīralagnaiḥ sīṃsrā api dveṣaviṣoṣmataptāḥ śamāmṛtaiḥ śītalatāṃ vrajanti  KAvk tatpūrvajanmavṛttāṇtaṃ bhikṣubhirbhagavān jinaḥ prabhāvavismayātpṛṣṭaḥ sarvadarśī jagādā tān  KAvk kṛkirnāma purā śrīmān vārāṇasyāṃ nareśvaraḥ kāśyapākhyād bhagavataḥ prāptavān dharmaśāsanam  KAvk amātyayoḥ sa vinyasya rājyaṃ nandopanandayoḥ babhūva bodhisaṃsaktaḥ satyadarśananirvṛtaḥ  KAvk dharmadahrmamayaṃ rājyaṃ kṛtvā tau tasya mantriṇau sarvopakaraṇairyuktaṃ vihāraṃ kāśyapāya ca  KAvk kālena jātau nāgendrāvetau nandopanandakau vihārārpaṇapuṇyena padaṃ merurabhūttayoḥ  KAvk iti jinanigaditaphaṇivaracaritaṃ paratanupariṇatiparicitasukṛtam śrutavati śamanayamuniparinivahe viṣadharaniyamanaguṇanutirudabhūt  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ nandopanandāvadānaṃ trayastriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  gṛhapatisudattāvadānam dattaḥ parahitabhāvanayā yadu tanudhanakaṇaśeṣaḥ aparikṣayaguṇakalpanayā bhavati supuṇyaviśeṣaḥ  KAvk atha vyatīte kasmiṃścit kāle bhagavato ntike nandopanandayordharmadeśanāṃ śrotumāyayau  KAvk rājā prasenajiddraṣṭuṃ bhagavantamupāgataḥ tābhyāmakṛtasatkārapraṇāmaḥ komapāyayau  KAvk sa praṇamya jinaṃ gatvā pradadhyau nigrahaṃ tayoḥ śastravṛṣṭiṃ saṃsṛjantau tau ca vyomnā samāgatau  KAvk sarvajñapreṣitastūraṇaṃ maudgalyāyana etya tām śastravṛṣṭiṃ narapateścakre padmotpalāvalim  KAvk punargatvā bhagavataḥ samīpaṃ pṛthivīpatiḥ saṃprāptau kṣamayāmāsa tasyādeśāt phaṇīśvarau  KAvk athārthitaḥ pārthivena bhagavān rājamandiram bhaktipūtaṃ yayau bhoktuṃ bhaktaṃ bhikṣugaṇaiḥ saha  KAvk bhakṣyeṣu pacyamāneṣu rātrau tatrāgnivilpavaḥ jāto jinaprabhāveṇa sahasā śāntimāyayau  KAvk bhuktvā gate bhagavati kṣitipaḥ svapure bhyadhāt jvalanajvālanaṃ rātrau vārayan daṇḍasaṃvidā  KAvk atrāṇtare gṛhapatiḥ sudattasyātmaji yuvā mithyādoṣadṛddhibalo nāma rājñābhighātitaḥ  KAvk pūrvaṃ bhagavataḥ śāstuḥ śāsanānugraheṇa saḥ labdhajñānadhṛtiḥ putraduḥkhe pyāsīdaduḥkhitaḥ  KAvk aputraḥ svadhanaṃ bhūri dīnebhyaḥ pratipādya saḥ cakārātirasādekapaṇaśeṣaṃ śanaiḥ śriyaḥ  KAvk paṇalābhakṛtāśeṣadharmaḥ svalpaprado tha saḥ abhūd gṛhī sudattākhyo gṛhaṃ hi svaplamucyate  KAvk kadāciddarśanāyātaṃ bhagavān purataḥ sthitam taṃ svalpadānanāmnaiva lajjitaṃ dayayāvadat  KAvk alpadānaṃ gṛhapaterna lajjāṃ kartumarhasi yāti śraddhārpito dānakaṇaḥ kanakaśailatām  KAvk purā bahutaraṃ dattaṃ velamena dvijanmanā śraddhāvirahasāmānyānna tathā vṛddhimāyayau  KAvk yaḥ sarvaṃ bhojayedbhaktyā jambudvīpagataṃ janam yaścaikaṃ bodhisaṃyuktaṃ tasya puṇyaṃ tato dhikam  KAvk iti vākyaṃ bhagavatastathyaṃ śrutvābhinandya ca nijagehaṃ gṛhapatiḥ prayayau praṇipatya tam  KAvk dīpaṃ datvā paṭhan rātrau tatar buddhānuśāsanam daṇḍāya rājapuruṣaiḥ sa nīto gnipravartanāt  KAvk daṇḍasya saṃbhavādbaddhaṃ bandhanāgāravartinam taṃ draṣṭumāyayurdevā rātrau śakrabrahmādayaḥ  KAvk sa tairdhanaṃ gṝhāṇeti prārthito nāgrahīdyadā tadā dharmopadeśo yaṃ pravṛttastsya mandire  KAvk rājāpi tatprabhāveṇa dṛṣṭvā prajvālitaṃ puram muktvā taṃ bandhanāgārānna dadarśa jalaṃ kkacit  KAvk sa gataḥ sugataṃ draṣṭuṃ kadācittatpuraḥ sthitaḥ nṛpaṃ jinapraṇāmāya prāptaṃ paścād vyalokayat  KAvk agre bhagavataścakre praṇayaṃ na sa bhūpateḥ jagatpūjyasya purataḥ pūjāmarhati nāparaḥ  KAvk jinamāmantrya nṛpatiḥ praṇataḥ svapuraṃ gataḥ vivāsanaṃ gṛhapaterādideśa nijāt purāt  KAvk prasādinī sudattasya devatā nṛpatiṃ tataḥ kṣudrajantubhirutsṛṣṭaiścakre daṃśaviṣākulam  KAvk sa trastastairnṛpaḥ prāptaḥ sāmātyāntaḥ purānugaḥ gatvā prasādayāmāsa sudattam jinaśāsanāt  KAvk iti sa satatapratyāsattyā parāmṛtanirbharaṃbhagavaduditaṃ śāntiṃ bheje sudattagṛhādhipaḥ svamiva labhate vighnayāsapravāsavivarjitaṃvimalamanasāmantevāsī vivekamahānidhim  KAvk iti kṣemendravicaritāyāṃ abhavadviṣaye tasya karmāntākarajīvanaḥ gṛhasthaḥ sudhano nāma dhanādhānavicakṣaṇaḥ  KAvk nṛpaḥ kadāciṃdāsthāne taṃ kāryārthinamāgatam vacasaiva parijñāya jagād vihitādaraḥ  KAvk jānāmyahaṃ gṛhapate hiraṇyopacitasvaram vipulaḥ saṃcayajñasya suvarṇanidhirasti te  KAvk ityuktaḥ sasmitaṃ rājñā sa tamūce kṛtāñjaliḥ satyamastyeva me rājan gṛhe kāñcanasaṃcayaḥ  KAvk sadvṛttacintānirate deve vātsalyapeśale kiṃ vā nāsti janāsyāsya pitari tvayi goptari  KAvk dhanino yāntyadhanatāṃ nidhanaṃ yānti cādhanāḥ vyāghratām yāti dedbhūbhṛdāmiṣāghrāṇanirghṛṇaḥ  KAvk niḥsaṅkairarjyate vittamarjitaṃ ca vibhajyate vibhaktaṃ bhujyate spaṣṭaṃ janairdharmadhane nṛpe  KAvk upapannaṃ vacaḥ śrutvā dhīmatastasya bhūpatiḥ tamūce daśanodyotaiḥ prasādaṃ darśayanniva  KAvk matimān kāryasacivastvaṃ me bhavitumarhasi dhīdhūryaistvadvidhaireva dhāryate dharaṇībharaḥ  KAvk iti rājavacaḥ śrutvā śudhanastamabhāṣata n avayaṃ rājasevāsu sabhāmaṇḍalapaṇḍitāḥ  KAvk svācchandyodyānavicchedaḥ sunidrāsukhavikrayaḥ sevā hi puṃsāṃ saṃsāraduḥkhadainyabhayaṃkaraḥ  KAvk īśvarairmastakanyastacaraṇaḥ kṛtakṛtyatām pādapīṭha ivāyāti sevako haṃ sthitaḥ sadā  KAvk sevāyāsaprayāsena prāptānāmapi saṃpadām saṃbhogaḥ piśunāsaṅgī prabhubhrūbhangabhaṅguraḥ  KAvk etāśca nāvatiṣṭhante prayatnena dhṛtā api darpogradurgrahagrāhadurgrahā nṛpasaṃpadaḥ  KAvk kṣaṇaṃ navanavāśliṣaviśeṣapraṇayodyatāḥ avācavāraramaṇīramaṇīyā vibhūtayaḥ  KAvk ityuktapratiṣedho pi sa rājñā sacivaḥ kṛtaḥ atikrāmati ko nāma prabhaviṣṇoḥ samīhitam  KAvk prāptaprauḍhapadaṃ rājñā nītaṃ sarvādhikāritām vidveṣadūṣitāḥ sarve mantriṇastaṃ na sehire  KAvk dharmajijñāsayā rājñā piśunapreritena saḥ naivākarodasatkāryaṃ niyukto pi puna punaḥ  KAvk āghātaṃ prekṣitaḥ so tha mithyākopena bhūbhujā tathāpyadharmasaṃyuktaṃ na śāsanamatanyata  KAvk ekajanmasukhāyaiva bahujanmaśatārditam na sādhuninditaṃ karma karomīti jagāda saḥ  KAvk bhayadharmopadhāśuddhaḥ pratimuktaḥ sa bhūbhujā dānasatramavicchinnamakarodakhilārthinām  KAvk sarvatra viśrute tasya dānasatre yaśasvinah kalpavṛkṣādaraḥ puṃsāṃ paraṃ pratanutāṃ yayau  KAvk atrāntare munigaṇāstīrthārthā dakṣiṇāpathāt āgatā kṛcchrakāntāramaviśan nirjanaṃ vanam  KAvk tatra tṛṣṇāturāḥ sarve mūrcchitāḥ śayanāśritāḥ ayācanta jalaṃ mohāduccairniścetanānapi  KAvk devagandharvanāgebhyaḥ kaścidyo tra dayāmbudhiḥ sthitaḥ prayacchatu jalaṃ so smākamiti te bruvan  KAvk tataḥ sa ratnakeyūrakkanatkaṅkaṇasaddhvaniḥ bhujasthamemabhṛṅgārastarumadhyādviniryayau  KAvk te tasmādamṛtāsvādaṃ pāṇipadmāvanāmitāt ākaṇṭhaṃ salilaṃ pītvā jahṛṣurlabdhajīvitāḥ  KAvk prārthitaḥ punarabhyetya papracchuste savismayāḥ adṛśyavṛkṣanilayādudbhūtaṃ ko bhavāniti  KAvk so bravīdviśrutayaśāḥ śrāvastyāmāśayaḥ śriyaḥ anāthapiṇḍado nāma sarvado sti gṛhādhipaḥ  KAvk saucikena mayā pūrvaṃ tadgṛhāntikavāsinā bhujamudyabhya tadveśma darśitaṃ nityamarthinām  KAvk tena puṇyena devatvaṃ prāpto tra viharāmyaham bāhurmam vibhātyeṣa dakṣiṇaḥ so rthidakṣiṇaḥ  KAvk te tamāmantrya munayaḥ punaḥ saṃprasthitā vane kṣudhitāḥ snigdhasacchāyaṃ dadṛśuḥ pādapaṃ param  KAvk tamapyuccairayācanta bhojanaṃ tadvadeva te uccacāra ca gambhīrā vāṇī vismayakāriṇī  KAvk atra puṣkariṇītīre droṇyāṃ divyānnabhojanam saṃpūrṇamasti tadgatvā bhujyatāṃ yadabhīpsitam  KAvk iti tena samādiṣṭaṃ bhuktvā te divyabhojanam ko bhavaniti papracchustaṃ divyatarusaṃśrayam  KAvk so pyācacakṣe śrāvastyāṃ gṛhastho nāthapiṇḍadaḥ asti tasyāhamabhavaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ saṃghahojane  KAvk caturaḥ paricaryāyāṃ dadhikumbhapracārakaḥ tadbhojanānte saṃprāpte svalpaśeṣānnabhojanaḥ  KAvk bhikṣuṇāṃ gauraveccāraṃ dṛṣṭvāhaṃ rājabhojanam ātmanaścānnamakṣāramabhavaṃ khinnamānasaḥ  KAvk anāthapiṇḍadagirā bhojane gauravāśayā tato mayāṣṭāṅgayuktaṃ gṛhītaṃ poṣadhaṃ vratam  KAvk asamāptavratenātha bhuktaṃ laulyānmayā niśi tenāhamabhavaṃ loke vijñātaḥ khaṇḍapoṣadhaḥ  KAvk khaṇḍenāpi vratenāhaṃ devaputratvamāgataḥ iti te tadvacaḥ śrutvā munayo vismitā yayuḥ  KAvk acintayan vrajantaste tīvreṇa tapasā vayam suciraṃ kevalaṃ kliṣṭāṃ nādyāpi kuśalaspṛśaḥ  KAvk adhunā poṣadhaṃ prāptuṃ vratameva yatāmahe nirapāyasukhopāye svahite kasya nādaraḥ  KAvk iti saṃcintayantaste kauśāmbīmabhito gatāḥ sudhanasya gṛhaṃ prāpurviśrutaṃ gṛhamedhinaḥ  KAvk tatra tena kṛtātithyā nivedyāsmai tadadbhutam anāthapiṇḍadaṃ draṣṭuṃ tenaiva sahitā yayuḥ  KAvk śrāvastyām te samāsādya pūjitāstena sādaram asmai nyavedayan sarvaṃ yathādṛṣṭaṃ yathāśrutam  KAvk sa tān vratārthina sarvān suhṛdaṃ sudhanaṃ ca tam nināya dharmasacivaḥ prīto bhagavato ntikam  KAvk bhagavānapi tadvākyāccakre teṣāmanugraham satyadarśanasaṃbuddhā yena te sugatiṃ yayuḥ  KAvk teṣu yāteṣu sudhanaṃ pakṣapātādrayā dṛśā vilokya bhagavān samyag vidadhe jñānabhājanam  KAvk satyasaṃdarśanāvāptaviśeṣakuśalodayaḥ gatvā jināya kauśāmbyām sa vihāramakārayat  KAvk yasmādbhagavatādiṣṭastasmin yātaḥ sahāyatām bhikṣuścundābhidhastasmāt so bhūccundavihārabhūḥ  KAvk rādhābhidhā tadā dāsī vihāraparicārikā dayayā bhagavānasyāḥ śīrṇavastraṃ samagrahīt  KAvk adāsī syāmiti śraddhāpraṇidhānārpitastayā sa cīvaro bhagavataḥ prayayāvekavarṇatām  KAvk sudhanasyojjvalaṃ dṛṣṭvāṃpuṇyasaṃbhāramadbhutam bhikṣubhirbhagavān pṛṣṭastatpūrvodayamabhyadhāt  KAvk sundhānākhyo gṛhapatirvārāṇasyāmabhūtpurā nodārakuznjarasyābhūd yasya dānaparikṣayaḥ  KAvk anāvṛṣṭihate kāle tasya dvādaśavārṣike avāritamabhūcchatramavicchinnānnamarthinām  KAvk tasya padmākaro nāma koṣāgārapatirgṛhe dānasāhāyyakaṃ cakre sahasthā hi samṛddhayaḥ  KAvk pratyekabuddhasaṃghasya bhaktakālanivedakah dharmadūtābhidhastasya mantrī dhīmānapasthitaḥ  KAvk karmavyākṣepatastasya jāte kālavyatikrame kadācit kukurasteṣāṃ kālasaṃjñāṃ vyadhātpuraḥ  KAvk sundhāno dya sa evāhaṃ koṣṭhiko nāthapiṇḍadaḥ saṃghasya dharmadūto yaḥ sa evodayano nṛpaḥ  KAvk saṃjñānideśako yaśca kukuraḥ sudhano pi saḥ rājñā ghoṣeṇa vijñāto ghoṣilāparanāmabhṛt  KAvk caritamityucitaṃ bhavabhedinā bhagavatā kathitaṃ kila bhikṣavaḥ sukṛtasaurabhasārasudhārasaṃ sumanasā śravaṇāñjalibhiḥ papuḥ  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ ghoṣilāvadānaṃ pañcatriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  pūrṇāvadānam vibudhasarasiḥ padmaiḥ śobhite paṅkajinyā śuciparisarajātaṃ spṛśyate na sthale bjam  sahajaparicitānāṃ nityamantargatānām bhavati sitaguṇānām kāraṇaṃ naiva jātiḥ  KAvk śrāvastyāṃ sarvasattvānāṃ svastidhyānaparāyaṇe jinakalpadrume jetavanārāmasthite purā  KAvk śūrpārakākhye nagare ratnasaṃcayasāgaraḥ bhavo nāmābhavatsārthaparirmatimatāṃ varaḥ  KAvk bhavilo bhavabhadraśca bhavanandī ca viśrutāḥ ketakyāṃ tasya jāyāyāṃ babhūvustanayāstrayaḥ  KAvk rogayogādupagaraḥ sa kadācinmumūrṣutām pāruṣyād bhṛśamudvignaiḥ patnīputrairupekṣitaḥ  KAvk bhaktyā dāsī tu tasyaikā paricaryāparā param mallikākhyābhavattasyāḥ sevayā svāsthyamāyayau  KAvk snehopakārapraṇataḥ kṛtajñaḥ sa tayānvitaḥ ṛtau saṃgamamabhyetya tasyāḥ putramajījanat  KAvk yadā tajjanmani pituḥ sarvārthāḥ pūrṇatām yayuḥ sa tadā pūrṇanāmābhūdbālaḥ pūrṇendusundaraḥ  KAvk jyeṣṭhāstrayaḥ kṛtidvāhā yayurabdhiṃ dhanārthinaḥ pūrṇastu bhāṇḍaśālāyāṃ pituścakre dhanārjanam  KAvk tataḥ pratinivṛttāste prāptārthaḥ sāgarātpunaḥ gaṇanāṃ hemalakṣāṇāṃ kṛtvā svamudire puram  KAvk samudragamane teṣām yāvānāsīddhanāgamaḥ pūrṇasya svagṛhe paṇyaurbabhūvābhyadhikastataḥ  KAvk taddṛṣṭvā janakasteṣāṃ vṛddhaḥ paryantavāsare tamūcehitamāyatyāṃ tṛṣṇā naikakṣayodayaḥ  KAvk dṛṣṭaṃ bhavadbhiḥ sāmudralābhe kṛtapariśramaiḥ pūrṇenoārjitaṃ vittamakleśena mahīyasā  KAvk śubhakarmavipākena bhavantyarthā dhanārthinām hastāt palāyate nyasya prāpnoti patitaṃ paraḥ  KAvk sanmārgasyāparityāgād yuktāyuktavivecanāt deśakālaparijñānātsatāṃ sarvatra saṃpadaḥ  KAvk bhavanti svagṛhe śanyāḥ sudhiyo dharmabhāginaḥ gatvā ratnākaraṃ cānye labhante prāṇasaṃśayam  KAvk yatnena boddhavyā sadbhiḥ dhanasyopaniṣtparā adrohaśuddhabuddhīnāṃ svādhīnānāṃ dhanācchriyaḥ  KAvk rakṣaṇīyo bhavadbhiśca bhedaḥ satatasaṃhateḥ bhinnāt skhalati kalyāṇaṃ kulāt kumbhādivodakam  KAvk athābhinnendhanasyāgnernaśyante sadṛśāstviṣaḥ tathā vipulavaṃśasya bhinnajñātervibhūtayāḥ  KAvk bhrātṝṇāṃ saṃtato bhedaḥ kathaṃ nāma nivartate adhyāpitānāṃ patnībhirdveṣavidyāṃ sadā niśi  KAvk unnatānāṃ svavaśānāṃ dvaidhaṃ tāvanna jāyate yāvatkuṭhāradhāreva yoṣidviśati nāntaram  KAvk bhrāturarthānuvādena guruṃ pāruṣyakutsayā mitramekābhilāṣeṇa nayanti dvaidhatāṃ striyaḥ  KAvk tadvadanti hasantyo pi bhrūvilāsena yoṣitaḥ yatprayāti suhṛtsnehamūlonmūlanahetutām  KAvk hitamuktveti putrāṇāṃ bhūtaye bhimataṃ bhavaḥ anityatāpariyuktaḥ kāle nidhanamāyayau  KAvk avibhakte dhane śaktā deśāntaradhanārjane jyeṣṭhā babhūvuḥ pūrṇastu gṛhe vittamacintayat  KAvk kālena gṛhamāptānām vastrāśanavivādinām strīmantradattakarṇānāṃ bhedasteṣāmajāyata  KAvk vitte vibhajyamāne th atairvidveṣavaśīkṛteḥ dāsīsuto yamtyuktvā nītaḥ pūrṇo niraṃśatām  KAvk so pi pūrṇaśanaḥ kāle śītasaṃkucitaṃ pathi dadarśa grīṣmatāpr pi vivaśaṃ dārubhārakam  KAvk ādāya dārumūlyena sa tasmāddārubhārakam divyacandanamadrākṣīddahanasyāpi śītadam  KAvk sukṛtenaiva mahatā tena labdhamahādhanaḥ sa sevyaḥ sārthavāhānāṃ pūjyo bhūtpṛthivīpateḥ  KAvk ratnākaraṃ sa ṣaṭkṛtvaḥ prayātaḥ sarvado rthinām cakāra sarvavaṇījāṃ taraśulkādyanugraham  KAvk srhāvastīvāsibhiḥ sārthavaṇigbhiḥ punararthitaḥ yayau pravahaṇārūḍhaḥ samudradvīpamāśu saḥ  KAvk pratyāvṛtte pravahaṇe so tha śuśrāva gāyatām vaṇijāṃ sthāvirāḥ śailagāthāḥ sugatasaṃśrayāḥ  KAvk kasyaitā iti te tena pṛṣṭāḥ sarve babhāṣire etā bhagavatā gītā gāthā buddhena dhīmatā  KAvk iti buddhābhidhāmeva śrutvā harṣamavāpa saḥ puṃsāṃ svavāsanārūḍhaṃ vyaktimāyātyudīritam  KAvk tairvistareṇa kathitāmākarṇya bhagavatkathām so bhavattadgatamanāstaddarśanasamutsukaḥ  KAvk sa śanairgṛhamāgatya tyaktvā sarvaparicchadam anāthapiṇḍadaṃ draṣṭuṃ śrāvastyāṃ suhṛdaṃ yayau  KAvk abhilāṣaṃ nivedyāsmai pravrajyāyāṃ jitendriyaḥ jagāma sahitastena bhaktyā bhagavato ntikam  KAvk dṛṣṭvaiva tatra sarvajñaṃ mohadhvāntadivākaram tatpādadarśanenaiva mene sa kṛtakṛtyatām  KAvk vijñāya tasya bhagavān saṃkalpaṃ tamabhāṣata daśanajyotsnayā kurvan vivekavimalā diśaḥ  KAvk ehi bhikṣi nirāśaṅke nirvipakṣe kṣayojjhite ākhyāte dharmavinaye brahmacaryāṃ carepsitam  KAvk iti prasādaśīlena jinenodīrite purah pravrajyā sahasaivāsya papātālakṣitā tanau  KAvk tataḥ sa śatrau mitre ca praśamāt samatāṃ śritaḥ śāstuḥ śāsanamādāya praṇipatya jagāma tam  KAvk śroṇāparāntakaṃ nāma deśaṃ śrūrajanāśrayam svayaṃ parīkṣituṃ kṣāntiṃ janena sa samāyayau  KAvk tato dṛṣṭvā tamāyāntaṃ mṛgayāyāmamaṅgalam lubdhakaścāpamākṛṣya hantuṃ kridhāt samādravat  KAvk nirvikāraṃ nirudvegaṃ sa taṃ vigatasādhvasam prahareti bruvāṇaṃ ca dṛṣṭvaiva śamamāptavān  KAvk śāmyatastasya sahasā prasādī lubdhakasya saḥ dharmaṃ dideśa yenāsau bodhiṃ prāpa sahānugaiḥ  KAvk sa tatra sugatārhāṇāṃ sarvopaskarasaṃpadām śatāni paznca ramyāṇāṃ vihārāṇāmakārayat  KAvk pūrṇo pi jñānasaṃpūrṇaḥ prāptistridaśapūjyatām vairāgyalakṣmyā yukto bhūnmunīnāṃ spṛhaṇīyayā  KAvk atha tasyāgrajo bhrātā bhavilaḥ kṣīṇavittatām kālenopagataḥ prāyāt samduraṃ draviṇāśayā  KAvk tataḥ pravahaṇārūḍhaḥ so nukūlaiḥ samīraṇaiḥ gośīrṣacandanavanaṃ prāpitaḥ svalpavāsaraiḥ  KAvk kuṭhārikaśataistasmin pañcabhiśchettumudyate taccandanavanaṃ divyaṃ bhujaṅgagaṇāsaṃkulam  KAvk tatsvāmī yakṣasenānāṃ maheśvaraṃ iti śrutaḥ kopādudasṛjad ghoraṃ kālikākhyaṃ mahānilam  KAvk marutā mahatā tena prāpitāḥ prāṇasaṃśayam cakrandurvaṇijaḥ sarve śarvaśakramukhān surān  KAvk tānārtarāvamukharān bhavilaḥ sārthanāyakaḥ uvāca saṃcintya ciraṃ paścāttāpasamākulaḥ  KAvk pūrṇaḥ kanīyān bhrātā sa hitaiṣī māṃ purāvadat bahukleśo hyalpasukhaḥ kka gantavyastvayāmbudhiḥ  KAvk akṛtvā dhīmatastasya vacanaṃ satyadarśinaḥ cyuto haṃ dhanalobhena ghore smin vyasanārṇave  KAvk śrutvaitadvaṇijaḥ sarve prabhāvaṃ lokaviśrutam pūrṇasya manasā dhyātvā tameva śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ  KAvk namastubhyaṃ jagatkleśaviṣadhoṣāpahāriṇe pūrṇayodīrṇakaruṇāsudhāsaṃpūrṇacetase  KAvk ityekasvararāveṇa teṣāṃ saṃpūrite mbare kṣaṇena gatvā tadvṛttaṃ pūrṇaḥ prāha svadevatāḥ  KAvk śroṇāparāntakagataḥ śrutvā teṣāṃ sa viplavam vyomnā samādhisaṃnaddhaḥ prāpa pravahaṇaṃ kṣaṇāt  KAvk tasmin paryaṅkabandhanena sthito merurivācalah pralayottālavegasya gatiṃ vāhorjahāra sah  KAvk pūrṇena pavanaṃ ruddhaṃ jñātvā yakṣagaṇāgraṇīḥ taṃ prasādya yayau tyaktvā tebhyaścandanakānanam  KAvk pūrṇaprasādādādāya bhavilaścandanadrumān hṛṣṭastenaiva sahitaḥ śūrpāraṃ svapuraṃ yayau  KAvk pūrṇo th saṃmate bhrātustatra gośīrṣacandanaiḥ cakre candanamālākhyaṃ prāsādaṃ sugato citam  KAvk tatra pūrṇena bhagavān dhyātastūrṇaṃ vihāysā samāyayau jetavanādullaṅghya śatayojanīm  KAvk āgacchato bhagavataḥ puraḥprasṛtayā jagat dehakāntyā kapiśitaṃ sarvaṃ himamivābhavat  KAvk puropāntanivāsinyastaṃ vilokya gṛhāṅganāḥ tīvracittaprasādena praśamonmukhatāṃ yayuḥ  KAvk kuśalopacitāṃ tāsāṃ bhagavān satyadeśanām cakre bhavādṛtāṃ kāntāstāh prāpuḥ kuśalaṃ yayuḥ  KAvk ṛddhyā bhagavatastatra caityaṃ paurāṅganābhidham tābhirvihitamadyāpi vandante caityavandakāḥ  KAvk munīnāṃ bhagavān kṛtvā tathā valkalino muneḥ pravrajyānugrahaṃ śuddhāṃ vidadhe dharmadeśanām  KAvk tataścandanamālākhyaṃ prāsādaṃ bhagavān jinaḥ praviśya sphāṭikaṃ cakre janasaṃghabharakṣamam  KAvk atha ratnāsanāsīnaḥ sa tatra karuṇānidhiḥ vidadhe sarvasattvānāṃ śāntyai nirvāṇadeśanām  KAvk atrāntare sānucarau munīndrau kṛṣṇāgautamau abhyetya dharmaśravaṇeśāstuḥ śāsanamāpatuḥ  KAvk tatra kṛtvātha bhagavān prāsādasya pratigraham punarjetavanaṃ gacchannudyayau saha bhikṣubhiḥ  KAvk vrahan mārīcilokasthām maudgalyāyanamātaram sagdirā cāryasatye tāṃ dharmamārge nyaveśayat  KAvk atha jetavanaṃ prāptaṃ bhagavantaṃ savismayāḥ pūrṇasya puṇyaṃ papracchurbhikṣavaḥ so pyabhāṣata  KAvk kāśyapasya purā samyaksaṃbuddhasyānyajanmani vihārādhikṛtaḥ pūrṇaḥ saṃghopasthāyako bhavat  KAvk sa kadācidasaṃmṛṣṭāṃ dṛṣṭvā vaihārikīṃ bhuvam prāha pravrajitaṃ tīvraṃ krodhādupadhivārikam  KAvk dṛptasyopadhivāro dya vihāro sminnamārjitaḥ kasya dāsīsutasyeti bruvāṇastamabhartsayat  KAvk tena pāruṣyapāpena bhuktvā narakadurgatim dāsīsuto bhavat pūrṇaḥ pañca janmaśatāni saḥ  KAvk saṃghopāsanamevāsya puṇyāyābhūnmahīyasā arhattvaṃ yena niḥśeṣabhavakleśojjhitaḥ śritaḥ  KAvk iti prabhāvaṃ kathitaṃ jinena pūrṇasya puṇyopacayapraṇitam śrutvādbhutaṃ saṃsadi bhikṣusaṃghaḥ puṇyaprasaṃśābhirato babhūva  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyām pūrṇāvadānaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  mūkapaṅgvavadānam ākiṃcanyasukhāya niḥspṛhatayā vairāgyalakṣmījuṣaḥsarvaṃ yānti vihāya kāyasacivāḥ santaḥ praśāntyai vanam tatrāpi vrataḍambare parikarārambhāya cet saṃcayastatkaḥ kośaparicchadopakaraṇairgehe parādhaḥ kṛtaḥ  KAvk jine jetavanārāmavihārābhirate purā śākyarājakumārāṇāṃ pravrajyāsaṃjuṣāṃ puraḥ  KAvk citracīvarasatpātrayogapaṭṭādisaṃcayam prabhūtataramālokya bhagavān samacintayat  KAvk aho bataiṣāṃ nādyāpi bandhaheturnivartate abhimānamayaḥ kāye priyaḥ parikaragrahaḥ  KAvk kāye kāyapariṣkārastasyopakaraṇāvalī tasyāḥ parikarādānamaho nu bandhaśṛnkhalā  KAvk iti saṃcintya bhagavān naikāntavihitasthitiḥ kāruṇyādupasannānāṃ kuśalāya samudyataḥ  KAvk māsatrayamupasthānaṃ kartavyaṃ yena kenacit adarśanāya bhikṣūṇāmakaroditi saṃvidam  KAvk pravṛtte niyame tasmin bhikṣurāraṇyakavrataḥ āyayāvupasenākhyaḥ kāryārthaṃ tanucīvaraḥ  KAvk pravāritaḥ sa saṃprāpya dhanyaḥ sugatadarśanam kṛtakṛtyaḥ kṣasṇaṃ sthitvā pratasthe praṇipatya tam  KAvk vrajantametya papracchurbhikṣavaḥ parivārya tam tavārya darśanamaho dattaṃ bhagavatā katham  KAvk māsatrayaṃ darśane sya niyamaḥ śāsanena yaḥ sa kathaṃ bhavatā bhagnaḥ saṃghasyonmārgagāminā  KAvk śrutvā tadvacanaṃ teṣāmupasenaḥ smitottaram tānuce n amayā kaścit kṛtaḥ samayaviplavaḥ  KAvk ahamukto bhagavatā darśanāvasare svayam āraṇyakasya me bhikṣorniṣedho nāsti darśane  KAvk paricchadopakaraṇatyāganirmuktabandhanāḥ avāryadarśanā vṛkṣamūlikāḥ pāṃśukūlikāḥ  KAvk idamadya paraṃ prātariti ye saṃcaye ratāḥ pātravīcaravargeṣu teṣāṃ nāstīha darśanam  KAvk pāthobhiḥ prasarattuṣāraśiśiraistṛṣṇāturāste paraṃte nityaṃ ca nidhānadhāmni vivṛte pyanyādalaṃ durgatāḥ teṣāṃ candanapādapādupanataḥ saṃtāpakaḥ pāvakoyaireṣa praśamavratopakaraṇe baddho bhimānagrahaḥ  KAvk ityuktamupasenena śrutvā te śākyabhikṣavaḥ vailakṣyakṣayitotsāhāḥ sahasaiva vyacintayan  KAvk etadbhagavatādiṣṭamasmānuddhiśya nāparān vicitracīvaracayaprāvārā vayameva yat  KAvk viratecchāḥ priyāh śāsturmahecchā vayamapriyāḥ tasmādicchāṃ parityajya bhavāmastasya saṃmatāḥ  KAvk iti saṃcintya te sarve cārucīvarasaṃcayam prāvṛtyābhyadhikaṃ tyaktvā yayurbhagavato ntikam  KAvk icchāvirāme bhagavān vyadhātteṣāmanugraham jñānavajreṇa satkāyadṛṣṭiśailaṃ bibheda yaḥ  KAvk śākyarājakumārāṇāṃ śrotaḥprāptiphalaspṛśām bhikṣubhiḥ pūrvavṛttāntaṃ pṛṣṭaḥ prāha tathāgataḥ  KAvk vārāṇasyāmabhūtpūrvaṃ brahmadatto mahīpatiḥ dānārdrahasto yadbāhuḥ kṣmāmadhāddigdvipopamaḥ  KAvk tasya brahmāvatī muktālateva guṇaśālinī kīrtiḥ satpuruṣasyeva viśrutā vanitābhavat  KAvk pratibimbopamaṃ patyuḥ sā sutaṃ vimalāśayā jalakrīḍāgatā kāle suṣuve divyalakṣaṇam  KAvk udakākhyaḥ sa bālo bhūt saṃjātaḥ salilāntare vardhamānaḥ pitustulyaṃ yauvarājyānorathaiḥ  KAvk śatāni pañcāmātyānāṃ tasya janmadinaṃ samam avāpustulyarūpāṇāṃ putrāṇām śatapañcakam  KAvk nijaṃ jātismaraḥ smṛtvā prāgvṛttaṃ sa śiśuḥ śanaiḥ acintayat prāptakālaṃ hitaṃ sukṛtamātmanaḥ  KAvk ṣaṣṭivarṣāṇi kṛtvā tu yauvarājyamahaṃ purā abhavaṃ kṛcchrasaṃtaptaściraṃ narakasaṃkaṭe  KAvk janmanyasminnapi punaryauvarājyamupasthitam sarvathā prārthyamāno pi na kariṣyāmi pātakam  KAvk iti saṃcintya sa ciraṃ rājabhogaparāṅmukhaḥ piturudvegajananīmagrahīt paṅgumūkatām  KAvk sarvalakṣaṇayukto pi rājavṛtterabhājanam sa mūkapaṅgurnāmābhūd bandhūnāṃ duḥkhavardhanaḥ  KAvk prāpteṣu mantriputreṣu śastraśāstrabalodayam rājaputraḥ pravṛddho pi nodatiṣṭhanna cāvadat  KAvk pṛṣṭastataḥ kṣitīśena vaidyāstaddoṣabheṣajam avadan vaikalyaṃ rājan rājasūnorna dṛśyate  KAvk abhyāsādyadi jāto sya doṣo pi sukhasevinaḥ tadeṣa bhayasaṃvegāduttiṣṭhati ca vakti ca  KAvk iti vaidyairabhihitaṃ tathetyuktvā kṣitīśvaraḥ mithyaiva vadhyavasudhāṃ bhayāya vyasṛjatsutam  KAvk sa bhartsyamānah puruṣaistamuvāca rathasthitam api kaścidvasatyasyāṃ vārāṇasyāṃ na vā janaḥ  KAvk iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā tairnītaḥ sa nṛpāntikam tatra pitrārthyamāno pi mūka evābhavat punaḥ  KAvk punarvadhyabhuvaṃ nītaḥ śavaṃ dṛṣṭvā jagād saḥ astyeṣa jīvati śavaḥ kiṃ vā sarvātmanā mṛtaḥ  KAvk śrutvaitat taiḥ pituḥ pārśve nyasto maunaṃ vyadhātpunaḥ punarvadhabhayāccaiva nītaḥ provāca tān pathi  KAvk rāśirya eṣa dhānyasya sa hi bhukto nubhujyate ityuktavākyo pi punarnoce kiṃcit pitu paraḥ  KAvk tataḥ khyātapratikṣepe tasyādiṣṭe mahībhujā so vadadvaradānena vacmi pradbhyāṃ vrajāmi ca  KAvk athāsya rājñā hṛṣṭena varadāne pratiśrute sa padbhyāṃ svayamabhyetya spaṣṭaṃ pitaramabravīt  KAvk nāhaṃ paṅgurna mūko haṃ naiva cāhaṃ jaḍāśayaḥ kiṃtu janmāntarakleśaṃ smṛtvā vaihvalyamāśritaḥ  KAvk yauvarājyasukhaṃ bhuktvā ṣaṣṭivarṣāṇyahaṃ purā ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi nyavasaṃ narakodare  KAvk rājabhītyā mayā tasmāt kṛteyaṃ mūkapaṅgutā pravrajyayā brahmacaryaṃ carāmyeṣa varo mama  KAvk iti tenoktamākarṇya tamuvāca mahīpatiḥ amūka ityāptadhṛtirvirakta iti duḥkhitaḥ  KAvk dharmamūlamidaṃ rājyaṃ putra na tyaktumarhasi yajñadānaprajātrāṇaiḥ puṇyapūrṇā nṝpaśriyaḥ  KAvk ekaputrastvayā putra parityāgarasādaham nidrādaridratām nītaḥ śokaśayyāsamāśrayaḥ  KAvk saṃpūrṇacandrarucirāṃ vyaktamauktikahāsinīm kathaṃ saṃpadamutsṛjya pravrajyābhimatā tava  KAvk kathaṃ śayyāḥ parityajya prājyarājyasukhocitāḥ vanāntavāsavyasanī sevase pāṃśulāḥ sthalīḥ  KAvk kāntālīlāmukuramaṇimanmandirīṃ rājadhānīmetāṃ tyaktvānanu vanabhuvaḥ saṃpatadvyāghraghorāḥ sarvaprītyai jaradajagarāśvāsavipluṣṭapatrāḥkliṣṭacchāyāh praviralalatāstāḥ kathaṃ te bhavanti  KAvk pituḥ śrutveti vacanaṃ rājaputrastamabravīt dantakāntādhararuciṃ vairāgyaṃ grāhayanniva  KAvk śītalā nirmalajalāh saṃtoṣaśaśiśītalāḥ vane vairāgyasubhagā bhuvaḥ kasya na vallabhāḥ  KAvk paradārā iva kṣiprasukhāvarjitadurjanāḥ narakapratyayāyāme sāpāyā na priyāḥ priyāḥ  KAvk dhyānaṃ mantraḥ parijñānamindriyāṇāṃ canirjayaḥ rājñāṃ hiṃsāprayatnena yogo yaṃ narakapradaḥ  KAvk hasantyaḥ saṃsāraṃ kusumakalilāḥ kānanabhuvaḥsvabhāvena prītiṃ vidadhati budhānāṃ śamamayīm dṛḍhaṃ cintāśrāṇtā vyajanapavanocchvāsabahulāvibhūtirbhūpānāṃ śiraḥsaktāmanityatām  KAvk anujānīhi māṃ tāta vrajāmyeṣa tapovanam jānīhi sarvabhāvānāṃ śiraḥsaktāmanityatām  KAvk iti putravacaḥ śrutvā tattatheti vicintayan uvācopacitāścaryastaṃ manīṣī mahīpatiḥ  KAvk vivekavimalaṃ putra tvamicchāsi sa cedvanam hitvāme saṃśayaṃ tāvat paścādyuktiṃ kariṣyasi  KAvk vrajatā badhyavaśudhāṃ tiryaguktaṃ tvayā vacaḥ pracuraṃ tadabhiprāyaṃ vaktumarhasi tattvataḥ  KAvk iti kṣitibhujā pṛṣṭaḥ so bravīttanmayoditam vasatyatra na kaścit tvā madvadhādyo nivartayet  KAvk sukṛtī jīvati śavaḥ sa pāpastu mṛto mṛtaḥ prāk puṇyaṃ bhakṣyate mūlāt sadhanairdhānyarāśivat  KAvk ityāśayānmayā tāta taduktaṃ vacanaṃ priyam iti śrutvā kṣitipatistaṃ pariṣvajya sādaraḥ ucitaṃ kriyatām putra kuśalāyetyabhāṣataḥ  KAvk tataḥ sa pitrānujñātaḥ sāśrunetreṇa kānanam prayayau mantriputrāṇāṃ sahitaḥ pañcabhiḥ śataiḥ  KAvk maharṣerantike tatra pravrajyāṃ prāpya sānugah teṣāṃ kālena so paśyat kuṇḍavalkalasaṃcayam  KAvk tataḥsa saṃcayadveṣī tadadarśanasaṃvidā ekākī vijane tasthau kaṃcit kālaṃmahāmatiḥ  KAvk darśanābhāṣaṇe baddhaniyamo pi yadṛcchayā prāptaṃ svāgatamityuktvā papraccha kuśalaṃ mṛgam  KAvk punaśca pūjitaṃ dṛṣṭvā muniṃ tena mṛgavratam amātyatanayāḥ sarve vilakṣāḥ samacintayan  KAvk mṛgo mṛgavrataścāyaṃ pūjitau niṣparigrahau etāvanajinau daṇḍasaṃbḥārāḍambarojjhitau  KAvk etadarthamanenāsmaddarśane niyamaḥ kṛtaḥ vratopakaraṇavyagrānnūnamasyāpi vārayet  KAvk iti saṃcintya sarvaṃ te vratopacārasaṃcayam nadyāṃ prakṣipya vārāyāṃ yayuḥ śuddhāstadantikam  KAvk tyaktvā gṛhabhūvaṃ teṣāmāśayānuśayocitām sa dhātuṃ prakṛtiṃ jñātvā vidadhe dharmadeśanām  KAvk rājaputraḥ sa evāhaṃ śākyāste mantrisūnavaḥ punastyāgopadeśo yamadyāpyeṣāṃ mayā kṛtaḥ  KAvk iti śākyakumāravṛttametat kathitaṃ bhikṣugaṇaḥ svayaṃ jinena avadhārya parāmapūjayat tāṃ karuṇāmāśritavatsalasya tasya  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ mūkapaṅgvavadānaṃ nāma saptatriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  kṣānyavadānam te jayanti dhṛtiśīlinaḥ paraṃ nirvikārarucisūcitādbhutāḥ śeṣavat pṛthulabhāranirvyathāḥ ye vahanti sukṛtakṣamāḥ kṣamām  KAvk purā purā puṇyaviparyayeṇa ripuḥ prajānāṃ janitaprakampaḥ udunbanāmā nibiḍopatāpairyakṣa kṣayāyaiva kṛtakṣaṇo bhūt  KAvk akālakālaṃ tamanāthabandhurlokānukampī bhagavān prasahya śikṣopadeśaṃ śaraṇaṃ prapannaṃ śamābhidhāyī vinaye nyayuṅkta  KAvk tasmin praśānte bhuvanopatāpe draṣṭuṃ prahṛṣṭaḥ sugataṃ sametya saṃcāriṇaṃ nākapatiḥ praṇamya tatkālajātasmitamityuvāca  KAvk kasmādakasmāt smitacandralekhā mukhāmbuje bhāti tavādbhuteyam akāraṇaṃ sattvasudhāsamudrā na lokasāmānyatayām hasanti  KAvk śrutveti vākyaṃ tridaśeśvarasya tat taṃ sarvadarśī bhagavān babhāṣe asmin pradeśe nijapūrvavṛttaṃ smṛtvā smtaṃ jātamidaṃ mamendraṃ  KAvk purā muniḥ kṣāniratirvane sminnuvāsa nirvāsitaroṣadoṣaḥ yo bhūdbhuvo rāgarajaḥsvabhāve vidveṣavānindurivāravinde  KAvk athottarāśādhipatirvasante vanāntarālokanakautukena sāntaḥpuraḥ kelisukhāya kāmī tadāśramopāntamahīmavāpa  KAvk rāgī kalirnāma sa bhūmipālaḥ pādaprahārairvadanāsavaiśca lebhe vilāseṣu nitambinīnāmaśokaśobhāṃ bakulaśriyaṃ ca  KAvk diśastapolopapṛthuprakopabhrūbhaṅgavṛndairiva tāpasānām tatra bhramadbhirbhramarairbabhūvuḥ kāmāgnidhūmairiva sāndhakārāh  KAvk līlāvilolāḥ pavanākulālīstanāvanamrāḥ stabakā latānām raktādharāḥ pāṭalapallavānām prāpurvilāsaṃ lalanā latānām  KAvk rājāṅganāḥ kautukavibhrameṇa vane carantyastamṛṣiṃ vilokya acañcaladhyānasamādhisaktaṃ vimuktarāgaṃ parivārya tasthuḥ  KAvk taddeśamabhyetya nareśvaro tha dṛṣṭvā vabhūbhiḥ parivāritaṃ tam īrṣyāprakopānaladurnirīkṣyaḥ ciccheda tasyāśu sa pāṇipādam  KAvk chinnāṅgavargo pi sa nirvikāraścukopa bhūpāya na nāma dhīraḥ nyavārayat krūrataraṃ ca tasmai gandharvayakṣoragadevasaṃgham  KAvk tataḥ prayāte nṛpatau puraṃ svāṃ sametya sarve munayo vanebhyaḥ taṃ tatra kṛtāvayavaṃ vilokya kṣāntā api krodhadhutā babhūvuḥ  KAvk śāpapradānābhimukhān nivārya kṣantavyamityeva sa tānuvāca kṣāmāsamāliṅgitamānasānām kopakriyābhiḥ kriyate na saṅgaḥ  KAvk vikāravego pi na pāṇipādacchede mamābhūd yadi vītamanyoḥ satyena tenākṣatadeha eva syāmityavādīt sa punaḥ prasādī  KAvk tataḥ kṣaṇāt saṃgatapāṇipādaṃ rūḍhavraṇaṃ pretya sadodayena apūjayat kṣāntiguṇaṃ stavena taṃ devatā sattvasitaiśca puṣpaiḥ  KAvk rājāpi tatkilbiṣakālakūṭavisphoṭasaṃghaṭṭavinaṣṭaceṣṭaḥ pūrotkaṭāvartavivartamānaḥ saṃvartapākaṃ narakaṃ jagāma  KAvk yo bhūtpurā kṣāntiratirmaharṣiḥ so haṃ kaliryaśca sa devadattaḥ atītavṛttasmaraṇena śakra nākāraṇaṃ jātamidaṃ smitaṃ me  KAvk iti bhagavataḥ śrutvā vākyaṃ sa vismayamānasaḥpramadavikacavyaktotsāhā vahannayanāvalīḥ taraṇikiraṇasparśeneva sphuṭaḥ kamalākarastridaśavasatiṃ prītaḥ prāyāt patistridivaikasām  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ kṣāntyavadānamaṣṭatriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  kapilāvadānam atyantamunnatimatāṃ mahatāṃ vināśadoṣasya durjanasamāgama eva hetuḥ kūladrumāḥ kila phalaprasavaiḥ sahaiva sadyaḥ patanti jalasaṃgatibhinnamūlāḥ  KAvk rucirāgāraśālinyām vaiśālyāṃ bhagavān purā valgumatyāstaṭe nadyā vicacāra tathāgataḥ  KAvk tasyāḥ kaivartasarthena gambhīre mbhasi dustare kadācid ghoramakaraḥ kṣiptvā jālaṃ samuddhṛtaḥ  KAvk aṣṭādaśaśirāḥ siḥsadviraprakharānanaḥ nṛṇāṃ sahasrairākṛṣṭaḥ parvatākāravigrahaḥ  KAvk taṃ dṛṣṭvā tatra vitrastāh srastākarṣaṇarajjavaḥ āścaryaniścaladṛśo na tasthurna yayuḥ kṣaṇam  KAvk gaṇanāṃ gahanāścaryaviśeṣaśataśālinām saṃsāre karmavaicitrye vikārāṇāṃ karoti kaḥ  KAvk atrāntare tamuddeśaṃ bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ jinah samāyayau sarvajanatrāṇakṛtakṣaṇah  KAvk savṛddhabālalalanaṃ janaṃ kautukasaṃgatam dṛṣṭvā tatrākarottīre bhagavānāsanagraham  KAvk bhikṣusaṃghaiḥ parivṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā tatra tathāgatam jano bhūdunmukhaḥ sarvaḥ pratyāvṛttaḥ ivodadhiḥ  KAvk taṃ vilokyaiva vinatāḥ kaivartāḥ prāṇibandhanam viśālajālaṃ sahasā saṃsāramiva tatyajuḥ  KAvk matsyakumbhīnakrādisaṃsāraṃ tadgirāmbhasi tyaktvā te viratāṭopā babhūvuḥ kilbiṣadviṣaḥ  KAvk tairnyastaṃ bhagavān dṛṣṭvā mahākamaramagrataḥ taṃ jagāda sṛjan dantakāntyaiva karuṇānadīm  KAvk api tvaṃ kapilaḥ putra kiṃ n asmarasi duṣkṛtam vacoduścaritasyāyaṃ paripāko nubhūyate  KAvk sāpyakalyāṇamitraṃ te jananī kkādya vartate sarvajñenetyabhihitaḥ smṛtvā jātimuvāca saḥ  KAvk vibho bhavāmi kapilaḥ smarāmi nijaduṣkṛtam vacoduścaritasyāyaṃ paripāko nubhūyate  KAvk yātā me narakaṃ mātā narakādeśinī purā ityuktvā makarastatra ruroda paruṣasvaram  KAvk taṃ śokasāgare magnaṃ babhāṣe bhagavān punaḥ akāle kiṃ karomyadya tiryagyonigatasya te  KAvk apuṇyaprārambhe rabhasahasitollāsavihitepramattānāṃ yāte narakaparipākapraṇayitām aśānteḥ saṃtāpaṃ ruditaśaraṇāni pratiniśaṃbhṛśaṃ kleśāveśairdiśati viṣatulyairanuśayaḥ  KAvk kṣaṇaṃ duḥkhakṣayāyaiva mayi cittaṃ prasādaya prasannamānasaḥ kāle yāsyasi tridaśālayam  KAvk śṛṇu vatsa hitaṃ cedaṃ vicārya kuru cetasi anityāḥ sarvasaṃskārāḥ śāntinirvāṇamakṣayam  KAvk ityājñayāḥ bhagavatastasmin yāte prasannatām janasaṃghaḥ sa suciraṃ babhūvāścaryaniścalaḥ  KAvk āryānandaḥ praṇayinā janenābhyarthitastataḥ tatpūrvavṛttaṃ papraccha bhagavantaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ  KAvk sa tena pṛṣṭaḥ provāca vimapajñānalocanaḥ asyākuśalaśīlasya vṛttāntaḥ śrūyatāmayam  KAvk bhadrakākhye purā kalpe varṣāyutayugāyuṣi jane babhūva bhagavān kāśyapākhyastathāgataḥ KAvk kṛkirnāma mahīpālaḥ kalpaśāla ivārthinām abhavat samaye tasmin vārāṇasyāṃ bahupradaḥ  KAvk kadācidvibudhāsthāne sahasrākṣamivāparam āsīnaṃ vādisiṃhākhyastaṃ vidvānāyayau dvijaḥ  KAvk avilambitasaṃprāptadarśanāsanasatkṛtiḥ sa dattāśīrnarapatiṃ śiṣyaśreṇivṛto bhyadhāt  KAvk svasti svastimate budhādhipasabhāsīnāya tubhyaṃ vibholubdhāḥ saccaritāmṛte tava paraṃ saṃdarśane rāgiṇaḥ sadveṣāḥ parabhūpanāmni mukharāste sudguṇodīraṇekasmātsarvaguṇāśrayeṇa bhavatā duṣairvayaṃ yojitāḥ  KAvk yadyācakā api nirantararatnavarṣe nānārthisārthaparipūrakatām prayānti sarvaṃ bhavānupamapuṇyanidhe vadānya nirdainyadānavibhavasya vijṛmbhitaṃ te  KAvk rājan kiṃcitparicitaguṇaiḥ sevayā sadgurubhyaḥprāpto smābhirvibudhavijayī ko pi vidyāṃśaleśaḥ asyāṃ vidvatkamalabharasaumyaprabhāyāṃ sabhāyāṃtasyotkarṣaṃ katipayapadaṃ pratyayaṃ darśayāmaḥ  KAvk nijaguṇagaṇane dhīrlajjate sajjanānāṃ mukharayati tathāpi prauḍhavādābhilāṣaḥ iyati jagati rājan kṣipramānviṣyatām me prativacanaruciśedasti kaścidvipaścit  KAvk saṃdarbhagarbhagambhīramiti tasyotkaṭaṃ vacaḥ śrutvā kṣitipatiḥ kṣipraṃ vilakṣaḥ samacintayat  KAvk aprāptapratimallo yaṃ yadi yāyānmadoddhataḥ tadeṣa mam adeśasya yaśaḥkhaṇḍanadiṇḍimaḥ  KAvk guṇāpamānakṛd yatra mūrkho bhavati bhūpatiḥ na karoti janastatra vidyārjanapariśramam  KAvk vivekavimalāloke dharmārāme mahīpatau loke vidyāḥ pravartante sadācārakriyā iva  KAvk tasmādasya prayatnena kartavyo madanigraha vidyādaridratā deśe doṣa eva viśāṃpateḥ  KAvk iti saṃcintya nṛpatirvipraṃ karvaṭavāsinam ānināya mahāmatyairanviṣaya viduṣāṃ gurum  KAvk abhūbhṛtsabhāmupādhyāya pretya taṃ tarkakarkaśam cakāra vādisiṃhasya darpakesarakartanam  KAvk tasya tena jitasyāśu vijitāśeṣavādinaḥ maunasūtraṃ samāpede lajjiteva sarasvatī  KAvk ārūḍhāḥ śubhramahasaṃ nakṣatrāṇāmivodayāḥ uparyupari dṛśyante guṇotkarṣā manīṣiṇām  KAvk vādisiṃhaṃ visṛjyātha datvā bhūri dhanaṃ nṛpaḥ dadau dvijāya jayine karvaṭaṃ nagaropamam  KAvk labdharājagajāśvo tha carukeyūrakaṅkaṇaḥ upādhyāyaḥ svabhavanaṃ praviveśa saha śriyā  KAvk bhujairjitā bhūmibhujāṃ vaṇijāṃ sāgarārjitāḥ vidyāvatāṃ virājante guṇotkarṣarjitāḥ śriyaḥ  KAvk kālena śrīmatastasya putrajanmotsavo bhavat sukhe pi sukhasaṃpattirlakṣaṇaṃ puṇyakarmaṇām  KAvk kapilo nāma sa śiśustejaḥpiṅgaśiroruhaḥ vardhamānamatirvidvān piturabhyadhiko bhavat  KAvk kule mahati vaiduṣyaṃ vibhavodbhavaḥ vibhave satsutotkarṣaḥ phalaṃ sukṛtaśākhinaḥ  KAvk kadācidvyādhisaṃyogātpratyāsannatanukṣayaḥ vijane putramāhūya so vadat putravatsalaḥ  KAvk bālye guṇārjanaṃ putra paralokasukhārjanam  KAvk uttamarṇa iva prāpte kāle sugaṇitāvadhau adhunā vivaśaḥ kkāhaṃ kka sā vidyā kka taddhanam  KAvk guṇapuṣpe sukhaphale baddhamūle dhanairjane vane vajra ivākālakālaḥ patatiḥ duḥsahaḥ  KAvk kṣapayati sakalābhirjanma vidyākalābhiḥ kṣaṇikasukhanimittaṃ saṃnidhatte ca vittam paśuśiśuṣu manuṣyaḥ prīyate mohaśiṣyaḥ tanuvirahamūrhūrte sarvamanyat sa cānyaḥ  KAvk idaṃ tu te hitaṃ vacmi snehamohavaśīkṛtaḥ saṃsārasāraśaraṇaṃ vatsa vetsi bahuśrutaḥ  KAvk santaḥ praṇamyāḥ paruṣaṇ na vācyaṃ kāryaḥ prayatnena paropakāraḥ pāpāvapāte satataṃ hi puṃsāmetāni puṇyānyavalambanāni  KAvk alobhaśobhābharaṇā vibhūtiradveṣasaktiḥ svasukheṣvamohaḥ mūlatraye smin kuśaladrumasya vasatyaśeṣākhilasatphataśrīḥ  KAvk yāvattapati tīkṣṇāṃśurasmin bhuvanamaṇḍale tāvattvatsadṛśaḥ putra vidvān vādī na vidyate  KAvk bhikṣubhistu na kartavyastvayā vādaḥ kadācanah gambhīrajñānadurbodhaprabuddhā bauddhabuddhayaḥ  KAvk purā bhikṣurmayā pṛṣṭaḥ padasyārthaṃ jahāsa mām praśnaṃ kartuṃ na jānīṣe vidvāniti jagāda ca  KAvk tasmād bhikṣuvivādaste paraṃ pāṇḍityapīḍanam balaprabhāvakāmo hi giriṃ mūrdhnāṃ na tāḍayet  KAvk ityuktvā tanayaṃ vipraḥ paralokabhuvaṃ yayau kāyāvasathapānthānāṃ dehinām na cirasthitiḥ  KAvk vāgmī kālena kapilaḥ khaṇḍitākhilapaṇḍitaḥ nṛpādbahugrṇaṃ prāpa dhanamānamahodayam  KAvk tataḥ kadācidekānte kapilaṃ kācarābhidhā saṃprāptaṃ vādisāmrājyaṃ jagāda jananī śanaiḥ  KAvk vādidarpacchidā putra digdvīpajayinā tvayā durjanāḥ śramaṇāḥ kasmāddarpāndhāḥ parivarjitāḥ  KAvk parotkarṣādhirūḍhasya pratipakṣe kṣamārateḥ akṣamo yamiti vyaktaṃ kṣaṇena kṣīyate yaśaḥ  KAvk iti māturvacaḥ śrutvā so vadad biduṣo vacaḥ na vādaḥ śramaṇaiḥ kāryaḥ pitrāhamiti vāritaḥ  KAvk iyaṃ durjīvikāsmākam patrālambanavādinām kriyate guṇamānyānāṃ mānamlānirmukhe yayā  KAvk dhigetaccaṇḍapāṇḍityaṃ guruvidveṣaduḥsaham mahatāṃ sukhabhaṅgāya sadā tasmin samudyamaḥ  KAvk yasyāṃ na mayā sā buddhiḥ sā śrīrlobhaṃ nihanti yā darpo na yasya vidyā sā śaktiryā ca kṣamāvatī  KAvk evameva na kartavyaḥ parairvidveṣavigrahaḥ kiṃ mātarjagatām pūjyabhikṣubhiḥ khyātalakṣmabhiḥ  KAvk vijetuṃ na ca te śakyāḥ praṃānapariniṣṭhitāḥ pratipakṣairavikṣiptaṃ yeṣāṃ nairātmyaśāsanam  KAvk iti putravacaḥ śrutvā kupitā tamuvāca sā abhūttava pitā nūnaṃ pāpaśramaṇacetakaḥ  KAvk mahati brāhmaṇakule jātaḥ prājño bahuśrutaḥ bhikṣapakṣe nipatitaḥ kathaṃ tvamapi tādṛśaḥ  KAvk pṛthupramāṇakhaṅgena kuru śramaṇanigraham avidāryābhrasaṃghātaṃ tīrkṣṇāṃśurna virājate  KAvk it sa prerito māturgirā tadbhaktiyantritaḥ bhikṣūṇāmāśramapadaṃ śanairgantuṃ samudyayau  KAvk vrajan sa saṃmukhāyātaṃ bhikṣuṃ jijñāsayā pathi granthasāraṃ pramāṇaṃ ca papraccha samayocitam  KAvk sa tena pṛṣṭaḥ provāca gāḍhaśabdārthanirṇayam lakṣatrayapramāṇaṃ na śastraṃ tīrthikadurlabham  KAvk kutaḥ pāre tivartante kka ca vartmātivartate sukhaduḥkhe ca lokasya kkacit samabhibandhataḥ  KAvk iti gambhīraśabdārthaṃ śāsturbhagavato vacaḥ anupāsitasarvajñairjñāyate na yathā tathā  KAvk etadākarṇya kapilaḥ ślokagāmbhīryavismitaḥ yayau bhagavataḥ puṇyaṃ kāśyapasya tapovanam  KAvk tathā bhikṣugaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā prasannahṛdayānanaḥ acintayat tadaśraddhāṃ vihāya gatamatsaraḥ  KAvk eteṣāṃ dveṣakāluṣyāt krauryaṃ kaḥ kartumarhati yeṣāṃ saṃdarśanenaiva vaimalyaṃ labhate manaḥ  KAvk iti saṃcintya sa ciraṃ tadvivādaparāṅmukhaḥ dūrādhvakhinnaḥ svagṛhaṃ gatvā provāca mātaram  KAvk mithyaivāhaṃ tvayā mātaḥ preritaḥ kalikarmaṇi ajayāḥ śramaṇā loke gūḍhārthagranthavādinaḥ  KAvk ślokamātraṃ mayā śrutvā bhikṣorekasya vartmani ajñātārthena vailakṣyāt suciraṃ vīkṣitāṃ kṣitiḥ  KAvk tadgrantheṣvakṝtābhyāsastān vaktuṃ kah pragalbhate kathayanti svaśastraṃ te na hi pravrajitādṛte  KAvk iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā jananī tamabhāṣata āyāsitāhaṃ bhavatā garbhabhāreṇa kevalam  KAvk saṃgharṣamarṣaśūnyena dainyāt sarvapraṇāminā dharṣaṇānirvimarṣeṇa kriyate puruṣeṇa kim  KAvk loke sakalaratnānāṃ tejasaiva mahārghatā ko hyarthaḥ puruṣaprāṇaistejojīvanavarjitaiḥ  KAvk mithyā tadgranthalābḥāya pravrajyā gṛhyate na kim mūrdhni kṛtteṣu jāyante kiṃ keśeṣu kuśaḥ punaḥ  KAvk iti māturgirā tasya manaḥ kaluṣatāṃ yayau sahasā kālavātālīrajoruddhamivāmbaram  KAvk tataḥ sa kūṭapraśamapraṇayī bhikṣukānanam gatvā gṛhītvā pravrajyāṃ avktuṃ samupacakrame  KAvk dharmaprahāravyathitairbhikṣubhiḥ sa pade pade nivāryamāṇastānūce kṛtvā vikṛtamānanam  KAvk ajñātvā darpamukharairayathā bahuvādibhiḥ bhavadbhiḥ sthūladantoṣṭhairvyākhyā mama visūditā  KAvk yūyaṃ gardabhamarkaṭoṣṭravadanā dvīpyāsyapaśvānanāmārjāraiṇavarāhakukkuramukhā durdarśavakrkraḥ param sahyā maunajuṣo pi naiva vikaṭāṭopaṃ raṭantaḥ kimubhrūbhaṅgairiti bhikṣusaṃghamasakṛnnirbhartsayan so bhyadhāt  KAvk tasya vākyaśaraistīkṣṇairvikṛttā iva bhikṣavaḥ anuktvaiva prativacastyaktvā taṃ yayuranyataḥ  KAvk tena vākpātakenātha paścāttāpamupāgataḥ tatyāja jananīmeva pravrajyām na tu tāṃ dvijaḥ  KAvk śramaṇairme hṛtaḥ putra iti sā vipralāpinī unmādinī tanuṃ tyaktvā prapede narakasthitim  KAvk tataḥ kālena kapilaḥ svayaṃ kalitakilbiṣaḥ dehānte vākyapāruṣyādimāṃ makaratāṃ gataḥ  KAvk tānyetāni mukhānyasya yānyūce bhikṣubhartsane phalaṃ sadṛśarūpaṃ hi karmabījāt prajāyate  KAvk ityuktvā tatra bhagavān dharmamādiśya śāśvatam janasyānugrahaṃ cakre nānābodhividhāyakam  KAvk tataḥ prayāte svapadaṃ jine tanmayamānasaḥ kamaraḥ projjhitāhārastyaktvā dehaṃ divaṃ yayau  KAvk cāturmahārājikeṣu deveṣu viśadadyutiḥ śrīmān sa jātaḥ sugate kṣaṇaṃ vyasananipatitānāṃ līlayā puṇyaśīlānikhilamatulamūlaṃ kleśamunmūlayanti  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ kapilavadānaṃ nāma ekonacatvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  udrāyaṇāvadānam tulyameva puruṣeṇa bhujyate kāyabhājanagataṃ śubhāśubham dehināṃ vividhakarmajaṃ phalaṃ na hyabhuktamupayāti saṃkṣayam  KAvk bhagavān sugataḥ pūrvaṃ pure rājagṛhābhidhe kalandakanivāsākhye vijahāra vanāntare  KAvk bimbisāraḥ kṣitipatistatrābhūdviśrutaḥ śriyā ākaraḥ saravratnānāṃ ratnākaram ivāparaḥ  KAvk babhūva samaye tasmin raurukākhye pure nṛpaḥ śrīmānudrāyaṇo nāma yaśaścandramahodadhiḥ  KAvk tasya candraprabhā nāma patnī candrānanābhavat śikhaṇḍī yuvarājaśca sūnurvikramakarkaśaḥ  KAvk hiruko bhirukaśceti tasyāmātyau babhūvatuḥ gaṇanīyau na vinaye yayuḥ śukrabṛhaspatī  KAvk jātā bhūmibhujaḥ prītirlekhakhatviṣastayoḥ raverdūrasthitasyāpi kamalākarayoriva  KAvk apūrvaratnanicayapreṣaṇairbahuśastayoḥ paripūrṇaṃ paraṃ prāpa sakhyaṃ prema vidhānataḥ  KAvk dūrasthāpi paraṃ prītiḥ satāṃ kīrtirivākṣayā saṃsaktāpi khalaprītistṛṇajvāleva na sthirā  KAvk kadāciddivyaratnāṅkaṃ kavacaṃ kāñcanojjvalam prāhiṇod bimbisārāya sāramudrāyaṇo nṛpaḥ  KAvk viṣahsastrāgnirakṣārhaṃ vicitraratnakaṃ ca tat suhṛtpreṣitamādāya provāca saciavān nṛpaḥ  KAvk idaṃ me prahitaṃ tena saujanyamiva bhūbhujā sarva rakṣākṣamaṃ varma gāḍhapremanivedakam  KAvk na paśyāmyasya sadṛśaṃ pratideyaṃ tathādhikam alpapratikriyā śalyamupakārāpakārayoḥ  KAvk ucitaṃ cintyatāṃ kiṃcit preṣaṇīyamato dhikam sarvairbhadbhirityuktvā nṝpaścintākulo bhavat  KAvk atha dhīmān mahāmātyaściraṃ dhyātvā tamabravīt KAvk bimbisārasya hastāṅkalekhāmudrāyaṇo nṛpaḥ paṭasya purataḥ prāptām hṛṣṭaḥ svayamavācayat  KAvk sugatacaraṇapadmanyāsapuṇyopakaṇṭhāttridaśapuraviśeṣānmāgadhodāraradeśāt prasannamadhuraṃ tvannetrapātrārpitaṃdhanyaḥ puṇyarasāyanaṃ piba haṭhādākaṇṭhamutkaṇṭhitaḥ  KAvk sanmārge viniyojanaṃ sguṇagaṇādhāne sadādhyāpanaṃdurvyāpāranivāraṇam thirasukhaprāptau paripreraṇam KAvk abhinandya tamānandāt sāmātyaḥ sapurohitaḥ hemasiṃhāsanotsaṅge sa prasārya nyaveśayat  KAvk lāvaṇyapuṇyanilayaṃ dṛṣṭvā tatsaugataṃ vapuḥ namo namah prabuddhāyetyavadajagatījanaḥ  KAvk bimbisārastatastasmai kṛtvā bhagavato rthanām kātyāyanaṃ ca vyasṛjat śailākhyām cāpi bhikṣuṇīm  KAvk udrāyaṇasya nṝpaterāryaḥ kātyāyano tha saḥ pūjāvidhāyinastatra vidadhe dharmadeśanām  KAvk dharmadeśanayā tasya saṃgataḥ sumahān janaḥ srotaḥsakṛdanāgāmiphalārhatpadamāptavān  KAvk tasmin gṛhapatī khyātau tiṣyapuṣyābhidhau pure śāntyai pravrajya tasyāgre parinirvṛtimāpatuḥ  KAvk kālena bhūpālah krīḍagāragatāṃ priyām tāmajñāsīnnimittajñaḥ saptāhāvadhijīvitām  KAvk jñātasaṃsāracaritastatastāṃ vaśudhādhipaḥ anujajñe śubhapadaṃ prātuṃ pravrajyayā puraḥ  KAvk svākhyāte dharmavinmaye bhikṣukyā nṛpatergirā devī pravrajitā dehaṃ dine tatyāja saptame  KAvk cāturmahārājikeṣu deveṣu sahasaiva sā prayātā devakanyātvaṃ jagāma jinakānanam  KAvk tatra pūrṇenduvadanā divyābharaṇabhūṣitā
