niśi suptasya cakre bodhiprakāśanam  KAvk yātāyāṃ svapadaṃ tasyāṃ prabhāte vasudhādhipaḥ pravrajyābhimukhaḥ putramabhiṣicya śikhaṇḍinam  KAvk prajātrāṇāya nikṣipya taṃ mahāmātyayostataḥ nṛpaterbimbisārasya suhṛdaḥ sa yayau puram  KAvk bimbisārastamāyātaṃ vigatacchatracāmaram nṛpopacāraiḥ praṇataḥ prītipūtairapūjayat  KAvk viśrāntamāsanāsīnaṃ sa tamūce savismayaḥ hṛṣṭhaḥ saṃdarśanenāsya śrīviyogena duḥkhitaḥ  KAvk rājannanantasāmantamauliviśrāntaśāsanaḥ pākaśāsanatulyastvaṃ kathamevamupāgataḥ  KAvk abhinnavakrkraprakṛterguptamantrasya dhīmataḥ pareṇa rājyaharaṇaṃ vīra saṃbhāvyate na te  KAvk iti pṛṣṭaḥ sa suhṛdā sasmitastamabhāṣata rājan vṛddhivibhūtirme na priyā sarvagāminī  KAvk viṣayāsvādavaimukhyād vitṛṣṇena mayā svayam utsṛṣṭamiva saṃtyaktamaiśvaryaṃ bhogabhājanam  KAvk tvayā kalyāṇamitreṇa sugatapratimāpaṭaḥ yo sau hitāya prahitaḥ s avairāgyagururmamaḥ  KAvk adhunā tvatprasādena gatvā bhagavato ntike icchāmyavāptuṃ pravrajyāmagārādanagārikaḥ  KAvk iti sakhyurvacaḥ śrutvā tattatheti vicintya ca sādarastadvivekena bimbisārastamabravīt  KAvk dhanyo bahumataścāsi satāṃ tvaṃ pṛthivīpate kathaṃ saṃsāravimukhī jātā te matirīdṛśī  KAvk saṃtoṣavibhavo bhogasubhagaḥ śobhase param lakṣaṇaṃ śuddhasattvānāṃ vairājyābharaṇaṃ manah  KAvk kiṃ sāmrājyamahaujasā sarajasā duḥsādhanaiḥ sādhanaiḥkiṃ bhogaiḥ kṣaṇabhojanaiḥ kulaṣadaiḥ kiṃ sattvaduḥkhaiḥ sukhaiḥ saṃsāroparamāya cetasi satāṃ janmāntaropārjitaṃvairāgyaṃ kurute padaṃ yadi mahāmohaprarohāpaham  KAvk yena prāṇamanaḥpriyā vasumatī saṃtyajyate līlayātrailokyābhimate pi yaḥ smarasukhe vaimukhyadīkṣāguruḥ saṃmohavysanāturaṃ jagadidaṃ yenānukampāspadaṃpuṇyaiḥ ko pi sa jāyate matimatāṃ saṃsāravāmaḥ śamah  KAvk ityuktvā bimbisārastaṃ nītvā veṇuvanāśramam sapraṇāmaṃ bhagavate tadvṛttāntaṃ nyavedayat  KAvk udrāyaṇo pi sugatākāraṃ suciracintitam vilokya harṣādātmānaṃ kṛtakṛtyamamanyata  KAvk parṇāmavyagraśirasā saṃsāracchedini tanau papāta bhagavaddṛṣṭistasya pravrajyayā saha  KAvk bhikṣubhāvamathāsādya pātrapāṇiḥ sa cīvarī nagare piṇḍapātārthī cakāra janavismayam  KAvk prajāḥ śikhaṇḍī dharmeṇa pālayitvā prasannadhīḥ yātaḥ kālena kāluṣyamadharmābhirato bahvat  KAvk kaluṣaṃ kāñcanarucivyaktavidyudvilāsinī na kasya kurute lakṣmīrmeghamāleva mānasam  KAvk anāyattaṃ mahāmātyau hiruko bhirukaśca tam adharmakarmanirataṃ kruddhau tatyajatuḥ prabhum  KAvk tatpade vihitau rājñā sacivau daṇḍamugdarau cittānuvṛttikuśalau svairaṃ saktaṃ tamūcatuḥ  KAvk prajārañjanasaṃsaktā rājadaurjanyavādinaḥ svayaśaḥkhyāpanāyaiva jāyante dhūrtamantriṇaḥ  KAvk na dharmaṃ na sukhaṃ nārthaṃ na kīrti na ca jīvitam gaṇayanti prabhorarthe te bhṛtyā bhavyabhaktayaḥ  KAvk nākhaṇḍitā nākṣayitā nātaptā nāpyapīḍitāḥ kurvantyarthakriyā rājñastilatulyāḥ kila prajāḥ  KAvk iti bruvāṇau tau rājñā niyuktau rājyacintane lobhāt pravṛttau durnītau hantuṃ niḥśaraṇāḥ prajāḥ  KAvk nirvicāre durācāre kumatau pṛthivīpatau luptasatye mahāmātye prajānāṃ jīvitaṃ kutaḥ  KAvk udrāyaṇo thācireṇa kadācid vaṇijaṃpathi nijadeśāgataṃ vārtāṃ papraccha nṛparāṣṭrayoḥ  KAvk so vadaddeva kuśalī sutastava mahīpatiḥ kiṃ tu sanmantrirahitaḥ kumantrivaśamāgataḥ  KAvk tatra prajānāṃ vitatopatāpaḥ ko pi pravṛttaḥ prabhuśāsanena yenādya tatkutsitadeśajanma divāniśaṃ śocati pauralokaḥ  KAvk yatra dhvāntaṃ sṛjati taraṇiryatra candro gnivarṣīyatrodeti prakaṭamamṛtādutkaṭaḥ kālakūṭaḥ yatra trātā harati nṛpatirjīvavṛttiṃ prajānāṃtatrākrandaṃ prasṝtavipulopaplavaṃ kaḥ śṛṇoti  KAvk ityāsaktanṛpāyāsakhinnasyārtimayaṃ vacaḥ duḥsahaṃ vaṇijaḥ śrutvā sa tamūce kṛpānidhiḥ  KAvk dadgirā tvamito gatvā tūrṇamāśvāsaya prajāḥ sthāpayiṣyāmyahaṃ dharme svayametya śikhaṇḍinam  KAvk ityuktastena sānandaḥ svadeśaṃ śanakairvaṇik gatvā prajānāṃ vidadhe svairamāśvāsanaṃ puraḥ  KAvk pravāde prasṛte tasminnamātyau daṇḍamudgarau atītabhūpāgamanatrastau bhūpatimūcatuḥ  KAvk sarvatra śrūyate deva pravādaḥ sādhuninditaḥ vṛddhaḥ pravrajito rājā rājyārthī yatnavāniti  KAvk tīvravrataparikliṣṭaḥ saṃbhogābhimukhādaraḥ lajjāṃ pravrajyayā sārdhaṃ tyaktvā sa punareṣyati  KAvk rājannapakkavairāgyāstyajanti sahasaiva yat tat pūrvābhyadhikaṃ teṣāṃ prayāti priyatāṃ punaḥ  KAvk lokasthitiviruddheṣu viṣayeṣu viśeṣataḥ spṛhā saṃjāyate jantorapathyeṣviva rogiṇaḥ  KAvk sukhotsekātparityaktaṃ prahastamupāgatam prāyaḥ sarvaṃ bhavatyeva jaḍasyāmramiva priyam  KAvk tasmādbhavantamutsārya pratāpanidhimāsanāt kṣīṇaḥ śaśīva sthaviraḥ sa rājyaṃ bhoktumicchati  KAvk cīvarodvignagātrasya varavastrābhilāṣiṇaḥ jātāsya muṇḍite mūrdhni ratnāṅkamukuṭaspṛhā  KAvk ratnaharmyeṣu navatāsaṃbhogavibhavodbhavam tyaktvā vilāsamāyāsaṃ vanavāsaṃ saheta kaḥ  KAvk mṛduśayanasukhārhā ye kathaṃ śerate tehariṇakharakhurodyatkatkaṇṭakāsu sthalīṣu madhu vidhukaraśītaṃ yairnipītaṃ kathaṃ tevanajagajamadoṣṇaṃ tiktamambhaḥ pibanti  KAvk adhunaiva tavāsannapraveśaviṣamasthiteḥ ādyaṃmataṃ nyāyavidāṃ rājaputra nipātanam  KAvk tasmādanāgato rājā pūrvaṃ vadhyastava prabho dīpaṃ hanti pataṅgo hi na dagdhaścetsamāpatan  KAvk tayoriti girā kṣipramabhūd bhūpatirākūlaḥ khalameghaiḥ kaluṣatāṃ nītaṃ kasya na mānasam  KAvk sa tau babhāṣe sāśaṅkaḥ krakacakrūratāṃ gataḥ bādhaḥ sādhāraṇaścāyaṃ yuvayormama cāgrataḥ  KAvk bhavadbhyāmeva vinayopāyaviśrāntayā dhiyā vicārya kāryatātparyaṃ yad yuktaṃ tadvidhīyatām  KAvk iti rājñā kṛtotsāhau tau visṛjyāśu ghātakān udrāyaṇasyāgrapathaṃ vadhāyaiva babandhatuḥ  KAvk so piprajñāparitrāṇe niyoktuṃ putramudyataḥ bhagavantaṃ samabhyetya vrajāmīti vyajijñapat  KAvk sarvajñenābhyanujñātaḥ svakṛtaṃ bhujyatāmiti karmapāśasamākṛṣṭaḥ sa yayau rorukaṃ puram  KAvk tasmādvrajantaṃ nirvyājamācāramiva durjanāḥ duṣṭāmātyaprayuktāste jagnurvartmani ghātakāḥ  KAvk tasya cāīvarapātrādīn gṛhītvā nihatasya te vyadevayan kṛtaṃ prītyau rājākāryamamātyayoḥ  KAvk tataḥ pāpaprahṛṣṭābhyāṃ nṛpastābhyāṃ pradarśitam dṛṣṭvā mumoha sahasā raktāktaṃ cīvaraṃ pituḥ  KAvk sa labdhasaṃjñaḥ śanakaiḥ śuśoca na tathā gurum yathā patitamātmānaṃ ghore narakagahvare  KAvk so vadadvatsa saṃprāptaṃ phalaṃ khalajanānmayā aiśvaryamadhulubdhena pāpapātamapaśyatā  KAvk aho bata nirālambe ghore narakasaṃkaṭe unnatārohiṇāṃ sadyaḥ pātakaṃ khalasaṃgatam  KAvk kṛtametanmahatpāpaṃ duṣṭāmātyadhiyā mayā patitasya mamedānīṃ pāvako pi na pāvakah  KAvk tulyaṃ pituścārhatasya vadhe kā mama niṣkṛtiḥ pītaṃ yatra mayaikasmin pātre sadahanaṃviṣam  KAvk vṛddhe pitari niḥsaṅke śamaṃ pravrajyayāśrite svacitta niśitaṃ śastraṃ lobhādvyāpāritaṃ mayā  KAvk yatsaṃcintitameva kampajanakaṃ śrotuṃ nayat śakyatedṛṣṭaṃ yacca karoti śokakalanāṃ niścetanānāmapi yatra krairyamapi prayāti mṛdutāṃ tīvrānutāpāgninātatrāpi prasaranti nirghṛṇadhiyām nistriṃśatīkṣṇāḥ kriyāḥ  KAvk ityuktvā duḥkahsaṃtaptaḥ pralāpamukharānanaḥ nyavārayattayoḥ kopātpraveśaṃ duṣṭamantriṇoḥ  KAvk guṇāntaraṃ parijñāya bhirukaṃ hirukaṃ ca saḥ ānināya prasādyāśu purāṇau sacivau pituḥ  KAvk tataścintākṛśe rājñi śokāt pāṇḍuratām gate svairaṃ tajjananīmetya duṣṭāmātyāvavocatām  KAvk devi tvatanayaḥ śrīmān svabhāvasaralāśayaḥ rājyarakṣāṃ na jānāti svajanocchedakarkaśām  KAvk pitā pravrajito pyasya rājyaṃ hartumupāgataḥ āvābhyāṃ praśamaṃ nītastatra kā nāma vācyatā  KAvk nīcatantropapannaścet kramo yamaśubhakramaḥ rājyābhilāṣiṇo bhikṣostasyāpi sa kathaṃ kramaḥ  KAvk āvāṃ pitṛvadhakridhād vāritau bhūbhujā padāt svayamadyāpi śokena kiṃ mithyā pariśuṣyate  KAvk sukṛtaṃ kṛtamāvābhyām prabhorduḥkhakṛśāṅgatā bhavanti sarvabhāveṣu bhṛjyā evāparādhinaḥ  KAvk gataṃ śocati kiṃ rājā yatkṛtaṃ kṛtameva tat upekṣyate tvayā devi kasmāccintākṛśaḥ sutaḥ  KAvk tābhyāmityuditaṃ śrutvā sā rājajananī śanaiḥ ūce taralikā nāma tadvākyavihitādarā  KAvk ānantaryamidaṃ karma dvayornarakapātakam yuṣmanmatādupanataṃ rājñaḥ pūrvakṛtena vā  KAvk ahaṃ tu vārayāmyasya śokaṃ pitṛvadhodbhavam arhadvadhodbhavaṃ duḥkhaṃ bhavadbhyāmapi vāryatāṃ  KAvk iti tau svairamādiśya sā gatvā pārthivāntikam tamuvāca śucākrāntaṃ parikṣīṇamivoḍupam  KAvk dharmādharmamayaṃ putra rājyaṃ rājñāṃ bahucchalam pāpānāṃ śaṅkayā tasmin kiṃ śucā pariśuṣyasi  KAvk piturvadhāt pratapto si yadi nāma gurupriyaḥ tatrocyate samutsṛjya lajjāṃ tvadduḥkhasaṃkaṭe  KAvk svairaṃ jātastvamanyena na sa taddharmataḥ pitā svecchāhārasukhāḥ putra striyo hi nirapatrpāḥ  KAvk ityapriyamapi śrutvā rājā tadvacanaṃ rahaḥ pitṛvaiśasapāpograduḥkhasaṃtāpamatyajat  KAvk prakurvantyastādrerudayagiriṇā kleśakalanāṃkṣaṇāt kṣoṇīkṣmābhṛdvighaṭanavonodaṃ vidadhati sṛjantyetā vahniṃ sapadi salilāttacca dahanādaśādhyaṃ nārīṇāṃ na hi bhavati kiṃcitrtribhuvane  KAvk atha so rhadvadhenaiva śalyatulyena pīḍitaḥ nṛpaḥ papraccha dharmajñānniṣkṛtiṃ tasya karmaṇaḥ  KAvk tatastau duṣṭasacivau tiṣyapuṣyākhyacaityayoḥ mārjārapotau dhṛtvāntaḥsaktāvāmiṣaśikṣayā  KAvk niṣiddhāvapi dhāṣṭaryena praviśya nṛpateḥ sabhām tamūcatustīvratāpasaṃtāpapraśamārthinam  KAvk deva mithyaiva bhavatā cittamāyāsyate bhṛśam sarvakalyāṇā loke smin nārhantaḥ santi te matāḥ  KAvk yadi satyaṃ bhaveyuste nabhaso rājahaṃsavat ṛddhimantaḥ kathaṃ teṣāmanyena vadhasaṃbhavaḥ  KAvk na santi tasmādarhantaḥ kutastadvadhapātakam sīmāvivādaḥ kastatr yatra grāmo na vidyate  KAvk tiṣyapuṣyau gṛhapatī yāvarhatpadamāpatuḥ mārjārāvantare jātau tāvevādy asvacaityayoḥ  KAvk prakaṭau tau ca dṛśyete pratyakṣaṃ kasya saṃśayaḥ pratyayo yadi nāstyeva svayaṃ kiṃ na nirīkṣyate  KAvk ityuktvā bhūpateḥ kṛtvā khalau dolākulaṃ manaḥ jagmatuḥ sahitau tena caityasaṃdarśanāya tau  KAvk apūrvakautukāveśāt tatra saṃghaṭite jane vilokanodyate rājño sāmātye duṣṭamantriṇau  KAvk āmiṣābhyāsasaṃbaddhatiṣyapuṣyābhidhānayoḥ dhūrtau cakraturāhvānaṃ śanairbālabiḍālayoḥ  KAvk tau tiṣyapuṣyāvarhantau mārjārau stho yuvāṃ yadi pradakṣīṇaṃ vā kriyatāṃ tena satyena caityayoḥ  KAvk māṃsadānakṣaṇe tābhyāmiti vācamudīritau tūrṇaṃ nirgatya mārjārau cakratustau pradakṣiṇam  KAvk taddṛṣṭvā sahasāvāptapratyaye sānuge nṛpe yāte durjanamāyaiva jagajjayamahīṃ yayau  KAvk muṣṭau vāyuṃ dṛṣadi kamalaṃ citramākāśadeśejihvāgre ca pracuraracanāsṛṣṭisaṃhāralīlāḥ kiṃ vā nānyat paśuśiśudhiyāṃ mohanāyendrajālaṃmūrtaṃ dhurtāḥ kṣaṇaparicitapratyayaṃ darśayanti  KAvk niṣpratyayaparo rājā tataḥ saugatadarśane āryakātyāyanasyāgre śraddhāpūjāmavārayat  KAvk rājadhānyāṃ niṣiddho tha bahireva sasānugaḥ vineyakṛpayā tatra tasthau śailā ca bhikṣuṇī  KAvk tataḥ kadācidāyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā kātyāyanaḥ puraḥ nṛpatiṃ janasaṃpātādavamānabhayād yayau  KAvk preṣitaṃ pūrvamantribhyāṃ vrajantamavalokya tam duṣṭāmātyau narapatiṃ dīrghavairāvavocatām  KAvk rājannamaṅgalanidhirmuṇḍo yaṃ viśiraḥ pathi dṛṣṭo dya bhikṣurasmābhirna vidmaḥ kiṃ bhaviṣyati  KAvk na paśyāmi mukhaṃ rājñaḥ pāpasyeti bhaṇatyasau tathā hi kṣaṇamekānte gatvā dūramitaḥ sthitaḥ  KAvk śrutvaitaddurjanāmarṣāduvācānucarān nṛpaḥ eṣa dūrasthitaḥ pāṃśumuṣṭibhiḥ pūryatāmiti  KAvk pūryamāṇaḥ sa taiḥ pāṃśumuṣṭibhirduṣṭaceṭakaiḥ divyāṃ kuṭīṃ praveśena parihārāya nirmame  KAvk amarṣakopitāḥ sarpāḥ vyāghrā vā pītalohitāḥ śānterāyānti mṛdutāṃ nat u bhūpaticeṭakāḥ  KAvk tataḥ prayāte nṛpatau pāṃśurāśiśatāvṛtam duḥkhādūcaturabhyetya hiruko bhirukaśca tam  KAvk ārya kṛcchramavāpto si rājñā krūreṇa duṣkṛtaiḥ locanāni dhigasmākaṃ yairidaṃ dṛśyate pureḥ  KAvk mohāndhaḥ pātakaśvabhre durjanaiḥ pātito nṛpaḥ karmaṇo vayamapyasya darśanāt pāpabhāginaḥ  KAvk bhūriyam bhūripāpārtā tyājyā prājyamatestava duḥsahaḥ khalasaṃvāsaḥ tyāgaḥ kasya na saṃmataḥ  KAvk prayāti na śamaḥ śamaṃ kṣayamupaiti naiva kṣamābhavanti na ca buddhayaḥ paruṣaroṣadoṣaspṛśaḥ vasanti na vimānanā manasi śalyatulyāḥ satāṃna duṣṭajanavarjanādaparamāsti loke sukham  KAvk aiśvaryaṃ guṇināmadhonipatanāyāsaprayāsapradaṃgāmbhīryaṃ timirākāraṃ praviśatāṃ prāṇāpahaṃ prāṇinām naṣṭā sāpi nikṛṣṭduṣṭkuṭilavyālairupādeyatākūpasyeva khalasya nāsti tadaho doṣāliyuktaṃ yataḥ  KAvk tayoriti vacaḥ śrutvā mahākātyāyano vadat na nikāre pi me kopaḥ karmaṇo gatirīdṛśī  KAvk etāvadeva me duḥkhaṃ yanmūḍhasya mahīpateḥ khalasaṃgamadoṣeṇa bhayaṃ mahadupasthitam  KAvk prathame hi mahāvāyuḥ pureasya nipatiṣyati dvitīye puṣpavṛṣṭiśca vastravṛṣṭistataḥ pare  KAvk rūpyavṛṣṭiścaturthe ca hemavṛṣṭiśca pañcame ratnavṛṣṭistataḥ ṣaṣṭhe pāṃśuvṛṣṭiśca saptame  KAvk tayā sabandhurāṣṭro say na bhaviṣyati bhūpatiḥ tasmād bhavadbhyāṃ gantavyaṃ ratnānyādāya bhūyase  KAvk iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā viniścitya tatheti tau hirukaḥ śyāmakaṃ putraṃ tasyopasthāpakaṃ vyadhāt  KAvk bhirukaśca sutāṃ śyāmāvatīmādāya pāṇinā abhyetya bhikṣukīṃ śailāṃ praṇayādidamabravīt  KAvk ārye bhavatyā me kanyā ghoṣilasya gṛhaprabhoḥ gṛhe samarpaṇīyeyamāsannapratipannayā  KAvk evamuktvārpayitvā tāvamātyau jagmaturgṛham śailāpi kanyāmādāya prayayau ghoṣilālayam  KAvk tataḥ krameṇa tadabhūdyathoktaṃ bhikṣuṇā pure jñānadīpavatī prajñā yathātattvaṃ hi paśyati  KAvk ṣaṣṭhe hni ratnavarṣe tha patite ratnapūritām yayaturnāvamādāya tāvamātyāvalakṣitau  KAvk tau dakṣiṇāṃ diśaṃ gatvā cakraturnagaradvayam hiruko hirukākhyānaṃ bhirukākhyaṃ tathāparaḥ  KAvk pare hni pāṃśuvarṣeṇamahatā patatā nṛpaḥ sabandhurāṣṭraḥ pralayṃ prayayau narakātithiḥ  KAvk sadaṇḍimudgare rājñi yāte kilbiṣaśeṣatām taṃ mantriputramādāya vyomnā kātyāyano yayau  KAvk tamevānugatā prītyā nabhasā puradevatā tadājñayā khavacanīkarvaṭe vidadhe sthitim  KAvk bhikṣupuṇyānubhāvena bhāgyairmantrisutasya ca adhiṣṭhānena devyāśca śrīmattadabahvat puram  KAvk tatrātha devatā cakre caityaṃ kātyāyanasya sā suravatyāṃ yadadyāpi vandante caityavandakāḥ  KAvk mantrisūnumathādāya lagnaṃ cīvarakarṇike lambanaṃ sa yayau vyomnā deśaṃ kātyāyanaḥ param  KAvk lambate lambate ko yamityukte vismayājjanaiḥ babhūvuste janāstatra lambakā iti viśrutāḥ  KAvk atrāntare divaṃ yāte tatrāputre mahīpatau sa kṛtaḥ śyāmako rājā lakṣaṇajñistadājñayā  KAvk gatvā bhokkānakaṃ nāma diśā kātyāyanastataḥ jananyāstatra saṃśuddhāṃ vidasdhe dharmadeśanām  KAvk sā dṛṣṭasatyā putrasya yaṣṭīmādāya sādaram vandyamādyapi mahatī yaṣṭicaityamakārayat  KAvk śrāvastīmatha sotkaṇṭhaḥ prāpya kātyāyanaḥ śanaiḥ jinaṃ vilokya sānandaścakre tatpādavandanam  KAvk udrāyaṇasutakathām tatra tena niveditām ākarṇya bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ sarvajñastānabhāṣata  KAvk lubdhakah kālapāśākhyaḥ karvaṭopāntakānane sakūṭāṃ mṛgabandhāya nidadhe vāgurām puraḥ  KAvk yantraṃ pāśāvṛtaṃ datvā yāte tasmin yadṛśchayā pratyekabuddhastaṃ deśaṃ prāpya viśrāntimāptavān  KAvk tasya puṇyānubhāvena bandhaṃ na viviśurmṛgāḥ na hi śuddhātmanāmagre prāpnotyakuśalaṃ janah  KAvk lubdhako pi tato bhyetya pāśānālokya nirmṛgān pratyekabuddhaṃ krodhāndho viṣadigdheṣuṇāvadhīṭ  KAvk tasya sāyakaviddhasya jvalajjvalanatejsaḥ prabhāvamadbhutaṃ dṛṣṭvā pādayornipapāta saḥ  KAvk akāryakaraṇodvegasaṃtāpādatha lubdhakaḥ nininda śocannātmānaṃ saṃtyajya śaravāgurāḥ  KAvk parinirvāṇamāptasya tasyāsthīni nidhāya saḥ chatradhvajādisaṃbhāraiḥ stūpaṃ cakre sadārcitam  KAvk lubdhakastena puṇyena babhūvodrāyaṇo nṛpaḥ vadhāt pratyekabuddhasya bahuśo vadhamāptavān  KAvk nandanāmno gṛhapatermadalekhābhidhā sutā babhūva dhanadhanyādisphūtiḥ karvaṭavāsinaḥ  KAvk sā kadācinmadotsiktāḥ gṛhamārjanareṇubhiḥ pratyekabuddhamāyāntaṃ pathi mohādavākirat  KAvk tasminneva dine tasyāściracintābhirarthitaḥ varaḥ stanabharārtāyā varaṇārthī samāyayau  KAvk mūdhni pratyekabuddhasya pāṃśumuṣṭiunipātanāt pratyāsannavivāhāhamiti bhrātaramāha sā  KAvk tatastasyāh pravādena cikṣipurvaraṇāptaye mūrdhni pratyekabuddhasya rajāṃsi prauḍhakanyakāḥ  KAvk guṇākārapravṛttena prayayena vimohitāḥ nirvicārya pravartante viruddheṣvapi vastuṣu  KAvk pravṛttapātakācāre tasmin buddhabudhābhidhau nivāraṇaṃ gṛhapatī karmaṇastasya cakratuḥ  KAvk saiva kanyā narapatiḥ śikhaṇḍī pāpabhāgabhūt pravādakartā tadbhrātā bhikṣuḥ katyāyano pyayam  KAvk jātau gṛhapatī rūḍhaduṣṭācāranivāraṇāt puripatāpānnirmuktau hiruko bhirukaśca tau  KAvk iti bhagavataḥ śrutvā vākyaṃ vicārya ca bhikṣavaḥphalapariṇatiṃ jñātvā citrām śubhāśubhakarmaṇām khalajanavacastulyaṃ śatruṃ vicārasamaṃ guruṃsukṛtasadṛśaṃ bandhuṃ loke na kiṃcana menire  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāmudrāyaṇāvadānaṃ catvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  kapilāvadānam yadbhūpālaviśāladānabibhavaprodbhūtapuṇyādhikaṃdānasyātikṛśasya satphalabharamapnotyalaṃ durgataḥ śuddhasyaiva vivṛddhadharmadhavalaśraddhāsamṛdhyānvitaṃniḥsaṃsāravijṛmbhitaṃ taducitaṃ cittasya vittasya ca  KAvk jine jetavanārāmavihāriṇi mahādhanah dhīrābhidhānaḥ śrāvastyāmabhūd gṛhapatiḥ purāḥ  KAvk tasya paṇḍitanāmabhūt putraḥ sukṛtapaṇḍitaḥ akhaṇḍitayaśaḥpuṇyadānālaṃkāramaṇḍitaḥ  KAvk sa bāla eva bhikṣūṇām rājārhairvastrabhojanaiḥ śāriputrapradhānānāṃ cakārātithisatkriyām  KAvk tataḥ kadācidakṣīṇādurbhikṣakṣayite jane yācyayācakatulyatve piṇḍicchedo thināmabhūt  KAvk bhikṣūṇāṃ saṃkaṭe tasmin kāle paramadāruṇe paṇḍitaḥ sugatāhūtaḥ pratasthe jetakānanam  KAvk taṃ vrajantaṃ turaṅgeṇa kāñcanādāmaśobhinam ūcurviṭāḥ samabhyetya guṇotsāhāsahiṣṇavaḥ  KAvk arthisārthārthanākalpavṛkṣastvaṃ dikṣu viśrutaḥ śatāni pañca saṃprāptāstvāmuddiśyāśayā vayam  KAvk alaṃkārāṃśukayugaṃ pratyekaṃ naḥ samīhitam adhunaivāvilambena dīyatām yadi śakyate  KAvk ityuktastaiḥ sadācāraḥ so vatīrya turaṅgamāt sādhu pūjāṃ vidhāyaiṣāṃ dhīmān kṣaṇamacintayat  KAvk bhagavantamadṛṣṭvaiva gacchāmi svagṛhaṃ yadi āsannāmṛtapānasya taṃ vighnaṃ kathamutaśe  KAvk adatvā priyamarthibhyo vrajāmi yadi nistrapah kathaṃ karomi dānasya tāṃ svayaṃ vratakhaṇḍanām  KAvk iti cintayatastasya bhittvā bhūmiṃ samudgataḥ nāgarājaḥ svayaṃ śeṣaḥ prādādarthisamīhitam  KAvk dattāni nāgarājena vastrāṇyābharaṇāni ca sa tebhyaḥ pratipādyāśu yayau niḥśalyatāmiva  KAvk te pi dṛṣṭvā tadāścaryaṃ puṇyāṃ sugatabhāvanām sarvārthasaṃpatsiddhīnāṃ jananīmeva menire  KAvk jātacittaprasādāste tenaiva sahitāstataḥ bhagavantaṃ yayurdraṣṭuṃ vinaṣṭadveṣakalmaṣāḥ  KAvk bhagavantamathālokya kumāraḥ praṇatānanaḥ tatpādapadmarajasā dhanyaścakre lalāṭikām  KAvk hāraṃ punaścaraṇayoḥ śāstuḥ śaśikarojjvalam vinyasya praṇatānagre sa tānasmai nyavedayat  KAvk dharmadeśanayā teṣāṃ bhagavān jñānavajrabhṛt bhittvā satkāyadṛṣṭyadriṃ srotaḥprāptiphalaṃ vyadhāt  KAvk dṛṣṭasatyeṣu yāteṣu tatasteṣu praṇamya tam kumāraṃpaṇḍitaṃ prītyā bhagavān svayamabhyadhāt  KAvk vatsa puṇyairavāpto si paryāptiṃ sukṛtaśriyām durbhikṣesvapi bhikṣūṇāṃ kuru bhojyādhivāsanām  KAvk parigraho me bhikṣūṇāṃ śatānyarhatrayodaśa anye cānviṣya kṛcchrārtāḥ saṃvibhajyāstvayā pure  KAvk iti śrutvā bhagavataḥ paṇḍitaḥ pramadākulaḥ bhaktyā saṃghasya vidadhe yāvajjīvaṃ nimantraṇam  KAvk tataḥ svagṛhamabhyetya rājārhaibhikṣusaṃmataiḥ saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ saṃghaṃ sadā bhojyairapūjayat  KAvk daridrānadaridrāṃśca yācyānapi ca yācakān anukampyān sa vidadhe dānenānyānukampinah  KAvk śeṣān kṛpaṇasaṃghātān so nviṣya karuṇāmbudhiḥ ratnarāśiṃ dadau tebhyo daurgatyatimirāpaham  KAvk sa ratnanikarasteṣāṃ jagāmāṅgārarāśitām nṛṇāṃ bhāgyāni ratnāni maṇayaḥ prasthajātayaḥ  KAvk te tamūcuḥ samabhyetya svapnadṛṣṭadhanā iva ratnanāmnā tvayāsmākaṃ sa datto ṅgārasaṃcayaḥ  KAvk dhanalābhena mahatā sadyaḥ prāptonnatirjanah tatsaṃkṣayāt kṣaṇenaiva paribhraṣṭo na jīvati  KAvk iti teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā paṇḍitaḥ karuṇānidhiḥ tānūce puṇyadīnānāṃ ratnānyāyāntyaratnatām  KAvk yuṣmābhirna kṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ mohāt sukṛtasaṃcayaḥ tenāyaṃ ratnarāśirvaḥ prayāto ṅgārasāratām  KAvk ratnāni yatnanihitānyapi yānti dūraṃ puṇyakṣayādupanayanti ca bhāgyayogāt vittārjanaṃ patitaśokanimittameva vittaṃ hi cittamucitaṃ sukṛtapravṛttam  KAvk tasmād bhavadbhirbhojyāya bhikṣusaṃgho dhivāsyatām bhogasaṃbhārasaṃpattimahaṃ saṃpādayāmi vaḥ  KAvk ityuktāstena taddattavittabhojanasaṃpadā te buddhapramukhaṃ saṃghaṃ dinamekamapūjayan  KAvk saṃghaṃ yathāvadabhyarcya praṇīdhānamakāri taiḥ m ākadācana dāridyraṃ syādasmākamiti kṣaṇam  KAvk tataste paṇḍitagirā gatvā dadṝśuragrataḥ tamevāṅgāranikaraṃ prayātaṃ ratnarāśitām  KAvk bhavane paṇḍitasyātha kumārasya prabhavataḥ vivṛtānāṃ nidhānānāṃ nirvighnaṃ śatamudyayau  KAvk sa prasenajite rājñe dharmajñaḥ sthitirakṣaṇāt dadau nidhānaṣaḍbhāgaṃ sa cāsyāṅgāratāmagāt  KAvk kumārasyaiva sukṛtairbhogyo yaṃ nidhisaṃcayaḥ ityantarīkṣādvacanaṃ tataḥ śuśrāva bhūpatiḥ  KAvk kumārasyaiva vacasā tānnidhīnnirdhitāṃ punaḥ prāptāṃ vilokya sāścaryaḥ prahiṇottadgṛhaṃ nṛpaḥ  KAvk tatastadakhilaṃ vittaṃ vitīrya vipulāśayaḥ kumāraḥ saṃpadāṃ cakre sthitiṃ durgataveśmasu  KAvk atha niḥsārasaṃsāravicāravirataspṛhaḥ anityatāṃ sa saṃcintyaḥ dīraḥ pitarabravīt  KAvk anujānīhi māṃ tāvat gantuṃ tāta patovanam imā janmaśatocchiṣṭāḥ kliṣṭā mama vibhūtayaḥ  KAvk trailokyasaṃpatsaṃprāptiryasmin vrajati bhogyatām tadidaṃ sarvabhūtānāmāyurbhājanamalpakam  KAvk śīte yasya karomi saṃtatamṛdusparśāṃśukaurgūhanaṃsaṃtāpe racayāmi yasya śiśiraśrīkhaṇḍacarcārcanam yasyārthe viṣaśastravahnibhujagavrātātparaṃ me bhayaṃprāptaḥ so pyamapāyataḥ parihṛte pyāyāti kāyaḥ kṣayam  KAvk bhogādviraktaḥ pravrajyāmādāya dayitāṃ vane viharāmi haran cintāṃ cintātaptasya cetasaḥ  KAvk ityuktvā sa parityajya viṣayasnehabandhanam kṛtābhyuopagamaḥ pitrā śāriputrāśamaṃ yayau  KAvk tatra pravrajitastena pātrapāṇiḥ sacīvaraḥ tasyaivānucaro bhūtvā vicacāra yatavfataḥ  KAvk sa dṛṣṭvā karṣakairdhārāṃ kṣetrāt kṣetrapravartitām nirdiṣṭena pathā yāntīṃ vismayādityacintayat  KAvk aho vihitamārgeṇa gacchatāmapyacetasām jalānāṃ karmasaṃsiddhardṛśyate natu dehinām  KAvk saṃcintyeti vrajannagre dṛṣṭvā yaṣṭīkṛtaṃ śaram prataptamiṣukāreṇa pradadhyau dhīmatāṃ varaḥ  KAvk tāpāt praguṇatāmete yānti niścetanāḥ śarāḥ na tu saṃsārasaṃtaptā api vakrāḥ śarīriṇaḥ  KAvk iti dhyāyan vilokyāgre takṣṇā śakaṭacakratām nītāni dṛḍharūpāṇi punaścintāṃ samāyayau  KAvk aho nu ghaṭanāyogād yānti karmaṇyatāṃ kṣaṇāt niścetanānid ārūṇi na cittāni śarīriṇām  KAvk it caṃcintya saṃyātaḥ sudharmaniyamādaraḥ vatsalaṃ pitaraṃ putra ivācāryamuvāca saḥ  KAvk ārya eva prayātvadya piṇḍapātāya matkṛte ahaṃ tu bhavatādiṣṭaṃ cintayāmi nijavratam  KAvk ityupādhyāyamabhyarthya bhaktakṛtyāya paṇḍitaḥ tasmin yāte tadādiṣṭaṃ vihārāgāramāviśat  KAvk tatra yaṣṭīkṛtatanuḥ kṛtvā pratimukhīṃ smṛtim sa pradadhyau nijaṃ dharmaṃ baddhaparyaṅkaniścalaḥ  KAvk tasmin samādhisaṃnaddhe vasudhā sadharādharā vicacālākhilāmbhodhijalaloladukūlinī  KAvk śakrastaṃ dhyānanirataṃ jñātvā nirvighnasiddhaye dideśa dikṣu rakṣāyai dikpālān sendubhāskarān  KAvk bhagavānatha sarvajñastasya siddhimupasthitām pākāt kuśalamūlānāṃ jñātvā kṣaṇamacintayat  KAvk āsannārhatpadasyāsya śāriputraḥ sametya cet dvāramuddhāṭayenmadhye vighna eṣa na saṃśayaḥ  KAvk tasmādāgacchatastasya gatvā svayamahaṃ puraḥ karomi kālahārāya nānāpraśnāśrayāḥ kathāḥ  KAvk iti saṃcintya bhagavān svayaṃ taddiśamāgataḥ bhikṣorāgacchatasyasya vjlambaṃ kathayākarot  KAvk suraprabhāvānniḥśabde nabhogatavihaṃgame loke nirvātadīpasya tulyatāṃ prāpa paṇḍitaḥ  KAvk srotaḥ prāptiphalādūrdhvaṃ sakṛdāgāmyavāpya saḥ anāgāmiphalaṃ prāpya tato rhatphalamāptavān  KAvk tataḥ kathānte sugate prayāte nijamāśramam śāriputraḥ praviśyarkamiva śiṣyaṃ vyalokayat  KAvk taṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasottīrṇaṃ viśīrṇabhavabandhanam siddhiṃ yugaśataprāpyāṃ tasya tām praśaśaṃsa saḥ  KAvk tāṃ tasyārhatpadaprāptiṃ śrutvā jagati viśrutām bhikṣubhirbhagavāṇ pṛṣṭastatkathāmabravījjinah  KAvk bhagavān kāśyapaḥ pūrvaṃ vārāṇasyāṃ tathāgataḥ saha bhikṣūsahasrāṇāṃ viṃśatyā puravāsibhiḥ  KAvk śraddhāpraṇītaiḥ śucibhiḥ sarvabhogyairmanonugaiḥ uvāsa pūjitah kaṃcit kālaṃ sattvahitodyataḥ  KAvk bhikṣupūjāpare tatra vartamāne gṛhe gṛhe acintyayadviniḥśvasya durgato nāma durgataḥ  KAvk dhiṅ māmatīva dāridyrāt nīcaṃ niṣkuśalakriyam naiko pi mandabhāgyena yena bhikṣurnimantritaḥ  KAvk tyājyā janasya sakalavyavahārabāhyāḥ vākyapramāṇapadasaṃdhiṣu naiva yogyāḥ naṣṭakriyā vigatakārakatarkahīnāḥ śabdā ivārtharahitāḥ puruṣā bhavanti  KAvk iti cintānalākrāntaṃ ninditaṃ dhanahīnataḥ taṃ samāhūya ko pyetya sukṛtaprerako bhyadhāt  KAvk kṣīṇārthenāpi bhavatā janmāntaraśubhāptaye yathākathaṃcideko pi bhikṣuḥ kiṃ na nimantritaḥ  KAvk ityuktastena saṃsaktaśalyaḥ punarivāhataḥ bhiokṣubhojanavaikalyāt sa bhṛdhaṃ vyathito bhavat  KAvk kathaṃcitkṣḥutparikṣāmaḥ sa gatvā śreṣṭhimandiram yatnena prāpa mūlyāṃśaṃ dārupāṭanakarmaṇā  KAvk kṛtvā tatraiva tadbhāryā śuddhataṇḍulakhaṇḍanam tadaṃśabhṛtimūlyāptaṃ bhaktyā bhartre nyavedayat  KAvk samudyatasya tasyātha bhikṣubhojanasiddhaye śuddhaye śuddhasattvasya śakro bhūdanusādhakah  KAvk divyavarṇarasāmode bhojye śakreṇa sādhite prītyā pracchannarūpeṇa bhikṣuṃ lekhe na durgataḥ  KAvk vibhūtimohitairgūḍhaiḥ pūrvaṃ puranivāsibhiḥ saṃghe nimantrite duḥkhāt durgato martumudyayau  KAvk kṛpayā tasya bhagavān svayamabhyetya kāśyapaḥ śuddhisiddhiṃ parijñāya cakre bhojyapratigraham  KAvk aho haṃ bhavato bhojyaṃ prayacchāmīti bhūbhujā prayatnāt prārtito pyarthaṃ naivāmanyata durgataḥ  KAvk guṇadraviṇasaṃpūrṇaḥ syāṃ daridraprasādanaḥ bhagavantamathābhyarcya praṇīdhānaṃ cakāra saḥ  KAvk svāśramaṃ kāśyape yāte surendre ca divaṃ gate durgatasya gṛhaṃ sarvaṃ divyaratnaipūrayat  KAvk viśvakarmā tatastasya vidadhe śakraśāsanāt bhavanaṃ rucirodyānaṃ ratnastambhavibhūṣitam  KAvk saṃprāptavimalaiśvaryaḥ sahitaṃ sarvabhikṣubhiḥ saptāhaṃ vibhavairbhogaiḥ sa kāśyapamapūjayat  KAvk kṣutkṣāmāṅganamarthibhiḥ parihṛtadvāraṃ rudaddārakaṃgehaṃ niścalakajjalānyapi sthalīkoṇasvananmakṣikam  cullīsuptabiḍālabālamaparaṃ yasyābhavadrauravaṃśrīstasyaiva nṛpaspṛhāspadatayāścaryaṃ na kasya svayam  KAvk tena dānaprabhāveṇa sudhāśuddhena durgataḥ janmāntare paṇḍitatāmavāpyārhattvamāgataḥ  KAvk iti paṇḍitapūrvajanmavṛttaṃ kathitaṃ sarvavidā guṇādareṇa avadhārya viśuddhadānapuṇyaṃ kuśalārhaṃ praśaśaṃsa bhikṣusaṃghaḥ  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ kapilāvadānaṃ nāmaikacatvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  kanakavarṇāvadānam sattvena sūryarucayastamasi sphuranti dharmeṇa ratnanicayā nabhasaḥ tapanti dhairyeṇa sarvavipadaḥ praśamaṃ vrajanti dānena bhogasubhagāḥ kakubho bhavanti  KAvk bhagavān sugataḥ pūrvaṃ śrāvastyāṃ jetakānane kuśalānāṃ prapānnānāṃ vidadhe dharmadeśanām  KAvk pūrvakalpāntarajane vatsarāṣṭāyutāyuṣi śrīmān kanakavarṇākhyo babhūva pṛthivīpatiḥ  KAvk kanakākhyā purī tasya śakrasyevāmarāvatī sarvalokeśvarasyāpi vasatirvallabhābhavat  KAvk nāyakārhaṃ yaśaḥśubhraṃ cāruvṛttaguṇocitam hṝdaye yaḥ prajākāryaṃ muktāhāramivāvahat  KAvk prajākarmavipākena pure paramadāruṇā avṛṣṭirabhavat tatra sarvabhūtabhayapradā  KAvk sā dhairyahāriṇī sarvalokasaṃtāpakāriṇī avṛṣṭiḥ prayayau bhūbhṛnmānasāyāsahetutām  KAvk kuṇṭhasarvapratīkāraḥ sa cintāstimitaṃ puraḥ uvāca suciraṃ dhyātvā pradhānāmātyamaṇḍalam  KAvk avarṣopanipāto yaṃ prajānāṃ niṣpratikriyaḥ karoti me yatnakṛtaṃ niṣphalaṃ paripālanam  KAvk nivṛttavarṣāḥ kakubho bhavantyabhrāśca svacchakāḥ pravṛttabāṣpavarṣāśca prajāḥ pāpena bhūbhujām  KAvk trāṇaṃ mahābhayādrājā prajānāṃ na karoti yaḥ tasya spaṣṭaṃ naṭasyeva kirīṭamukuṭagrahaḥ  KAvk tadā kṝtayugaṃ loke yadā rājā prajāhitaḥ  KAvk durbhikṣakṣayitāḥ pṛthutarakleśāvalīvihvalāḥ hāhākāraviśṛṅkhalāḥ khalatarairatyarditā vallabhaiḥśocantyaḥ pralayaṃ prayāntaśaraṇāḥ pāpairnṛpāṇāṃ prajāḥ  KAvk tasmātsamastakoṣeṇa rakṣaṇīyā mayā prajāḥ rājñāṃ prajāparitrāṇapuṇyaṃ ratnamayo nidhiḥ  KAvk ityuktvā sarvalokasya saṃcintya koṣṭhakoṣayoḥ sa nināya nijaṃ sarvaṃ sadā bhogyopabhogyatām  KAvk tataḥ kālena tasyogradurbhikṣeṇānnasaṃcayaḥ yayau mahāvyayādekapuruṣāśanaśeṣatām  KAvk tasminnavasare vyomnā samabhyetya raviprabhaḥ pratyekabuddhastasyātha vidadhe bhojanārthanām  KAvk niyame saṃśaye tasminnātmanaḥ prāṇadhāraṇe nirvikalpya sa tatasrvaṃ dadau tasmai prasannadhīḥ  KAvk svaprāṇavṛttiṃ tenāsau kṛtvātithyaprasādinā prayayau nabahsā tasya prasaṃśan sattvaśīaltām  KAvk athodyayau vyaomamahādvipasya nīlālimāleva sadambulekhā meghāvalī paścimadikpralambā kapolakālāgurumañjarīva  KAvk tataḥ samastaṃ gaganāntarālamutphullanīlotpalakānanābham ācchādyamānaṃ sarasairbabhāse bhṛṅgapravandhauriva meghasaṃghaiḥ  KAvk tataḥ papātākhilabhojyavṛṣṭiriṣṭā prajānāṃ bhuvi sapta rātrīḥ dhānyādivṛṣṭistadanantaraṃ ca ratnadivṛṣṭiśca tataḥ krameṇa  KAvk iti sa kanakavarṇaḥ kṣmāpatirbhūpatīnāṃ mukuṭamaṇirivoccairbhrājamānaḥ prajānām akṛta sukṛtasaṃpatprīṇitah prāṇarakṣāṃ prabhavati hi parārthe sajjanānāṃ prabhāvaḥ  KAvk bhūpatiḥ kanakavarṇa eṣa yaḥ so hameva vapuṣātmanādhunā ityudīrya bhagavān jinaḥ satāṃ dhīmatāṃ vyadhita dharmadeśanām  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ kanakavarṇāvadānaṃ nāma dvicatvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  hiraṇyapāṇyavadānam sarvopakārapraṇayī prabhāvaḥ sarvopajīvyā mahatī vibhūtiḥ puṇyāṅkurārhasya phalaṃ viśālapalārhametat prathamaṃ hi puṣpam  KAvk jine jetavanārāmavihārābhigate purā śrāvastyāṃ devasenākhyaḥ śrīmānāsīdgṛhādhipaḥ  KAvk hiraṇṃyapāṇistasyābhūtputraḥ satputramāninaḥ yasya hemamayaṃ jātaṃ pāṇidvitayamadbhutam  KAvk rūpyalakṣadvayaṃ tasya prātaḥ prātaḥ karadvaye prādurāsītsa tenābhūdarthināṃ kalpapādapaḥ  KAvk tasya vyaktavivekena paripākena bhūyasā kāle kuśalamūlānāṃ jine bhaktirajāyata  KAvk atha jetavana gatvā bahgavantaṃ tathāgatam sa dṛṣṭvā vidadhe tasya sānandaḥ pādavandanam  KAvk bhagavānapi saṃṣāratāpapraśamacandikām sudhāsakhīṃ dideśāsmai dṛśaṃ kuśalavṛtikām  KAvk sa śāsturdarśanenaiva saṃmohatimitojjhita babhāse suryakiraṇaprabuddhakamalopamaḥ  KAvk bhagavān vidadhe tasya tataḥ saddharmadeśanām yayā dharmamayaṃ cakṣurakṣuṇṇālokamudyayau  KAvk prākpuṇyapariṇāmena jātavairāgyavāsanaḥ praṇamya vimalaprajñaḥ sa sarvajñamabhāṣataḥ  KAvk śaraṇya śaraṇāptasya bhagavan bhavahāriṇī aśeṣakleśanāśāya pravrajyā me vidhīyatām  KAvk capalaṃ prāṇināmāyuṣtato pi navayauvanam vidyudvilāsacapalāstato pyetā vibhūtayaḥ  KAvk iti tasya bruvāṇasya sugatānugrahoditā papāta vitarajasaḥ pravrajyā vapuṣi svayam  KAvk raktacīvarasuvyaktāṃ bibhrāṇaḥ sa viraktatām pātragraheṇa tatyāja punaḥ saṃsārapātratām  KAvk tasya tāmadbhutāṃ siddhiṃ pratyakṣaṃ vīkṣyaṃ bhikṣavaḥ tatpūrvavṛttaṃ papracchurbhagavantaṃ sa cābravīt  KAvk vārāṇasyāṃ purā rājā kṛkirnāma tathāgate kāśyapākhye bhagavati prayāti parinirvṛtim  KAvk śarīramasya samkṛtya stūpaṃ ratnamayaṃ vyadhāt svargāvagāhanaprauḍhaṃ mūrtaṃ puṇyamivonnatam  KAvk tasminnāropyamāṇāyāṃ yaṣṭayāṃ pūjāparigrahe kitavaḥ kandalo nāma nidadhe rūpakadvayam  KAvk cittaprasādaśuddhena tena puṇyena bhūyasā hiraṇyapāṇiḥ prāpto dya mahatāṃ spṝhaṇīyatām  KAvk bhavati vibhavastyāgodāraḥ samagraguṇo bhuviprasaratiḥ yaśaḥ śuklaṃ loke sudhāṃśusahodaram pariṇatipade puṇyaṃ dhatte yadalpamanalpatāṃvimalamanasaḥ śraddhāśuddhaṃ tadeva vijṛmbhitam  KAvk iti prabhāvaṃ kathitaṃ jinena puṇyānubhāvasya hiraṇyapāṇeḥ śrutvaiva harṣādaravismayānāṃ sa bhikṣusaṃghaḥ praṇayī babhūva  KAvk iti kṣemandraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ hiraṇyapāṇyavadānaṃ tricatvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  ajātaśatrupitṛdrohāvadānam durjanaduḥsahaviṣadharabhīṣaṇataratimirapatitānām ālambanajananaṃ bhavabhayaharaṇaṃ jinasmaraṇam  KAvk pure rājagṛhābhikhye bhagavān bhūbhṛtaḥ purā kaṭake gṛdhrakūṭasya vijahāra tathāgataḥ  KAvk tasminnavasare rājā bimbisāraḥ sutapriyaḥ ajātaśatruṇā tatra putreṇa krūrakāriṇā  KAvk suhṛdaḥ pāvakasyeva devadattasya saṃmatam ghorāndhabandhanāgāraṃ niḥsaṃcāraṃ praveśitaḥ  KAvk patnyā praveśitaṃ tasya bandhane gūḍhabhojanam jñātvā sa tatkṣayākāṅkṣī kṣutkṣāmasya nyavārayat  KAvk rūkṣaḥ kṛśo timalinaḥ so bhavat pṛthivīpatiḥ akālakālameghārtaḥ kṛṣṇapakṣa ivoḍupaḥ  KAvk saṃkīrṇavāsasaṃtāpātprāyaḥ peśalacetasām karotyāliṅganaṃ prauḍhā gāḍhapraṇayinī vipat  KAvk sa samuddhiśya śokārtaḥ sugatādhyuṣitāṃ diśam kṛtāñjalirnataśirāḥ kṣāmasvaramabhāṣata  KAvk nāmastubhyaṃ bhagavate mahārhāya mahārhate dīnoddharaṇasaṃnaddhasamyaksaṃbodhibodhicetase  KAvk namaste ghorasaṃsāramakarākarasetave jināya janatājanmakleśapraśamahetave  KAvk namo nityaprabuddhāya sarvasattvaikabandhave viśuddhadhānme buddhāya karuṇāmṛtasindhave  KAvk iti bhaktisudhāṃ śiktvā sugataśravaṇocitām puṇyapuṣpaprasavinīṃ sa cakre stutimañjarīm  KAvk sarvajñastasya vijñāya kāyakleśaśamayīṃ daśām bandhanāgāravivarālokairāpyāyanam vyadhāt  KAvk ajātaśatrustadvṛttaṃ jñātvā śaṅkākulaḥ pituḥ nyavārayadbandhagṛhe susūkṣmavivarāṇyapi  KAvk tatastasya tadādeśāt cakrurbandhanarakṣiṇaḥ kṣureṇa gāḍhabaddhasya pādayostadvikartanam  KAvk sa tīvravaiśasakleśavyathitah pārthivaḥ param namo buddhāya buddhāyetyārtasaṃkrandanaṃ vyadhāt  KAvk bhagavānatha sarvajñaḥ puraḥ pratyakṣatāṃ gataḥ śakradattāsanāsīnaḥ kāruṇyāttamabhāṣataḥ  KAvk rājan kiṃ kriyate krūrakarmaṇāṃ gatirīdṛśī śubhāśubhasamudbhūtaṃ na bhuktaṃ kṣiyate phalam  KAvk rāgadveṣaviṣāsakte nānāvyasanaduḥsahe evaṃvidhaiva niḥsāre saṃsāre duḥkhasāratā  KAvk saṃkleśakalile kāle vipatsaṃpadvisaṃkaṭe dhairyameva paritrāṇaṃ vairāgyaṃ ca nirākulam  KAvk saṃsāraghoragahanāntaravardhamānaiḥ duḥkhānalavyatikaraprasṛtairasiktāḥ dhūmodgamairiva punaḥ sukṛtocitānāṃ bāṣpāmbubindukalilā na dṛśo bhavanti  KAvk bhajasva dhairyaṃ duḥkhe smin bhogāśāṃ tyaja bhūpate pariṇāmavirodhinyaḥ sarvāḥ saṃsāravṛttayaḥ  KAvk adhunaiva tavāsannā dehātte kuśalasthitiḥ ityuktvā taṃ samāśvasya bhagavān svapadaṃ yayau  KAvk bimbisāro pi dehānte tasminneva kṣaṇe divi abhūjjinarṣabho nāma śrīmān vaiśravaṇātmajaḥ  KAvk ajātaśatrurjanakaṃ jñātvā vigatajīvitam śarīramasya satkṛtya nininda nijaduṣkṛtam  KAvk tasyātitīvrapāpārtaṃ cittaṃ durvṛttadūṣitam paścāttāpāgnipatanaṃ prāyaścittamivākarot  KAvk so vadadbata saṃmohādaiśvaryamadalubdhadhīḥ durvṛttapātakaśvabhre patito hamadhomukhaḥ  KAvk śrutaprajñādaridrāṇāṃ nijanidrāsukhāpahā cintā dahati gātrāṇi khalamantrānuvartinām  KAvk patitasyāvasannasya pāpapaṅke pramādinah anālambasya saṃtrāṇaṃ jinasaṃsmaraṇaṃ mama  KAvk iti saṃcintya suciraṃ sa gatvā sugatāntikam jugupsamānaḥ kukṛtātparaṃ saṃkocamāyayau  KAvk tatrāpavitramātmānaṃ manyamānaḥ sapatrapaḥ praṇanāma jinaṃ dūrāt pāpasparśabhayādiva  KAvk sāśrunetraḥ paritrāṇaṃ sa sarvajñaṃ vyajijñapat sakampaḥ kāyasaṃsaktaṃ vidhunvanniva duṣkṛtam  KAvk bhagavan kṛtapāyo hamāsannanarakānalaḥ uttaptaḥ karuṇāsindhuṃ tvāmeva śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  KAvk māmiyaṃ śoṇaparyantā dṛṣṭiste puṣkaraprabhā  KAvk khalamantrapravṛttena durvṛttena pramādinā mayā vibhavalubdhena pāpena nihataḥ pitā  KAvk iti pralāpinastasya vacaḥ śrutvā tathāgataḥ sasarha tatpāparajaḥśuddhyai puṇyasarasvatīm  KAvk rājanna cintitaḥ pāpaḥ khaleneva svakarmaṇā preritastvaṃ pitṛvadhe patitaḥ pāpasaṃkaṭe  KAvk duḥkhaṃ tattena bhoktavyaṃ prāptavyaṃ kilbiṣaṃ tvayā tava tasya ca bhūpāla tulyaiṣā bhavitavyatā  KAvk nijakaṇṭhasamutkīrṇāṃ lalāṭapaṭavartinī śilāśakalalekheva niścalā niyatirnṛṇām  KAvk kurvatā kaluṣaṃ karma khalapreraṇayā tvayā pratyāsannāmṛtaśreyaḥ svahastena tiraskṛtam  KAvk adyāpi yadi te pāpaṃ hantuṃ prāptuṃ ca saṃpadam vāñchāsti tatkuru matiṃ puṇye pāpaśamātmani  KAvk dīpavṛttyā sukhaṃ sūte jīvayatyujjvalaṃ yaśah amṛtasya prakāro yaṃ suvṛttaḥ satsamāgamaḥ  KAvk paścāttāpāgnupātena sādhunā saṃgamena ca saṃkīrtanena dānena pāpaṃ naśyati dehinām  KAvk pātraṃ pavitrayati naiva guṇān kṣiṇoti snehaṃ na saṃharati naiva malaṃ prasūte doṣāvasānaruciraścalatāṃ na dhatte satsaṃgamaḥ sukṛtasadmani ko pi dīpaḥ  KAvk guṇigaṇavipaddīkṣādakṣaḥ kṣapākṣaṇasaṃnibhaḥsakalanayanavyāpārāṇāṃ janeṣu nirodhakaḥ asamaviṣamāyāsāvāsaḥ prakāśaparikṣayātsṛjati hi mahāmohāgdāḍhaṃ tamaḥ khalasaṃgamaḥ  KAvk pratyekabuddhastvaṃ rājan kālena kṣīṇakilbiṣaḥ bhaviṣyasi vivekena kṛtālekaḥ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ  KAvk iti tasya dayāśvāsaṃ cakāra bahgavān jinah patiteṣvadhikaṃ santaḥ karuṇāsnigdhalocanāḥ  KAvk tataḥ praṇamya sugataṃ prayātaḥ svapadaṃ nṛpaḥ mahataḥ pāpabhārasya viveda laghutāmiva  KAvk tasmin prayāte sarvajñaḥ pṛṣṭastatkarma kautukāt bhikṣubhiḥ kṣitipālasya pūrvavṛttamabhāṣata  KAvk vārāṇasyāṃ nirāyāsavilāsavyavasāyinaḥ catvāraḥ śreṣṭhitanayā babhūvuḥ śrīviśṛṅkhalāḥ  KAvk te kadācit sukhakṣībā mithaḥ kalikathāsthitāḥ pratyekabuddhamāyāntaṃ dadṛśuryauvanoddhatāḥ  KAvk taṃ dṛṣṭvā jātavidveṣāḥ śamasaṃyamanindakāḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ sundarako nāma bhrātṝn provāca sasmitaḥ  KAvk ayaṃ cīvarapātrāṅkaḥ pānena gatajīvitaḥ kṣibo vidhīyate bhikṣurityayaṃ me manorathaḥ  KAvk ityukte cāpalāt tena dvitīyaḥ kundarābhidhaḥ uvāca bhikṣuṃ kṣiptvemaṃ hantumicchāmyahaṃ jale  KAvk tatastṛtīyo pyavadat pāpaḥ sundarakābhidhaḥ  eṣa bhikṣurvaraṃ tasyāṃ vīthyāṃ nikṣipyate javāt  KAvk caturtho pyavadat krūramatiḥ kandarakābhidhaḥ bhikṣoḥ kṣureṇa kriyate niścarma caraṇadvayam  KAvk iti teṣāṃ bruvāṇānāṃ kaluṣo bhūnmanorathaḥ yena janmāntare prāpuste svecchāsadṛśaṃ phalam  KAvk dhanaṃ paśyati lobhāndhaḥ kridhāndhaḥ śatrumeva ca kāmāndhah kāminīmeva darpāndhastu na kiṃcana  KAvk dhanidbhūtavikārāṇāṃ prayātyaniyatātmanām madamandavicārāṇāmānandaḥ kleśabandhatām  KAvk krudhyantyakāraṇamakāraṇamutpatanti snihyantyakāraṇamakāraṇamāmananti mohāhatāḥ khalu hitāhitanirvicārāḥ tṛptāḥ paraṃ nṛpaśavaḥ samadā bhavanti  KAvk jyeṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhisutaḥ pāpātsa evāparajanmani śāriryānābhidhaḥ śākyaḥ pītvā madyaṃ vyapadyata  KAvk dvitīyo pi mahānnāma śākyastoye kṣayaṃ gataḥ tṛtīyaśca svaputreṇa vyasto rājā prasenajit  KAvk bimbisāraścaturtho sau dhṛtaḥ putreṇa bandhane prayuktaṃ dhanavatkarma bhujyate hi savṛddhikam  KAvk mohāhatairiha hi sadbhirasadbhireṣāṃ niḥśarma karma sahasaiva viḍambyate yat bāṣpāmbupūrṇanayanairanayopanītaḥmastokaśokavivaśairanubhūyate tra  KAvk  KAvksugatakathitametat pūrvajanmapravṛttaṃ viṣaviṣamavipākaṃ bimbisārasya vṛttam vibudhasadasi bhikṣuḥ spaṣṭamākarṇya mene vyasanaśatanimittaṃ dūṣitaṃ cittameva  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyām bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāmajātaśatrupitṛdrodāvadānaṃ nāma catuścatvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  kṛtajñāvadānam andhīkṛto pi svadṛśā tamasā khalena lakṣmīvihāravirahe vinipātito pi kaṣṭāṃ daśāmiva niśāmativāhya padmaḥ svāmeva saṃpadamupaiti punarguṇāḍhyaḥ  KAvk śrāvastyāṃ sugate jetavanodyānavihāriṇi devadattaḥ paridveṣavyādhivyāpto vyacintayat  KAvk tulyaḥ samāno me bhrātā manuṣyaḥ śākyavaṃśajaḥ prāptaḥ puṇyaprabhāveṇa trijagatpūjyatāṃ jinaḥ  KAvk jīvitodvṛttaye tasmāt taysya yatnaṃ karomyaham na hyanastaṃgate bhānau paratejaḥ prakāśate  KAvk vijñānenānubhāvena vidyayā tapasā śriyā paraprakarṣaṃ sahate na hi mānonnataṃ manah  KAvk viṣaṃ nijanakhāgreṣu dhṛtvā tasya praṇāmakṛt saṃcārayāmi vapuṣi nediṣṭhaḥ pādapīḍaṇaiḥ  KAvk iti saṃcintya kaluṣaṃ vidveṣavivaśaḥ khalah sa tiṣyapramukhānetya bāndhavānidamabhyadhāt  KAvk krūraḥ kṛtāpakāro haṃ sugatasyādya pādayoḥ saralasya prasādāya ptāmi gurupātakah  KAvk iti bruvāṇastaiḥ sarvaiḥ sudattānumataiḥ saha jinaṃ jetavanāsīnaṃ draṣṭuṃ duṣṭamatiryayau  KAvk bhagavantaṃ vilokyābhūttatra yāvatsa sarvaśaḥ tāvaddagdho hamityuccairutkṣiptacaraṇo vadat  KAvk huiṃsāsaṃkalpapāpena vrajreṇeva samāhataḥ saśarīraṃ kṣaṇe tasmin narakāgnau papāta saḥ  KAvk sarvajñaḥ sahasā dṛṣṭvā taṃ ghoranarake cyutam uvāca śrutatadvṛttavismitāṃ bhikṣusaṃsadam  KAvk eṣa kilbiṣadoṣeṇa patitaḥ kleśasaṃkaṭe tīvram hi timira sūte sarvathā malinaṃ manaḥ  KAvk nagaryāmatighoṣāyāṃ ratisomasya bhūpateḥ kṛtajñaścākṛtajñaśca purā putrau babhūvatuḥ  KAvk kṛtajñaḥ kṛpayārthibhyaḥ kalpavṛkṣaḥ ivāniśam nijaṃ vimucya pradadau ratnābharaṇasaṃcayam  KAvk avibhaktaṃ piturdravyaṃ sarvaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ tayoḥ vadannityakṛtajñpo pi ten adattaḥ jahat tat  KAvk tataḥ ślādhyāya vacasā matighoṣābhodho nṛpaḥ janakalyānikāṃ nāma kṛtajñāya sutāṃ dadau  KAvk svayamevārjitaṃ vittaṃ dātuṃ jātamanorathaḥ āruroham pravahaṇaṃ kṛtajño tha mahodadhau  KAvk ratnārjanodyataṃ yāntaṃ taṃ dveṣaspardhitādaraḥ tamevānuyayau lobhādakṛtajño pi durjanaḥ  KAvk saṃpūrṇaṃ vaṇijāṃ sārthaiḥ tataḥ pravahaṇaṃ śanaiḥ ānukūlyena matutāmavāpa dvīpamīpsitam  KAvk tasmin pratinivṛtte tha svadeśaṃ gantumudyate ratnarāśibhirāpūrṇasaṃklape svadeśaṃ gantumudyate  KAvk kṛtajñaḥ pṛthivīmūlyaṃ ratnānāṃ śatapaḥñcakam ādāya granthipaṭṭena babandhāṃśukapallave  KAvk ratnabhārapariśrāntaṃ tataḥ pravahaṇaṃ mahat abhajyata mahāvātairaiśvaryamiva durnayaiḥ  KAvk tataḥ phalakavāhastaṃ kṛtajñaḥ prāptajīvitaḥ akṛtajñaṃ nimajjantaṃ pṛṣṭhena samatārayat  KAvk tāritaḥ kṛpayā bhrātrā sa ghoramakarākarāt apaśyadañcale tasya ruciraṃ ratnasaṃcayam  KAvk sa tasya ratnalobhena dveṣena ca vaśīkṛtaḥ samudratīre śrāntasya bhrāturdrohamacintayat  KAvk tasya nidrānilīnasya śastreṇotpāṭya locanam gṛhītvā ratnanicayaṃ kṛtaghnaḥ sa yayau javāt  KAvk krūreṇāṅgīkṛtastena rāhuṇeva divākara lokopakāravihato duḥkhitaḥ so pyacintayat  KAvk adhunārthipradāne rthe vyarthībhūte manorathe kiṃ mamāndhasya vandhyena jīvitena prayojanam  KAvk aprāptaviṣayāḥ prāṇā na prayānti yadi kṣayam tadasaṃgatayo yogāḥ kleśaynti kṣyakṣamāḥ  KAvk kṣaṇe dhane jane dveṣamānavaikalyavihvale pūjye puṃsāṃ samenaiva śeṣasya ca yaśovyayaḥ  KAvk iti saṃcintya sa śanairvrajansārthena tāritaḥ avāpa nagaropāntaṃ matighoṣasya bhūpateḥ  KAvk gopālabhavane tatra sa kaṃcitkālamāsthitaḥ udyānayātrāgatayā rājaputryā vilokitah  KAvk taṃ dṛṣṭvāndhamapi vyaktarājalakśaṇalakṣitam prāgjanmapremabandhena sābhilāṣā babhūva sā  KAvk tataḥ svayaṃvaravidhiṃ sā kṛtvā śāsanātpituḥ rājñāṃ madhye ca mānyānāṃ vavre vigatalocanam  KAvk bhūmipālān parityajya vṛto ndhaḥ pāpayā tvayā uktveti pitrā kopena nirastā śuśubhe na sā  KAvk udyāne sā nidhāyāndhaṃ yatnenāhṛtya bhojanam sadā tasmai dadau premapraṇayopacitādarā  KAvk kadācittāṃ cirāyātāmāhārāvasare gate uvāca rājatanayaḥ paraṃ mlānānanaḥ kṣudhā  KAvk asamīkṣitakāriṇā tvayā kevalacāpalāt vṛto hamandhaḥ saṃtyajya nṛpān vipulalocanān  KAvk paścāttāpena nūnaṃ tvaṃ mayi paryuṣitādarā adhunā tāṇḍavaṃ premṇah pradarśayitumudyatā  KAvk andhasaṃdarśanodvignā surūpālokanonmukhī āhārakāle tikrānte cireṇeha tvamāgatā  KAvk ityuktvā paruṣaṃ tena kampamānā lateva sā uvāca guñjanmadhupaśreṇīmadhuravādinī  KAvk nātha mithyaiva me śankāṃ na kopātkartumarhasi vāgbāṇapātaṃ sahate na cetaḥ prītipeśalaṃ  KAvk tvāmeca devatāṃ jāne yadyahaṃ śuddhamānas ā tena satyena sālokamekaṃ nayanamastu te  KAvk ityukte sattvaśālinyā tayā tasyāśu locanam utphullakamalākāramekaṃ vimalatām yayau  KAvk tasyāh satyaprabhāveṇa saṃjātapṛthuvismayah satyapratyayasotsāhaṃ kṛtajñastāmabhāṣata  KAvk bhrātrā tenākṛtajñna pāṭite locanadvaye tasmin vikāro vairaṃ vā na nikāro pyabhūnmama  KAvk svacchaṃ tenāstu satyena dvitīyamapi locanam ityukte takṣaṇenāsya spaṣṭaṃ cakṣuralakṣyata  KAvk ataḥ kathitavṛttāntaṃ kṛtajñamucitaṃ patim prahṛṣṭā janakalyāṇī gatvā pitre nyavedayat  KAvk pūjitaḥ śvaśureṇātha sa ratnagajavājibhiḥ śriyeva kāntayā sārdhaṃ jagāma nagaraṃ pituḥ  KAvk sa tatra pitrā hṛṣṭena caraṇālīnaśekharaḥ janānurāgasubhage yaivarājye pade dhṛtaḥ  KAvk akṛtajño pi nirlajjastaṃ prasādayituṃ śaṭhaḥ vicintya pādapatane tasya drohaṃ samāyayau  KAvk unmanā hantumāyātaḥ sa taṃ kuṭulaceṣṭitaḥ hāhā dagdho smi dagdho smītyuktvaiva narake patat  KAvk sa eva devadatto sau kṛtajño pyahameva ca janmāntarānubandhena dveṣo sya na nivartate  KAvk sarvajñabhāṣitamiti pracuropakāraṃ taddevadattacaritaṃ paritāpakāri janmāntaropacitapātakasaṃnibaddhaṃ śrutvā babhūva vimanā iva bhikṣusaṃghaḥ  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ kṛtajñāvadānaṃ pañcacatvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  śālistambāvadānam dānaikatānamanasāṃ pṛthusattvabhājāmutsāhamānaguṇabhogavibhūṭipūtaḥ prākuṇyasaṃcayamayaḥ kuśalabhidhānaḥ kāle phalatyavikalaḥ kila kalpavṛkṣaḥ  KAvk kosalendrasya bhūbhartuḥ śrāvastyām bhagavān purā vijahāra va rodyāne saha bhikṣagaṇairjinaḥ  KAvk ādimadhyāṇtakalyāṇaṃ bahvābhibhavasādhakam saṃdideśa sa saddharmaṃ trailokyakuśalodyataḥ  KAvk atrāṇtare nāgarājaputrāḥ sāgaravāsinah catvāraḥ sugatodīrṇaṃ saddharmaṃ paramāmṛtam  KAvk abhiratyākhyayā svasrā preritāḥ śrotumāgatāḥ te balātibalaśvāsamahāśvāsābhidhāḥ samam  KAvk krakucchandasya sudhiyaḥ kāle bhagavataḥ pura kanakākhyasya ca muneḥ kāśyapasya ca yatnataḥ  KAvk ājagmuḥ śrīsukhāsaktāḥ śrotumaprārthitā api tatpuṇyapariṇāmena prāptāḥ śākyamuneḥ purā  KAvk teṣu praṇamya śāstāraṃ caraṇālīnamauliṣu vidhāya mānuṣaṃ rūpamupaviṣṭeṣu parṣadi  KAvk saddharmamāyayau śrotuṃ kosalendraḥ prasenajit lakṣmīmandasmitacchāyaṃ nivārya cchatracāmaram  KAvk śāstuḥ pādapraṇāmāya viśatastasya saṃsadi avakāśaṃ natāścakruḥ sarve nṛpatigauravāt  KAvk tasyābhinandyamānasya varṣāśramagurornṛbhiḥ nāgarājasutāścakrurnāvakāśaṃ na satkṛtam  KAvk tasyābhinandyamānasya varṇāśramagurornṛbhiḥ nāgarājasutāścakrurnāvakāśaṃ na satkṛtam  KAvk sa saṃjñayā samādiśya nijaṃ parijanaṃ puraḥ gamane nigraham teṣāṃ nirvikāra ivābhavat  KAvk bhagavānapi sarvajñastasya jñātvā ca niścayam dharmopadeśaparyante provāca racitasmitaḥ  KAvk na vidveṣarajaḥpūrṇamanomalinadarpaṇe bhāti dharmopadeśasya pratibimbapratigrahaḥ  KAvk avihitasamatānāṃ kopamohāhatānāṃ kṛśamapi kuśalāṃśaṃ nopadeśaḥ karoti na hi vahutaradoṣe śuddhihīne śarīre vrajati hatamatīnām bheṣajaṃ bheṣajatvama  KAvk iti yuktaṃ bhagavatā hitamuktaṃ mahīpatiḥ śrutvāpi na ca tatyāja nāgeṣu vimanaskatām  KAvk bhagavantaṃ praṇamyātha prayāte svapadaṃ nṛpe nāgāstatsainikābaddhamārge vyomapathā yayuḥ  KAvk te vicintya svabhavane kṣmāsaṃkṣayakṛtakṣaṇāḥ ghoranirghātameghaughagrastalokāḥ samāyayuḥ  KAvk teṣāṃ vyavasitaṃ jñātvā sarvajñaḥ pakṣapātinām rakṣḥākṣamaṃ kṣitipatermaudgalyāyanamādiśat  KAvk atha nāgagaṇotsṛṣṭā vajravṛṣṭirmahīpatau bhūbhartustatprabhāveṇa prayayau puṣpavṛṣṭitām  KAvk śastrāstravṛṣṭirnibiḍakṣiptā tairatha duḥsahā maudgalyāyanasaṃkalpādyayau rājārhabhojyatām  KAvk tatprabhāvātprayāteṣu bhognotsāheṣu bhogiṣu gatvā vavande sugataṃ nṛpatirvītaviplavaḥ  KAvk sa maudgalyāyanasyārghyamucitaṃ bhogasaṃpadā bhaktisaṃskārasubhagaṃ vidadhe jianśāsanāt  KAvk tataḥ svargocitām bhikṣurvibhūtiṃ vīkṣya bhūpateḥ papraccha kautukavaśāt sarvajñaṃ caritāñjaliḥ  KAvk bhagavan kasya puṇyasya prabhāveṇa prasenajit sarvairvirājitaṃ bhogaiḥ prājyaṃ rājyamavāptavān  KAvk ikṣustambavadetasya śālistambaśca jāyate divyapānānnasaṃpattiḥ phalaṃ tatkasya karmaṇaḥ  KAvk iti pṛṣṭaḥ praṇayinā bhikṣuṇā bhagavān jinaḥ uvāca śrūyatāṃ rājñaḥ kāraṇaṃ bhogasaṃpadām  KAvk kosale smin janapade khaṇḍākhyaguḍakarṣakaḥ dadau pratyekabuddhāya pūrvamikṣurasaudanam  KAvk bhuktenekṣurasānnena tena vātagadārditaḥ pratyekabuddhastatpuṇyaiḥ prasannaḥ susthatāṃ yayau  KAvk rājā prasenajit so yaṃ puṇyavān guḍakarṣakah tena puṇyaprabhāveṇa bhogabhāgī virājate  KAvk upakāraḥ kṛtajñānāṃ nikāraḥ krūracetasām sukṛtāṃśaśca śādhūnāmaplo pyāyātyanalpatām  KAvk sarvajñeneti kathite pūrvapuṇye mahīpateḥ babhūva sukṛtotkarṣe bhikṣurāścaryaniścalah  KAvk atha bhaktyā bhagavataḥ kṛtvā rājādhivāsanām upaninye svayaṃ tāṃ tāṃ surārhāṃ bhogasaṃpadam  KAvk paropacārai rucirairarcite kāñcanāsane sukhopaviṣṭaṃ provāca naranāthastathāgatam  KAvk bhagavan me bhavadbhaktivibhaktasukṛtaśriyaḥ cayah kuśalamūlānāmanirmuktyai bhaviṣyati  KAvk vinayātpārthiveneti pūrṇapuṇyābhimāninā pṛṣṭaḥ smitasitālokaṃ jagāda sugataḥ sṛjan  KAvk rājan saṃsāramārgo yamanādinidhanodbhavaḥ helālaṅghyaḥ kathaṃ puṃsāmaprāpya kleśasaṃkṣayam  KAvk ciraparicitaiścakrāvartairasaktagatāgatiḥprakṛtigahanaḥ saṃsāro yaṃ sukhena na laṅghyate asati hi vinā yogābhyāsaṃ kṣaye kila karmaṇāṃsphuṭaphalatatirdharmo pyasminnibandhanatām gataḥ  KAvk sarvato vinivṛttasya dānābhyāsena bhūyasā mamāpi dharmasaṃsāro babhūva bhūrijanmakṛt  KAvk dhaniko nāma dhanavān vārāṇasyāmabhūtpurā tāpāpahaḥ phalasphīṭaśchāyāvṛkṣa ivārthinām  KAvk durbhikṣakṣapite loke viṣamakleśavihvale bhojyaṃ pratyekabuddhānāṃ so rthitaḥ pañcabhiḥ śataiḥ  KAvk sa teṣāṃ parabhogārhaṃ durbhikṣāvadhi bhojanam akalpayadanalpaśrīḥ koṣṭhāgārī gatasmayaḥ  KAvk śatapañcakasaṃghātairbhoktuṃ tasya gṛhaṃ tataḥ kramātpratyekabuddhānām sahasradvayamāyayau  KAvk tasya tatpuṇyavāsena jāto labdhaphalaśriyā durbhikṣadānajanito ratnakośastadākṣayaḥ  KAvk sukhaṃ sanātanaṃ puṇyabhogyatvaṃ praṇidhānataḥ śāstustataḥ pareṇāyaṃ samyaksaṃbodhimāpitaḥ  KAvk puṇyena pāpena ca veṣṭiteyaṃ saṃsāriṇāṃ karmaphalapravṛttiḥ sitāsitā bandhanarajjureṣā tatsaṃkṣaye mokṣapathaṃ vadanti  KAvk iti kṣitīśaḥ kathitaṃ jinena mohavyapāyena niśamya mokṣam kleśakṣayārhaṃ śamameva matvā puṇyābhimānaṃ śithilīvakāra  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ śālistambāvadānaṃ nāma ṣaṭcatvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  sarvārthasiddhāvadānam svārthapravṛttau vigataspṛhāṇāṃ paropakāre satatodyatānām kleśeṣvabhītā vyasanairanītā vighnairapīḍākarameti siddhiḥ  KAvk śrāvastyāṃ bhagavān pūrvaṃ jino jetavanasthitaḥ dharmākhyānaprasaṅgena bhikṣusaṃghamabhāṣata  KAvk āsīdakhilabhūpālamaulilālitaśāsanah siddhārtho nāma sukṛtī sārvabhaumo mahīpatiḥ  KAvk sāgarākhyasya nāgasya sūnurjaladhivāsinah sarvārthasiddhaḥ putratvaṃ prayayau tasya bhūpateḥ  KAvk sa bhādrakalpiko bodhisattvaḥ sattvojjvalaprabhaḥ jātamātraḥ kṣititalaṃ cakre pūrṇaṃ svaṛddhibhiḥ  KAvk tasya pravardhamānasya dharmasyeva samudyayau samastabhuvanavyāpi vibudhābhyarcitaṃ yaśaḥ  KAvk sa kadācidvarodyāne syandanena yuvā vrajan dadarśa vṛddhapuruṣaṃ devatānirmitaṃ puraḥ  KAvk taṃ vilokya jarājīrṇaṃ jātavairāgyavāsanah saṃsāramiva niḥsāraṃ sa śarīvamamanyata  KAvk udyānayātrāvirataḥ śanaiḥ pratinivṛtya saḥ dāridyravidrutacchāyānadrākṣīt kṛpaṇān pathi  KAvk dṛṣṭvā tānasukhakleṣṭān karuṇākṛṣṭamānasaḥ acintayadaho duḥkhaṃ sahante bhuvi durgatāḥ  KAvk adānaprabhavaṃ duḥkhaṃ vadantīti visaṃgatāḥ pṛthivyāṃ ratnapūrṇāyāṃ parapiṇḍopajīvinaḥ  KAvk idamevāvisaṃvādi cihnaṃ kaluṣakarmaṇām dīnāṃ yadete yācante puruṣaṃ puruṣāḥ param  KAvk aho duṣkṛtameteṣāmavadhūtāḥ pade pade yadete mārgaṇodvignā bhikṣitvāpi bubhukṣitāḥ  KAvk iti saṃcintya suciraṃ viścakleśakṣayodyataḥ yadaridraṃ jagatkartuṃ ratnārthī jaladhiṃ yayau  KAvk kathacidiva saṃsaktaḥ sa pitrā dṛḍhaniścayaḥ smāruhya pravahaṇaṃ ratnadvīpamavāptavān  KAvk tatra pravahaṇārūḍhān vaṇijaḥ sahayāyinaḥ so bravītkriyatām kāmaṃ yuṣmābhirmaṇisaṃgrahaṃ  KAvk etaiḥ sāmānyaratnaistu mama nāsti prayojanam kośe mahānti bhāsvanti santi ratnottamāni naḥ  KAvk kiṃ tu cintāmaṇiprāptyai vipulo yaṃ mamodyamaḥ tena vidrutadāridyrāṃ kartumicchāmi modenīm  KAvk śrutaṃ mayā nāgarājaḥ sāgarākhyo mahodadhau vasatyasti gṛhe tasya cintitārthaprado maṇiḥ  KAvk vilaṅghya viṣamaṃ mārgaṃ tamādātuṃ vrajāmyaham nāsti dhairyasahāyānām durgamaṃ vyavasāyinām  KAvk na ca madvirahe kiṃcid vyasanaṃ vo bhaviṣyati satyameva parārtho yaṃ yadi me sukṛtodyamaḥ  KAvk ityuktvā tān samāmantrya pratasthe sthiraniścayaḥ mahatīṃ dhṛtimālambya sattvavān pārthivātmajaḥ  KAvk gulphamātreṇa saptāhaṃ gatvā gaṅgamavartmanā jānudaghnena saptāhaṃ saptāhaṃ pauruṣeṇa ca  KAvk catvāri saptarātrāṇi tataḥ puṣkariṇījalaiḥ gatvā dṛṣṭiviṣān ghorān dadarśa phaṇinaḥ puraḥ  KAvk maitrīyuktena manasā kṛtvā tānatha nirviṣān krūrakopairvṛtaṃ yakṣairyakṣadvīpamavāpa saḥ  KAvk tatra maitreṇa manasā vītakrodhān vidhāya tān śuśrāva tairabhihitaṃ vipulotsāhavismitaiḥ  KAvk kumāra sphīṭasattvena tathā vīryeṇacāmunā nāgarājasya bhavanaṃ samāhitamavāpya tam  KAvk kālena samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ sarvajñastvaṃ bhaviṣyasi śrāvakāśca bhaviṣyāmo vayaṃ tvadanuyāyinaḥ  KAvk prasannairiti tairuktamabhinandya nṛpātmajaḥ rakṣevarāvṛtaṃ prāpa rākṣasadvīpamutkaṭam  KAvk tathaiva vigatakrūravikāraistaiḥ sa pūjitaḥ bhūjotkṣepeṇa nikṣiptaḥ kṣaṇānnāgendrasadmāni  KAvk sa tatra dīptavibhave divyotsāsasukhocitaḥ aśṛṇoddīrghaduḥkhārtisūcakaṃ rodanadhvanim  KAvk sa tamākarṇya sodvegaḥ prakṛtyaiva dayārdradhīḥ kimetaditi papraccha dṛṣṭvāgre nāgakanyakām  KAvk sā taṃ babhāṣe saṃsaktaśokoṣmapiśunairmuhuḥ mlānayantīṃ svaniśvāsaurbimbādharadalatviṣam  KAvk guṇāvān nāgarājasya putraḥ kamalalocanaḥ jyoṣṭhaḥ sarvārthasiddhākhyaḥ priyaḥ pañcatvamāgataḥ  KAvk tataḥ pratigatānande vinivṛttasukhotsave dhanena rodanenāsminna bhavedbhavane sthitiḥ  KAvk iti tasyā vacaḥ śrutvā so ntaḥ paricitāṃ vahan svadeśadarśanaprāpto nāgarājāntikaṃ yayau  KAvk nāgarājastamāyāntaṃ parijñāya priyāsakhaḥ ehyehi putreti vadan babhūvānandavihvalaḥ  KAvk martyajanmakathām tena svaṃ cāgamanakāraṇam śrutvā niveditaṃ nāgaḥ pariṣvajya jagāda tam  KAvk cintāmaṇirayaṃ putra mama maulivibhūṣaṇam gṛhyatām tava saṃkalpaṃ na vandhyaṃ kartumutsahe  KAvk deyaḥ kṛtajagatkṛtyo mamaivāyaṃ punastvayā ityuktvāsmai dadau divyacūḍaṃ ratna vimucya saḥ  KAvk hṛṣṭaḥ praṇamya nāgendraṃ yayau pravahaṇāntikam  KAvk samudradevatā tatra taṃ dṛṣṭvā śrutatatkathā uvāca kīdṛśaḥ sādho prāptaścintāmaṇīstvayā  KAvk samudre patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā ratnaṃ kṛcchratarārjitam sa jagāda dṛḍhodyogavaiphalyodveganiścalaḥ  KAvk aho guṇocitākārā praṇayānmṛduvādinī vidveṣakaluṣaṃ karma kṛtvā tvaṃ na vilajjase  KAvk parotkarṣeṣu saṃgharṣaśokakleśamupaiti yaḥ śītalā api tasyaitā jvālāvalayitā diśaḥ  KAvk paritsāhaḥ priyo yasya tasya sattvamahodadheḥ karpūradhavalaṃ dhatte trilokītilakaṃ yaśaḥ  KAvk devi prayaccha me ratnamasmādvirama pātakāt apavādalatāṃ karma na sādhoradhirohhati  KAvk lobhātpramādāddveṣādvā ratnaṃ cenna prayacchasi śoṣayāmyeṣa jaladhiṃ tadimaṃ te samāśrayam  KAvk ityuktvā pyasakṛttena sā ratne na dadau yadā sa tadā svaprabhāveṇa śoṣāyābdheḥ samudyayau  KAvk dhyātamātraṃ sahasrākṣavacasā viśvakarmaṇā nirmitaṃ sahasā tasya patramāvirabhutkare  KAvk sa tenāgastyaculukākāreṇāmbhaḥ payonidheḥ antarīkṣe samutkṣipya cikṣepa kṣamaṇodyataḥ  KAvk kṛte bhūbhāgaśeṣe bdhau tenātyadbhutakāriṇā suranirbhartsitā bhītā devatāsmai maṇīṃ dadau  KAvk nirvyājaṃ sāhasaṃ dīptiṃ ratnānāmiva tattvataḥ prabhāvaṃ vetti mahatāṃ mantrāṇāṃ tapasāṃ ca kaḥ  KAvk sphārastāvadapāravārivirasavyāpārahelābalātkallolāvaliyantritāmbaratayā ratnākaraḥ śrūyate gambhīraḥ punaraprameyamahimā ko pi prabhāvaḥ satāṃyasmin vismayadhāmni cintanavidhāvante plavante dhiyaḥ  KAvk tataścintāmaṇiṃ buddhvā nijasārthena saṃgataḥ rājasūnuḥ svanagaraṃ prāpa pūrṇamanorathaḥ  KAvk kṛtakṛtyaḥ prahṛṣṭenaḥ sa pitrā tatra pūjitaḥ dhvajāgre ratnamādhāya jagāda janasaṃsadi  KAvk parārtha eva yatno yaṃ nātmārtho yadi me kkacit tena satyena loko ya sarvaṃ yātvadaridratām  KAvk ityukte sattvanidhinā tena dīnadayālunā ratnavṛṣṭiraparyantā nipapāta mahītale  KAvk tena ratnasamūhena dikṣu sarvāsu bhāsvatā yayau janasya dāridyramayaṃ niḥśeṣatāṃ tamaḥ  KAvk āśāpāśavatāṃ balāptraviśatāṃ bāhyāṅgaṇaṃ śrīmatāṃdvāḥsthāghātavatām muhurvicalatāṃ dvārodare sīdatām dīrghairniḥśvasitaiḥ śucā nipatitāṃ dehakṣayaṃ kāṅkṣatāṃdīnānāṃ maṇirāśiraśmiśabalaḥ śrīsaṃgamaḥ ko pyabhūt  KAvk tacchāsanāduraganāyakameva yāte cintāmaṇau vigatadainyajane ca loke sarvatra dānarasikasya janasya cetaḥ sarvārthisārthaviratākulitaṃ babhūva  KAvk sarvārthasiddhaḥ kṣitipālasūnuḥ yo bhūtsa evāhamihānyadehaḥ śrutvetivṛttaṃ kathitaṃ jinena te bhikṣavastanmayatāmavāpuḥ  KAvk iti kṣemendraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ sarvārthasiddhāvadānaṃ satpacatvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ  hastakāvadānam mattebhakumbhoccakucābhirāmāḥ karpūrahārāṃśuvilāsahāsāḥ prītipradāḥ puṇyavatāṃ bhavanti prauḍhā yuvatyaśca vibhūtayaśca  KAvk tathāgate bhagavati śrāvastyāṃ vanacāriṇi abhavatsuprabuddhākhyaḥ śrīmān gṛhapatiḥ purā  KAvk babhūva hastako nāma tasyātidayitaḥ sutaḥ pūrvārjitānāṃ puṇyānāṃ sākāra iva saṃcayaḥ  KAvk tasya janmadine jātaścāmīkaramayo mahān ekībhūta ivāścaryavrajaḥ pravarakuñcaraḥ  KAvk sa gajendraḥ kumāraśca tatpituśca manorathaḥ lokakautukakośāśca pūrṇatāṃ tyulyamāyayuḥ  KAvk sa śaśīva śiśuḥ kāle kalānilayatāṃ gataḥ ruruce rucimān sarvalokalocanabāndhavaḥ  KAvk sa śanaiḥ pūritābhogabhujastambhavibhūṣaṇam lebhe manobhavārambhabhavanaṃ navayauvanam  KAvk kadācidatha bhūbhartuḥ sa prasenajitaḥ sutām tanucīvaracihnena sahajena virājitām  KAvk kanyāṃ cīvarakanyākhyāṃ lāvaṇyalalitānanām udyānadarśanāyātāṃ dadarśāyatalocanām  KAvk akliṣṭarūpāmālokya tāmaparyuṣitadyutim vismayasmarayostulyamāyayau sahasā vaśam  KAvk so cintayadaho kāntamidamatyadbhutaṃ vapuḥ yasmin bhāti mukhavyājādadoṣaviśadaḥ śaśī  KAvk lāvaṇyamapratimameva bibhati tanvī bandhūkabandhuradharo madhurasvabhāvaḥ drohodyataḥ sarasavidrumapallavānāṃ bimbaprabhāprasabhabhramavandhyakāraḥ  KAvk vakrkraṃ na kṣamate madaṃ śaśamṛtaḥ kleśnāti kāntiḥ sudhāmutphullotpalakānanasya kurute dṛṣṭiḥ prabhābhrtsanam manye manmathasaṃgamocitatanoḥ sāptnyabhītipradālīlāyāsyāḥ sahasā vilāsalaharīśoṣaṃ vidhatte rateḥ  KAvk udvṛtte kaṭhine parodharayuge naśyadviveke ciraṃyasyā doṣamaye pyaho guṇavatā hāreṇa baddhā sthitiḥ yaccāsminnavalambate mbujadhiyā rolambarekhā mukhelolākṣyāḥ kimapi praśāntanayane līnaṃ munīnāṃ manaḥ  KAvk iti cintayatastasya vapuḥ puṣpaśaropamam vilokya bhūpatisutā babhūvāścaryaniścalā  KAvk hṛte lajjāṃśuke tasyāḥ smareṇa smitakāriṇā pratyagrapulakākīrṇaṃ vapuḥ spaṣṭamadṛśyata  KAvk ruddhā navābhilāṣeṇa vailakṣyeṇa nivartitā manastatraiva nikṣipya sā śūnyeva śanairyayau  KAvk rājadhānīṃ samāsādya lajjāvismayamanmathaiḥ mīliteva nilīneva proṣiteva babhūva sā  KAvk kumāro pi svabhavane samudbhūtamanobhāvḥ tāmevendumukhīmagre saṃkalpairalikhanmuhuḥ  KAvk sa tāṃ mānasasarvasvaṃ smaravidyāmiva smaran pradadhyau kurlabhām matvā tanayām cakravartinaḥ  KAvk janmāntare tanuryasya tapaḥparicitā ciram dhanyaḥ sa tāmavāpnoti latāṃ sukṛtaśākhinaḥ  KAvk ramyapradānapuṇyena taddarśanamavāpyate na jāne tāni puṇyāni yeṣāṃ tatsaṃgamaḥ phalam  KAvk tadvakrkraśītakiraṇasmaraṇotsavenatasyāśca durlabhatayā virahoṣmaṇā me no vedmi kiṃ dhṛtiriyaṃ kimayaṃ vimohaḥkiṃ jīvitaṃ kimasubhiḥ sahaḥ viprayogaḥ  KAvk tadvakrkrabjajitaḥ prasahra bhajate kṣaiṇyaṃ kṣapāvallabhaḥtadbhūvibhramalajjitaṃ ca vinatiṃ dhate dhanurmānmatham tasyāh pallavapeśaladyutimuṣā śoṣādhareṇārditaṃnūnaṃ prāpya parājayaṃ vanamahīṃ bimba samālambate  KAvk iti pūrṇenduvadanāvadanadhyānaniścalah niśāṃ nināya saṃtyaktaḥ serṣyayeva sanidrayā  KAvk kanyādarśanavṛttāntaṃ tatastena niveditam śrutvā pitāsya saṃkrantacintāparicito bhavat  KAvk sa tamūce vayaṃ putra rājño sya puravāsinah sa kathaṃ te duhitaraṃ cakravartī pradāsyati  KAvk aśakyaṃ naiva kurvanti samīhante na durlabham asaṃbhāvyaṃ na bhāṣante mānakāmā manīṣiṇaḥ  KAvk cūtacampakavallīṣu svādhīnāsu nirādaraḥ cintayan pārijātasya latām śuṣyati ṣaṭpadaḥ  KAvk tava tasyāśca saṃbandhaḥ prājganmavihito yadi tadavaśyaṃ bhavatyeva niṣprayatnaphalodayah  KAvk āśāpāśairanākṛṣṭaṃ vicārairakadarthitam prayatnabhārairaśrāntaṃ vidhatte bhavitavyatā  KAvk ityākarṇya piturvākyaṃ tattatheti vicintayan na cetaḥ kanyakānītaṃ samānetuṃ śaśāka saḥ  KAvk sa gatvā dantayugalaṃ yayāce hemakuñcaram navasaṃdarśane rājñaḥ prītiyogyamupāyanam  KAvk puṇyabandhena kariṇā dattaṃ dantayugaṃ tataḥ sa hemamayamādāya draṣṭuṃ bhūmipatiṃ yayau  KAvk sa ratnaruciraṃ prāpya bhavanaṃ pṛthivīpateḥ praviśyaḥ praṇataḥ prītyai hemadantadvayaṃ dadau  KAvk bhūbhujā viśrutaguṇaḥ prasādenābhinanditaḥ varaṃ gṛhāṇetyuktaśca sa na jagrāha kiṃcana  KAvk tasyādīnadyuteścakre mānamabhyadhikaṃ nṛpaḥ aucityacārucaritaḥ priyaḥ kasya na niḥspṛhaḥ  KAvk sa sadā darśane rājñaḥ kāñcanāṅgāni dantinaḥ punarjātanavāṅgena dattāṇi prīyate dadau  KAvk tamuvāca mahīpālaḥ sevāpraṇayayantritaḥ dūtīṃ manaḥprasādaya vadanadyutimudvahan  KAvk prabhūtahemasaṃbhārāṃ gurvīṃ sovāmimāmaham na sahe prauravārgo hi bhavaṇīyo mahībhṛtām  KAvk saṃvibhajya janānītaiḥ kā prītirmama kāñcanaiḥ tavānarghaguṇā mūrtiriyameva mama priyā  KAvk lobhaḥ puruṣaratneṣu bhūṣaṇārheṣu śobhate rājñāṃ kośeṣu sīdanti hemaratnāśmasaṃcayāḥ  KAvk samīhitatamaṃ tubhyaṃ kiṃ prayacchāmi kathyatām niḥśeṣakośadānena na nāmānuśayo stu me  KAvk rājñṃ dṛkpātapātreṇa prāpyante yadi na śriyaḥ tadanarthaṃ gatārthinyā ko thaḥ pārthivasevayā  KAvk ityuktaḥ kṣitipālena kumāraḥ kalitāñjaliḥ tamabhāṣata bhūpāla dātumarhati ko paraḥ  KAvk anarthitena ratnāni vibudhebhyaḥ prayacchatā tadunnidraṃ samudrasya mudritaṃ bhavatā yaśaḥ  KAvk mahatāpi prayatnena pūryate na mahāśayaḥ alpakānāṃ tadairśvaryaṃ dāridyaṃ tanmahīyasām  KAvk kiṃ tu tvadbhujaguptānāṃ dharmamārgeṇa jīvatāṃ janānāṃ nāsti dāridyaṃ draviṇaṃ yena mṛgyate  KAvk dhanārthino na tu vayaṃ na ca sevādhikāriṇaḥ dhanaṃ dhanaṃ dhanadhiyāṃ māna eva manasvinām  KAvk mīladguṇena parameśvarasevanena nurmūlatām sumanasāṃ sahasā gatānām dainyātpunaḥ kṛpaṇapaṇyapathe cyutānāṃ na sparśamātramapi sādhujanaḥ karoti  KAvk arthitvānmaraṇam varaṃ tanubhṛtām dainyāvasannātmanāṃarthī sarvajanāvamānavasatiḥ satkārayogyaḥ śavaḥ kumbhastāvadadhah prayāti guṇavān kūpāvatāre paraṃyāvanmohatamaḥpraveśavivaśaḥ prāpto rthitā lambate  KAvk sāmānyā dhanasaṃpadaḥ krayakṛṣiprāpyā sadā dhīmatāṃsaṃtoṣo yadi nāsti tatkimaparā bhūmirnidhānāvṛtā santyevātiśayaprasādaniratāstā hemaratnakriyāḥkasyeṣṭaḥ priyasaṃgamāya vapuṣāṃ sevāmayo vikrayaḥ  KAvk ityapāradhiyastasya vacaḥ śrutvā mahīpatiḥ gṝhyatāmaparaṃ kiṃcidityabhāṣata sādaraḥ  KAvk aucityacaturālāpaḥ karkaśo pi nṛpāṃ priyaḥ kṛpaṇaścāṭukāro pi karṇaśūlāya kevalaḥ  KAvk aurdāryaparituṣṭena sa rājñabhyarthitaḥ param tamūce yadu tuṣṭo si sutā mahyaṃ pradīyatām  KAvk ityukte tena nṛpatiḥ saṃdehāndolitāśayaḥ prātarvaktāhamityuktvā kṣaṇaṃ kṣmātalamaikṣata  KAvk sa kumāraṃ visṛjyātha pradhānāmātyamabravīt prasādarabhasenaiva kṛtaṃ vākcāpalaṃ mayā  KAvk cakravartikulotpannā kanyā puṇyapaṇocitā kathaṃ sāmānyapaurāya guṇamātreṇa dīyate  KAvk dadāmīti pratiśrutya paścādanuśayākulaḥ kathaṃ sarādhano bhūtvā bhaviṣyāmyarthiniṣphalaḥ  KAvk kathaṃ prāptasya tasyāhaṃ prātardraṣṭ mukhaṃ puraḥ priyo pyapriyatāṃ yātaḥ sa me durlabhayecchayā  KAvk nūnaṃ guṇopapanno pi prakṛtyaiva śarīriṇām vakti yāvanna dehīti tāvadgavati vallabhah  KAvk iti bhūmipateḥ śrutvāḥ vaco dolāvalambinaḥ tamuvāca mahāmātyaḥ saṃcintyāvasarocitam  KAvk anālocitaparyantāḥ pratyagrasarasādarāḥ svabhāvarabhasā eva bhavanti prabhubuddhayaḥ  KAvk aśakyārthanayā tena lubdheneva guṇodayaḥ rājasevāpravṛttena hemahastī vināśitaḥ  KAvk vācyo sau bhavatā svairaṃ kanyārthī punarāgataḥ hemahastinamāruhya prāptaḥ prāpsyasi me sutām  KAvk tenotkṛttaḥ svahastena kutastasya sa kuñjaraḥ na cāsau tadvirahitaḥ punarāyāti lajjayā  KAvk ityamātyasya vacasā nṛpatiryuktimāśritaḥ prāptaṃ kumāramanyedyustadevābhimukho vadat  KAvk kumāro pi gṝhaṃ gatvā vivāhocitamaṅgalaiḥ haumadviradamāruhya svajanena sajāyayau  KAvk svarṇavāraṇasaṃrūḍhaṃ tamāyāntaṃ mahīpatiḥ vilokyāścaryavibhavaṃ mene puṇyavatāṃ varam  KAvk kautukādatha bhūpālastaṃ gajaṃ hemavigraham āruroha mahotsāhaḥ sumerumiva vajrabhṛt  KAvk ārūḍhe pṛthivīpāle na cacāla sa kuñjaraḥ prasarsarpa kumāreṇa punaścālaṃkṛtāsanaḥ  KAvk taṃ jñātvā nṛpatirdevaṃ tatprabhāveṇa vismitaḥ dhanyo smīti vadan kanyāṃ dadau tasmai smaraśriyam  KAvk abhyarcya kanyāratnena nṛpatiḥ puruṣottamam harṣotsavasamuddhūtaḥ sudhāsindhurivābabhau  KAvk tataḥ kumāre dayitāmādāya svagṛhaṃ gate saphalo bhūdanaṅgasya kārmukākarṣaṇaśramaḥ  KAvk nave vayasi bhogārhe navakāntāsamāgame tasyābhūdvibhavodāraḥ sadā navanavotsavaḥ  KAvk tataḥ kadācidbhūpālaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ prasenajit puṇyaprabhāvaṃ jāmātuḥ kalayan samacintayat  KAvk aho divyaḥ prabhāvo sau kumārasya pradṛśyate na hi sāmānyapuṇyānāṃ pāko bhavati tadvidhaḥ  KAvk kulaṃ lakṣmīharmyaṃ hṛtaśaśimadā rūpalaharīvayaḥ saṃbhogārhaṃ guṇaparicayo bhūṣaṇacayaḥ yaśaḥ puṇyodyānaprasṛtakusumollāsaruciraṃna vidmaḥ kasyāyaṃ kuśalapariṇāmasya vibhavaḥ  KAvk iti saṃcintya suciraṃ sa saṃjātakutūhalaḥ sarvajñadarśanāvaddhamāruroha manoratham  KAvk sa jātātaramāhūya sutāṃ ca sacivaiḥ saha bhagavantaṃ yayau draṣṭuṃ manasā prathamaṃ gataḥ  KAvk yāte dṛṣṭipathaṃ jetavane saṃtyajya vāhanam upasṛtyaḥ nṛpaḥ padbhyāṃ bhagavantaṃ vyalokayat  KAvk sa taṃ praṇamya tatpādapadmabhūtiśikhāmaṇiḥ sutāṃ jāmātaraṃ cāsmai namro nāmnā nyavedayat  KAvk upaviṣṭeṣu sarveṣu praṇāmānatamauliṣu papraccha rājā sarvajñaṃ bhagavantaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ  KAvk ayaṃ guṇagaopetaḥ kumāraḥ śrīmatāṃ varaḥ haimeva dantināyāto bhagavan kena karmaṇā  KAvk iyaṃ cīvarakanyā ca matsutāsya navā vadhūḥ kena puṇyaprabhāveṇa jīvitādadhivallabhā  KAvk iti pṛṣṭaḥ kṣitīśena sarvavidbhagavān jinaḥ tamūce bhūpate puṃsāṃ puṇyodbhūtā vibhūtayaḥ  KAvk yadudāro yaducito yad bhrājiṃṣṇu yadadbhutam spṛhaṇīyaṃ ca yalloke tattatpuṇyasamudbahvam  KAvk vipaśvī bhagavān pūrvaṃ sugataḥ saha bhikṣubhiḥ cacāra lokakṛpayā rājño bandhumataḥ pure  KAvk tasminnavasare tatra kumāryā saha dārakaḥ vikrīḍāvartmani puraḥ kṛtvā dārumayaṃ gajam  KAvk tau vilokya samāyāntaṃ dhmātajambūnadadyutim phullapadmadalākārakaruṇāsnigdhalocanam  KAvk bhagavantaṃ samudbhūtatadbhaktisarasonmukhau krīḍāgajaṃ nivedyāsmai praṇatau tasthatuḥ puraḥ  KAvk bhagavānapi sarvajñastayorjñātvā manoratham dayayā caraṇasparśaṃ vidadhe dārudantinaḥ  KAvk samyak cittaprasādena dṛṣṭau bhagavatātha tau praṇīdhānaṃ vivāhāya cakraturdārakau mithaḥ  KAvk kulaprabhāvavibhavairbhūyājjanma mamocitam vāhanaṃ hemadantī ca kumārasyetyabhūnmatiḥ  KAvk dṛṣṭvā bhagavataḥ kanyā saṃsaktre cārucīvare janmacīvarayuktāṃ syāmahametacintayat  KAvk sa eṣa praṇidhānena jātasteneha hastakaḥ iyaṃ cīvarakanyā ca tanucīvaralakṣaṇa  KAvk iti kṣrutvā kṣitipatistadvṛttaṃ sugato ditam mukuṭaspṛṣṭatatpādapadmaḥ svabhavanaṃ yayau  KAvk yāte savismayaṃ rājñi kumāraḥ saha jāyayā kathyamānaṃ bhagavatā dharmaṃ śuśrāva śuddhadhīḥ  KAvk tatastau jātavairāgyau kṣīṇasaṃsāravāsanau pravrajyayā jitakleśau śuddhāṃ bodhimavāpatuḥ  KAvk vitatasukṛtapuṇyābhyāsayogena puṃsāṃ bhavati kuśalabhājāṃ dharmakāmārthasaṃpat abhimatamatha bhuktvā tatphalaṃ sadārāste vighanagaganakāntiṃ śāntimante bhajante  KAvk iti kṣemandraviracitāyāṃ bodhisattvāvadānakalpalatāyāṃ hastakāvadānamaṣṭacatvāriṃśaḥ pallavaḥ
